NVTP_1.1.1.1–1.1.1.2^1	mātar sarasvati punar punar aṣa natvā baddhāñjaliḥ kim api vijñapayāmi avaihi vāc cetasoḥ mama tathā bhava sāvadhānāḥ vācaspateḥ vacasi na skhalataḥ yathā ete viśva ārādhyaḥ iti atra viśva śabdena saṃsāri cetana vargaḥ vivakṣitaḥ tasya eva tad ārādhaka tvāt viśveśānaḥ iti atra samīhita phala saṃdohaḥ tasya bhagavat eka adhīna tvāt viśva kṛt iti atra upādāna samūhaḥ tasya eva tad kṛti vyāpya tvāt viśva saṃhāra kārī iti atra yāvat anitya nivahaḥ tasya eva tad vināśya tvāt viśva śaktiḥ iti atra yāvat kāryāḥ tomaḥ tasya eva tad śakti viṣaya tvāt viśvajñātā iti atra yāvan jñeya prapañcaḥ tasya eva pad jñāna viṣaya tvāt viśva vyāpīyatra yāvat mūrttimat dravya rāśiḥ tasya eva viśeṣataḥ tat vyāpya tvāt 
NVTP_1.1.1.2^2	 itarasya tu tad dvārā viśvamūrtiḥ iti atra yāvat kāraka grāmaḥ tasya eva sākṣāt tad prayatna adhiṣṭheya tayā asmad ādi śarīra samāna tvāt atas eva na tatra śarīra antara apekṣā sākṣāt prayantān adhiṣṭheyeṣu hi sā syāt daṇḍa ādi vat na tu sākṣāt prayatna adhiṣṭheyeṣu śarīra vat pinākī iti tu viśiṣṭa śastradhāradham ittaka nāma saṃkortanena prārabdha vighnasya protsāraṇam eva samīhitam iti sūcayati hetu hetumat bhāvena śaḍka uttarābhyām yojanā jyāyasī yathā avasthita yojanāyām tu artha pauna rūkti aprasarktā stuti tvam eva samādhāna madhyavaseyam iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.3	 namāmi ityādi dharmaḥ nivartakaḥ vijñānam śarīra ādi vivikta ātma sākṣātkāraḥ vairāgyam rāga abhāvaḥ aiśvaryam bhūta indriya jayaḥ tat śānipe atas eva nidhaye vāc viśat hīnām adharma hetukaḥ hi avivekaḥ aviveka hetukam avairāgyam avairāgya mūlam anaiśvaryam tad mūlāḥ ca vacasām aviśuddhayaḥ tisraḥ khalu etāḥ tatra prathamā nirabhidhayatā dvitīyā viparīta āmidheya tā tṛtīyā niṣprayojanāmigheya tā tāḥ etāḥ katham bhūta indriya jayinaḥ mahā muneḥ bhaviṣyanti ajita bhūtasya hi vivakṣoḥ tathāvidha prayatna aniṣpatteḥ nirabhidheyā vāc bhavati ajita indriyasya ca viparyāsa vipralipsā hetukaḥ viparīta arthaḥ vacana sandarbhaḥ ajita manasaḥ ca pramāda unmādavataḥ niṣprayojanaḥ etāḥ ca vacasām aviśuddhīḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthāneṣu sūtrakāraḥ eva prapañcayiṣyati saḥ ayam na tathā iti bhavati vāc viśuddhīnām nidhiḥ atas eva tāyī tattva adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇa kṣama saṃpradāya pravartakaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.4	 evam parāpara gurūn natvā śiṣya buddhi samādhānāya samāhita vaiśiṣṭyam darśayati grantha iti nanu tātparyaṭīka iti vadatā pravṛtti pāṭava artham grantha saṃkṣepaḥ darśitaḥ na ca śiṣyāṇām kathantā saṃbogha vidhurāṇām rāddhānta mātra parigrahaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ vivakṣitaḥ tathā tve vā upaniṣadaḥ eva santu santu vā śava muṣṭi nyāyena ācārya upadeśāḥ kim anena iti atas āha nirasta akhila dūṣaṇa iti nanu evam grantha tātparyām vyākhyeyam dūṣaṇāni ca nirasyāni iti punar api grantha gauravam iti atas āha grantha vyākhyā= chalena eva iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.5	 nanu cirantare asmin nibandhe mahājana parigṛhīte bahavaḥ nibandhāḥ tathāvidhāḥ santi iti kṛtam anene iti atas āha icchāmi iti nanu yadi granthakāra saṃpradāya vicchedena te nibandhāḥ katham kunibandhāḥ atha saṃpradāyaḥ vicchinnaḥ katham tava api iyam vicchinna saṃpradāyā tātparyaṭīkā su nibandhaḥ iti atas āha ati jaratīnām iti uddyota kara saṃpradāyaḥ hi amūṣām yauvanam tat ca kāla paripāka vaśāt galitam iva kim nāma atra trilocana guroḥ sakāśāt upadeśa rasāyanam āsāditamamūṣām punarnavībhāvāya dīyate iti yujyate na ca kunibandha paṅka magnānām tat dātum ucita matas tasmāt utkṛṣya sva nibandha sthale sanniveśana rūpa samuddharaṇam eva sāṃpratam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.6^1	 tatra bhagavataḥ akṣapādasya muniṣu madhye pravara tvam śruti ādibhyaḥ eva su prasiddham kim anena saṃkīrtanena na ca etat atiśayena sāṃpratam upayujyate jagat upaśama nidāna śāstra praṇetṛ tvam ca tasya tad praṇayanam eva prakaṭayat asti tena api kim prakaṭitena sva nibandhasya tat viṣaya tā api tad vyākhyānāt eva labhyate iti kim tayā api kathitayā na ca asya nyāya mahodadheru utta ānatā pratibhāsaḥ eva agratas kartum ucitaḥ tasmāt bhavitavyam atra tātparyeṇa tat āha atha iti tat apanīyate iti tat iti diś rāga ādi samutthāpitam śāstra ācchādakam kuhetu saṃtama samapaneya tvena parāmṛśatā śāstrasya eva ayam nibandhaḥ iti darśitam 
NVTP_1.1.1.6^2	 bhāṣyasya ca tad vivaraṇa rūpasya śāstra śarīra rūpa tayā na śāstrāt ādhikyam manyate mīmāṃsāyāḥ iva vedāt atas eva na atratyaṭīkāyāḥ vāttikāntena virodhaḥ etena śāstrasya yaḥ nibandhaḥ bhāṣya granthaḥ sa ku tārkikā jñāna nivṛtti hetuḥ kariṣyate iti vyākhyānam ṭīkā virodhena upekṣaṇīyam nanu sūtra ukta prayojana anuvādaḥ punar kim artham na hi idam anūdya kiñcid vidheyam pratiṣedhyam vā iha vidyate iti atas āha sūtra iti atha sva nibandhasya prayojana vattā pradarśanena kim siddhi ati iti atas āha prekṣāvat iti nanu vyutpitsavaḥ vyutpattim aghikṛtya pravartante atas vyutpādana pravṛttau vyutpattiḥ eva amīṣām prayojanam iti kim apareṇa prayojanena iti atas āha vyutpāda mātrasya iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.7–1.1.1.8	 dvividham hi prayojanam mukhyam gauṇa ca tatra mukhyam puruṣa arthaḥ eva itarat tu tad aṅgam iti tatra mukhya arthinaḥ tad sādhānam abhyarthayamānāḥ tatra pravartante iti tat api prayojanam evati atas mukhye prayojane sati gauṇam prayojanam tasmiḥ tu asati tat api na syāt iti niṣprayojana tā eva avatiṣṭhate na ca svātantryeṇa eva asya mukhyam prayojanam asti iti atas yasya idam aṅga tasya mukhyam prayojanam asti iti darśite prekṣāvān pravarttitaḥ bhavati iti abhisandhiḥ vārttika kṛtaḥ iti arthaḥ itas api ṭīkā khaṇḍalakāt antar bhāvita phala vat sannidhauvaphalam tat aṅgam iti nyāyāt śāstra aṅgām eva idam na bhāṣya aṅgam iti mantavyam na hi bhāṣyasya svātantryeṇa mukhyam prayojanam asti yena vārttikam tad aṅga tām iyāt tasmāt yathāśruti sundaram iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.9^1	 nanu karmendriya niyamaḥ śamaḥ iti su prasiddham śāntaḥ dāntaḥ ityādi upaniṣatsu na ca asau puruṣa arthaḥ atas na mukhyam prayojanam iti atas āha atra ca iti nanu jagataḥ śamāya iti durghaṭam asaṃbhāvitā tvāt aśakyā tvāt ca na tāvat kaścid jagat upacikīrṣuḥ kvacid pravartate yatas muneḥ api tathātvam saṃbhāvayāmaḥ paṭhanti ca muneḥ api vanasthasya ityādi na ca śakyam etat bubhukṣūṇām pravartayitum aśakyatvāt na ca jagat eva mumukṣati tasmāt anuṣṭhātā eva vyutpādyaḥ śāstra antara labdha brāhmaṇa tva dirūpaḥ śiṣyaḥ tasya ca rūpāṇi śama dama ādi saṃpattiḥ nitya anitya vivekaḥ aihikā muṣmika bhāga vairāgyam mumukṣutā ca iti yaḥ tu anadhikārī eva pravartate karma kāṇḍaḥ iva brahma kāṇḍe sa na phala bhāj bhavati 
NVTP_1.1.1.9^2	 tatra etat syāt na tāvat upeya viṣayeyam adhikāra cintā tasya puruṣa prayatna aviṣaya tvāt iṣyamāṇa tā mātrasya ca aniṣadhāt kim nāma upāya viṣayāḥ tasya eva śāstra viṣaya tvāt puruṣa pravṛtti viṣaya tvāt ca iha ca apavargaḥ iva tad artha tayā tattva jñānam api upeyam eva asiddha tvāt upāyaḥ tu pramāṇam na ca veda adhyayana vat anumānasya pratyakṣasya ca upādānam śūdra ādikam prati niṣiddham yena tatra api etasya an adhikāraḥ syāt tathā sati dhūmāt api vahim adhigacchan pratyakṣāt vā pratyavāyī syāt adhīyānaḥ iva vedam na ca ātma gocare pratyakṣa anumāne śūdra ādeḥ viśeṣataḥ niṣiddhe snātasya caṇḍāla darśanam iva brāhmaṇa ādeḥ prāyaścitta anupadeśāt pratyuta 
NVTP_1.1.1.10–1.1.1.11^1	 striyaḥ vaiśyāḥ tathā śūdrāḥ ye ca anye pāpa yonayaḥ ityādi smṛteḥ adhikāraḥ eva avasīyate tasmāt yathā saḥ eva viśiṣṭaḥ svargaḥ vaidika yāga ādi anadhikṛtena api upāya antareṇa traivarṇika śuśrūṣā ādinā sādhyate tathā upāya anteṇa anumāna ādinā yadi ātma adhigamaḥ kriyate śūdreṇa api tadā kīdṛśaḥ doṣaḥ satyam kim tu anumānam api āgama avirodhena anusandhīyamānam atha niścāyakam na tu tad viruddham api yat āha yat tu pratyakṣa āgama viruddham nyāya ābhāsaḥ saḥ iti sa ca āgama avirodhāt avirodha niścayaḥ tad artha niścaya adhīnaḥ tatra ca anadhikṛtaḥ eva ayam śūdrāti tad nirapekṣaḥ tu anumāna mātra śaraṇaḥ nara śiraḥ pāvitrya ādi vat anartham eva samāsādayet 
NVTP_1.1.1.11^2	 tasmāt āgama eka vākya tayā pravṛtte śāstre tad adhikārī eva adhikārī iti śūdra ādayaḥ anadhikṛtāḥ iva atas yāvat adhikāri paraḥ ayam jagat śabdaḥ iti kecid tatra āha parama kārūṇikaḥ hi iti santi eva hi kecid karuṇā mṛdu manasaḥ yeṣām jagat eva mitram anyathā bhūtevaḥ abhayam dattvā iti vidhi vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ niṣkāraṇam eva para duḥkha prahāṇa icchā kāruṇyam sā ca yathā ekam duḥkhita paśyataḥ bhavati tathā jagat eva duḥkhita paśyataḥ kim na syāt bhavati ced tad prahāṇa upāya pravṛttau kā nāma anupapattiḥ nanu 
NVTP_1.1.1.12–1.1.1.15	 karuṇā ārdra hṛdayaḥ apyam vyutpisum ā iva vyutpādayet na tu viparītam na hi badhireṣu gāyanaḥ gāyati iti atas āha tatra yadi na kaścid iti na hi rogī mandabhāgya tayā caraka ādi upadeśe na pravartate iti tad artha tā tasya nivartate iti arthaḥ nanu anadhikṛta vyutpādane pratyavāya mātrakam apaśyan= ayam katham avadheya vacanaḥ syāt paśyan vā na pravarteta kāruṇika tayā paśyan= api pravartate ced pramādī syāt tathā ca para lokāt abibhyataḥ asya vacane kaḥ śraddhā asyati iti atas āha na ca iti yadi api prahīna moha tvāt eva asya pāpa puṇyayoḥ utpattiḥ eva na asti vakṣyati hi na pravṛttiḥ pratisandhānāya hīna kleśasya iti tathā api kleśa hāneḥ durūha tvāt pratyavāya utpattim abhyupagamya tad abhāvāya tapaḥ prabhāvaḥ uktaḥ nanu evam api prakṣālanāt hi paṅkasya dūrāt asparśanam varam 
NVTP_1.1.1.16	 iti atas āha tathā ca iti na hi gāḥ paṅka magnāḥ paṅka pralepa bhayāt anukampā paravaśāḥ samarthāḥ na uddharanti api tu uddhṛtya paḍkam prakṣālayanti iti arthaḥ nanu yadi anadhikṛtaḥ katham phala bhāgī tathā ced katham anadhikṛtaḥ iti abhisandhāya uktam prapañcayati tapaḥ prabhāvaḥ eva hi iti yathā hi teṣām tapaḥ prabhāvāt evaṃvidhāḥ pāpmānaḥ vilīyante tathā tapaḥ prabhāvāt eva satya saṃkalpa tayā anadhikāriṇaḥ api phala bhāginaḥ iti na kaścid virodhaḥ na ca phala apekṣayā teṣām anadhikāraḥ kim tarhi karma apekṣayā anadhikṛtena tu kṛtam karma viguṇam sat na phalāṃya paryāptam iti api na viśiṣṭa yājaka sāt guṇyāt eva tasya paripūrṇa tvāt yājakaḥ eva tvayā ājyam yājayan pratyavāyam āsādayet rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇan= iva vidvān sa ca tīvra tadeṇa tapasā eva vilīyate iti arthaḥ tarhi mahājanaḥ yena gataḥ sa panthāḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.17–1.1.1.19	 iti nyāyena vayam api anadhikṛtān vyutpādayāmaḥ iti atas āha na ca iti nanu kutārkikāṇām ajñānam nivartayatā kim anena śāstrasya upakṛtam syāt iti āha ku tārkikaiḥ iti ajñānam asamyak jñānam iha karma ārambhe prārabdhasya antarāya viraheṇa parisamāpti kāmayamānāḥ abhīṣṭa devatāḥ namaskāra pūrvakam prekṣāvantaḥ pravartante dṛśyate ca tatra tatra bahuśom vyabhicāraḥ kṛta namaskārasya api samīhita asiddheḥ viparītasya api samīhita siddhaḥ viparītasya api samīhita asiddheḥ na ca atra vṛṣṭi kāmaḥ kārīrī nirvapet 
NVTP_1.1.1.20^1	 iti vat prārabdha parisamāpti kāmaḥ devatām namaskuryāt iti śrutiḥ asti yena vyabhicore api karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyam kalpayāmaḥ tasmāt ar tha kāmaḥ iha vaṭe prativasantam yakṣam pūjayet itiva daprāmāṇika prasiddhi vijṛmbhitam etat iti abhisandhāya kimu na kṛtaḥ vāttika kṛtāḥ iṣṭadevatā namaskāraḥ iti atas āha avigīta iti pratyakṣam iva avigīta śiṣṭa ācāraḥ api śruti sadbhāve pramāṇam eva nirmūlasya ca śiṣṭa ācārasya asambhavāt apramāṇa mūlakasya ca prāmāṇika vigāna viraha anupapatteḥ tathā ca satyabhāvaḥ karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyam avalambate 
NVTP_1.1.1.20^2	 asati ca bhāvaḥ janmāntarīya su kṛta saṃpattim anvaya vyatireka abhāva darśanam tu āgama itara pramāṇa gocaram kārya kāraṇa bhāvam apākaroti iti arthaḥ yadyavam kim anena na kṛtaḥ iti atas āha parama iti yadi kṛtaḥ tat kim indraluptena gataḥ yena na dṛśyate iti atas āha na niveśitaḥ iti atra eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ na khalu iti na khalu iṣṭa devatā namaskāra vat tad niveśanam api kvacid upayujyate iti arthaḥ nanu evaṃbhūtam śiṣṭa ācāram śiṣyāḥ api grāhayitavyāḥ na ca tad niveśana vyatirekeṇa te grāhitāḥ syuḥ iti atas āha maṅgalya antara vat iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.21^1	 tatra iti śāstre vyākhyātavye nanu daṇḍaka sūtrasya anuvādaḥ na asti iti atas uktam saṃkṣepate iti nanu ādi sūtra tvam asya su prasiddham eva abhisaṃbandha vākya tvāt tat kim anena udīritena iti atas āha ādi grahaṇena iti nanu śāstra niḥśreyasayoḥ anena saṃbandhaḥ varṇyate tatas saṃbandha vākyam idam iti yuktam abhiḥ tu kimartham iti atas āha abhimataḥ iti asti hi śāstra niḥśreyasayoḥ vācya vāyaka bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ api saṃbandhaḥ na ca asau= iha abhimtaḥ prekṣāvat pravṛtti anaṅga tvāt na hi vācakāt vācya pratīteḥ vācyasya niṣpattiḥ yatas mumukṣuḥ vācake pravartatām 
NVTP_1.1.1.21^2–1.1.1.22	 upāye tu upeya arthaḥ pravartate tena hetu hetum at bhāvaḥ eva vivakṣitaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu na atra śāstram tasya niḥśreyasa hetu tvam vā śrūyate iti atas āha pramāṇa ādi iti rūḍha padātikrame kim tātparyam iti atas āha na hi iti yadi api śiṣyate anuśiṣyate pramāṇa ādi kam anena iti śāstram iti vyutpattyā atra api kāraṇa tā gamyate tathā api śāsaka saṃbaddha vyāpāravat tayā na tu śiṣya saṃbaddha vyāpāravat tayā sā ca iha vivakṣitā anyathā pramāṇa ādīni tattvataḥ jñātvā api tāvat na mucyate yāvat na anuśiṣyāt iti tat idam uktam padārtha tattva avagama karaṇa tayā iti na svarūpeṇa iti ca nanu hetu tva karaṇa tve na viṣaya bhedena bhavitum arhate iti atas āha tena iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.23–1.1.1.24	 ubhayoḥ api hetuḥ śāstram karaṇam ca kim tu padārtha tattve jñāpakatayā niḥśreyase tad vyāpāravataḥ karaṇatayā iti arthaḥ tat idam uktam tathā ca iti evam ca sati śāstrasya niḥśreyase karttavye padārtha tattva jñānasya nirūkti balena vyāpāra tve darśite vyāpāra vyāpāriṇoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tathā vyāpāravatā śāstreṇa vyāpāra viṣayasya pramāṇa ādeḥ pratipādya pratipādaka bhāvaḥ tathā vyāpāra viṣayeṇa pramāṇa ādinā vyāpārasya tattva jñānasya viṣaya viṣayībhāvaḥ tathā vyāpāreṇa tattva jñānena vyāpārulasya niḥśreyasasya kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tathā vyāpāra viṣaya phalayoḥ hetu hetumat bhāvaḥ saṃbandha sūcitaḥ na antarīyaka tvāt na hi atad hetukaḥ tat vacā pāraḥ nāma na api atat karma tad vacā pāra viṣayaḥ na api tad phala an anuguṇaḥ tad vacā pāraḥ tad vacā pāra viṣayaḥ vā iti pajcasu vaktavyeṣu upalakṣaṇa artham dvayam āha śāstra pramāṇāt iti enam eva vyutpatti labhyam vyāpāram abhipretya tattvasya jñānam iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī bhāṣya kāreṇa darśitā iti na karaṇa vyutpattiḥ virūddhā 
NVTP_1.1.1.25	 nanu śiṣya ācārya śāstra tad vyākhyānānām api saṃbandhāḥ kaiścid samāna tāntrikaiḥ pradarśitāḥ te kasmāt na pradarśyante iti atas āha tat idam abhidheya iti na hrāsti iti etāvat mātreṇa eva pradarśanīyam kim nāma yāvatī apratipādite prekṣāvat pravṛttiḥ na syāt tāvat pradarśyate na ca śiṣya ācārya ādi saṃbandhāḥ prekṣāvat pravṛtti aṅgam teṣām pravṛtti phala tvāt pravṛtti uttara kālam hi śiṣyaḥ pratipādyaḥ pratipādakaḥ ca ācāryaḥ śāstram vyākhyeyam vyākhyātā ca saḥ ityādi sidhyati na ca śāstra ācārya ādīnām svarūpa pratipādanam api upayujyate pramāṇa antara siddha tvāt tasmāt prayojanam abhidhayam tayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ abhidheyaḥ tad dvārā śāstrasya prayojanena saṃbandhaḥ iti etad artha tva ime prathama sūtrasya nyāyyam iti arthaḥ nanu yasya mithyājñānam saṃsāram pratanoti tasya eva tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa hetuḥ ātmā ca tathā tad anyeṣām tu śāstra abhidheyānām api na niḥśreyasa hetu tvam tathā ca na niḥśreyasa saṃbandhaḥ iti atas āha yat padārtha iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.26	 nanu pramāṇa ādi padārtha tattva jñānasya yadi niḥśreyasa hetu tā śāstra pravṛtteḥ pūrvam eva pramāṇa siddhā niṣprayojanam śāstre prayojana abhidhānam māna antara siddhe upadeśa anapekṣaṇāt atha itas eva tat niścayaḥ dusttaram itaretara āśraya tvam pravṛttaḥ hi prayojanam niścinuyāt niścita prayojanaḥ ca pravarteta na ca pravṛtteḥ prāk eva muni vacanāt niścinoti prathama sūtraḥ eva prayojana aniścayena pravṛtti anupapatteḥ tatra api ca pravṛtti artham prayojana antara abhidhāne anavasthā tad aniśvaye api ādyā pravṛttiḥ ced uttarottara pravṛttau= api tathā tva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt prayojana ādi abhidhānam anarthakam iti kecid tad anupapannam tridhā hi puṃsām citta vṛttayaḥ anubhavaḥ icchā prayatnaḥ ca iti tatra anubhavaḥ na icchām anuvidhatte aniṣṭasya api upalabdheḥ icchā tu puruṣa arthe svarasa utthitā tad sādhane ca tathā tva anumāna utthāpyāḥ prayatnaḥ tu sādhana viṣayaḥ eva tatra sādhana gocara āviccha prayatnau ādyā pravṛttiḥ iti ucyate na tu anubhavaḥ phala gocarāḥ vā icchā pravṛttiḥ cena tayoḥ api prayojana niścaya apekṣā syāt na 
NVTP_1.1.1.27^1	 hi upekṣaṇīyam niṣprayojanam iti na anubhūyate na api sukham prayojana antara śūnyakiti na iṣyate na api mumukṣuṇā anapekṣite svarge yāga ādikam tad sādhana tayā na anubhūyate puruṣa artha sādhane tu icchā lakṣaṇāḥ vā prayatna lakṣaṇā vā pravṛttiḥ na svarasa siddhāḥ na hi kaścid kṣudhī duḥkha prahāṇam tṛpti sauhitya sukha vā ananusaṃdhāya annamattum icchati prayatate vā tasmāt yatra yaḥ pravartayitavyaḥ sa tat sādhyam artham daśayitvā yatas ca yaḥ nivartayitavyaḥ sa tat sādhyam anartham darśayitvā iti uktam pracojana ādikam tat tu śrotā katham śraddhāsyati aśraddadhānaḥ vā katham pravartsyati iti avaśiṣyate tatra āha viniścitā iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.27^2	 yadi api muneḥ āpta tva avadhāraṇe prayojana anabhidhāne api prayojana sāmānya niścayaḥ bhavati eva prayojana vat idam śāstram āpta ukta tvāt iti tathā api na asau pravṛtti aṅgam na hi prayojana vat iti eva pravartate kim tarhi asmad apekṣita prayojana vat idam iti kṛtvā sa ca prayojana viśeṣaḥ vacanāt eva avasīyate iti sārthakam etat abhidhānam tat idam uktam prayojana ādi viniścitya viśeṣate iti śeṣaḥ viniścayaḥ ca śāstra upāyakam eva idam niḥśreyasam iti ākāraḥ na tu avaśyaṃbhā vi prayojana ākāraḥ kṛṣi ādau= avagraha ādi vat atra api antarāya saṃbhavāt tat idam prayojanasya pravartaka tvam uddeśya tayā na tu pravṛtti viṣaya tayā tena na iṣṭa abhyupāyatā vidhi virodhaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.28–1.1.1.29	 nanu muneḥ āpta tva aniścaye kim tad vacane pravṛttiḥ na asti eva tathā sati tasya āptatva niścayaḥ api katham iti atas āha āpta tva aniścaye tu artha saṃśayāt śāstra sādhyatayā iti śeṣaḥ nanu saṃśayān asya katham prekṣāvataḥ pravṛttiḥ ityaḥ āha na khalu iti yadi api ca sasya adhigamasya kṛṣi ādi sādhya tayā saṃśayaḥ na asti tathā api bhaviṣyat tayā asti eva tathā api 
NVTP_1.1.1.30^1	 tam uddiśya prekṣāvantaḥ pravartante yathā ca tatra śata ekāṃśikaḥ phala abhāvaḥ phalakoṭiḥ tu utkaṭā tathā atra api na hi indriyā pāta jaḥ ayam saṃśayaḥ kim nāma āpta tva aviniścaya hetukā prāmāṇya śaḍkyā samākṛṣṭaḥ vastutas tu sūtrāt prayojana ādi niścaya ākāram eva vijñānam iti arthaḥ nanu saṃśayaḥ prayojana ādi vākya abhāve api sulabhaḥ viśeṣa smṛtiḥ tu arthi tva viśeṣāt bhaviṣyati iti āha na ca iti yat vacanena hi yaḥ pravartate sa tad vacanāt eva viśeṣa smṛtim apekṣate na svātantryeṇa na hi roga ārtaḥ mama idam roga nivṛtti sādhanam bhavet na vā iti yatra tatra ucchṛṣ khalaḥ svayam utprekṣya pravartate kim nāma anavadhṛta āpta tvasya api vaidyasya eva vacanāt 
NVTP_1.1.1.30^2	 anyathā tu ayam prayojana abhidhānam anadhigacchan anartham api āśaṅketa kim niṣprayojanam idam kāka danta parīkṣā grantha vat uta aśakya sādhana prayojanam mṛtyu hara hima mahīdhara uttarasā anusiddha saṃjīvanī kathana vat atha anabhimata prayojanam āryāvarta nivāsinam prati dākṣiṇāti asya mātula kanyakā pariṇaya prakrama upadeśa vat atha abhimatasya api śakyasya api prayojanasya laghīyasi upāya antare sati api guruḥ ayam upāyaḥ pipāsum prati gīrvāṇa taraḍgiṇī tīra samīpa kūpa khanana upadeśa vat etāsu ca anartha saṃbhāvanāsu na pravartate na ca prayojana abhidhāne api etāsām avakāśaḥ loka vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt na hi kaścid vaidya vacanāt eva māśaḍkya nivartate yathā 
NVTP_1.1.1.31	 svayam utprekṣya iti bhāvaḥ tad anarthakam niṣprayojanam iti arthaḥ aśakya anuṣṭhāna tvam upāyasya asiddham iti atas āha tathā hi iti iha dvividhaḥ pramāṇa śabdasya arthaḥ pramīyate anena iti ca pramāṇam pramitiḥ pramāṇam iti ca tatra prathamam adhikṛtya uktam prameya ādīnām tattva jñānam pramāṇa tattva jñāna adhīnam iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.32^1	 nanu idindrayā ādīnām ajñāyamānānām eva sva viṣaya pariccheda janaka tvam paśyan= api katham evam brūyāt iti atas āha na hi iti pramāṇa tvena ajñāyamānam pramāṇam sva viṣayam paricchinatti na tu avadhārayati tat ca iha vivakṣitam iti arthaḥ kim iti na avadhārayati na hindriyam ajñāyamānam aniścaya ākāram eva jñānam janayati iti atas āha tāvat mātrasya iti yadi api niścaya ākāram eva jñānam ādhatte tathā api tathābhūtasya eva bhūyas bhūyas prameya virahaḥ labdheḥ viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ ca saṃdehaḥ tat avaskandati iti arthaḥ tat kim kvacid api avadhāraṇam na asti eva tathā sati toyam eva idam iti ādikaḥ laukikaḥ pratyayaḥ tathā pūrva pakṣiṇaḥ kvacid api viniścayaḥ na asti eva iti ādikaḥ ca abhimānaḥ viruddhi eta iti atas āha api tu iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.32^2	 yadi kvacid prameya tattva avadhāraṇam parama arthaḥ tadā pramāṇa tattva avadhāraṇa dvāreṇa eva pramāra antareṇa tu bhavat na pāramārthikam iti arthaḥ bodhaka tvam bodha janaka tvam bodha janana avacchinnā sattā iti yāvat avyabhicāri tvam aviparīta anubhava janaka tvam aviparīta anubhava janana avacchi nnā sattā iti yāvat evam ca upadhi dvaya avacchinnāyāḥ sattāyāḥ upādhi bhedāt bhinnāyāḥ iva ekasmin= arthe samavāyaḥ kṛta ka tva anitya tvayoḥ iva na viruddhaḥ tena avyabhicāri tvena jñāyamānena iti śeṣaḥ pramāṇya avadhāraṇam tarhi kkopa yujyate iti atas āha tat eva hi iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.33^1	 pramāṇam hi pramākaraṇam na ca karaṇa tva ādayaḥ sāmānya viśeṣāḥ santi sāmānya saṃkara prasaṅgāt kim nāma sādhakatama tvam eva karaṇa tvam tad viśeṣakaḥ tu kriyā viśeṣaḥ eva sa ca atra pramā lakṣaṇaḥ pramā ca aviparīta upalabdhiḥ atas aviparīta anubhava janaka tva lakṣaṇam avyabhicāri tvam eva prāmāṇyam iti arthaḥ yadi evam tad avadhāraṇa pūrvakam eva prameya ādi avadhāraṇam astu iti atas āha tat ca iti pramākaraṇa tvam hi na anavadhāritāyām pramāyām avadhārayitum śakyam iti arthaḥ tarhi pramātvam eva avadhāryatām na hi tat api aupādhikam yena upādhi anavadhāraṇe na eva avadhāryeta iti atas āha tathā hi iti vijñānasya pramāyāḥ prāmāṇyam pramātvam svatas vā iti asya sva ātmanā vā sva grāhakeṇa vā iti arthaḥ tatra prathamam dūṣayati na khalu iti dharma dharmiṇoḥ abheda pakṣe anātma saṃvedanam iti etat eva dūṣaṇam 
NVTP_1.1.1.33^2	 āna ātma saṃvedana tā ca upapādayiṣyate iti hṛdayam bheda pakṣe prāk eva iti yaḥ hi yat gṛhṇāti sa tad dharmam api gṛhṇīyāt iti saṃbhāvyeta api yaḥ tu dharmiṇam eva na akalayati tasya dharma grahaṇa vārtā api kva yadi api ca śabda gandha ādayaḥ vyoma bhūmi ādya grahe api gṛhyante tathā api na tad dharmatayā iti arthaḥ sva grāhakeṇa vā iti dūṣayati na api iti tat hi mānasam vā syāt laiḍgikam vā ubhayam api manasaḥ jñāta tā la kṣaṇāt liṅgāt vā aviśiṣṭāt jāyamānam katham iva tad ābhāsa viśiṣṭam gṛhṇīyat viṣaya viśeṣāt tu tathā tve apramāṇyasya api svatas eva grahaṇa prasaṅgāt tatra api viṣaya vaiśiṣṭa casya sattvāt pramāyāḥ prāyika tayā tad vāsanāyāḥ samutkaṭa tvāt apramā api samutkaṭa tvāt apramā api pramā iti eva gṛhyate tatas bādhaka adhīnam eva aprāmāṇyam āsaṃjita rajata tāyām iva 
NVTP_1.1.1.34–1.1.1.35	 śuktikāyām śuktikātvam iti yadi tathā āpi āsaṃjakasya api yadi āsaṃjaka tvam avagatam katham na svatas aprāmāṇya grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tatra api prāmāṇya ārope tu katham na anavasthā na ca kṛtrimam rūpam aparibhūya grahaṇam grahaṇām iti ucyate saṃśayena abhibhūta tvāt māyā liḍgini jhaṭiti parivrājaka buddhi vat tasmāt jñānam gṛhyate eva iti eva na yadi tu daivāt gṛhyate tadā jñānam iti eva na tu pramāṇam apramāṇam vā iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.36	 nanu yadi svīyāt svatas iti na nirvahati vakṣyamāṇena ca nyāyena na api paratas asti ca ayam pramāṇa apramāṇa pravibhāga vyavahāraḥ niḥśaṅkaḥ tatas sva saṃvedana nayaḥ eva astu tena hi ayam nirvahet na hi tatra kiñcid anavasthā ādikam paśyāmaḥ iti atas āha etena iti sva saṃvedana nayaḥ hi na tāvat pramāṇa siddhaḥ kadācid pramāṇa vyavahāra sauṣṭhavāt svīkriyeta api yadi ayam tena nirvahet na tu etat asti yathā hi pramāṇam sva ātmānam gṛhṇat prāmāṇyam api gṛhṇāti tathā tad ābhāsam api tad ābhāsa tva gṛhṇīyāt tathā ca sarva mithyā jñānāt apravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ na ca tatra api pramāṇi āropāt pravṛttiḥ sva ātma bhūtasya apramāṇi asya svasa vedana tayā grahaṇe samāropa asaṃbhāvāt agrahaṇe vā sva saṃvedana naya anupapatteḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedāt sva rūpa grahaṇe api na aprāmāṇya rūpa dharma grahaṇam iti yadi tadā prāmāṇyasya api agrahaṇam syāt tasmāt sva saṃvedana naye api sva rūpa vedana mātram syāt na tu prāmāṇya ādi vedanam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.37–1.1.1.38	 paratas vā iti dūṣayati na api iti tad gocaram tad gocara gocaram madhya pada lopāt prātyakṣike ca vahni jñāne prātyakṣikam eva vahni jñāna antaram iti yāvat tat ca dvividham samāna indriya jam indriya antara jam ca evam anumāne api anumāna jñāna antaram tat liṅga jam liṅga antara jam ca evam śābde api śābda jñāna anantaram tad āpta śabda jam āpta antara śabda jam ca iti samāna jātīya saṃvādaḥ darśitaḥ artha kriyā ityādinā kārya liṅgakam tad gocara ityādinā ca akārya kāraṇa liṅgakam anumāna trayam vijājīya saṃvāda rūpam darśitam upalakṣaṇam ca etat āpta upadeśa jam api saṃvādakam jñānam bhavati eva jñānam bhavati eva saḥ ayam pramāṇye niścetavye saṃvādaḥ yadi api vyadhikaraṇaḥ tathapi artha tathā tvam ava dhārayan= arthavat tvam pravartakasya api avadhārayati iti etāvatā tathā eva upavarṇitaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.39	 dūṣayati tat ca sarvam iti evam pramātu asya duradhigama tvam āpādya tad āyatta avadhāraṇe pramāṇānām pramāṇa tve yojayati yadā ca iti nanu yadi prāmāṇya avadhāraṇena eva pravṛttiḥ tadā sā eva sārvalaukikī svatas ityādi vikalpān phalgūkariṣyati atha tad avadhāraṇa vyatirekeṇa api pravṛttiḥ apratyūhā tadā mā avadhāri prāmāṇyam kim naḥ chinnam iti atas āha tat evam iti vaidikam vyavahāram adhikṛtya ca idam śāstram pravṛttam na laukikam iti abhisandhiḥ prakṛte yojayati tasmāt iti nanu nitya yoge matubh iti durghaṭam pramāṇa arthayoḥ eva anitya tvāt paraspara samavāya bhāvāt ca iti atas āha nitya tā ca iti nanu avyabhicāraḥ api vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ pramāṇa prameyayoḥ na asti iti atas āha iyam eva ca iti saḥ ayam avisaṃvadādaḥ visaṃvāda abhāvaḥ avyabhicāra lakṣaṇam avyabhicāra svarūpam tu lakṣya bhūtam bhūta artha paricchedaka tvam lakṣya lakṣaṇayoḥ abhinna āśraya tvāt avyabhicāra svarūpam tu lakṣya bhūtam bhūta artha paricchedaka tvam lakṣya lakṣaṇayoḥ abhinna āśraya tvāt 
NVTP_1.1.1.40–1.1.1.41	 sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti mantavyam yadi api deśa avasthā bhede kāla bhedaḥ api artha siddhaḥ tathā api yathākathañcit kāla bheda mātram vivakṣitam atra iti jñāpana artham tad grahaṇam tathā hi dūra sthe sthāṇau puruṣarpatyayasya kāla antare api visaṃvādaḥ na asti yāvat na pratipattā nikaṭa sthaḥ bhavati pratyetavyaḥ eva vā yāvat na nediṣṭhaḥ syāt evam svapna avasthāyām artha pratyayasya kāla bhede api tāvat na visaṃvādaḥ yāvat na jāgara avasthā anubhavaḥ na ca vācyam evam sati kim kāla bheda grahaṇena iti deśa avasthayoḥ abhede api kāla krameṇa api kvacid visaṃvāda darśanāt yathā su nipuṇa nibhāla nāt āpāta jātasya kāma ātura kāminī jñānasya bhede api kvacid kāla antare visaṃvādāt tad upagrahaḥ tat anena indriya ādīnām kāla krama bhāvinaḥ sahakāri bhedāḥ sphuṭatara pratīti hetavaḥ sarve eva saṃgṛhītāḥ yadi api ca pramāra viṣayau= eva visaṃvāda avisaṃvādau saṃbhava vyabhicāra lakṣaṇau tathā api avisaṃvādasya dhruva viṣaya tva pratipādana artham svarūpa grahaṇam sarvasya jñānasya dharmiṇī avisaṃvādāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.42–1.1.1.43	 pravṛtti sāmarthyāt iti vyadhikāraṇaḥ hetuḥ atas tad artham āha samartha pravṛtti janaka tvāt iti yadi api samartha pravṛtti tvāt iti uktesamañjasam tathā api pravṛttiḥ yasya iti sambandhe ṣaṣṭhī sa ca pramāṇa pravṛttyoḥ janya janaka bhāvaḥ eva iti saḥ eva darśitaḥ nanu na tāvat pramāṇyasamartha pravṛtti janakatvayoḥ avinābhāvaḥ pratyakṣeṇa śakya grahaḥ tayoḥ eva apratyakṣa tvāt prāmāṇyam hi samartha pravṛtti janakatva anumeyam tat ca anvaya vyatireka anumeyam eva iti na api anumānena anvaya grahaḥ prāmāṇyasya 
NVTP_1.1.1.44–1.1.1.46	 kvacid api asiddheḥ siddhau vā kim anumānena anumā anantara siddha tve tu anavasthā eva iti atas āha yadi punar iti atra ca upekṣā jñānānām pakṣa tvena anupādānāt na bhāga asiddhiḥ vyatirekī ca sarvatra sa pakṣa abhāvam abhyupetya pravartate iti nāsādharaṇa anaikāntika tā na ca vācyam etasya eva anumānasya arthavat tva anavadhāraṇe katham pramāṇānām arthavat tva siddhiḥ tad avadhāraṇe vā katham kevala vyatireki tvam iti dvividham hi anumānasya arthavat tvam avinābhāva lakṣaṇam pramā janana lakṣaṇam ca tatra sva viṣaya paricchede kartavye avinā abhāva avadhāraṇam eva apekṣate na pramākaraṇa tva avadhāraṇam iti anavaghṛta prāmāṇyena eva anena pramāṇānām pramāṇa phala tva lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam sādhyate iti sarvam sundaram 
NVTP_1.1.1.47^1	 etena etat api nirastam yat prāmāṇya anavadhāraṇe aprāmāṇya anavadhāraṇam api katham prāmāṇya niścayena hi tat niścīyate tad anavadhāraṇe tu vyatireka niścayaḥ api katham vipakṣasya tathā tva aniścayāt iti svarūpataḥ dharmataḥ ca anavadhāritena eva satā pramāṇena sva viṣaya niścaya siddheḥ nanu na asti eva asau vādī yaḥ prāmāṇya aniścaye api vipratipadyeta na hi prāmāṇyam svīkṛtya tat niścaye vipratipattiḥ svīkārasya niścaya mūla tvāt na ca asvīkṛtya pramāṇa śūnya vipratipatteḥ sarvatra sulabha tayā sarva vāda vidhi niṣedha vyavahāra vilopa prasaṅgāt aniścite ca prāmāṇye tat atad rūpa saṃdehaḥ api kvacid durlabhaḥ viśeṣa smṛteḥ abhāvāt tad pūrvaka tvāt ca sarva saṃśayānām 
NVTP_1.1.1.47^2–1.1.1.48	 na api sarvatra aprāmāṇyāsañjanam prāmāṇya grahaṇa upāya nirākaraṇasya aprāmāṇye api tulya tvāt vikalpa nirmitam avicāra manoharam prāmāṇya ādikam ādāya api na asya durvicārasya nirvāhaḥ prāmāṇya anabhyupagame vikalpa nirmāṇasya api asiddheḥ na ca vikalpa nirmite na saṃśaya ādi vyavahāraḥ samasti na hi vāji viṣāṇam vā iti kaścid sandigdhe na api nara viṣāṇam iti kasyacid viparyayaḥ tasmāt asti prāmāṇya ādikam tat niścayaḥ ca tad upāyaḥ tu cintām arhati evam ca anvayaḥ asti eva tat katham kevala vyatireki anumānam iti āśaḍkya saṃpratipatti ru uttaram anvaya vyatirekī vā iti kevala vyatireki vādaḥ tu anvaya anabhyupagamena kṛtaḥ iti abhisandhiḥ anumānasya iti upalakṣaṇam svatas iti ca tad itarasya api svatas paratas ca prāmāṇya siddheḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.49	 nanu samartha pravṛtti janaka tvāt iti etāvatā eva sādhya siddheḥ pramāṇator a tha pratipattauviti asamartha viśeṣaṇam vayadhikaraṇa ca iti atas āha pravṛtti janaka tvam tu iti prāmāṇya ādi abhidhāna dvārāḥ hi śāstrasya niḥśreyasena saṃgatiḥ na tu svarūpeṇa tatas yathā pramāṇa ādi tattva jñānam sādhya tayā prayojanam pratijñāyate tathā pramāṇa ādi abhidheya tayā api pratijñā iyam bhavati yathā atha atas dharma vyākhyāsyāmaḥ iti dharmasya vyākhyeya tvena eva pratijñā samānatantre na ca tad abhidheya tā pratijñānam atra tasmāt abhidheyat tva apratijñānāt na pramāṇa ādayaḥ śāstreṇa abhidhīyante iti śrotṛ buddha canurodhena aśaḍkya sūtrakāra hṛdaya anurodhena vārttikam uttarayati syāt etat iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.50	 śiṣyā kāṅkṣā krameṇa hi śāstram idam pravṛttam anapekṣita abhidhāne anavadheya tva prasaṅgāt na ca śiṣyā kāṅkṣā kim vakṣyati bhavān iti kim tu niḥśreyasam kutas adhigamyate iti tatra uttaram pramāṇa ādi tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti tatas katham iti tatas ke kati kiṃlakṣaṇāḥ pramāṇa ādayaḥ iti tatra uddeśa vibhāga lakṣaṇāni iti tatas katham iti tatra dvitīya adhyāya ādi iti etat ca sarvam anubhava siddham na atra api vacana apekṣā ukta āboddhāram prati tu vyākhyātāraḥ bhavanti yata 
NVTP_1.1.1.51–1.1.1.52	 evam ayamāha iti tad anubhava siddham api pramāṇa ādi abhidhāyaka tvam yaḥ kutaścid vyāmohāt na pratipadyate tam prati vyākhyātā śāstrasya puruṣa śreyaḥ abhidhāyaka tvāt iti āha iti arthaḥ nanu śreyaḥ abhidhāna mātreṇa api na pramāṇa ādi abhidhānam sidhyati na hi pramāṇa ādi padārthāḥ eva śreyaḥ atha svayam eva vivarīṣyati tad padārthāḥ pramāṇa ādayaḥ iti tathā api tat śāstram śreyaḥ abhidhattaḥ iti anene kim atha śreyaḥ śabdasya pramāṇa ādayaḥ eva arthaḥ tarhi śreyaḥ punar sukham ahita nivṛttiḥ iti kim iti atas āha yadi api iti yadi api śāstra punar puruṣaḥ punar śreyaḥ punar iti pratipadam gṛhītvā vivaraṇam prakṣayeṇa iti antena sphuṭa avabhāsam na ca puruṣāḥ rāga ādi mante iti ādau= api 
NVTP_1.1.1.53–1.1.1.54	 vivaraṇa tva aśaḍkāḥ prakṛtena asaṃbandhāt na hi rāga ādi mantam prati śāstram na sa sādhanam śreyaḥ abhidhatte na ca tam prati na tat śreyaḥ yena vīta rāgaḥ vivicya gṛhyatām tathā api tasmāt tat śāstram puruṣa śreyaḥ abhidhattaḥ iti madhya patita upasaṃhāra eva vivaraṇa viccheda bhramaḥ mā bhūt iti etad artham avacchinatti upabhogāt prakṣayeṇa iti antena iti nanu samūhaḥ vyūha viśiṣṭaḥ iti asaṃgatam paryāya tvāt iti atas āha vyūhaḥ iti te khalu amī samūhāḥ praṇetṛ puruṣa icchā anurodhinaḥ sva artha anurodhinaḥ vā iti atas āha ekasmṛti iti yadi api ekārtha pratipādana avacchinnāḥ varṇāḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.55	 padam iti etāvat eva lakṣaṇam tathā api etat eva lakṣaṇam kṣaṇa bhaḍgurāṇām katham iti etat uktam eka smṛti samārūḍhāḥ iti samūhaḥ padam iti vārttike śeṣaḥ pada samūhaḥ sūtram iti vārttikam tat ca anupapannam vākya viśeṣaḥ hi sūtram na ca vākya sāmānyam api pada samūha mātram gauraḥ caḥ puruṣaḥ hastī ityādeḥ api vākya tva prasaṅgāt iti atas āha evam sva artha iti samūhaḥ veditavyaḥ sūtra tvena iti śeṣaḥ sūtra samūhaḥ prakaraṇam iti vārttikam tatra ca avāntara samūha bhede kāraṇa abhāvāt śāstram eva sūtra samūha rūpam prakaraṇam iti prāptam iti atas āha evam kvacid iti tat yathā prayojana abhidheya saṃbandha pratipādanam ekam artham adhikṛtya prathama dvitīya sūtrayoḥ samūhaḥ prakaraṇam evam pramāṇa prakaraṇam prameya prakaraṇam nyāya pūrva aṅga prakaraṇam nyāya āśraya prakaraṇam nyāya āśraya prakaraṇam nyāya svarūpa prakaraṇam nyāya uttarāṅga prakaraṇam iti ādyūhyam 
NVTP_1.1.1.56	 prakaraṇa samūhaḥ ca āhnikam iti vārttikam tat idam prakaraṇānām avāntara eka vākya tāyām asatyām na sidhyati iti atas āha prakaraṇānām iti asti hi amīṣām prakaraṇānām sa parikara nyāya lakṣaka tvam ekam iti tad samūhaḥ āhnikam uttarasmiḥ ca āhnike nyāya nyāya ābhāsa viveka upāya lakṣaṇam ekam tatra api kathā prakaraṇam hetvābhāsa prakaraṇam chala prakaraṇam puruṣa aśakti liṅga prakaraṇam iti evam prathame lakṣaṇa madhyāya arthaḥ dvitīye pramāṇa parīkṣā tṛtīye kāraṇa rūpa prameya ṣaṭka parīkṣā caturthe kārya rūpa prameya ṣaṭka parīkṣā pañcame puruṣa aśakti liṅga viśeṣa lakṣaṇam iti evam dvitīya adhyāyāt au= āhnika prakaraṇa saṃgatīḥ tatra eva darśayiṣyāmaḥ tat idam uktam evam tatra tatra veditavyam iti tatra tatra iti āhika ādau= iti arthaḥ nanu ca tatra eka prakāraḥ api na darśitaḥ katham tatra tatra veditavyam iti atas āha etāḥ ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.57–1.1.1.59	 nanu śāstrasya sa sādhana puruṣa śreyaḥ abhidhāyaka tvam pratijñāya śāstra svarūpa darśanam kkopa yujyate iti atas āha tat evam iti śāstra svarūpa ākhyāna pūrvakam tad artha kathanam sugamam bhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ nanu pratīti siddham pramāṇa ādīnām ṣoḍaśa tvam kim iti anūdyate iti atas tad nirākaraṇīyām āśaḍkām āha nanu iti sāmānya viśeṣaḥ sādharmya viśeṣaḥ yatas asya iti pada samūhasya śāstrasya padārthāḥ padānām samūhinām arthāḥ pramāṇa ādayaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.60^1	 tasmāt śāstram vākya rūpam puruṣa śreyaḥ vākya artha rūpam abhidhatte samādhānam iti śeṣaḥ katham niḥśreyasāya kalpante iti āpātataḥ paramārthataḥ teṣām kālpanika tve niḥśreyasam api kālpanikam tatas tad artham prayāsaḥ viphalaḥ tasya āyatna siddha tvāt iti āśayaḥ kalpanā kośasya ananta prasara tvāt ananta ātmānaḥ iti āpātataḥ paraka arthataḥ nirātmānaḥ iti āśayaḥ pratyakṣa anumānā iti pramāṇa dvaya upanyāsaḥ sva siddhānta viruddhaḥ vāttika kṛtaḥ iti āha pramāṇa ādayaḥ iti na upamāna viṣayāḥ iti yadi api upamānasya saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pariccheda phalasya śabde pramāṇe asti eva upayogaḥ agṛhīta samayasya śabdasya apramāpaka tvāt samayasya ca prāyaśas upamānena akalanāt tathā api na tena te sākṣāt viṣayīkriyante pramāṇa ādayaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu yadi sākṣāt upamānasya prakṛta anupayogāt anabhidhānam tarhi śabdaḥ abhidhīyatām sa hi sākṣāt upayogī iti atas āha yadi api iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.60^2	 tatra api iti āgama viṣaya parāmarśaḥ āgamaḥ hi yatra pravartate tad viṣayam eva pratyakṣam anumānam vā apekṣate te tu samūle api na su iṣaya pravṛttam pramāṇam apekṣete tatas mūlā saṃpluta viṣaya tvāt te eva darśite iti arthaḥ vainayikā iti viśiṣṭaḥ nayaḥ śāstram nyāya śāstram tad janya buddhi virahiṇaḥ iti arthaḥ na etāna viviñcate samāropitāt rūpāt iti śeṣaḥ śuśrūṣā ādiḥ iti ādi grahaṇena śravaṇa ādau pāṭavam saṃdigdhasya api jijñāsā na bhavati eva anabhimata apavargasya iti atas uktam śiṣyasya iti śiṣya tayā mumukṣuta ādi saṃpattim upalakṣayati vipratipannaḥ api kathām ārabhamāṇaḥ api amumukṣuḥ galite ahaṅkāre na sa apekṣaḥ bhavati iti atas niṣphalaḥ jalpa vitaṇḍa ārambhaḥ iti atas āha śiṣyamāṇasya iti mohāt api mokṣam icchate iti arthaḥ jalpa vitaṇḍābhyām vigalite ahaṅkāre iti yojanā sa apekṣasya sataḥ pratipādyata iti vākya śeṣa agre kenacid pramāreṇa iti prathama sūtra pāṭha prakāreṇa iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.61–1.1.1.64	 nanu asaṃdigdhasya api saṃdigdhīkaraṇe kim asya prayojanam iti atas āha asaṃdigdhaḥ api iti tathā ca pramātaṇām sa apekṣāṇām iti śeṣaḥ te abhī durlalitāḥ śiṣyāḥ yadi mokṣa ādau= api indriya ādi apekṣante tadā katham pratipādyāḥ iti atas vārtikam pūrayati kañcid iti dṛṣṭa prayojana upayoginam pratyakṣa upalabhyamānam iti arthaḥ dṛṣṭa prayojana upayoginam eva anumeyam jijñāsavaḥ iti uttaratra api pūraṇīyam iti āha evam uttaram api iti nanu etāvatā api jijñāsavaḥ iti uttaratra api pūraṇīyam iti āha evam uttaram api iti nanu etāvatā api sa apekṣāḥ anena eva śāstreṇa pratipādyāḥ pratyakṣa anumānābhyām ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.65	 paraspara vyāhatam iti atas āha ayam abhisandhiḥ iti parama puruṣa artha sādhanam tu jijñāsavaḥ iti śeṣe nyāyena iti śeṣaḥ iha yadi api sukham dṛṣṭam eva vidhāyaka pramāṇa gocaraḥ eva ahita nivṛttiḥ adṛṣṭā eva niṣedhaka pramāṇa gocaraḥ eva iti yathāsaṃkhyam api saṃbhavati tathā api śreyaḥ punar sukham ahita nivṛttiḥ ca iti atas na kiñcid adhikam uktam bhavati iti pramāṇa aviśeṣa saṃbandha kathanam eva param na ca tena idānīm asti prayojanam na ca abhimata śreyaḥ viśeṣa nirdhāraṇe kartavye vidhi niṣedha gocara tva upavarṇanam upayujyate iti abhisaṃdhāya anyathā vyācaṣṭe tatra api iti tat śreyaḥ sukham ahita nivṛttiḥ ca iti tad śabdena dvayam api śreyaḥ tvena parāmṛśyate iti arthaḥ yathāsaṃkhyam śaḍkām nivārayati na vyāsa jya iti dṛṣṭam sukham iti atra 
NVTP_1.1.1.66–1.1.1.67	 drṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa śabdayoḥ artham udāharaṇa mukhena spaṣṭayati sraj candana iti aihikam iti arthaḥ svarga ādi iti āmuṣmikam iti arthaḥ uktam anyatra api iti diśati evam iti ahita nivṛttiḥ api aihikyāmuṣmikī ca iti arthaḥ na evam vāttike rūyate iti atas āha cakāra lopāt iti cakārayoḥ loparat iti arthaḥ tena dṛṣṭam sukham adṛṣṭam ca tathā 
NVTP_1.1.1.68	 ahita nivṛttiḥ ca iti vāttika arthaḥ tat ayam saṃkṣepaḥ dṛṣṭam śreyaḥ tat ca sukham ahita nivṛttiḥ ca sukham api aihikam āmuṣmikam ca duḥkha nivṛttiḥ api aihikyāmuṣmikī ca iti tatra sukha lakṣaṇam śreyaḥ dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam vā na etat śāstra sādhyam tasya sraj ādi yāga ādi sādhya tvāt ātyantikasya ca tasya abhāvāt ahita nivṛttiḥ api anātyantikī dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa bhinnā na etat śāstra sādhyāḥ tasyāḥ prasakta kaṇṭaka ādi hisā ādi parihāra sādhya tvāt tad aprasaktau tu asādhya tvāt ata 
NVTP_1.1.1.69	 ātyantikīm ahita nivṛtti nirdhārayitum punar bhinatti iti āha ahita nivṛtteḥ iti nanu yadi nivṛttiḥ iti nanu yadi nivṛttiḥ prāgabhāvaḥ duḥkhasya sa katham ātyantikaḥ uttara anta anavacchedaḥ hi ātyantika tvam prāgābhāvasya ca tathā tve prāk iti eva na syāt atha nivṛttiḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ sa ca sarve eva ātyantikaḥ iti kutas nivṛtteḥ ātyantika tva vyutpādanam iti atas āha ātyantika tvam iti nivṛttasya nivṛtta jātīyasya punar anutpādaḥ tatra eva ātmani iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.70	 nanu ekaviṃśati prabheda bhinna duḥkṣahāniḥ eva ātyantikī duḥkha nivṛttiḥ tat katham ha anyeti vāttikam iti atas āha sa ca iti nivṛttyā nivṛtti svarūpeṇa lakṣyate atra ca kārya śabdena duḥkham uktam kāraṇa śabdena śarīra indriya viṣaya buddhayaḥ anuṣaḍgi sukham duḥkhena eka kāraṇa tvāt atha śarīra ādiṣu nivṛtteṣu api dukham kim na bhavet mā bhūt duḥkham sukham kim na bhavet na 
NVTP_1.1.1.71	 hi anyasmin= atyanta nivṛtte anyat na bhavati tathā ca anuṣaḍgā sukhi ni vṛttiḥ kim upavarṇyayaḥ iti atas āha na hi iti kāraṇa vinā bhavat kāryam kārya tām ava jahyāt atḥ śarīra ādiṣu asatsu duḥkha vat sukham api na bhavati tasya api tad kāryatvāt bhavat vā śarīra ādiṣu satsu eva bhavet tathā ca duḥkham api bhavet kāraṇa sadbhāvāt iti arthaḥ atra eva arthe vāttikam yojanayati tat idam uktam iti anena eva kāraṇam avidyā tṛṣṇe kāryā pravṛttiḥ anuṣaḍgiṇau dharma adharmau= iti ṭīkā vyākhyānam apahastitam śarīra ādīnām duḥkha tvam anubhava bādhitam iti atas āha gauṇa iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.72^1	 nuna ghrāṇa ādi sūtre pañca indriyāṇi prasiddhāni na ca pradeśa antare api ṣaṭ iti atas āha ṣaṣṭham iti tantra yuktyā iti bhāvaḥ nanu viṣayāḥ api anitaretara sādhana sādhyāḥ pajcā eva vibhāge parīkṣāyām ca siddhāḥ na tu ṣaṭ iti atas āha tasya iti yadi api buddhi sukha duḥkhāni api manasaḥ viṣayaḥ tathā api tasya eva viṣaya tvena duḥkha tva upacāraḥ cat viṣayīkriyamāṇam duḥkham upajanayati vakṣyati hi viṣayā bodhya tvāt iti na ca buddhiḥ budhyamānāḥ duḥkha hetuḥ vakṣyati hi buddhayaḥ tu sākṣāt iti sukha duḥkhayoḥ tu duḥkha hetu tvam eva na asti sukhasya vijātīya ārambhaka tve api rāga mātra ambhaka tvāt 
NVTP_1.1.1.72^2	 duḥkhasya tu vijātīya ārambhaka tvāt eva icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ tu pratīyamānāḥ eva sākṣāt duḥkha janayanti tathā hi mumukṣuḥ tāvat icchāmi dveṣmi yoga abhyāsāt anyatra prayate iti pratītya eva duḥkhī bhavati ahita sādhana tvena icchā dveṣa prayatnānām tena avadhārita tvāt anyaḥ apīṣyamāṇa alābhe bubhukṣitaḥ asmi pipāsitaḥ asmi iti pratītya duḥkhī bhavati hitam eva ahitam upalabhya dviṣataḥ nivṛtta bhramasya hitam eva dveṣmi dhiḍ mām iti duḥkham evam aniṣṭaḥ eva arthe iṣṭa buddhyā prayatamānasya nivṛtte bhrame tathā alasasya prayatnam upalabhya eva duḥkham iti etāvatā ete eva manasaḥ viṣaya tvena nirdiṣṭāḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.73–1.1.1.74	 nanu jarā kuṣṭa ādi upahata dehasya upalabhyamānam eva śarīram duḥkha hetuḥ tatra api viṣaya tvena eva duḥkha tva upacāraḥ syāt iti atas āha yadi api iti anyathā asya duḥkha hetu bhāvaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ iti śeṣaḥ viṣaya tvena puraridam na ṣaḍbhyaḥ bhidyate asādhāraṇa indriya saṃbandhāt tu bhidyate na tu svarūpeṇa viṣayāṇām ananta tvāt iti arthaḥ iha yadi api anuṣaḍgaḥ avinābhāvaḥ iti vakṣyati vāttikakāraḥ tad upapattaye ca samāna nimitta tā sā māna ādhāra tā samāna upalabhyatāḥ tathā api na 
NVTP_1.1.1.75–1.1.1.77	 tāvat mātreṇa āvinā bhāvaḥ nirvahati sādhāraṇa nimittāyām api hi anyatarā sādhāraṇa nimitta nivṛttau= ekatara nivṛttau itarāna vṛtti saṃbhavāt atas eva ādhārasya upalabdhi sādhanasya ca sāmye api ekatarasya kāraṇa abhāvena abhāve a pyanyatara sabhdau= ena avinābhāvaḥ iti āśaḍkya sukhasya duḥkha anuṣaḍga upapattaye duḥkha hetu anuṣaṅgam eva āha sādhana iti atas na dvitīya sūtra vārti kaṭīkābhyām virodhaḥ sādhana pāratantryam kāryātvāt akāryasya ca sukhasya abhāvāt pāratantryam ca daṃḥkha hetuḥ yat āha sarva para vaśam duḥkham iti kṣayitvam ca sukhasya samavāyikāraṇavat tvāt tat api duḥkha hetuḥ iṣṭa viyogaḥ hi duḥkham janayati iti kṣayitvam kāme sati iti tu vyākhyānam duḥkha hetavaḥ iti bahuvacana viruddham atas svatantram eva idam hetu trayam 
NVTP_1.1.1.78	 kāmaḥ icchā sā ca sukha tad sādhanayoḥ vyāpikā na hi sukha tad sādhanam vā anicchataḥ sukham nāma sukha sādhanam ca tat api sulabham durlabham ca tatra durlabha icchā duḥkha eka phalā eva sulabha icchātu aniṣiddha sādhana gocarā niṣiddha sādhana gocarā ca tatra niṣaddha sādhāna gocarā api svarūpataḥ kāryataḥ ca adharma janana dvāreṇa avaśyam duḥkha phala iti aniṣiddha sulabha sādhāna gocarā api śarīra pāṭave satsati vā tatra asati duḥkha hetuḥ eva śarīra ādi pāṭave api sa vighnā nirvighnā ca tatra sa vighnā duḥkham eva prasūte nirvighnā api aniṣṭa saṃbhinna viṣayā tad viparītā ca tatra prathamā avaśyam 
NVTP_1.1.1.79	 duḥkha hetuḥ dvitīyā tu viphalā saphalā ca tatra prathamā duḥkha hetuḥ eva dvitīyā tu sa vilamba phalā avilambphalā ca tatra prathamāḥ avaśyam eva duḥkha hetuḥ dvitīyā api anāyati viśuddhā tad viparītā ca tatra prathamā duḥkha hetuḥ eva dvitīyā tu viṣayasya piriṇati virasa tvāt duḥkham eva prasūte ati vyāmohāt viṣayeṣu eva magnasya icchā antaram eva vā ubhayathā api anartha mūlam iti evam sukha anuṣaktaḥ kāmaḥ api duḥkha hetuḥ iti iha yadi api rāga dveṣa moha pravṛttayaḥ api duḥkha tadanuḍgi sādhana bhāvāt indriya ādi vat duḥkha tvena parisaṃkhyātum ucitāḥ tathā api na śarīra indriya ādi vyatirekeṇa amūṣām ātma lābhaḥ duḥkham prati vyāpāraḥ vā indriya ādīnām punar deṣa pravṛtti abhāve api duḥkham prati vyāpāraḥ jīvanmuktasya asti eva pravṛtti phalam tu dharma adharmau yadi api sukha duḥkha hetū tathā api ekaviṃśatividha duḥkha maya saṃsāra nṛtya śālā mūla stambha tvāt anayoḥ na atra parisaṃkhyānam na hi bhāvini janma antare śarīra indriya aviṣaya buddhi sukha duḥkhāni āhatya vyāpriyante yathā dharma adharmau 
NVTP_1.1.1.80–1.1.1.81^1	 etat eva abhisaṃdhāya kāraṇa rūpa dharma adharma uccheda krameṇa kārya rūpa ekaviṃśatividha duḥkhasya ucchedaḥ vārttika kṛtā darśitaḥ iti tathā eva vāttikam avatārayati ukta prakāra iti iha ca āgāmi dharma adharma nivṛttau= upāyaḥ tad sādhana pravṛtti parityāgaḥ utpanna nivṛtau tu upabhogaḥ iti darśitam tat ubhayam api anupapannam vāc buddhi śarīra ambham parityajya jīvitum aśaktayatvāt mṛte api śadīra ādi antarajra lepasya dupaneya tvāt upabhāgaḥ ca aśakyaḥ aniyata vipāka samaya tvāt ananta tvāt ananta phala tvāt ca bhoga avasthāyām api ananta karma antara utpāda natāyāḥ avarāmāt atha kathañcid upabhoga anutpādābhyām utpanna an utpannayoḥ śakyaḥ prakṣayaḥ tarhi śāstra vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ tatas eva tad siddheḥ iti āśaḍkya vārttikasya upaskurūte saṃśaya ādi iti saṃśaya ādi ityādi padena caturdaśā api nyāya parikara tvena saṃgṛhītāḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.81^2	 param anyāya iti anene mūlamūlībhāva vyavasthitāni catvāri api pramāṇāni nyāyaḥ mārgaḥ iva nyāya mārgaḥ niḥreyasa bhūmeḥ prāpti hetu tvāt dvādaśavidhā iti ātma ādi prameyam tat anena śāstrasya avasara upayogau darśitau tattva paribhāvanā iti anena abhyāsasya tat evam pūrva uktena nyāyena mokṣamāṇasya śāstre pravṛttiḥ tatas parikara parijñānam tatas nyāya mārga pariśodhanam tatas tena dvādaśavidha prameya āsādanam tatas abhyāsaḥ tatas prasaṃkhyānam tatas sa mūla doṣa anuṣaṅga nirmokṣaḥ tatas apravṛttiḥ tatas āgāminoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ asaṃcayaḥ iti evam anāgataḥ pravāhaḥ nivāritaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.82–1.1.1.84	 yadi api ca yāvat śarīra ādi bhāvinī pravṛttiḥ tathā api doṣa anuṣaṅga sahakāri virahāt na asau pravṛttiḥ tad kārya asamartha tvāt iti utpanna bhogam upapādayati anādi iti yadi api yathā anādau bhāva paramparāyām karmāṇi pracīyante tathā apacīcante api na hi ārambhe param bhavasya anāditā na nu upabhoge karma ārambhaḥ hi adhikāriṇi śarīre tat ca śarīra koṭi madhya patitam ekam śarīram kadācid kiñcid kvacid eva bhogaḥ tu na asti eva tat śarīram yatra na asti bhogasya tad āyatana tvāt tasmādāya vyaya paryālocanayā parimitam eva karma atas eva niyavipāka samayam api tasya ca krama bhāvibhiḥ api kiyadbhiḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.85	 kaiścid eva śarīrai rūpa bhogāt prakṣayaḥ api na durūpa pādaḥ tathā api āgama prāmāṇyāt kāya yaugapadyasya api prasaṃkhyāna phala tayā siddha tvāt ananta ām a niyata vipāka samaya tām ca abhyupagamya eva parihṛtam vibhūtimatā aneka kāla upabhogyam api ekadā bhujyate iti atra samudra pānam udāharaṇam yogardhi prabhāva sampannaḥ vividha phala bhoginaḥ vicitra svabhāvān ekadā eva bahūn kāyān icchā mātreṇa eva nirmimītaḥ iti atra daṇḍaka araṇya sṛṣṭiḥ u udāhaṇam iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.86–1.1.1.88	 iha kecid āhuḥ duḥkha nivṛtti puruṣa arthaḥ eva svarūpataḥ na bhavati sa upādhi tvāt sukham duḥkha abhāve satyeva bhavati iti sukha sādhana antara vat duḥkha abhāvaḥ api mṛtyate na nu saḥ eva puruṣasya samīhitaḥ iti tat uktam varam vṛndāvane araṇye kroṣṭa tvam abhivāñchitum na tu vaiśeṣikī muktim gautamaḥ gantum icchati 
NVTP_1.1.1.89	 iti tad anupapannam viparyāsasya api saṃbhavāt bhojana ādi sukhe sati eva hi bubhukṣā ādi duḥkham nivartate iti duḥkha nivṛtti artham eva bhojana ādi sukham mṛgyate na punar tat eva tasya samīhitam iti kim na kalpayate kvacid duḥkha bhāve api sukhasya iṣyamāṇa tvā diti ced na duḥkha nivṛtteḥ api kvacid sukha abhāve apīṣyamāṇa tvāt eva duḥkha nivṛttau satyām sukham eva bhaviṣyati iti abhisandhiḥ tāvat asti iti ced na sukha avasthāyām niyamataḥ duḥkha virahaḥ bhaviṣyati iti abhisandheḥ tatra api saṃbhavāt tasmāt yadi api duḥkha hānau sukham sukhe ca duḥkha hāniḥ niyatā tathā api 
NVTP_1.1.1.90–1.1.1.93	 paraspara nirapekṣam eva puruṣa artha tvam anayoḥ icchayoḥ api asaṃkīrṇa viṣaya tvāt anyaḥ tu āha bhavati eva hi duḥkha hāniḥ puruṣa arthaḥ kim tu anubhūyamāna tayā na hi viṣa ādi janya moha avasthāyām duḥkha nivṛttiḥ iti tad artham prekṣāvantaḥ pravartante tasmāt mokṣe duḥkha hāneḥ ananubhūyamāna tvāt na puruṣa artha tvam iti tat uktam duḥkha abhāvaḥ api na āvedyaḥ puruṣa artha tayā iṣyate na hi mūrcchā ādi avastha artham pravṛttaḥ dṛśyate sudhīḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.94	 iti tat api anupapannam putra ādi viyoga janya duḥkha hānim icchataḥ keṣāñcid viṣa śastra udūndhana dau= api pravṛtti darśanāt prekṣāvantaḥ na evam kurvanti iti ced na puruṣa artha tva avirodhāt na hi para dāreṣu śāstra niṣedhāt kuśa nivāritāḥ prekṣāvantaḥ na pravartante iti na tatra kāmaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ api tu alpīyaḥ sukham mahān anarthaḥ iti nivṛttiḥ tathā viṣa ādau= api pravṛttasya śāstra garhita tvāt alpīyān anarthaḥ nivartate mahīyān pravartate iti na te pravartante iti iyam eva hi prekṣā yat puruṣa artha tve api loka śāstra virodha parāmarśaḥ na tu apuruṣa artha tvāt eva sva rūpeṇa iṣyamāṇa tā mātra nibandhana tvāt puruṣartha tāyāḥ ataeva na yatra loka śāstra virodhaḥ tatra vyādhi ādi paripīḍitāḥ prayāga vaṭa prapāta anaśana ādinā api deham tyajantaḥ prekṣāvantaḥ dṛśyante na hi kaścid duḥkha nivṛttim anubhaviṣyāmi iti tad sādhane pravartate api tu duḥkha hāsyāmi iti api ca duḥkha nivṛtteḥ anubhūyamāna tā mātram vivakṣitam 
NVTP_1.1.1.95	 duḥkha nivṛtti sattau= adhiḥ vā ādyaḥ ced tuṣyatu durjanaḥ carame janmani anubhūyate eva samādhi prabhāvāt ātyantikī duḥkha nivṛttiḥ anāgatā vartamānā api aciram anubhūyate eva dvitīye tu prasakta kaṇṭaka ādi hetuka daḥkha nivṛtteḥ apuruṣa artha tva prasaṅgaḥ sarva dānanubhūyamāna tvāt tathā tve vā viṣaya antara saṃcāra abhāva prasaṅgāt nivṛtteḥ sarvadā tādavasthyāt iti tasmāt sarva dā ananubhūyamānā api yathā kaṇṭaka ādi janya duḥkha nivṛttiḥ puruṣa artha tayā puruṣam prayojayati tathā śāstra artha bhūtā api tat idam duḥkha nivṛtteḥ apuruṣa artha tvam ananubhūyamāna tayā eva ca apuruṣa artha tvam iti pakṣa dvayam ati nirvalam iti etat iti upekṣya tṛtīyam śaṅkate syāt etat iti tat uktam 
NVTP_1.1.1.96–1.1.1.101	 asatyāni durantāni samavyaya phalāni ca aśakyāni ca vastūni na ārabheta vicakṣaṇaḥ iti siddhānta vārttikam uddīpayati yadi api iti tat anena madhu viṣa saṃpṛkta anna bhojana dṛṣṭāntena samavyaya phala tvam apavargasya nirākṛtam yathā hi atra anarthasya bhūyas tvam arthasya tu kṣudra tvam na tathā apavarge api iti etena etat api nirastam yat uktam yathā duḥkha śabalam saṃsāra sukham anādeyam tathā sukha śabala tayā duḥkham api upādeyam kim na syāt dṛśyante hi sukha arthinaḥ yagādi duḥkham anubhavantaḥ iti yasya duḥkham upādeyam heyam tasya kim ucyatām heya hīnasya kā muktiḥ kena vā api upadiśyate 
NVTP_1.1.1.102	 iti yaḥ tu ghanatara duḥkha timira nirantarāt saṃsāra kāntārāt sukha khadyotikāsu dyotamānāsu api bibheti tam prati ayam nirasta tamaskatayā sugamaḥ mārge upadiśyate iti tat idam uktam tena mā bhūt atat ityādi nanu evam sati na asya sarva artha tā tathā ca jagataḥ śamāya iti anena virodhaḥ iti atas āha avivekinām api iti yadi api kasyacid apravṛttau= api na sarva artha tā asya hīyate iti prapañcitam adhastāt tathā api heyam heya tvena agṛhṇantaḥ mandāḥ kāruṇikeṇa grāhayitavyāḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.103	 nanu śāstreṇa tattva jñānāt vairāgyam vairāgyāt ca śāstre pravṛttiḥ iti durūttaram itaretara āśraya tvam iti atas āha śāstre pravṛtti iti duḥkhāt udvijataḥ bhoga vaimukhya mātram iha vairāgyam vivakṣitam na tu rāga abhāvaḥ eva iti arthaḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra artha tayā dvaividhya śaḍkām apanayati aika rūpyam dvairūpyam ca iti nanu puruṣa bhede api pravṛtteḥ dvaividhyam eva na hi kaścid sukham prāptum iva duḥkham api āptum pravartate na api kaścid duḥkha hānāya iva sukha hānāya api iti atas āha puruṣa bhedaḥ rāga vairāgyābhyām iti nanu sukhasya heya tvam eva kutas iti atas āha prāptavyasya iti avivekinām tu pravṛttiḥ dvi rūpa iti uktam vārttika kṛtāḥ iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.104	 prakṛtam upasaṃharan= eva aprakṛta upanipāta śaḍkām api apanetum vṛttavartiṣyamāṇe anukīrtayati tat anena iti tad avayavam vivarītu mukta tātparya sphoraṇa artham iti śeṣaḥ alaukika tvāt lokasya asmad ādeḥ niti aparokṣa tvāt ayuktam aprāmāṇikam vipratiṣiddham mithas vyāpaka viruddham pravṛttyai niṣkampa pravṛttyai kim tarhi pramāṇam iti gṛhītam iti anuvartate rajata jñānam idam śukla bhāsvara rūpavat dravyam rajatam iti evam jñānam iti arthaḥ paricchinatti uktam artham ālambya paricchitti rūpam jāyate iti arthaḥ śuktikā jñānam api iti idam śukla bhāsvara rūpam śuktikā dravyam na rajatam iti jñānam iti arthaḥ yadi evam katham anayoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ iti atas āha kevalam iti rajata samāropa apavādābhyām iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.105–1.1.1.106^1	 samāropa apavāda svabhāvatayā iti arthaḥ tat evam pariccheda dvāreṇa paricchedakam unnīyate iti paricchedasya eva sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ pariccheda tva apariccheda tve darśite na ca ekasya eva jñānasya viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ jātyā hi buddhiḥ anubhavaḥ smṛtiḥ ca tatra smutiḥ apramā eva anubhavaḥ tu svarūpa anubhavaḥ asvarūpa anubhavaḥ ca saḥ ayam viṣaya kṛtaḥ viśeṣaḥ nānā viṣayā ca ekā buddhiḥ bhavati eva tatas ca sā eva buddhiḥ svarūpa avasthitena arthena nirūpyamāṇā pramā asvarūpa avasthitena nirūpyamāṇā tu apramā iti tathābhūta avacchinnā anubhava tvam eva pramāṇa tvam atathābhūtena tu avacchinnam apramāṇa tvam iti bhavati apramāṇasya api sāmānya paricchedaka tvam iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.106^2	 racitā bhūmiḥ kim etāvatā iti āha asti tāvat asādhāraṇam kāraṇam asamarthāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ tathā eva unnīyamānam tasya ca vyāpāraḥ viparīta artha paricchedaḥ eva asādhāraṇaḥ tat ca evaṃbhūta vyāpāra upakaraṇam apramāṇam iti vyavahniyate evam ca pravṛtti sāmarthyā sāmarthya saṃdehe api yadi tad janakam apramāṇam asamarthā eva sā atha na tad apramāṇam tad janyā pravṛttiḥ api na asamartha iti apramāṇān niyataḥ samartha pravṛtti vyatirekaḥ pramāṇam ca atra ubhaya vyatireka grāhakam viruddha kārya tvam liṅgam prakṛta kāryasya tad vyatireka grāhi ca pratyakṣa madhyavasā iyam iti na apramāṇāt artha vyabhicāriṇor athavyabhicāri jñāna vyāpārāt iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.107	 siddhaḥ vyatirekaḥ ki ca atas iti atas āha tathā ca iti arthavat tvam artha avyabhicāri tvam artha avyabhicāri anubhava janaka tvam iti arthaḥ nanu tasyāḥ iti atra katham anantara tvena prakṛta ām asamarthām vihāya vyavahitvena aprakṛtā api samartha eva pravṛtti parāmṛśyate iti atas āha asamarthā tu iti pūrva prakāntam yogyam eva prakṛtam ucyate na tu anantara uktam iti arthaḥ nanu anuditasya anuvādaḥ kkopa yujyate iti atas āha saṃprati iti pūrvam vyākhyātum idānīm ākṣeptum iti arthaḥ ākṣepa samādhānayoḥ sphuṭa avabhāsi tve api saṃgraha vivaraṇayoḥ pauna rūktyam pariharan= āha ākṣipati iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.108	 saṃdehāt api pravṛtteḥ tatra tatra darśanāt niru ucchvāsam ākṣepam ujjīvayati na tāvat iti amum eva artham bhāṣyeṇa saṃvadati sā iyam iti uktā bhāṣya kutā iti śeṣaḥ kim atas yadi evam iti atas āha na ca iti artha viniścayaḥ ukta rūpaḥ śreyaḥ hetuta anumāna sahitaḥ iti yāvat prāmāṇya avadhāraṇam śreyaḥ hetu ta aliṅga parāmarśa prasava ucitam antareṇa iti arthaḥ evaṃrūpa tā ca 
NVTP_1.1.1.109	 prāmāṇya avadhāraṇasya vyāpti smaraṇa sāhityam eva iti tasya api bījam samuccinoti śreyaḥ hetuta anumāna nimitta vyāpti grahaṇam ca iti tābhyām vinā iti svarūpa niścaya śreyaḥ hetuta anumānābhyām vinā iti arthaḥ vyāpti grahaṇa ānantarye api tad phalasya eva anumānasya yogyatayā prakrānta tvāt imam eva vārtika artham pariśodhayan sphuṭayati tat idam uktam iti niścaya anumāne na prāmāṇya avadhāraṇa anumāna bīja bhūta vyāpti grahaṇābhyām vinā te ca na pravṛttyā vinā pravṛttiḥ ca na niścaya anumānābhyām vinā iti ākṣepa saṃkṣapaḥ iha ca dvidhā pravṛttiḥ aihikaphalā āmuṣmikaphalā ca tatra amuṣmika phalā prāmāṇya avadhāraṇa pūrvikā eva aihika phalā tu apekṣita upāya tā jñāna mātra adhīnāḥ artha niścayam api na apekṣate prāk eva pramāṇa srūpa jñānam kutastarām tad viniścayam yatra api pravṛtteḥ prāk eva pramāṇa tattva viniścayaḥ tatra api asau sva hetu balāt āyataḥ na pravṛttim prati prayojakaḥ anyathā ekāntika vijayā niścaye prāmāṇya ākṣepakaḥ eva vijigīṣuḥ kathāyām na pravarteta 
NVTP_1.1.1.110^1	 na hi jalpataḥ vitaṇḍayataḥ vā avaśyam aikāntikaḥ vijayaḥ tasmāt artha aniścaye api pravṛttiḥ iti ubhaya vādi siddham hṛdi nidhāya siddhāntam upakramate tatra brūmaḥ iti dṛṣṭa artheṣu iti adṛṣṭa artha āgama ādi vyudāsaḥ tatra pravṛtteḥ phala abhisaṃbandha aniścayāt anabhyāsa daśā āpanneṣu iti abhyāsa daśa āpannā pitṛ vacana ādi vyudāsaḥ te hi pramāṇa tayā pravṛtteḥ prāgava niścīyante abhyāsa śva aviparītaḥ vivakṣitaḥ tena sva ātmani abhyāse api pravṛtti sāmarthyāt eva tat niścayaḥ viparīta abhyāsa virahāt sa ca viṣaya gocaraḥ tat na antarīyaka artha gocaraḥ vā tad jātīya tva avadhāraṇa upāyaḥ yatra svarūpataḥ api na asti tatra pravṛtti sāmarthyāt eva tad gocarasya prāmāṇya avadhāraṇam yathā vaidya vacanāt anartha nivṛtti saṃbhāvayataḥ asaṃstuta pradeśa sthiteṣu mūleṣu 
NVTP_1.1.1.110^2	 yatra tu svarūpa abhyāsaḥ asti eva tad gatam tu śreyaḥ sādhanam abhyastam tatra pravṛtti sāmarthyena tad sādhana tva grāhiṇaḥ prāmāṇyam yathā angiḥ pāka ādi samarthaḥ iti saṃbhāvita āpta tvasya vacanāt upalabhya svayam pacataḥ yatra api śreyaḥ sādhana tve abhyāsaḥ svarūpe tu anabhyāsaḥ tatra api svarūpa gocarasya eva prāmāṇyam pravṛtti sāmarthyāt avasīyate yathā agniḥ pāka ādi samarthaḥ eva iti niścitavataḥ apariśīlita vana vahnau sarvatra eva artha bhūyaḥ tvam viparyaye tu anartha māndyam saṃbhāvayataḥ pravṛttiḥ sva rūpa śreyaḥ sādhana tva niścaye api phala saṃdehaḥ iva iti āha no khalu iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.111	 tat amī saṃśayānāḥ api pravartamānāḥ phalaḥ iva sva rūpa śreyaḥ sādhana tvayoḥ iti śeṣaḥ pramāṇasya svarūpa grāhiṇaḥ śreyaḥ sādhanatva grāhiṇaḥ ca iti arthaḥ tattvam pramāṇa tvam artha avyabhicāri pramāsādhana tvam iti yāvat viniścitya artha avi abhicāri pramāvi niścaya dvāreṇa iti śeṣaḥ tad jātīyasya anyasya etāvatā eva samartha tve abhyāsadaśā āpannasya iti dṛṣṭa artha pramāṇa saṃgraha artham pravṛtti sāmarthyāt prāk eva samarthāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ pūrvam eva iti tena ayam arthaḥ yadi api dṛṣṭa artheṣu abhyāsadaśā āpanneṣu api pravṛtti sāmarthyam asti tena api ca prāmāṇyam avadhārayitum tatra śakyate tathā api tad jātīya tva lakṣaṇena eva liḍgena pravṛtteḥ prāk eva avadhārite prāmāṇye tad pramāturu uttara kālam pramitsā eva na asti tad nibandhana tvāt ca anumāna pravṛtteḥ yadi punar pramitsā anapekṣam eva samartha pravṛtti janaka tvam parāmṛśyate tadā kā kṣatiḥ tena api anumīyatām prāmāṇyam pramāṇa saṃplavasya api vyavasthāpanāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.112	 nanu kim idam tat jātīya tvam na tāvat pramāṇa jātīya tvam sādhya aviśiṣṭa tva prasaṅgāt na api samartha pravṛtti janaka jātīya tvam tat hi samartha pravṛtti saṃbandhaḥ vā syāt tad upahitaḥ vā niyata prāc abhāvaḥ na tāvat ādyaḥ pravṛtteḥ prāk eva iti vacanāt na api uttaraḥ tasya atīndriyasya liḍgam vinā pratyetum aśakyatvāt liḍgam ca tasya prāmāṇya eka niyatasya yadi asti tadā prāmāṇyam eva tena anumīyatām kim tad jātīyatva anumānena prāmāṇya aniyatasya tu tasya anumānena kim na api pratyakṣa siddhaḥ eva kaścid dharmaḥ tad jātīya tvam pratyakṣa tve tu tasya anabhyāsa daśa āpanana gocare api pramāṇe pratīti prasaṅgāt tathā ca 
NVTP_1.1.1.113	 tatra api pravṛtteḥ prāk eva prāmāṇya avadhāraṇam syāt vyāpteḥ api prāk eva pratīta tvāt na hi ayam kvacid api tad jātīya tvena prāmāṇyam na anumitavāt tatra na asti eva tat jātīya tvam kim pratyakṣeṇa pratīyatām iti ced na abhyāsa daśā āpanneṣu tad jātīya tvena prāmāṇye anumīyamāne pravṛtti sāmarthya anumita prāmāṇyasya sādhana vikala tayā dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa tva prasaṅgāt tasmāt tad jātīya tvam atiriktam na paśyāmaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.114	 satyam tathā api jñānasya viṣya nibandhana tvāt tad tad viṣaya upādhayaḥ eva te te jñāna upādhayaḥ taiḥ tairūpādhibhirūpādhīyamānam jñānam eva tat jātīyam tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam bhavati te ca upādhayaḥ pratibhedam sva saṃjñābhiḥ abhidhātum aśakyāḥ iti tad jātīya tvam iti anayā vācaḥ bhaḍgyāḥ darśitāḥ atas eva atra vīpsā draṣṭavyā 
NVTP_1.1.1.115^1	 tat tat jātīya tvam iti tathā hi anubhavaḥ tāvat svarūpa prakārau= ālambate tatra dharmi svarūpeṇa upadhīyamānaḥ anubhavaḥ pramaiva iti tena rūpeṇa anubhūte tasmin pramātvam eva anubhūtam bhavati iti agre sphuṭībhaviṣyati prakāra viṣayaḥ tu anubhavaḥ ubhayathā kaścid svarūpa prakāreṇa upādhīyate kaścid asvarūpa prakāreṇa api iti atas kvacid saṃśayaḥ tatra svarūpa prakāreṇa upahitam anubhava vivektum viśiṣṭāḥ prakāra upādhayaḥ bhavanti te ca niyamena vibhrama viṣaya virodhitayā nirdhārita svabhāva bhedāḥ guṇa ādayaḥ eva tat idam sāmānyatas tāvat lakṣaṇa sahacarita lakṣya viṣaya jñāna tvam eva jñāna gatam tat jātīya tvam iti pratyakṣe gatiḥ yadā tu apratyakṣe lakṣye lakṣaṇena jñānam janyate tadā anumānam tat iti tasya anyathā eva gatiḥ bhaviṣyati iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.115^2	 tatra dravye gandhavati pṛthivī jñānam ityādi sāmānyatas kara caraṇa ādimati śarīra jñānam ityādi viśeṣataḥ guṇeṣu ketakī ādau saurabha jñānam śaḍkha ādau śveta jñānam ityādi karmaṇi tu avātulena tiṣṭhatā tīvra vega asaṃskṛtena calat jala ādi su accha vilokana ādi virahiṇā yat dravyam calati iti upalabhyate tat tathā iti evam teṣu teṣu viśeṣeṣu te te viśeṣāḥ vyabhicāra virodhinaḥ na pratipadam anukramitum śakyante tat evam tad tad upādhi viśiṣṭa tad tad viṣaya anubhava tvam eva tat jātīya tvam iti mantavyam tat evaṃbhūtasya jñānasya viṣayana antarīyaka tvena upādhi abhyāsaḥ eva abhyāsa daśā āpanna tvam yatra tu saḥ eva arthaḥ bhūyas bhūyas abhyastaḥ tatra saṃvādaka tvam eva tat jātīya tvam evam tāvat bāhya pratyakṣam samarthitam 
NVTP_1.1.1.116–1.1.1.117	 pratyakṣa samāna nyāya tayā āgamasya prāmāṇyam samarthayati evam ca iti atra api tad jātīya tvam āpta praṇetṛka tvam abhyāsadaśā āpanna tvam punar etasya bhūyas darśanena mantrāyurvede tad jātīya tvāya prāmāṇya avinā abhāva siddhiḥ mantra āyurvedasya anabhyāsa daśā āpanna tvam tat asiddhaḥ nivedayiṣyate sūtrakāreṇa dvitīya adhyāye yathā ca prāmāṇyam pravṛtti sāmarthyena avadhāryate anabhyāsa daśā āpanneṣu tathā prāmāṇyam api pravṛtti viparyayeṇa yathā ca pravṛtteḥ prāk eva abhyāsa daśā āpanneṣu tad jātīya tayā prāmāṇyam avadhāryate tathā prāmāṇyam api iti mantavyam upādhi virodhaḥ ca tat jātīya tvam tad abhyāse eva abhyāsa daśā āpanna tvam yathā candramasi candra dvaya jñānam śaḍkhe pīta jñānam guḍe tikta jñānam ityādi tasmāt sandigdhe pravṛtti sāmarthyam avadhāraṇīyam iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.118	 syāt etat sāmarthya punar asyāḥ phalena abhisaṃbandhaḥ atha phala jñānasya eva prāmāṇyam katham avadhāraṇīyam iti atra keṣāñcid matam āha na ca iti na punar ūdanyā upaśamam api parīkṣyate iti udanya upaśamanam api iti arthaḥ tat etat anupapannam phala jñānam hi phalasya siddha avasthasya sādhanān arha tayā niṣprayojanī bhūta tvāt vā na parīkṣyet tad tad jātīya jñānasya sarvāsu avasthāsu artha avyabhicāritayā niḥśaṅka tvāt vā iti na tāvat ādyaḥ phalasya siddha avastha tve tadvat tad sādhanībhūtasya api niṣprayojanī bhūta tvāt aparīkṣya tva prasaṅgāt uttara uttarulābhisaṃdhānena tad sādhanam parīkṣyate iti ceta 
NVTP_1.1.1.119	 phale api evam astu siddhaḥ eva hi phale parīkṣite tad sādhanasya tathā atva siddhau= uttara uttarulābhisandhiḥ syāt na api dvitīyaḥ phala jñānasya api bhūyas bhūyas spapna ādi avasthāsu vyabhicāra darśanāt svastha avasthasya phala jñānam na vyabhicarati iti ced evam tarhi pirīkṣitam eva phala jñānam syāt tathā hi yat svastha avasthasya phala jñānam tat avyabhicārī iti vyāpti siddhau yatra eva tathābhūta jñāna tvam paśyati tatra eva avyabhicāram avadhārayati iti anena abhiprāyeṇa āha vayam tu iti asya api abhyāsa daśa āpanna tvam prāmāṇya avinā mūta liḍga upalambhaḥ tathā tad jātīya tvam punar svastha avasthasya phala jñāna tvam eva etena icchā dveṣa prayatna jñānam vyākhyātam 
NVTP_1.1.1.120–1.1.1.121	 nanu yat vijñāna dṛṣṭāntayitavyam tasya api prāmāṇyam katham sādhanīyam evam tat tad sādhanasya api dṛṣṭānta paramparāyāḥ katham iti atas āha na ca iti phala jñānasya iti upalakṣaṇam tad jātīya tvena liḍgena prāmāṇye sādhiyitavye yat yat dṛṣṭāntīkriyate tasya tasya iti mantavyam yat yavam pravṛtti sāmarthyam anavakāśam eva na hi asti tat vijñānam yat sarvathā eva apūrva viṣayam tathā ca pramāṇator atha pratipatti pravṛtti sāmarthyayoḥ katham anādi tvam āha vārttikakāraḥ iti atas āha eteṣu ca madhye iti śaḍkita vyabhicāram tad jātīya tva aparāmarśāt iti śeṣaḥ yadi api phalam na pravṛtti viṣayaḥ tathā api tad sādhana gocarāyāḥ tad saṃtāna gocarāyāḥ eva vā pravṛtteḥ tad jātīya phala antara saṃbandhaḥ tat na āntarīyaka vijātīya phala saṃbandhaḥ vā svasya nara antarasya vā pravṛtti sāmarthyam phala jñānasya draṣṭāvyam 
NVTP_1.1.1.122–1.1.1.123	 tat evam samāna nyāya tayā rūpa ādi bāhi artha pratyakṣa prāmāṇya samarthana anantaram śabdra prāmāṇyam samarthya tad ubhaya upapattaye samāna nyāya tayā eva āntara pratyakṣa jñāneṣu madhye phala jñāna prāmāṇyam samarthitam samāna nyāya tayā eva icchā dveṣa prayatna gocarasya api jñānasya prāmāṇya samarthanam sūcitam iti anaṃvyavasāyaḥ avaśiṣyate tasya ca anumāna samāna nyāya tayā anumāna prāmāṇya samarthana anantaram eva samarthanam kariṣyate iti abhiprāyavān āha anumānasya iti dvidhā hi vyabhicāra śaḍkā kāraṇataḥ svarūpataḥ ca sā ca vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā grāhakaiḥ eva pramāṇaiḥ apanīyate iti bhavati nirasta samasta vyabhicāra śaṅkam anumiti jñānam tasya evaṃbhūtasya svatas eva prāmāṇyam niścīyate iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.124^1	 nanu pramāṇa tva aviśeṣe api katham anumiteḥ eva svatas na pratyakṣa ādeḥ iti atas āha anumeyā iti anumiti jñānam hi arthasya tathātvam vyavacchindat eva utpadyate vahnimān eva ayam iti tathā ca anuvyavasānena anuvyavasīyamānam idam sva sva artha avadhāraṇa ātmakam eva avasīyate na ca aviparīta arthaka tvam anubhavasya anadhyavasya tā avadhāraṇa ātmaka tvam asya avasitam bhavati tathā ca tat avaśyam avaseyam tat eva ca prāmāṇyam kadācid evaṃbhūta anuvyavasāye api viparyaya tva śaḍkā tad avaskandati iti avaśiṣyate sā ca liṅga samuttha tvāt eva na asti na hi viśeṣa darśana grasta utpattau śaḍkā avakāśaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.124^2	 tat etat āha na hi iti liṅga ākāram vijñānam niścita avyabhicāram iti śeṣaḥ pratyakṣa śābda jñāne tu na ayoga vyavaccheda ātmake api tu āropānārāpa sādhāraṇa viṣaya mātra avabhāsinī tathā ca anuvyavasāyena api tathā eva anubhūyete na tu avadhāraṇa ātmaka tayā iti na tayoḥ svatas prāmāṇya grahaḥ atha daivāt ayoga vyavaccheda ātmake eva utpadyete anuvyavasīyete ca tadā ca niyāmakam antar bhāvya eva tad abhāve tu aviśeṣāt avadhāraṇa ātmaka tvam paribhūya tad atad rūpa sādhāraṇam eva avatiṣṭheta iti āśayavān niyāmaka abhāvam eva āha pratyakṣa jñānam tu iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.125	 dhūma ādi yukta dhūma dhvaja ādi jñāne hi yadi api arthasya api arthena avyabhicāraḥ asti yadi api ca arthāt api tathābhūtāt eva tat jñānam jāyate tathā api avyabhicāraḥ vā tad grahaḥ vā prāktanaḥ tatrākiścitkaraḥ eva indriya āpāta mātrāt eva yugapad ubhayoḥ api eka jñāna avabhāsitayā parāmarśa kāla anapekṣaṇāt aparāmṛṣṭasya ca aniyāmaka tvāt tat idam uktam api tu sattā mātreṇa avasthitāt iti avyabhicāriṇaḥ api iti śeṣaḥ etena śaḍkā mātram apanīyate jñāna antaraiḥ iti yat uktam kaiścid tat nirastam śaḍkā hi saṃśayaḥ eva abhidhīyate sa ca tattva nirṇaya vyatirekeṇa apanetum aśakyaḥ eva iti tattva nirṇaya upāyaḥ anusartavyaḥ tathā ca jñāna svarūpa grāhiṇaḥ kauṇṭhye pratyakṣa ādi antara abhāve ca anumānam eva upāyaḥ iti tat āha pravṛtti sāmarthyam iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.126^1	 syāt etat yadi pratyakṣa śābda jñānayoḥ paratas prāmāṇyam tat kim idānīm anuvyavasāyasya api paratas eva tathā ca liḍgam niścitam eva niścāyakam iti anena nyāyena liṅga antara paramparā jñānam anavasthām avatārayati iti atas āha jñāna gatā iti atra api sā eva yuktiḥ atad rūpa vyudāsena eva sva viṣayam ālambya eva utpatteḥ tathā eva anubhavaḥ utpatteḥ eva ārabhya viṣaya viśeṣa grahaṇa grasta tvāt ca na śaḍka avakāśaḥ viśeṣaḥ ca anuvyavasāya tvam eva na hi ajānanna api kaścid jānāmi iti anuvyavasyati na ca śuktikā ākāre jñāne rajatam jānāmi iti syāt iti tat idam uktam tādṛśasya iti upalakṣaṇam ca etat sa bāhī abhyantaram dharmi mātra gocaram api pratyakṣam svatas eva pramāṇam vibhramasya api nirālamba nasye kvacid anupapatteḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.126^2	 uktu yuktim hṛdi nidhāya ati diśati etena iti upamānam upamitiḥ iti arthaḥ vyākhyātam svatas avadhārya prāmāṇyatayā iti śeṣaḥ na hi ati deśa vākya artha jñāna sādṛśya jñānayoḥ prāmāṇye niśvite upamitiḥ ābhāsībhavati yadi api ca anumāna upamāna anuvyavasāya dharmi jñānānām api prāmāṇyam paratas api śakya graham eva santi hi tatra api yathāyogam liṅga sādṛśya jñāna samuttha tva ādīni tad jātīya tva liṅgāni tathā api koṣṭha gatyā svatas eva prāmāṇya grahaḥ atra na svayam iti saḥ eva darśitaḥ vipratipannam prati tu paratas eva sādhanīyam tat iti parama arthaḥ atas svatas eva iti avadhāraṇam na ayoga vyavacchede na api anya yoga vyavacchede kim tarhi atyanta ayoga vyavacchedaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.127	 nanu etāvatā api vijñāna karaṇānam indriya ādīnām prāmāṇyasya kutas siddhiḥ na hi phala yathārtha tvam eva amīṣām prāmāṇyam iti atas āha sevadanasya ca iti nanu indriya ādayaḥ yadi artha vyāmi cāriṇaḥ katham artha dhiyam avyabhicāriṇī janayeyuḥ tathā tve vā rāsabhaḥ api vahna dhiyam avyabhicāriṇī jana ced aviśeṣāt iti atas āha na ca iti yathā ārdra indhanam dahana vyamicārī api dahana saṃbandhāt 
NVTP_1.1.1.128–1.1.1.129	 dahana avi abhicāriṇam dhūmam janayan na niyoga paryanuyogau= arhati kāraṇa svābhāvyāt tathā indriya ādi api artha vyabhicāriṇam tathāvidha sahakārī upabṛṃhitam tena arthena saṃbandhāt tad artha avyabhicāri jñānam janayet iti arthaḥ tat etat prāmāṇyam na avaśyam sarvatra avadhāryate tadā śrayasyā eva saṃvedanasya sarvatra anavadhāraṇāt tathā sati ca anavasthāyāḥ viṣaya saṃcāraḥ na syāt tasmāt tīvra saṃvegi tayā yat tu saṃvedanam avaśyam saṃvedanīyam yatra yatra ca aparaḥ viśaṣataḥ sāmānyatas vā vipratipadyate jijñāsate vā tatra tatra prāmāṇyam uktena apāyena avadhāraṇīyam iti atas na anavasthā iti āśa yavān upasaṃhāra vyājena uktam artham saṃkalayya āha tasmāt atha saṃdehāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.130–1.1.1.132	 nanu artha aniśvayena api pravartamānaḥ na hi tad sādhana tām anumāya pravartitum arhati arthi tva abhāvāt na hi tad sādhanatva anumānam vyāpti grahaṇam vinā na ca saḥ api pravṛtti vinā iti tad avastham eva itaretara āśraya tvam iti atas āha arthasya iti yadi api prāmāṇya aniścaya vat apekṣita upāya tva aniścayena api tatra tatra pravartate tathā api apekṣita upāya tām pākṣikīm api uḥ arīkṛtya pravṛttiḥ na ca tad saṃśayaḥ tasyām api anupalabdhāyām anyatra api syāt atas punar api upalabdhiḥ āyātā iti atas anāditām ādāya eva parihṛtam artha pratipattiḥ iti vārttike yadi api artha śabdaḥ apekṣita upāyam eva āha tasya eva pravṛtti viṣaya tvāt aryamāna tvāt ca tathā api dharmi mātra pratipatti anumeya pratipattyoḥ bhinna kāla tvāt apekṣita tvāt ca tathā eva vyācaṣṭe artha pratipattiḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.133	 nanu pramāṇasya prayojanavat tvam ākṣiptam vā samādhīyeta jijñāsitam vā jñāpyeta na tāvat ādyaḥ na hi asti puruṣaḥ yaḥ pramāṇam niṣprayojanam iti brūyāt tad mūla tvāt sarva puruṣa artha siddheḥ yasya tu puruṣa arthaḥ na asti sa nirūcchvāsaḥ eva śīryeta na api dvitīyaḥ tasya saṃśaya ādi vat sūtra pāṭhā anantaram eva jñāpayitum ucita tvāt iti atas āha tatra idam iti na iyam pramāṇa prayojana jijñāsā kim nāma śāstra arthaubhūtasya parama nyāyasya niḥśreyasam prati guru pāya tve manyamānena laghīyati pravṛtti upāyam vidyamāne śāstra ārambhaḥ eva ākṣipyate sa ca samādhātum ārabdhaḥ iti arthaḥ daśānām duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam mumukṣutā dāḍhrayā artham ātmanaḥ yāthātmyam sakala upādhi vinirmukta tvam tasya bhāvanam dhyānam ādi grahaṇena tu tad upāya bhūtāḥ pravṛttayaḥ yama niyama āsana prāṇāyāma dhāraṇa alakṣaṇa gṛhyante ātma tattva sākṣātkāraḥ iti samādhiḥ vairāgyam 
NVTP_1.1.1.134	 paramā vaśīkāraḥ paripākaḥ sa vāsana kleśa nirmokṣaḥ etena sāḍgopāḍgaḥ yogaḥ darśitaḥ śaḍkāmukvāḥ bhāṣyam uttarayati tatra idam upaniṣṭhate iti tathā api nyāyasya guru pāya tve na parihṛtam nyāya nirṇota arthasya api pravṛtti apekṣāṇāt pravṛttasya nyāya anapekṣaṇāt ityataḥ āha etat uktam bhavati iti nanu ubhayoḥ api tulya tve kutas viśeṣāt pramāṇam eva vyutpādyate na pravṛtti parīti ate āha tathā api iti śravaṇa manana nididhi a āsana sākṣātkāra lakṣaṇāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ svarūpataḥ phalataḥ ca pramāṇa antarbhūta tvāt tad vyutpādanam eva pravṛtti vyutpādanam na ca pravṛtti vyutpādanena pramāṇam vyutpāditam bhavati na hi pravṛtteḥ phalam pramāṇam tad svarūpam vā iti arthaḥ nanu śāstra arthasya prayojana vyutpādana avasare pramāṇam arthavat iti kutas na hi pramāṇam śāstrarthaḥ api tu nyāya iti atas āha sāmānya abhidhānam ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.135	 tat anena prabandhena niṣprayojana tva aśakya prayojana tva anabhimata prayojana tva upāya gaurava śaḍkāḥ parihṛtāḥ tat kim aparam avaśiṣyate yad artham loka vṛttam anūdyate iti atas prathama tātparyam anusmārayan= eva vārttikam avatārayati prāmāṇya iti apramāṇena iti atra api yadi api vā añmanasa visaṃvādaḥ niṣedha vidhi upāyaḥ eva hi pramāṇam tasmāt niṣedha upāya tām jānataḥ api apramāṇena niṣedhāmi iti vacanam manaḥ visaṃvādyava tathā api vyāmohāt api upapatteḥ evaṃbhūta abhiprāya sthairye api na asmākam kācid kṣatiḥ iti etāvatā anujñā eva āttaram dattam vāḍmanasayoḥ visaṃvādaḥ iti prāmāṇya agrahe pramāṇena iti evam vaktum na śakyate 
NVTP_1.1.1.136–1.1.1.137	 tatas pramāṇena iti evam vadataḥ avaśyam prāmāṇyam manasi viparivartate tathā ca agṛhīta prāmāṇyena iti vacanam manaḥ visaṃvādi iti arthaḥ loka vṛttam abādhitaḥ vyavahāraḥ iti arthaḥ nanu pramāṇena khalu ayam jñāta ityādi bhāṣyam loka vṛtta anuvādaḥ astu pramāṇataḥ ityādi punar katham iti atas āha kāraṇa pradarśana dvāreṇa iti na hi loka vṛttam svarūpeṇa upayujyate kim tarhi tasya avaśya abhyupeya tayā tad upāyaḥ api avaśya abhyupeyaḥ iti anena abhisandhinā sa upāyam eva tad anūdyate iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.138	 āgāmi bhāṣye heya ādīnām sphuṭa tvāt tasya idānīm akṣara arthaḥ vyākriyate iti mā śaḍkiṣṭhāḥ iti āha asya eva iti vārttika saṃbaddhaḥ granthoḥ athapadāni iti ākāraḥ vārttika granthaḥ tasya tādṛśaḥ eva bhāṣya gataḥ bhāṣya saṃbaddhaḥ granthaḥ tasya iti arthaḥ amidheyānām paurvāparya niyamāya guṇa pradhāna bhāve jijñāsyamāne abhidhāna rūpasya śāstrasya kaḥ prastāvaḥ iti atas āha śāstra śabdaḥ iti evam tarhi heya ādīnām śāstra artha rūpa tayā na pṛthak koṭi tvam tathā ca eka koṭika tayā kim apekṣya guṇa pradhāna bhāva cintā iti atas āha atra ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.139–1.1.1.140	 katham punar anena pramāṇa ādi caturvargaḥ atra labhyate iti vārttikam anukta upālabhbhaḥ mā bhūt iti atas āha tena iti tad mūla tvāt itara siddheḥ iti siddhiḥ pratītiḥ niṣpattiḥ ca tatra heya upāyayoḥ pratītiḥ eva adhigantavyasya tu pratītiḥ niṣpattiḥ ca yadi api ca hānasya api pramāṇa rūpasya pratītiḥ asti eva tathā api pramāṇāt eva iti tat itarā iti uktam niṣpattiḥ tu hānasya ajñānāt eva yasmāt kim tad jñānena jñānāt tu yasmāt tasya pramāṇa āyattatvam eva iti bhāvaḥ pramātṛ ādi caturvarge tu pramātṛ prameyayoḥ siddhiḥ pratītiḥ eva pramāyāḥ ca niṣpattiḥ api iti tat idam uktam pramāyāḥ ca tad kārya tvāt iti nanu pramātṛ ādīnām api prayojanavat tvāt arthavat iti anena kim pramāṇasya ādhikyam āhitam iti atas āha atiśāyane matuciti 
NVTP_1.1.1.141^1	 nanu asya caturvarga dvayasya niḥśreyasa adhigamam prati vikalpaḥ samuccayaḥ vā ubhayam ā api anupapannam abhinna tvāt tathā hi yaḥ eva arthaḥ pramātā prameyam pramitiḥ iti saḥ eva heyaḥ adhigantavyaḥ iti yaḥ eva arthaḥ hāna upāyau= iti saḥ eva pramāṇam iti saṃśaya ādīnām api nyāya parikara tayā nyāya śarīra tvāt tasya ca pramāṇa tvāt iti tasmāt abhinna tvāt na vacana bhaḍgi bheda mātreṇa vikalpaḥ na api samuccayaḥ na hi bhavati tarūṇā vā vṛkṣeṇa vedam sādhanīyam tarūu ṛkṣābhyām vā iti atas āha vivakṣā bhedenati tad anupapatteḥ iti ata anena nimitta bhedam abhipraiti tena ayam arthaḥ yadi api ubhayatra api ṣoḍaśa eva padārthāḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ tathā api yathā pramāṇtvena pramāṇam jñeyam tathā hāna tvena api anyathā hāna antaram anuśriyeta nirarthakam ca pramāṇaṃsyāt 
NVTP_1.1.1.141^2	 pramāṇa tve ca ajñāte hānatā na nirvahet yathā ca svarūpeṇa saṃśaya ādayaḥ jñeyāḥ pramāṇa parikara tayā tathā hāna upāyatayā api anyathā upāya antaram anuśriyeta nirarthakāḥ ca ete syuḥ parikara tve ca ajñāte upāya tā na nirvahet yathā ca śarīra ādayaḥ daśa prameya tayā jñeyāḥ tathā heya tayā api anyathā aheyāḥ syuḥ heya antaram ca anuśriyeta prameya tve ca ajñāte heya tā na nirvahet yathā ca apavargaḥ prameya tayā jñeyaḥ tathā adhigantavya tayā api anyathā adhigamya antaram anuśriyeta anupādeyaḥ ca syāt prameya tayā ca ajñāte adhigantavya tā na nirvaheta yathā ca ātmā prameya tayā adhigantavyaḥ tathā pramātṛ tayā api anyathā pramātṛ antaram anuśriyeta anavasthā ca syāt prameya tve ca ajñāte sa upādhi nirūpa adhi rūpa tayā 
NVTP_1.1.1.142–1.1.1.143	 heya upādeyate na nirvaheca ātām yathā ca buddhiḥ buddhi tvena tathā tabhdedaḥ pramiti tayā api anyathā pramiti antaram anuśriyeta niṣphalam vā pramāṇam syāt prameya tve ca ajñāte heya tā na nirvahet iti tasmāt te eva pramāṇa ādayaḥ ubhayathā jñāyantām iti vivakṣitvā ubhaya caturvarga upādānam kṛtam iti arthaḥ yat api uktam kaiścid heya hāna upāya adhigantavyeṣu eva caturṣu puruṣa arthaḥ parisamāpyate yathā loke heyaḥ kaṇṭakaḥ hānam upānat tad upāyaḥ tu pādukā kṛdātiḥ adhigantavyaḥ duḥkha abhāvaḥ śāstre ca heyaḥ rogaḥ cikitsā hānam tad upāyaḥ nidāna jñānam adhigantavyam ārogyam iti atas caturṣu vaktavyeṣu ṣoḍaśa padārtha varṇanam kkopa yujyate iti tadā api nirastam caturvargasya eva vivakṣā bhedāt ṣoḍaśadhā bhedena abhidhānāt vivakṣā bhedasya ca upapatti pratipadam bhāṣya kāraḥ eva darśayiṣyati etad avagamyā eva yena adhikam coditam tat matam apākaroti etena iti 
NVTP_1.1.1.144	 vyākhyāyate avayavaśas iti viśeṣaṇe kriyāyāḥ tātparyam na tu viśeṣye iti arthaḥ etat eva attaratra sphuṭayati tatra asya avayaveṣu iti kasmāt pramāṇāt iti na abhihitam evam hi asaṃdigdhā eva pañcamī syāt iti arthaḥ asya iti prakṛta pañcamī parāmarśe liṅga asaṃgati riti ataḥ āha asya iti pañcamyāḥ taseḥ prayogam darśayitvā pañcamī vyatirekeṇa taseḥ ākṣepa samādhāne asaṃgate iti ākṣepam vyākhyāya avatārayati vacana vyāpti artham iti nanu pramāṇābhyām pramāṇaiḥ iti bhavatam saṃplavaḥ pramāṇena iti tu katham iti atas āha yatra dvaya uditi viṣaya eka tāmā atra saṃplavaḥ na tu kāraṇānām samuccayaḥ tathā sati phala bhedaḥ na syāt na api samuccitānām karaṇa tvam tathā sati vyāpāra bhedaḥ na syāt iti jñāpana artham iti arthaḥ atas eva iti eva kāraḥ sādhakatama antaram vyavacchindan tasya vyāpāram phalam ca vyavacchinatti na tu asya sva vyāpārulayoḥ ita reta ra naiḥ apekṣyam darśayati tasya saṃplave api saṃbhavāt iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.1.145	 kasmāt punar karaṇa arthaḥ gamyate prakṛti pratyayayoḥ katarasmāt iti arthaḥ ayam āśayaḥ yadi tṛtīyayā karaṇa tvam abhidhīyate kim prakṛti sthena lyuṭpratyayena atha tena eva kim tṛtīyayā iti jñāpakasya kāraka tva śaḍkāḥ mā bhūt iti atas āha artham artha adhigatim iti nanu hetu karaṇa bhāvaḥ avagamyatām iti etad artham vibhakti vyāptiḥ āsthīyate pramāṇam iti prātipadikāt eva sākṣātkaraṇa tvam arthataḥ hetu tvam gamyate iti kim vibhakti vyāptyā iti atas āha atra ca iti na ca vācyam karaṇa bhāvena api pramāṇa phalayoḥ tādātmyam pratiṣedddhum śakyam tat ki tat na āntarīyaka hetutabhdāvāmidhāna artham pañcamya iti sādhāka tva mātrasya eva sāmarthye tam abarthasya asamartha tvāt tatra vipratipatteḥ ca kasmāt iti praśna artham abhipretya āha pramāṇa pratipadikā iti tat evam anuvādaka tvam 
NVTP_1.1.1.146–1.1.1.147	 samarthayatā lyuṭtṛtīyayoḥ pauna rūktyam samāhitam na ca anuvādaka tvam śabda abhyāsasya prayojanavat tā vyatirekeṇa sidhyati iti atas prayojanam darśayati pramākāraka antarebhyaḥ iti laukike tu prayoge saṃkhyā abhidhānāt vibhakteḥ sārthaka tvam draṣṭavyam iti viśiṣṭa viṣaya tvena saṃplava ākṣepaḥ asaṃgataḥ eva agni ādi viśiṣṭe parvata ādau pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ saṃplavāt iti atas āha viśiṣṭaḥ bhinnaḥ iti viṣaya tva sāmānya abhiprāyam eka vacanam artha samārthya samuttham pratyakṣam yatas ator atha gocaram tat kim hetu tvam eva viṣaya lakṣaṇam na iti āha saḥ eva ca arthaḥ iti kim atas cadyevam iti atas āha na ca sāmānyam iti
