NVTP_1.1.4.54	 nanu viśiṣṭa karma abhinirvartita tvena prasanna andha anandha kṛṣṇa sārāṇām na kaścid viśeṣaḥ na hi rūpa upabhogān arthinaḥ kṛṣṇasāre tṛṣṇā tad karma saṃbhavaḥ asaṃbhave ca katham asya utpattiḥ iti atas kārye api karmaṇaḥ sahakāritām āha etat uktam bhavati iti karma kṣayāt iti upalakṣaṇam pratibandhāt sahakāri virahāt ca iti api draṣṭavyam yadi hi ratha ādi saṃyogānām nabhaḥ vyāpaka tvam bhavet tadā tad kāryasi api śabdasya sarvatra utpāda prasaḍgeḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa prādeśika tva anurodhena hi 
NVTP_1.1.4.55–1.1.4.56	 vyāpaka guṇāḥ pradeśa avacchedena jāyante iha tu tad abhāvāt anavacchinna deśa tā eva syāt tatas ca tad dvāreṇa upalamyamānāḥ ratha ādayaḥ tad saṃyogāḥ ca na niyata deśa tayā pratīyerat nitya āśayavān āha mā bhūta sarvatra iti nanu ākāśa pratyakṣa tāpakṣaḥ kim iti na aśaḍkitaḥ iti pariharatna āha na asmākam iti tvac ādibhiḥ iti tatra tvac udāhaṇam uktam rasanā udāharaṇam tu tikta tva abhāva viśiṣṭaḥ madhurataraḥ guḍaḥ tathā ghrāṇa udāharaṇam pūti grandhā bhāva viśiṣṭā surabhitarā kastūrikā iti atas bahuvacana avirodhaḥ bauddha siddhānte ca guṇa guṇinā ūḥ abhedāt guṇi mūrta tvam eva guṇa mūrta tvam guṇa grāhakam eva indriyam guṇi grāhakam guṇa abhāvaḥ eva ca guṇya bhāvaḥ atas mūrta abhāva viśiṣṭa grahe udāharaṇīye 
NVTP_1.1.4.57–1.1.4.58	 alpa abhāva viśiṣṭa grahamāhā iti nanu mā bhūt saha antareṇa grahaṇam sāntaraḥ iti vā grahaṇam hetu arthaḥ śarīra indriya adhiṣṭhāna asambandhasya grahaṇam arthaḥ bhaviṣyati na hi ayam anyathā siddhaḥ etasya eva uttara upādhi tvena prayojaka tvāt iti atas āha indriya sambandhaḥ bhavatu mā vā iti yat śarīra sambddham tat avaśyam indriya sambaddham iti yat indriya sambaddham tat avaśyam śarīra sambaddham iti vā na pramāṇam asti 
NVTP_1.1.4.59	 tayoḥ vibhinna tvāt vibhinna āśraya tvāt ca na hi asti niyamaḥ yat pradīpena sambaṇsate tat avaśyam malli mayā api yat vā malli mayā tat avaśyam pradīpena api tasmāt tatra sādhāka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt sandehaḥ eva iti arthaḥ tasmāt tad anyathā siddhiḥ eva iti asiddhi vyavaccheda artham sa jalasa tejaḥ paṭa ādi grāhiṇā prāpya kāriṇā tvac indriyeṇa viruddham api saha antareṇa grahaṇam draṣṭavyam 
NVTP_1.1.4.60–1.1.4.62	 āvaraṇa anupapatti rūpasya tarkasya upaskurvāṇaḥ prayogeṇa pramāṇam āha prayogaḥ tu iti iha dvividhaḥ sambandhaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ yathā āloka ādīnām ghaṭa ādibhiḥ tad viparītaḥ ca yathā abhidhāna jñāna ādīnām abhidhayajñeya ādi bhaḥ tatra sva viṣayam prāpya iti siddha sādhana vyudāsa artham janaka tvāt iti ukte śabda ādibhiḥ aprāpta sva viṣaya pratipatti ādi janakaiḥ anaikāntikam atas tad aprāpta avajanaka tvāt iti etāvat mātreṇa tu sarvathā ajanakaiḥ anaikāntikam atas janaka tve sati iti yukti antaram tarka antaram dūra antikān anuvidhāna prasaṅgaḥ asya api viparyayeṇa prayogaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.63	 nanu prāpta tva aviśeṣe sūrya maṇḍala vat merū pṛṣṭha madhyandina ulkā prakāśau= api gṛhṇīyāt atha anubhdūta abhibhūta tayā na sūra sadana ādīnām grahaṇam ubhdūta anabhibhūta tvāt sūrya maṇḍalam gṛhyate iti evam tarhi viṣayaḥ eva sa kaścid tādṛśaḥ yaḥ gṛhyate na itaraḥ iti abhyupeyatām kim vyabhicāri prāpti parigrahegoti atas āha prāptau tu iti viṣaya māhātmyam hi prāpti sahakāri na tu svatantram na hi sparśa rasa ādayaḥ grahaṇa yogyāḥ iti aprāptaiḥ eva tvac ādibhiḥ gṛhyante prāpya kāri tvāt vā taiḥ anubhdūta abhibhūtāḥ api te prāpta tva mātreṇa gṛhyante iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.64	 yadi api kṣaṇa bhaṅga pariṇāma naye api prāptānām eva parasparam kartṛ karaṇa karmaṇām kārya jananam na tu aprāptānām api na hi parasparam apratyāsīdantaḥ sahakāri pratyayāḥ bhāvān atiśāyayantaḥ dṛśyante pratyāsattiḥ tu nirantara utpādaḥ eva teṣām sā eva ca svarūpya ugya tā tathā ca svarūpa yogya tām indriya arthayā ubruvatā nirantara utpādaḥ eva vaktavyaḥ na punar vyavahita viprakṛṣṭa utpannānām kvacid api svarūpa yogyatā nāma tasmāt prāptau svarūpa atiriktāyām vipratipadyeta na tu nirantara utpāde api tatra adhika aprāptiḥ sādhanam arhati iti āśa yavān āha niṣetsyete hi iti evam nivārita abhimānaḥ para darśane api pramāṇam apaśyan sandigdhaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.65	 nanu janaka tve sati iti nirṇaya hetum paśyan katham nāma sandigdhaḥ iti atas āha ayam abhisandhiḥ iti adṛśyamāna prāptau= ayaska ante api dṛṣṭa tvāt anaikāntikasya abhimanyate paraḥ iti arthaḥ tvac ādīnām daṇḍa ādīnām ca prāptānām eva kārya janaka tvam paśyan katham iva sarvatra vipratipadyate iti atas vipratipatti bījam āha yogyatayā eva iti nanu ayaskāntasya aprāpya kāri tve hetu antare api kaḥ pratīkāraḥ iti atas āha ayaskānta maṇeḥ iti nanu tasya vṛtti bhedaḥ anupalambha bādhitaḥ iti atas uktam cakṣuṣaḥ iva iti tulya yogakṣema tvāt iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.66–1.1.4.68	 vyavadhāna vipra karṣau hi anirantara utpādaḥ vā syāt aprāptiḥ vā sva rūpa yogya tā vā tatra anirantara utpāda abhāvaḥ nirantara utpādaḥ syāt na ca kṛṣpāsārasya arthena maṇeḥ vā lohena nirantara utpādaḥ saṃbhavati aprāpti abhāvaḥ tu prāptiḥ eva tathā ca kaḥ pratikūlaḥ anukūlam ācarati ayogya tā bhāvaḥ tu yogya tā eva sa ca bauddha naye kāraṇa jātīyasya nirantara utpādāt na bhidyate iti uktam tasmāt sthira naye kāryam janayanti kāraṇāni paraspara prāptim vā vyabhicaranti prāptiḥ vā sva rūpa yogya tā prayuktām vyāptim upajīvati iti avaśiṣyate tatra āha prāpteḥ eva iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.69	 nanu lakṣaṇa antareṇa vyavasthite lakṣye katham anyonya āśraya tvam iti atas āha agatiḥ vā iti tat hi lakṣyasāpekṣam anapekṣam vā ādye anyonya āśraya tva doṣāt eva āgatiḥ uttaratra tu avagate lakṣye tad sāpekṣeṇa lakṣaṇena kim gamayitavyam iti agatiḥ eva iti arthaḥ asti hi iti yadi vijñāna abhinna hetu ja tvāt sukham vijñāna jātīyam syāt sukha abhinna hetu ja tvāt tat api sukha jātīyam bhavet vijñānam na sukhena abhinna hetu jam iti ced evam tarhi katham sukham api vijñānena abhinna hetu jam iti arthaḥ nanu jñāna hetu anugamaḥ sukhe api asti na tu sukha hetu anugamaḥ jñāne atas yat kāraṇa anugamaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.70–1.1.4.71	 yatra tad jātīya tvam tatra astu yathāḍkura mātra kāraṇa anugame yavāḍkurasya api aḍkurajātīya tvam na tu sarvasya yavāḍkura tvam tad kāraṇa anugama abhāva ādityāśayavān āśaṅkate avāntara iti na hi asti niyamaḥ yat jātīya kārya hetu ca krān agamaḥ yatra tatra tat jātīya tvam iti bīja jātīya kārya hetu cakra anugame api aḍkurasya bīja ajātīya tvāt iti sāmānya upasaṃhāre anaikāntika tvam viśeṣa upasaṃhāre tu sandigdha anaikāntika tvam āha na kiñcid iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.72	 ākasmika tva prasaṅga bhayāt hi kārya bheda upapattaye sakala kāraṇa bhedam anusaran prayasyati bhavān sa ca kārya bhedaḥ kiñcid kāraṇa bhedena eva bījāḍkura ādi vat jñāna sukha ādau= api anākasmikaḥ iti arthaḥ tat idam uktam tad artha tvāt ca iti nanu rūpa rasa gandha sparśānām hi upādāna bheda abheda mātra anuviddham tat jātīyātat jātīya tvam na hi asti saṃbhavaḥ rūpa ādi upādānam cārūpa ādikam ca iti atas jñāna upādāna tve sukham jñāna jātīyam eva syāt ajñāna tve vā na jñāna upādāna tvam iti yadi pratyavatiṣṭhate tatra āha na ca iti yadi hi eka jātīya upādāna tayā eka jātīya tvam bhavet avāntara eka jātīyam api kim na syāt tathā ca ekasmāt samanantara pratyayāt aneka avāntara jātīnayā anutpāda prasaṅgaḥ dṛśyate ca rūpa jñānāt rūpa jñānam rasa jñāna ādi jātīyam ca sākṣātkāriṇaḥ sākṣātkāraḥ ca asākṣāt karaḥ ca ityādi 
NVTP_1.1.4.73–1.1.4.75^1	 atha vilakṣaṇa aneka sahakāri praveśāt aneka avāntara jātīya kārya karaṇa svabhāvasya kasyanacid eva utpāda niyamaḥ upapādya evam avāntara jāti bheda upapādana vat vivakṣita eka jātīya upādāna tve api vilakṣaṇa aneka sahakāri praveśāt vivakṣita aneka jātīya kārya karaṇa svabhāvasya kasyacid eva utpāda niyamaḥ upapatsyate iti arthaḥ saḥ ayam ekopādānaka tve api avāntara jāti bheda abhyupagamaḥ pareṣām dṛṣṭānta artham ubhdāvitaḥ api ca ityādi ubhdāvitam sandigdha vyāvṛttika tvam sphuṭhayitum ataḥ na asaṅgatam iti tat etat sakalam bauddha siddhānta abhyupagamena uktam paramārthataḥ tu yat upādāna vat tat sajātīyam yat vyāpaka upādāna vat tad guṇa jātīyam iti niyamaḥ atas parama niyamaḥ tat yadi sat tayā guṇa tvena vā sukha jñānayoḥ eka jātīya tvam sādhyate tadā siddha sādhanam anyatra aniyame asaḍkīrṇam udāharaṇam āha atas eva iti eka upādāna tve api rūpa ādīnām na vyaktikṛtaḥ bhedaḥ na api avāntara jāti kṛtaḥ na api guṇa tayā piṭhara upādāna tve api karmaṇaḥ aguṇa tvāt 
NVTP_1.1.4.75^2	 atra upādāna mātra balena yathā dravya guṇa karmaṇā ām asatām eva sattvam bahis tathā āntaram api jñāna sukha ādīnām yathā ca teṣa abhava antara kāraṇa bhedāt dravya tvam pṛthivī ādīnām guṇtvam rūpa ādīnām karma tvam utkṣepaṇa ādīnām tathā avāntara kāraṇa bhedāt darśana sparśana smaraṇa ādīnām jñāna tvam nirūpa adhyanukūla ānūkūlatara ādīnām sukha tvam ityādi ekam avānta rāsa ādhāraṇa nimitta ādi bhedāt yathā pṛthivyāḥ ghaṭa ādi bhedaḥ rūpasya śukla ādi bhedaḥ utkṣepaṇasya ca pāṭava ādi bhedaḥ tathā jñānasya api darśana ādi bhedaḥ sukhasya api tāratamya ādi bhedaḥ bhaviṣyati iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.76	 syāt etat ajñāna rūpa tāyām punar kim pramāṇam iti atas upasaṃhāra vyājena āha tasmāt iti yadi api vijñāna sukha ādīnām bhinna jātīya tvam anubhava siddham na hi candanam aham jānāmi iti atra sukham parisphurati tadā aham sukhī iti syāt na api sukhī aham iti atra jñānam parisphurati tadā jānāmi iti syāt na ca etat asti jñāna viśeṣaḥ sukham tathāvidhe ca sukha buddhiḥ bhavati eva iti ced hanta bhoḥ tasya jñāna viśeṣasya viṣaya viśeṣaḥ api asti na vā na asti ced nirviṣaya jñānam sukham iti prāptam na ca etat dṛṣṭam iṣṭam śakayam vā sādhayitum asti ced bāhyaḥ ābhyantaraḥ vā na tāvat bāhyaḥ kaścid viṣaya bhedaḥ asti yat eva hi rāgavatā gītam anubhūyate tat eva vīta rāgeṇa api tat eva gītam param rāgavatā anukūla tayā vīta rāgeṇa tu tad viparīta tayā iti ced kim anukūla tvam asya nirūpa adhikam sa upādhikam vā katham kañcid prati sa upādhika tve saḥ eva ucyatām icchā eva upādhiḥ iti ced na itaretara āśraya tva prasaḍgāt iṣyamāṇa tvāt anukūla tvam tena ca iṣyamāṇa tvam iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.77	 tasmāt tasya jñāna viśeṣasya sukha tvena abhimatasya abhyantaraḥ eva viṣaya viśeṣaḥ nisarga anukūla svabhāvaḥ eṣṭavyaḥ yat hetu tayā bāhyaḥ viṣayaḥ anukūla tayā abhimata tvena iṣyamāṇaḥ bhavati saḥ eva ukta rūpaḥ viṣayaḥ sukham iti ucyate tathā api mūḍhadhiyām vyavahāra artham samāna asamāna jātīya vyavacchedakāḥ dharmāḥ jñāna ādīnām uktāḥ tatra artha pravaṇa tvam jñānasya artha nirūpaṇa adhīna nirūpaṇa tvam iti arthaḥ tad apravaṇa tvam ajñāna lakṣaṇam tatra api anukūla vedanīya tvam sukha lakṣaṇam pratikūla vedanīya tvam duḥkhasya iti evamādi samāna tantra anusādeṇa boddhavyam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.78–1.1.4.79	 nanu ajñāna ātmaka tve ghaṭa ādi vat avaśya saṃvedyāḥ sukha ādayaḥ na bhaveyuḥ avaśya saṃvedyāḥ ca te na hi asaṃvidite sukhe pramāṇam anyat asti tat etat jñāna ātma tve param upapadyate sva saṃvedana tvāt iti atas āha tīvra saṃvegitayā iti santi hi padārthāḥ sva karma upārjita tva aviśeṣe api kecid adhyakṣāḥ eva yathā sva śarīra ādayaḥ kecid tu parokṣāḥ eva yathā tad antargata nāḍī saṃsthāna ādayaḥ evam ajñāna tva aviśeṣe api kāraṇa labdha svabhāva bhedāḥ kecid avaśya saṃvedyāḥ sukha ādayaḥ kecid anyathā iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.80	 sagotram utthāpayati syāt etat iti tathā api jāgara avasthāyām tāvat anubhava janana dvārā sukha utpattau= indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ upayujyate anyathā sukha vat anubhavaḥ api tena vinā eva syāt na ca sākṣātkāraṇam eva kāraṇam tathā sati vyāpāriṇaḥ udāsīnāḥ prasajyeran vyāpāra avi avadhāyaka tva vādaḥ tu atra api tulyaḥ iti atas āha indriya artha sannikarṣasya tu iti jñāna mātram avyāpārībhūtam tatra upayogāt iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.81	 ayam āśayaḥ bhavet evam yadi indriya artha sannikarṣasya jñānam vyāpāraḥ syāt sa hi kārya āsavānaḥ vyāpārya vyabhicārī bhavati jñānam punar kārya avasānam api indriya artha sannikarṣam atipatati eva svapna antike anyathā tu vyāpāra kalpanā āyām aniyama prasaṅgaḥ iti pariharati tat ayuktam iti asiddheḥ apratīteḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt iti śeṣaḥ nanu mānasaḥ atra anubhavaḥ pramāṇam iti atas āha tad jñānasya iti kutas mithyātvā avagatiḥ iti atas āha yathā hi iti ālambnam tu asya viparyāsasya yathā pūrva anubhūtā smaraṇa arhā kāminī iti evam tad jānma pūrva anubhūtam smaraṇa arham sukham eva viparyāsa tvam punar etāvatā eva asya yat viprakṛṣṭa deśa kālayoḥ kāminī tad janya sukhayoḥ sannikṛṣṭa deśa kāla tayā avabhāsaḥ na punar akāminya sukhayoḥ kāminī sukha tvena pratibhānam tathā sati kāminī tva sukha tva niṣedhena anyasya kasyacid pratibhāsanam bādhakam bhavet na ca vācyam yadi na svapna antike sukham utpadyate na 
NVTP_1.1.4.82–1.1.4.83	 nasmai ghirahī spṛhayet iti mohāt asādhane api pravṛtti darśanāt śīta apanuttaye guñjā puñjaḥ iva markaṭānām tat idam uktam smaraṇa viparyāsaḥ iti smaraṇe prāpte viparyāsaḥ smaraṇa viparyāsaḥ anubhava lakṣaṇaḥ tad viṣayaḥ eva iti arthaḥ nanu sukha duḥkha utpāda prayojanau dharma adharmau yat asukha duḥkha arūpān deha ādīn utpādayataḥ tad tad artha tayā eva evam tayoḥ sarva utpattimatām nimitta tvam nirvahati idam tu svapna jñānam na sukha rūpam saṃkha sādhanam api yadi na syāt na tarhi dharma nimittakam na api adharma nimitta kamaduḥkha tvāt atad hetuka tvāt ca tatas ca adṛṣṭa nirapekṣa utpattiḥ asya ca bahu ākulayet iti atas āha sukha iti sukha ādi upabhogaḥ hi adṛṣṭasya pradhānam prayojanam na ca sukha ādi svarūpataḥ upabhogaḥ kim tu tad anubhavaḥ sa ca pratyutpanna sukha ādi anālambana tve api pūrva utpannam ālambya jāyamānaḥ sarvam samañjasayati na ca sarvatra evam astu sāmagrī vaicitryāt satya mithyā pratyaya vibhāga vyavasthāpanāt 
NVTP_1.1.4.84^1	 na hi ekadā upalabdha rajata viṣaya saṃskāra vaśāt a rajate api rajata pratyayaḥ iti sarvadā evam eva astu iti vaktum ucitam yaḥ tu manyate svapne tāvat sukha ādikam anubhūyate iti avivādam tatra tu bādhakam bhavat dvi rūpam bhavet asukham etat iti vā na āsīt sukham iti vā na ca etat asti jāgara avasthāyām tu na āsīt kāminī iti yujyate bādhakam sthira tvāt sahasā apasaraṇasya api asaṃbhavāt tad kāryāṇām ca daśana nakha kṣata ādīnām ananuvṛtteḥ carama dhātu visarga ādīnām ca anuvṛttau= api atad kārya tvāt tad kārya tvena tad anuvṛttau= anyeṣām api tad kāryāṇām anuvṛtti prasaḍgāt 
NVTP_1.1.4.84^2	 na asti idānīm sukham iti tu idāni intara sukhasya bādhaḥ na prāktanasya kṣaṇika tvāt tasya tad kāryāṇām ca harṣa aśru pulaka ādīnām anuvartamānānām upalambhāt anyathā āśutara vināśinām kṣaṇa antare adarśanāt tad anubhavānām aprāmāṇika tvam eva syāt tasmāta bādhita anubhava siddha tvāt asti svapna antike sukham iti tam pratyāha na ca asati iti yadi api svapna antika sukhasya jāgara avasthāyām āhatya bādhakam na asti tathā api svapna antikaḥ eva tad kāraṇa tvena pratītānām candana vanitā ādīnām asti bādhakam kāraṇe ca bādhite kāryam bādhitam eva yathā svapna antika dṛṣṭa payoda paṭala bādhe 
NVTP_1.1.4.85–1.1.4.86	 tad āśrayaḥ vidyut udyotaḥ harṣa aśru prabhṛtayaḥ tu na sukha kāryāḥ kim tu sukha jñāna kāryāḥ iti na tāvat mātreṇa tad saṃbhava upapattiḥ tasmāt svapna antika udāha raṇa balena jñāna mātra kāryataḥ sukhasya sidhyati iti manoratha ādi udāhṛtya parihṛtam caturdhā khalu saṃsāriṇām sukham utpadyate kiñcid abhyāsāt yathā mṛgayā ādiṣu kiñcid abhimānāt yathā candana ādiṣu kiñcita viṣaya saṃbhogāt yathā surabhi madhura gaura gān dhāra ādiṣu kiñcid manoratha ādi saṃpratyaya mātrāt yathā bhaviṣyat putra ādi janma dina mahā utsava anucintana ādiṣu te ca amī svarūpa bhedavantaḥ anubhūyante na hi yathā manoratheṣu sukham tathā viṣaya saṃbhoge tathā sati tad parityāgena anya upādāna vaiyarthyāt tāvat eva hi bubhukṣitaḥ modakāt manorathayati 
NVTP_1.1.4.87–1.1.4.88	 yāvat amī na asya paramārthataḥ sannidhīyante atha manoratha vyasanam apahāya tatra eva niyamataḥ pravartate tat eka jātīya tve sarvam asamañjasam syāt jāti bhede tu kāraṇa bhedaḥ avaśya abhyupetavyaḥ iti arthaḥ tat atra indriya artha sannikarṣasya sattvam anuvidha tve sukha utpattiḥ iti siddhāntinaḥ vivakṣitam tat ca anyathā siddham iti manvānaḥ punar pūrva uktam smārayati jñāna mātram eva iti na atra tad sattva anuvidhāna mātram vivakṣitam kim nāma jāti bhedaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.89–1.1.4.90	 kāraṇa bhedam ākṣipati sa ca kāraṇa bhedaḥ anuvihita bhāva abhāvaḥ eva sidhyati iti atra vivakṣitam iti pratipipādayiṣuḥ uktam eva anubhāṣate na viṣaya āsannidhānaḥ iti tat idam uktam tādṛśasya sukha bhedasya anutpādāt iti yādṛśaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpadyate iti śeṣaḥ śaṅkate viṣaya iti jñāna abhede hi bhinna jātīyam sukham kāraṇa antaram bhinnam ākṣipet iha tu jñānam eva bhinna jātīyam iti arthaḥ pariharati hanteśvarasya api iti nanu viṣaya sākṣātkāraḥ api iṣṭa upalabdhi lakṣaṇaḥ sukha hetuḥ sa ca tādṛśaḥ na asti īśvare tasya bubhukṣā virahāt katham tasya sukha utpāda prasaṅgaḥ iti atas āha yoga ṛddhi sampannānām iti nanu te api alaṃpratyayavantaḥ katham iva sukha bhājaḥ bhaveyuḥ iti atas āha asatyām iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.91–1.1.4.92	 na hi te sarvadā eva pratipakṣa dhāraṇāvantaḥ mā bhūt amīṣām sarvadā bhoga virahāt dharma adharma pracaya tādavasthyam tasmāt yadā pratipakṣa dhāraṇā na asti tadā viṣaya sākṣātkāra mātrāt eva teṣām sukham prasajyeta iti arthaḥ na ca vācyam yadi bhavet evam kīdṛśaḥ doṣaḥ iti kāya vyūhe śarīra indriya nirmāṇa vaiyarthya prasaḍgāt iṣṭa aniṣṭa sākṣātkārasya ekasmin= eva śarīre manasā eva siddha tvāt na ca indriyāṇām arthānām ca parasparam asannikṛṣṭānām eva sattā mātraiṇa kvacid ātma dharma samutpāde sāmarthyam adhigatam tasmāt yoga ṛddhimatām sati api viṣaya sākṣātkāre indriya artha sannikarṣa abhāvāt sukham na asti iti abhipretya upasaṃharati tasmāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.93–1.1.4.94	 tat ayam pramāṇa arthaḥ yoga ṛddhīni indriyāṇi sukha duḥkha samutpāda prayojanāni sukha duḥkha tabdaḥ dhānya tve sati anyatra ācārita artha tvāt iṣṭa aniṣṭa upalabdhi vat na ca ayam asiddhaḥ anyatra hi caritārtha tvam sākṣātkāre saṃbhāvyeta sa tu yoga ja dharma saha kṛtena manasā eva janitaḥ te ca sukha duḥkhe sannikṛṣṭaiḥ eva indriyaiḥ janyete bāhya indriya janya tve satya ātma gharma tvāt asmāt ādi viṣaya sākṣātkāra vat iti saḥ ayam sannikarṣaḥ yadā na asti tadā teṣām api na sukha ādikam iti tat idam uktam sa ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.95	 nanu indriya artha sannikarṣa janmā viṣaya sākṣātkāraḥ sukha ādi hetuḥ na ca tathā siddhānām asti atas na teṣām sukha utpāda prasaṅgaḥ iti atas āha api ca iti na tāvat indriya janyā janyayoḥ sākṣātkārayoḥ kaścid ājānataḥ viśeṣaḥ kim tu indriya artha sannikarṣa rūpa kāraṇa sambandhaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ sa ca yadi kārye vivakṣitaḥ katham na tasya kāraṇa tā sukha ādikam prati avivakṣitaḥ ced siddhānām api tad utpāda prasaḍgaḥ durvāraḥ tulya yogakṣema tvāt tasmāt carama bhāvinī ā iva sākṣātkāre sati kim indriyeṇa iti ahṛdayasya abhiprāyaḥ avaśiṣyate tatra ca atiprasaṅgaḥ iti arthaḥ atra eva arthe vṛddha saṃmatim āha sraj ādi iti atra sraj ādi iti kāraṇa cakra kathanam yat utpadyate iti anukūla pravedanīyam sva rūpam anugraha ādi iti kāryam anugrahaḥ bhoga apara nāmā sukha pratyayaḥ abhiṣvaṅgaḥ punar punar sukha pravāhasya aviccheda icchā prasādaḥ sukha viṣaya grahaṇa pāṭavam iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.96	 nanu avyapadeśya vyavasāya ātmaka padayoḥ saṃgrāhyam vyavacchedyam vā na paśyāmḥ pratyuta paraspara viruddhayoḥ anayoḥ ekasmin pratyakṣe asamāveśaḥ eva iti atas āha iha dvayī iti saṃgṛhītā api sva śabdena upāttā kim iti ced iti śaḍkāśeṣaḥ uttaram tatra vipratipatteḥ yatas tatra vipratipattiḥ tatas tām niṣeddhum iti arthaḥ vyapadiśyate vyavacchidyate anena iti vyapadeśaḥ sā ca vyavacchittiḥ vyāvṛtti pratīti rūbhābhyām kriyate iti tat ubhayam āha viśeṣaṇam iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.97	 tatra samāna adhikaraṇam vyavacchedakam viśeṣaṇam vyadhikaraṇam tu upalakṣaṇam yathā daṇḍī devadattaḥ jaṭābhiḥ tātasaḥ iti na tu sedava viśeṣaṇam ati vyāpaka tayā alakṣaṇa tvāt lakṣaṇa viśeṣaṇam etat iti ced atha lakṣaṇam kim sva uparakta pratīti janaka tvam iti ced etat eva kim uktam syāt avacchedaka tvam anyat vā na tāvat ādyaḥ upalakṣaṇasya api avacchedaka tvāt atas eva sat iti viśeṣaṇam iti ced na sataḥ api kasyacid upalakṣaṇa tvena iṣṭa tvāt anyuttu samāna adhikaraṇa vyavacchedaka tvāt na anyat tasmāt sat vā asat vā samāna adhikaraṇam vyavacchedakam viśeṣaṇam viparītam upalakṣaṇam iti atas eva viśeṣaṇa mātram udāharat na upalakṣaṇam tat kasya hotoḥ tat eva vyādhi karaṇa tayā upalakṣaṇa 
NVTP_1.1.4.98	 yatas vyapadeśyam viśeṣyam iti yāvat iti vyavacchedyam iti yāvat iti arthaḥ evam uttaratra api nāmadheya anvitāḥ nāmadheya ātmānaḥ iti arthaḥ etat eva vyatirekataḥ darśayati na asti iti nāmadheyena saha viyujyate vibhidyate iti arthaḥ taiḥ iti atra kāraṇa tā bhramaḥ mā bhūt iti etad artham upetadena āpūrya vyācaṣṭe arthā hi iti tat ayam samudāya arthaḥ nāmadheya ātmānor athāḥ tad sāmāna adhikaraṇyena pratīyamāna tvāt yat punar yad ātmakam na bhavati na tat tad sāmāna adhikaraṇyena 
NVTP_1.1.4.99–1.1.4.101	 pratīyate yathā goḥ aśvasā mānādhikaraṇyena pratīyante ca arthāḥ śabda sāmānādhikaraṇyena tasmāt tad ātmānaḥ iti nanu gavāśu ādīnām sāmānādhikaraṇya vyāvṛtti kim abheda vyāvṛtterūta tad pratītyaḥ rūpāya upeya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ iti saṃdihyate iti atas āha na ca iti api ca yadi śabda arthayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇye upāya upeya bhāvaḥ upādhiḥ syāt upāya tva nivṛttau= eva tat api nivarteta na ca nivartate iti atas āha api ca iti hetu antaram āha kim ca iti utkarṣaḥ prāśastyam upakarṣaḥ aprāśastyam na ca idam vyavahāra mātram śabda nibandhanaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.102	 hi utkarṣa apakarṣa vyavahāraḥ tathābhūta vastu pratyayāt eva bhaviṣyati yathā ṣaḍja ādi utkarṣa apakarṣa vyavahāra nibandhanaḥ mayūra ādi utkarṣa apakarṣa vyavahāraḥ iti dṛṣṭānta artham ṣaḍja ādiṣu iti uktam anyathā nāmadheya tādātmya prasādhana prastāve kim anena atas eva siddhānte saṃjñā niveśanam iti āha prayogaḥ tu nāmadheya ātmā anor athā tad utkarṣa apakarṣa anuvidhāyi tvāt yat punar yad ātmakam na bhavati na tat tad utkarṣa ādi anuvidhāyi yathā gauḥ aśvasya iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.103	 nanu yadi artha pratyayaḥ nāmadheya utkārṣādya vidhatte tat tasya eva tādātmyam astu kim āyātam arthasya iti atas āha pratyayasya iti sākṣāt anabhidhāne api guṇa guṇyādeḥ api yogyatayā sa pakṣa tvena tad gata sāmānā adhikaraṇyena virodhaḥ ubhdāvayitum na śakyate iti tad upekṣya anyathā śaṅkate asti iti asti hi śukla bhāsvara tva ādibhiḥ yuktikā gataiḥ rajata tvasya sāmānādhikaraṇya pratyayaḥ na tu tādātmyam parasparam dharmiṇoḥ iti arthaḥ punarukta bhramaḥ mā bhūt iti etad artham āha uktam api vyapadeśam iti vyākhyānasya ca etat prayojanam yat hetu antara sūcanam tathā ca prayogaḥ rūpa ādi artha viṣayam jñānam rūpa ādi śabda viṣayam niyamataḥ tena vyapadiśyamāna tvāt yat tu yat viṣayam na bhavati na tat niyamataḥ tena vyapadiśyate yathā rūpa vijñānam rasena iti anuviddha tā saṃśleṣa lakṣaṇa arthena eva vijñānasya na asti kutastarām tad ātmanā api śabdena bhaviṣyati iti atas uktam iva iti yathā hi arthaḥ jñāna antar niviṣṭaḥ iva viṣaya tayā 
NVTP_1.1.4.104	 parisphurati tathā śabdaḥ api iti arthaḥ śabda anuvyādha vat eva śabda saṃbhinna viṣayam eva iti arthaḥ na ca idam aprāmāṇikam yat avocat pramāṇam ityādi śeṣau śabdasya anubhavaḥ saṃskāraḥ smaraṇam samuccāraṇa icchā prayatnaḥ sthāna abhighātaḥ śabda abhivyaktiḥ iti sva ātmāni eva krama avagamaḥ tat atas bāle api prathamatas śabdam uccārayati eṣaḥ eva kramaḥ unnīyate iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.105	 prathame pakṣe asiddhaḥ hetuḥ aprasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ ca pakṣaḥ śabdabrahmaṇaḥ eva vāji viṣāṇāyamāna tvāt dṛśya tvāt ṛśya tva lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma adhyāsasya bheda āpādaka tvāt viparīta pramāṇa upapattiḥ ca iti api draṣṭavyam dvitīye tu bhāga asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti arthaḥ na hi aviśade api bāla mūka ādi śabde pramāṇam asti na hi bhāvanā vā tad janitā smṛtiḥ vā pūrva anubhūtasya sattāyām idānīm anubhūyamāna saṃbhede vā pramāṇam asti tathā sati vinaṣṭaḥ ghaṭaḥ smaryamāṇa tvāt san= ā iva syāt anubhūyamānam na bhū talam ghaṭa saṃbhinnam bhavet evam ca ucchinnam aghaṭam bhū talam iti tasmāt abhyupetya viruddha dharma adhyāsa vādaḥ mantavyaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.106	 nanu bālena anubhūyamānam rūpam tāvat viśadam eva tatas ca tad ātmā rūpa śabdaḥ api katham aviśadaḥ syāt katham ca aprāmāṇikaḥ rūpasya prāmāṇika tvāt kevalam avyutpannaḥ api śabdena vyavaharet iti prasajyeta tad asaṃbaddham na hi śabda ātma tā pratyayam vyavahāra aṅgam ācakṣmahe kim tu sambandha grahaṇam iti atas āha na ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.107–1.1.4.108	 ayam api abhyupagamavādaḥ eva śabdaḥ hi vaktṛ vaktra avaruddha nabhaḥ bhāga avacchinna tayā śrotreṇa pratīyate apratīyamāne api arthe arthaḥ api puras varti tayā cakṣuṣā pratīyate anavagate api śabde tat ayam bālaḥ yat rūpam paśyati saḥ eva rūpa śabdaḥ iti loṣṭa laḍḍuka dṛṣṭāntam anuharati iti saḥ ayam bheda pratyayaḥ bhrānataḥ iti yadi śaṅkate tatra āha na ca iti ayam api abhyupagamavādaḥ eva na hi asti bhrānta tve asya pramāṇam syāt etat bāla mūka ādi jñānānām śabda saṃbhedaḥ tāvat sāndehikaḥ eva astu vyutpannānām punar sa vikalpāḥ dhiyaḥ śabda sāmānādhikaraṇyena jāyamānāḥ śabda ātmaka tvam arthasya vyavasthāpayantu tathā sati bāla mūka ādi vijñānānām 
NVTP_1.1.4.109	 tad viṣaya tvāt śabda saṃbhinna viṣaya tvam arthataḥ siddham bhavati iti atas āha sāmānādhikaraṇya nirāsāya iti sāsnādi mat rūpasya iti na tu gakāra ādi rūpasya iti tātparyam ayam śabdaḥ gakāra ādi ākāraḥ na tu sāsna ādi ākāraḥ iti tātparyam nanu yaḥ ḍitthaḥ iti ḍittha śabdam eva uccārayasi na tu ayam ḍittha śabdaḥ iti tam eva niṣedhasi ca iti kim idam iti atas āha autsargikam hi iti artha para tā hi asya sva paratā niṣedhena eva avirodhataḥ siddhi ati iti arthaḥ tat kim sarvatra evam eva na iti atas āha kvacid punar iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.110	 yatra tarhi asaṃbhadena saṃketa grahe nitya ādi padāni santi tatra asaṃketita tvāt na tāvat artha paraḥ sva paraḥ api yadi na syāt vyarthaḥ prayogaḥ syāt iti atas āha yatra api iti yathā hi gauḥ vāhīkaḥ iti atra go tvam go guṇa yoga lakṣaka tvena vāhika upādhiḥ na tad samavāyāt tādātmyāt vā tathā hi ḍitthaḥ ayam iti atra api ḍittha śabdaḥ vācya tva upalakṣaka tayā piṇḍa upādhiḥ na tu tad samavāyāt tādātmyāt vā iti yathā ca atra vāhīke gauḥ iti pratyaya abhāvaḥ pramāṇam tathā atra api vṛkṣa viśaiṣe ḍitthaḥ ayam iti pratyaya abhāvaḥ pramāṇam iti samudāya arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.111	 nanu śabda puraḥsara tva niyamāt vikalpasya tad upāya tā vā tad viṣaya tvam vā syāt tad puraḥsara tva niyamasya ātad upāyāt atad viṣaya tvāt niyamataḥ vyāvṛtteḥ tatra yadi artha vikalpaḥ tad śabda vipayaḥ tadā siddham naḥ samīhitam atha upāyaḥ tadā jñātaḥ ajñātaḥ vā ajñāta tve nirvikalpaka tva anupapattiḥ eva tasmāt śabdaḥ upāyaḥ bhavan jñātaḥ eva vaktavyaḥ na ca asat nihite jñānam asti tasmāt artha tādātmyāt śabdasya artha sannidhānam eva tad sannidhiḥ iti artha ālocanam eva tadālocanam iti anicchatā api svīkartavyam iti atas āha yat tu iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.112	 na tāvat śabdaḥ pūrvam niyamataḥ bhavati vikalpasya kim nāma vyutpannasya śabda smaraṇa puraḥsara tvam niyama vat dṛṣṭam na ca etāvatā eva ghaṭa jñānasya ghaṭa śabda viṣaya tvam tathā sati ghaṭa abhāva jñānasya api ghaṭa viṣaya tā syāt tad smaraṇa puraḥsara tvāt tasmāt ghaṭe vikalpayitatavye anupāyaḥ viṣayaḥ ca ghaṭa śabdaḥ kim iti niyamataḥ smaryate iti avaśiṣyate tatra iyam smaraṇa paripāṭī kathitā iti śabda puraḥsarā śabda smaraṇa puraḥsarāḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.113	 atra eva vṛddha saṃmatim āha yat āhuḥ iti pratisambandhi piṇḍa darśana sahakṛtaḥ tad saṃskāraḥ smṛtim janayati dhūma anubhava saha kṛtaḥ iva mahānasa stha dahana anubhava prabhavaḥ saṃskāraḥ tad smṛtim na ca etāvatā niyama iva śabda smaraṇa piṇḍa vikalpayaḥ rūpāya upeya bhāvaḥ śabdasya vā vikalpa viṣaya tvam sidhyati yena tayoḥ tādātmyam āśaḍkyeta tathā sati vahni smaraṇa dhūma vikalpayoḥ api tathā abhāvaḥ syāt vahneḥ api vā dhūma vikalpa viṣaya tā bhavet iti vārttika arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.114–1.1.4.115	 syāt etat sarve eva vyavahāraḥ sva arthaḥ para arthaḥ vā vikalpa sādhyaḥ na tu ālocanena api kaścid arthaḥ sādhayitavyaḥ asti atas niṣprayojanam idam katham utpadyate iti atas āha tasmāt iti na tāvat sarvasya eva utpattimataḥ prayojanam piśita cakṣuṣaḥ sākṣātkurmaḥ na ca prayojana apratipatti mātreṇa paṭutara pratyakṣa parikalitam api kāryam na anumanyāmahe tat etat prayojana apratipatti lakṣaṇam alīkam uttaram tathā api sphuṭam sa vikalpaka utpattiḥ eva asya prayojanam iti sa ādarśitā iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.116–1.1.4.117	 nāmadheya smaraṇāya iti nāma avacchinne vikalpe kartavye yatas na viśiṣyate viśeṣeṇa na gṛhyate atas vaidharmyasya yogya pramāṇa bādhita tvāt tad artha jñānam tādṛś eva bhavati tad samāna jātīyam eva bhavati iti arthaḥ atas bhāṣya pauna rūktyam pariharataḥ na sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ hetuḥ iti vyapadeśa vyākhyayā bhāṣya kāreṇa sūcitam hetum sphuṭayati nanu iti artha vyapadeśa ākāram artha vyapadeśa viṣayam viṣayi rūpa jñānasya tāvat rūpa viṣayatā ubhaya vādi siddhāḥ tasya ca tad vyapadeśa viṣaya tā tadā syāt yadi rūpa tad vyapadeśayoḥ abhedaḥ syāt iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.118–1.1.4.119	 anyena anyasya vyapadeśe atiprasaḍgaḥ vyavahāra vilopaḥ ca vipralambhāt iti atra tad nāmadheya tvāt eva niyamaḥ iti sphuṭam bhāṣyaḥ eva sva rūpeṇa eva viṣayeṇa eva vā kim iti jñānam na vyapadiśyate iti etat vivṛṇvan pariharati artha ākāram eva iti ātmānam prati tāvat sva rūpeṇa eva jñānam ajñānāt vyavacchidyate jñāna antarāt tu viṣayeṇa api iti etat kaḥ nāma na abhyupaiti parasya tu nitya parokṣam para jñānam atas eva tad viṣayaḥ api tat katham sva rūpa viṣayābhyām paraḥ bodhyatām katham vai abodhitaḥ vyavaharatām tasmāt tat jñāna vācakena jñānam artha vācakena ca āryam asau pratipādyaḥ na ca ajñātena 
NVTP_1.1.4.120–1.1.4.121	 vācakena vācyam adhigattum arhati iti avarjanīya tayā pratipādakaḥ vācakam uccārayati na ca etāvatā artha śabdayoḥ abheda siddhiḥ na hi pramāṇa vyatirekeṇa prameyam adhigantum na śakyate iti etāvatā eva tayoḥ abhedaḥ syāt iti tat idam uktam anyathā aśakya tvāt iti nanu kadācid artha jñāna kāle api śabdaḥ vyāpriyate eva yadā prayojaka vṛddhāt prayojya vṛddhoḥ atham adhigacchati ityaḥ āha pratīyamāna tayā viṣayatayā iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.122–1.1.4.123	 syāt etat utkarṣa apakarṣa ādi anuvidhāyi tvam hetuḥ kīdṛś iti ate āha tat anena iti na tāvat tāratama tva āderu utkarṣāt mayūra ādeḥ iva gavā ādeḥ api utkarṣaḥ pratīyate na hi go śabde karṇa japite apabhraṣṭe vai aṇīyān gauḥ kṛśaḥ upahata ākṛtiḥ vikṛtaḥ vā pratīyate viparīte vā viparītaḥ na api sādhu tva ādi bhedavataḥ go śabdasya prāśastyam aprāśastyam ca kiñcid asti nanda abhadrā iti ādi maṅgala saṃjñā niveśasya tu artha maṅgalya ādi vyabhicāraḥ sphuṭataraḥ eva abhadra ādau= api bhadra ādi vyapadeśāt tasmāt vyavahāra utkarṣa apakarṣa mātreṇa nobhada siddhiḥ ati prasaḍgāt iti arthaḥ asya eva sākṣāt avyapadeśya padāt pratīyamānasya eva śabda anuvyādha rahita tā śabda artha anuvyādha rahita tā upapattiḥ iti atas asya nirākaraṇam sūcitam iti pūrva uktena na virodhaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.124	 nanu vārttika tātparyavyākhyānam upakramya bhāṣya vyākhyā akāṇḍa kūṣmāṇḍa patana vṛttāntam anuharati iti atas āha tat etat dāṣyam iti tat etat vārttikam vyākhyātum ayam asmākam bhāṣya vyākhyā pariśramaḥ iti arthaḥ śabdaḥ hi yat kāryaḥ yat kāraṇam yat grāhyaḥ yat pramāṇam yat virodhi yat dharmā yad rūpaḥ yat viṣayaḥ tat akāryaḥ tad akāraṇam tat agrāhyaḥ tad apramāṇam tad avirodhi atad dharma ātad rūpaḥ atat viṣayor athaḥ pratyakṣatas eva avasīyate tat etat asya artha jñānasya viṣaya bheda anuvidhāyi tvam śabdābhdedagrāhaka tvam yadi punar eṣā pratītiḥ bhedam ullikhanti api avadhīryate tadā ukta dharmāṇām avirodhe dharmi parivartena api upalambhāḥ syuḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.125	 tatra udāharaṇa artham kāṃścid āha cākṣuṣam hi iti cākṣuṣam hi cakṣuṣā eva janyate rūpaḥ eva niyatam rūpeṇa iva nirūpyate na śabde pravartate na śabdena eva nirūpyate iti arthaḥ evam uttaratra api viṣayi viṣaya aniyama prasaḍgām uktvā karma karaṇa aniyama prasaṅgam āha api ca iti nanu śrotram eva asya kadācid na asti iti atas āha asti hi iti kim atra pramāṇam atas āha śabda jñānam ca iti nanu locana abhāve api agrahaṇam upapadyate iti atas āha asti hi iti kim atra pramāṇam atas āha rūpa jñānam ca iti upalakṣaṇam ca etat artha sāmānyasya sarva indriya grāhya tvāt śabda sāmānyam api sarva indriyaiḥ gṛhyeta śabda sāmānyasya vā śrotra indriya eka vedya tvāt artha sāmānyam api śrotra indriya eka vedyam bhavet tathā ca indriya antarāṇām vaiyarthyam iti api draṣṭavyam iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.126	 itaretara abhāvavat tā vyavahāra abhāva prasaṅgam āha aśabdaḥ iti upalakṣaṇam ca etat anutpannaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ atyanta āsat niti atra api abhāva traye vivakṣita viparītam āpadyate iti mantavyam itaretarābhāva vyapadeśe virodha prasaṅgam āha abhāvaḥ iti atra api anutpādaḥ vināśaḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ iti viruddham syāt iti mantavyam iha hi artha śabdena indriya grāhyaḥ eva abhipretor ayamāṇa tayā iti vyākhyānāt indriyasya ca grāhyaḥ saḥ eva yaḥ tad janya jñāna viṣayaḥ tat amī cakṣuḥ ādi sannikṛṣṭāḥ api anya viṣaya jñāna apekṣāyāḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.127–1.1.4.128	 atad arthāḥ eva evam ca indriya gati jñāne kaḥ pratyakṣatāyāḥ prasaṅgaḥ na hi tad apekṣayā dhaṭa ādayaḥ tad arthāḥ tasmāt aprasakte api artha śabdasya padārtha mātra paratvam abhyupagamya parihāre gati antaram vārttika kṛtā darśitam tat ca duḥkha bodham iti vyācaṣṭe na etat iti na etat indriya artha sannikarṣāt upajāyate sattā mātra vyavasthitāt indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ hi ajñāyamānaḥ eva sattā mātra vyavasthitaḥ pratyakṣe vivakṣitaḥ anumāne tu liṅgasya jñāyamāna tvam eva vivakṣitam na tu sattā iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.129	 nanu anumāne api liḍgāsattā eva ki na vivakṣitā iti atas āha atas eva iti tad smaraṇa mātrāt eva iti mātra grahaṇam sattām ami pretya na tu anumeya jñānam prati kāraṇa tām ami pretya dhūmasya eva jñāyamānasya tad kāraṇa tvāt anyathā tad kālān anuvidhāna prasaḍgāt catra hi viṣaya anapekṣam jñānam eva kāraṇam tatra na viṣaya kāla anuvidhānam yathā abhāva jñāne pratiyogi jñāna janye pratiyoginaḥ api ca liḍga anapekṣasya liṅga jñānasya liḍgi jñāna janaka tve pramāṇa ādīnām gati dvaya vādaḥ api tatra tatra na syāt 
NVTP_1.1.4.130–1.1.4.132	 tat ayam arthaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣāt sattā mātra vyavasthitāt utpadyate jñānam tad sādhakatamam pratyakṣam liḍgāt tu pañca rūpa sampannāt api jñāyamānāt eva asataḥ api yat utpadyate jñānam tat anumānam iti nanu indriya viṣayeṣu iti adhyāhāraḥ tarhi sūtre pūrveṣām kim mūlam iti atas āha imam ca iti na hi anumeyasya indriyeṇa sannikarṣāt iti vadatā hi evam uktam yasya indriyeṇa sannikarṣāt tat jñānam utpadyate na asau tasya viṣayaḥ yaḥ tu viṣayaḥ na tasya indriyeṇa sannikarṣāt idam jāyate tasmāt indriya artha sannikarṣāt upajātam vijñānam yadi tad artha viṣayam eva bhavati tadā tad pratyakṣam na ca etat sūtrāt labhyate tasmāt vārttika kṛtāḥ eva kṛtaḥ ayam adhyāhāraḥ iti keścid buddham sa 
NVTP_1.1.4.133–1.1.4.134	 ca ayam asaṅgataḥ bodhaḥ adhyāhārasya ubhayathā api anupapatteḥ tad vyāvarti asya anyathā eva vyāvartita tvāt aprasakteḥ cati arthaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpannasya hi jñānasya vyabhicāra saṃbhāda vyabhicārī iti viśeṣaṇam yadi api na anupapannam tathā api etat vyāvartti asya sāmānya lakṣaṇena eva vyāvṛtta tvāt niṣprayojanam idam avaśyam ca tat anuvartanīyam na hi yatas iti adhyāhṛta padena karaṇa mātram parāmṛśyate tasya aprakṛta tvāt kim tu pramākaraṇam tathā ca ayam arthaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam yatas pramāṇāt bhavati tat pratyakṣam evam ca vyabhicāriṇi kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ iti atas āha yadi api iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.135–1.1.4.136	 nanu avyabhicāri pada karaṇam pramāṇa pada anuvartanam vā iti kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti atas āha anyathā iti avyabhicāri padam pramāṇa param iti arthaḥ pramāṇasya eva avyabhicāri tvāt yadi api tatra tad pūrvakam iti lakṣaṇa pada paryālocanayā eva vyabhicāri nirāsaḥ na hi ukta rūpe dve pratyakṣe pūrvam yasya jñānasya tat vyabhicāriṇīm api pramām janayet atas eva tad artham tatra sāmānya lakṣaṇa anuvartanam asāram eva tathā api evaṃbhūta pratyakṣa dvaya janite saṃskāre nirṇaye ca anumāna tva prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva tasmāt tad nivṛtti artham pramāṇa padam na kṛtam ced avaśyam anuvartanīyam iti arthaḥ yadi evam kim avyabhicāri pada prayojanam iti atas āha tathā api iti na upayujyate na ca śakyate paraspara āśraya prasaḍgāt iti api draṣṭavyam tathā api niyamaḥ na sphuṭībhūtaḥ iti atas āha tatra iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.137–1.1.4.138	 nanu anumāna vat avyabhicāra siddhyā phala siddhiḥ na pratyakṣe yathā tathā śabde api tatas tad avabodhana artha tatra api avyabhicāri pada avatāra prasaṅgaḥ iti atas āha śabda ādau tu iti pratyakṣe phala avyabhicāra nirṇayena eva avyabhicāra niścayaḥ iti niyamaḥ na anyatra ityarthaḥ avyabhicāri pada upādānam phala viśeṣaṇa tayā iti śeṣaḥ ayam ca niyamaḥ svarūpataḥ api phala dvārā eva pratyakṣam unnīyate na tu anyathā iti anumāna ādikam tu pratītam sat phalāya kalpate na tu anyathā iti niyame sati syāt iti ayam api artha ākṣipta tayā prāk eva darśitaḥ dvayī iti aparam api utpatti jñaptibhyām niyama dvayam śliṣṭam āha athavā iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.139–1.1.4.140	 kāraṇam utpādakam pratyāyakam ca ubhayam sādhayati na hi iti upādhi śaḍkā ni vṛtti artham tarka sahāya tva upavarṇanam āgamasya api ca vaktṛ śrotṛ gata tvena pratyakṣa apekṣā utpattau jñaptau ca cataḥ atas saṃmugdham āha evam iti tathā api ayam arthaḥ katham avyabhicāri pada upādāna mātrat labhyate iti atas āha na hi iti tat ayam saṃkṣepaḥ saḥ ayam sūtrakārasya iha viśeṣataḥ prayatnaḥ jñāpayati yat etasmin= avyabhicāriṇī anyatra vyabhicāra śaḍkā eva na asti atas iha eva tad grahāya viśeṣataḥ yatitavyam iti yadi api jñāpti pakṣe laukika vacasām pravṛtti sāmarthya ādinā vyabhicāra abhāva grahaḥ tathā api pāralaukika āgama avi abhicāra niścayaḥ āpta ukta tvena eva tat ca mūla bhūta pratyakṣa śuddheḥ eva iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.141	 nanu bhāṣya vārttikāyoḥ kā gatiḥ na hi ayam arthaḥ tatas pratīyate kim nāma vyabhicāri vyāvṛtti mātram iti atas āha tasmāt suṣṭhu uktam iti saḥ eva arthaḥ kim tu niyamya tayā na tu vidheyatayā iti āśayaḥ uccāvacam uccalate iti jala sādṛśya saṃkīrtanam bhrānti bīja tayā upaghāta doṣān nayanasya ātapa ādinā etat uktam bhavati upadarśita artha aprāpaka tvam vyabhicāraḥ na ca arthena kaścid arthaḥ upadarśitaḥ yama prāpayan= arthaḥ vyabhicaret anyathā artha upadarśana svabhāvasya ca utpattiḥ na 
NVTP_1.1.4.142	 ca artha upadarśana svabhāvaḥ na ca anyathā utpannaḥ tasmāt evaṃbhūtaḥ vyabhicāraḥ jñānasya eva na ca arthasya tat idam uktam pratyayaḥ bhrāntaḥ jāyate iti vṛddha saṃmatim āha yathā āhuḥ iti andhaḥ iti yamyak darśana upāya rahita tva mātra param na paśyati iti api samyak jñāna abhāva mātra upalakṣaṇa param tena puruṣa aparādhaḥ sa bhavati iti atra adarśanam viparīta darśanam vā iti aparādhaḥ iti arthaḥ yathā hi sthāṇuḥ adṛśyamānaḥ tathā eva puruṣa tvena api daśyamānaḥ iti tātparyam 
NVTP_1.1.4.143–1.1.4.144	 yat yani saṃśayaḥ api sāmānya lakṣaṇa anuvṛttyā eva nirastaḥ tasya apramāṇa phala tvāt tathā api avyabhicāri padam niyama jñāpana artham avaśyam kartavyam tena ca vyabhicāri vyudāsa mukhena eva niyamaḥ pradarśayitavyaḥ saṃśayaḥ api vyabhicāri jātīyaḥ atas tena eva asya vyudāsaḥ yuktaḥ iti āśayavān āha avyabhicāri padena eva iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.145–1.1.4.148	 nanu vyabhicāri tvam eva asya katham viparyājñānam hi niścaya ākaram ayam tu na tathā iti atas āha no khalu iti na hi niścaya tvam prayojakam atra kim tu visaṃvādaḥ sa ca prāpti ayogaḥ na ca prāpti yogaḥ dvi rūpasya vastunaḥ kvacid kadācid kenacid aprāpteḥ iti arthaḥ na ca vācyam bhrānteḥ abhrānti pratiyogi tvāt aniyatasya ca arthasya kvacid api pramāṇa agocara tvāt asat khyāteḥ anabhyupagamāt ca sarvam idam asamañjasam iti no khalu dolāyamānaḥ sthāṇu puruṣa vyatiriktaḥ kaścid aniyataḥ nāma arthaḥ parisphurati yatra asamañjasam syāt 
NVTP_1.1.4.149^1	 nanu sthāṇu puruṣau= ubhau= api yadi āropitau tadā ubhaya upamarda ātmanā bādhakena bhavitavyam atha anya tadasya āropaḥ tadā aparasya pāramārthika tvāt tad pratipatteḥ abādhya tvam eva syāt yathā yuktau rajata aṃśasya mithyātve śukla bhāsvara tva ādi niścayasya satya tvam tathā ca sthāṇu aṃśe niścayaḥ puruṣa aṃśe tu eka koṭi sanniveśavān eva vibhramaḥ iti saṃśayaḥ datta jala añjaliḥ prasaktaḥ tasmāt ubhaya smaraṇa mātra ātmakaḥ ayam iti syāt na syāt yatra tāvat ubhayoḥ anubhaya ātmake pāṣāṇa stambha ādau samāropaḥ tatra ubhaya upamarda ātmakaḥ eva bādhakaḥ iti kim atra vaktavyam 
NVTP_1.1.4.149^2	 yatra api ekatara āropaḥ tatra api na apara aṃśe niścayaḥ paraspara pratikṣepa upasthiti vyāhatyāḥ aniścaya ātmakasya eva jñānasya utpādāt yatra hi rajata tva ārope api śukla tva ādau niścayaḥ tatra āropitānāna upitayoḥ mithas virodha abhāvaḥ tasmāt āropitān āropita tva aviśeṣe api yatra āropitān āropitau paraspara aviruddhau sa viparyayaḥ yatra tu paraspara viruddhau sa saṃśayaḥ iti sarvam avadātam yadi evam saṃśayaḥ api viparyaya antarbhūtaḥ tad apākaraṇena eva apākṛtaḥ ca kimartham tarhi vyavasāya ātmaka padam sūtra ākāraḥ cakāra san vā saḥ udāra arthaḥ vyākhyātṛbhiḥ kim iti upekṣitaḥ tathābhūtor avācīnaiḥ katham unnīyate iti atas āha tasmāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.150	 syāt etat iti syāt tad avabodha artham yadi tat pratyakṣam syāt na tu etat asti iti arthaḥ hetum āha abhilāpa iti abhidhāna ākāra saṃsarga yogyā abhidheya ākāram hi tat iti arthaḥ vipakṣāt vyatirekam āha na ca iti abhidhāna abhidheya saṃsarge hi tad ākārayoḥ saṃsarga niyamaḥ sa ca saṃyoga samavāya kārya kāraṇa bhāva rūpaḥ tāvat na saṃbhavati iti āha na hi arthe śabdāḥ santi iti saṃyogena samavāyena kārya tayā vā iti śeṣaḥ tad ātmānaḥ vā iti na hi iti anuṣajyate upapattim āha tathā sati iti na ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.151	 sa hi saṃvedana dharmaḥ grāhya ākāra rūpaḥ vā syāt tad nirapekṣa grāhaka ākāra rūpaḥ vā na tāvat ādyaḥ artha asaṃsparśī yatas artha asaṃsparśaḥ ca asya atad vṛtti tvāt atat utpatteḥ ca iti pūrvā eva yuktiḥ iti āśayaḥ na api dvitīyaḥ artheṣu tad niyojanāt aryamāneṣu bāhyeṣu artheṣu eva tasyāmilāpasya niyojanāt niyogataḥ bāhya sāmānādhikaraṇyena pratīteḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.152	 etat uktam bhavati saṃvedana ākāraḥ hi jñātṛ tva ādiḥ tad sāmāna adhikaraṇyena pratīyate abhilāpaḥ tu bāhya sanniyuktaḥ tad sāmāna adhiraṇyena iti atas na saṃvedana dharmaḥ tasmāt viṣayataḥ svarūpataḥ ca yatas asya na abhi bhalāpa saṃsarga yogya tā sambhavaḥ tasmāt idam arthāt sarūpakāt upajāyamānam jñānam vikalpa rūpam artham eva ādarśayet iti prasaṅgaḥ nāmilāpam artha saṃsargitayā iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.153–1.1.4.154	 syāt etat sva kāraṇat upajātasya kāraṇam akāraṇam vā kaścid eva viṣayaḥ evam ca arthāt upajātasya api anekaḥ abhilāpaḥ api asya viṣayaḥ yadi syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ iti atas āha na hi iti rūpāt cakṣuṣaḥ viṣayāt upajāyamānam cākṣuṣam vijñānam nayanā viṣaya rasa sahitam atat rūpam iti etat uktam bhavati sa ākāra vāda siddhau tāvat anupaplutam ākāram ādadhadeva arthaḥ viṣayaḥ na ca śabda saṃsarga yogya tā 
NVTP_1.1.4.155–1.1.4.156	 arthasya asti yena tat ākāram jñānam bhavet na ca indriya vijñānam śabdaḥ svatantraḥ eva ākāra ādhāyakaḥ vikalpa kāle tad abhāvāt bhāve api vā svatantraḥ pratibhāseta na artha saṃsargitayā iti uktam nirākāra pakṣe api ātmānātma prakāśana śakteḥ vijñānasya saḥ eva viṣayaḥ yatra indriyam niyata sāmarthyam anyathā ati prasaḍgāt na ca cakṣuḥ indriya antara viṣaye samartham na ca cakṣuḥ viṣayasya eva śabda saṃsargaḥ asti iti cintitam iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.157–1.1.4.159	 prasaṅgam uktvā viparyaya artham āha tasmāt iti amilāpa saṃsarga an apekṣam artham tad saṃsargiṇam ādarśaya dadhyavasyat vikalpa vāsanā utthāpitam na artha sāmarthya samuttham iti bhāvaḥ viparyaye kim bādhakam iti atas āha aniyata artha grāhi yatas vikalpa gatam artha ākāram pratyaniyāmaka tvāt tasya iti arthaḥ etat uktam bhavati yadi hi pratibhāsamānor atha upi vikalpasya janakaḥ bhavet tadā tad ākāram niyamayet na tu niyamayati tad asannidhau= api vikalpa vāsanā vaśāt tasya tathāvidha ākāra upasthiteḥ nanu indriyam asya janakam aḥ tu na hi tasya ākāra niyāmaka tayā kāraka tvam iti atas āha mānasam iti manaḥ mātra prabhavam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.160–1.1.4.161	 indriyam api hi jñāna janakam bhavat ākāra niyāmaka artha sannikarṣeṇa eva na tu tad nirapekṣam na ca asya tathāvidha artha sannikarṣaḥ asti iti uktam iti bhāvaḥ nanu vivāda adhyāsite vikalpe dṛśya tayā eva artha ākāraḥ parisphurati na ca evam ubhaya va ādi siddhārtha sannidhi nipekṣa vikalpeṣu aparokṣa tayā arthaḥ prakāśate tad viśeṣaḥ vikalpoḥ atha sannidhi sāpekṣaḥ tathā ca arthasya tad ākāra niyāmaka tvāt tad janaka tvam anicchatā api abhyupeyam anyathā utprekṣā vyāpāra tvāt vikalpasya pravartaka tvam api na nirvahet iti atas āha ātmīyam iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.162	 utprekṣāḥ asat āropaṇam yatas bhavati avaśyam atas api evam utprekṣāmahe iti vyāhāraḥ tiraskāraḥ anadhyavasāyaḥ darśanam sākṣātkaraṇam puraskāraḥ bheda āgrahaḥ vā tad hetukaḥ āropaḥ vā tat siddham iti prasaḍga ādi upanibandhena yadi vivāda adhyāsitāḥ vikalpāḥ artha sāmarthya labdha janmānaḥ tadā na śabda kalpanā anugatāḥ iti arthaḥ tad anugata tvam iti śabda kalpanā anugata tvam tasya upalabdhiḥ abhilāpa anugata tvam nirākurvatī artha sāmarthya ja tvam virūṇat hi iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.163	 asiddha viruddhayoḥ asambhavāt iha sambhāvita tayā pūrva ukta smāraṇa puraḥsaram sandigdha anaikāntika tva aśaḍkām eva apanayati na ca iti artha rūpam anukuryāt artha rūpa sadṛśa ākāram bhavet iti arthaḥ tādātmya tad utpattibhyām asaṃbaddha rūpa anukāre niyāmaka abhāvāt sarva rūpa anukāreṇa sarveṣām sarvajña tā āpattiḥ sat rūpa anukāra mātra tvāt tad viṣaya tāyāḥ iti bhāvaḥ na hi tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ svarūpeṇa upapujyate ki nāma niyāmaka tayā tat atra saḍketa eva niyāmakaḥ yadi syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āśa yavān āśaṅkate saḍketa iti tat eva dṛṣṭam sat smārayet etān niyamena iti śeṣaḥ kim etau= api iti atas āha tatra eva ca iti anugatam anugama gocaraḥ atas eva sāmānyam deśa kāla anugatam tatra eva saḍketasya sukara tvāt iti bhāvaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.164	 kim etāvatā api iti atas āha na ca tat tat dṛṣṭam sākṣātkṛtam kim tu sva lakṣaṇam darśana gocaraḥ sarūpaka tvāt iti śeṣaḥ sarūpaka tvam eva asya kutas iti atas āha tat eva hi iti parama arthaḥ akṛtrimam anāropitam rūpam tena asti iti parama artha sat etat eva kutas iti atas āha vijñānasya kāraṇam vijñānasya iti prakṛta upayogāt kāraṇam artha kriyā samartham yatas iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.165	 nanu sāmānyam api kim na darśana gocaraḥ iti atas āha na tu sāmānyam iti kutas sarva sāmarthya rahitam hi tat sarvaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ heya upādeya rūpaḥ tasya sāmarthyam śaktiḥ tat rahitam yasmāt tat na hi kiñcid puruṣa prayojanam sāmānyasādhyam asti ator athakriyāyām aśakta tvāt na tat paramārtha sat asattva anna tat vijñāna janakam ajanaka tvāt na sarūpakam asarūpaka tvāt na darśana gocaraḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.166	 nanu sāmānyasya tāvat artha kriyā virahāt darśana gocara tvam mā bhūt darśana gocarasya eva tu vā ācya tāḥ tu saḍketaḥ api tatra kena api upāyena bhaviṣyati tat nirvicikitsam eva tarhi artha kriyā samartha vaspu pratipādana abhiprāyavantaḥ prayojaka vṛddhāḥ prayojya vṛddhāḥ ca tathāvidha artha pratipattimantaḥ śābde vyavahāre upalabhyante iti atas āha api ca iti na hi aupṇyāt atiriktaḥ vahniḥ nāma asti bauddha rāt ha ante na ca ubhaya vādi saṃpratipatti viṣayaḥ pratītam auṣṇyam śīta apanodanam karoti iti api kadācid akurvat hi sarvathā apratītam na kuryāt āropitam vā na ca vahni śabdāt sarvathā vahneḥ apratītiḥ tasmāt 
NVTP_1.1.4.167–1.1.4.168	 śabda kalpanā ullikhitam avastu eva vastu ābhāsam iti abhiprāyaḥ jāti ādīn paramārthikān abhyupetya āha tat na iti vivekena deśa bhedena iti arthaḥ avacchedya avacchedaka bhāvena hi mithas yojanāḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ sa ca vivikta deśa tā pratītyā vyāptaḥ sā ca atas nivarttamānā sva vyāpyam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvam ādāya eva nivartate tatas ca jāti ādīnām parasparam asambandhāt na sva tanatreṣu teṣu śabdaḥ api sukara saḍketeḥ tathā ca na saṃsṛṣṭa vedanam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.169–1.1.4.172	 etena śabdasya viveka graha saṃbhave api tad yojanā nirastaḥ boddhavyā ekam asamuditam avibhāgam anaṃśam sva lakṣaṇam trailokya vilakṣaṇam tathā tathā iti guṇa karma ādi samudita tvena sādhāraṇa tvena vikalpyate na tu daśyate iti arthaḥ api ca parama artha sat vastu traya vedane api vivekena iti śeṣaḥ nanu na hi eka jñāna viṣayau samāna kāle aḍgulyau na kārya kāraṇa bhūte iti niyata pūrva aparatve api te sarvajña eka vijñāna gocarau na tathā iti yuktam vaktum yadyucyeta kaḥ doṣaḥ na hi upalabdhi bheda abheda prayukte kāraṇa akaraṇa tve kim tarhi yat anapekṣam tat kāraṇam sa apekṣam ca kāryam iti tat atra api samānam eka jñāna gocara tve api yat avacchedakam 
NVTP_1.1.4.173	 tad viśeṣaṇam avacchedyam ca viśeṣyam iti yat tu na evam na tat yathā iti atas āha viśeṣaṇam khalu iti na anyathā iti atiprasaḍgāt iti śeṣaḥ tarhi upakāraḥ api kaścid astu iti atas āha na ca ekā iti kim iti na syāt iti atas āha tayoḥ iti prasaḍgāt iti śeṣaḥ svarūpataḥ paurvāparya niyamaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ jñāptitaḥ tu jñāpya jñāpaka bhāvaḥ sa ca ayam eka jñāna gocarayoḥ eka kālayoḥ ca dvi rūpaḥ api niyataḥ na asti yasmāt iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.174	 syāt etat yadi api ukta svarūpam upakāra dvayam na saṃbhavati tathā api ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ bhavet sa hi samāna kālayoḥ eva kuṇḍa badarayoḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ tu tvayā api upapādanīyaḥ mayā apibhañjanīyaḥ iti atas āha api ca iti yadi api tīrthikaiḥ kuṇḍādhā vaśān na badarasya eva apatana dharmakasya utpādaḥ svīkriyate sthaima śraddhā jaḍa tvāt tathā api gati nivṛtti lakṣaṇām guru tva pratibandhaka saṃyoga lakṣaṇām vā sthitim tad dharma bhūtāḥ vidadhadeva badarasya kuṇḍamādhāra tayā abhyupetam taiḥ kim ca atas atas āha tadvat iha api iti etāvatā api kim iti atas āha na ca śakti antaraiḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.175–1.1.4.177	 yadi api badara vat jāti ādīnām dharmasya kasyacid upajana apāya rūpam upakāram na abhyupagacchati eva paraḥ tathā api abhyupagama vādaḥ ayam saugatasya iti mantavyam tathā ca iti san= iti anena hi vikalpena sattva upakāra samarthaḥ viṣayīkṛtaḥ na ca tatas anyaḥ kaścid dravya tva ādi upakāra samarthaḥ asattva upakāra samarthaḥ asti yatra dravya ādi vikalpāḥ sārthakāḥ syuḥ tasmāt ete dravyavatu ādi upakāra samarther athe sattva upakāra samartha abhedini pravartamānāḥ tad adhikaraṇam artham aspṛśantaḥ anarthakāḥ prasaktāḥ iti samudāya arthaḥ bauddhasya ati parāmarśa kuśala tām ca udyasya ca ati tucchatām ālakṣya asmākam eva mati lāghavam saṃbhāvayiṣyati iti āśaḍkya tad grantham likhati yadā aha iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.178	 ayam vārttika arthaḥ yasya darśane nānā upādheḥ api arthasya dhīḥ vikalpa dhīḥ grāhikāḥ bhedinaḥ viśiṣṭasya nānā upādhi upakārāḍgam yā śaktiḥ tat eka ātmanaḥ tasya sarva ātmanā sarvaiḥ upādhibhiḥ eka svabhāvasya eva upakāryasya viśeṣyasya grahe sati kaḥ bhedaḥ bhidyate iti bhedaḥ viśiṣyate iti yāvat aniścitaḥ syāt api tu sarva upādhimiḥ viśiṣṭaḥ niścitaḥ eva syāt iti arthaḥ emasya upādheḥ upakāraka svabhāve grāhye gṛhyamāṇe sati na upakārāḥ upakārakāḥ svabhāvāḥ upādhi antarāṇām tatas apare bhinna vidyante ye tasmin= eka upakāraka svabhāve dṛṣṭe api na dṛṣṭāḥ syuḥ kim nāma saḥ erveka svabhāvaḥ sarveṣām upakārakaḥ tatasat grahe tad eka upādhi viśiṣṭa grahe sakala grahaḥ sakala upādhi viśiṣṭa grahaḥ prasaktaḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.179	 nanu varam vastu svabhāva vādam āsthāya anupakāryānupakārakayoḥ api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvam spaṣṭa dṛṣṭam upapādayitum śaktāḥ pare upādhu pādhim abhdedāt ca apauna rūktyam na punar saugatāḥ sattva ādīnām upādhīnām vastu tva anabhyupagamāt evam ca tvad śarāḥ tvayi eva nipatitāḥ iti atas āha asmākam tu iti yat ca gṛhṇanti sāmānya mātram yat ca adhyavasyanti santānam na manāk api sāmānyena api rūpeṇa gāhante gocaranti tasya alīka tayā vastu dharma tva abhāvāt iti arthaḥ tarhi katham avisaṃvādakāḥ pravartakāḥ vā iti atas āha pāramparyeṇa iti tatas kim iti atas āha atas iti yatra viṣaya adhīnā dhīḥ tatra 
NVTP_1.1.4.180–1.1.4.181	 tad āyattau viśeṣa aviśeṣau atra tu viparyayaḥ viṣayasya eva pratibhāsa sattayā buddhi adhīna tvāt tat iha vikalpasya viṣayaḥ viśeṣyaḥ tad tadvat viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭa tayā api kim bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā iti atra vikalpaḥ eva sākṣī na vicāraḥ iti arthaḥ nanu parama artha sannarthaḥ mā bhūt vikalpasya viṣayaḥ janakaḥ tu bhaviṣyati iti atas āha api ca iti na vikalpikām api iti apiḥ bhinna kramaḥ arthaḥ vikalpasya na gocaraḥ janakaḥ api na iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.182–1.1.4.183	 artha upayogaḥ sannikarṣaḥ na ca yat eva ityādi nyāyāt iti vācyam iti śeṣaḥ no khalu iti smaraṇa indriyayoḥ eka viṣaya sāmarthya abhāvāt na paraspara apekṣa tvam tatas ca saḥ eva artha upayogī aviśiṣṭaḥ iti arthaḥ eka gocara tvam eva anayoḥ kutas na iti atas āha tad gocara tve ca iti ananubhūta pūrvāṇām api arthānām cakṣuṣoḥ vyāpāra mātreṇa 
NVTP_1.1.4.184–1.1.4.185	 pūrva avasthā smaraṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti api draṣṭavyam tena syāt tathā sati prasajyeta iti arthaḥ akṣa apāye api netra dhīḥ iti upalakṣaṇam vāsanā abhāve smṛti dhīḥ iti api draṣṭavyam sahate pratīkṣate iti arthaḥ siddhāntam upakramate atra iti gauḥ ayam ityādeḥ vikalpasya tāvat abhilāpa saṃsarga yogya pratibhāsa vat artha sākṣātkāraḥ api anubhava siddhaḥ asti ca usya indriya artha anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam 
NVTP_1.1.4.186	 tat anyathā siddham tayoḥ ālocana mātraḥ eva caritārtha tvāt iti ced tat kim idānīm ālocanasya ayam mahimā vikalpa upajananam prati tathā sati tasmāt na kadācid api ālocanam jāyeta vāsanā paripāka virahāt na tathā iti ced sa khalu vāsanā paripākaḥ yadi niyamāt indriya artha madhyam adhiśete katham na tad apekṣā kāryasya kākatālīyaḥ ced sannidhi sannihiteṣu api indriya artheṣu kadācid viśiṣṭāt vāsanā paripākāt sākṣātkāravān vikalpaḥ utpadyate na vai sākṣāt kāvān vikalpaḥ kaścid kim tu nirvikalpaka bheda āgrahāt tat vān iva avabhāsate iti ced na pramāṇa abhāvāt na 
NVTP_1.1.4.187–1.1.4.188	 hi vivāda adhyāsita vikalpa gataḥ darśana vyāpāraḥ ayam aupādhikaḥ iti asti pratyakṣam na api anumānam darśana vyāpāra tā kalpanā apoḍha tvena vyāptā tat ca atas nivartamānam tām api nivartayati iti ced na viparyayasya api vaktum sukara tvāt tathā hi darśana vyāpāra tvam kalpanā anugata tvena vyāptam tat ca tad anugata tvam ālocanāt nivartamānam sva vyāpyam darśana vyāpāra tvam api nivartayati tathā ca vikalpa sānnidhyāt aupādhikaḥ darśana vyāpāraḥ ayam ālocanam iti kim na syāt anubhavaḥ tu upādhi śaṅkayā tvayā eva asākṣīkṛtaḥ anāgate vikalpe katham iva tad dharmaḥ nirvikalpake pratibhāseta iti ced na kāla bhedasya ubhayatra api tulya tvāt upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ ca niyama hetuḥ samānaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.189	 nanūpāda adharmāḥ upādeyam anugacchanti na tu upādeya dharmāḥ upādānam iti ced na vastutas avastu dharmāṇām apratisaṃkramāt ābhimānike tu pratisaṃkrame aniyamaḥ upādāna pratyaya balāt upādeya pratyayaḥ tathā utpadyate iti ced hanta yadi sākṣātkāraḥ sākṣātkāravān utpadyate katham asya tathā atvam aupādhikam tāvat mātrā deva indriya ādi nirapekṣāt upajātam iti etāvatā eva tat aupādhikam iti ucyate iti ced na samanantara pratyaya sākṣātkāra mahimnā sākṣātkāra utpattau= asākṣātkāra anutpāda prasaḍgāt na ca asākṣātkāriṇaḥ sākṣātkāraḥ kadācid upapadyeta sahakāri viśeṣāt evam api syāt iti ced tarhi yādṛśi kārye yādṛś anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam dṛṣṭam tādṛśasya tatra sahakāri tvam āstheyam dṛṣṭam ca ubhaya vādi saṃpratipanna nirvikalpake sākṣātkāram pratīndriya arthayoḥ sāmarthyam na vikalpasya iti ukta prāyam 
NVTP_1.1.4.190	 evam tāvat arthaṃsākṣāt karaṇam svābhāvikam tat na antarīyaka tayā indriya artha sāmarthya samuttha tvam asya sthitam avisaṃvādi tvam api asyāna upādhikam tathā hi yadi asya pāramārthikaḥ visaṃvādaḥ syāt tadā pratīyamānaḥ api aupādhikaḥ ayam avisaṃvādaḥ iti saṃbhāvyeta sa ca deśa kāla ākāra kṛtaḥ tāvat na bhavati ananugatam eva anugata tayā darśayati iti ced na asādhāraṇasya sva lakṣaṇasya vikalpena asaṃsparśāt saṃsparśe vā tad janya tva prasaṅgaḥ ajanakasya eva tu vastu sataḥ viṣaya tve pratyakṣa tvam artha sāmarthya samuttha tvena vyāptam iti supta pralāpaḥ vikalpaḥ tāvat sādhāraṇam svarūpam ullikhan= ā iva pravartayati tat ca sarva sāmarthya rahitam na ca artha kriyā arthī tat asamartham dṛṣṭvā pravartate tatas asamartham eva samāropita sāmarthyam vikalpyate 
NVTP_1.1.4.191–1.1.4.192	 tathā ca katham asya viparītāroparūpasya saṃvādaḥ nāma iti ced na yadi hi sāmarthyam eva āropayet asādhāraṇam eva ullikhet na hi anyat asā dhāraṇāt rūpāt samartham nāma tava darśane tasmāt samartham iva tat darśayati vikalpaḥ iva arthaḥ ca na tatra āropyaḥ vikalpa arthasya samarthena āsādṛśa tvāt nanu asāmarthya vyāvṛtti mātram eva sāmarthyam na tu tattva antaram tasya ca na sādhāraṇa rūpa virodhaḥ tathā ca aikātmya prathanam na viruddham iti ced na avirodhe sati samāropa anupapatteḥ na hi yat yatra aviruddham sat prathate tat tatra āropitam nāma tasmāt bheda agrahāt pravṛttiḥ na ca saḥ eva visaṃvādaḥ tathā ca satya ālocanam api visaṃvādi syāt kalpanā locanayoḥ bhedān ullekhāt etena sva pratibhāse anarthe artha adhyavasāyena pravṛtteḥ iti parāḥ tam 
NVTP_1.1.4.193–1.1.4.194	 anartha tvam hi vikalpāt abhedaḥ vikalpyasya syāt ālocanīyāt bhedaḥ vā na tāvat kalpanā gocarasya alīkasya kalpanayā abhedaḥ saṃbhavati yena bheda ullikhanam āropaḥ syāt ālocanīyāt bhede api nābheda prathā iti na āropaḥ sva pratibhāse anarthaḥ iti vacanāt na eṣa doṣaḥ sa khalu ākāraḥ vikalpāt abhinnaḥ api bhinnaḥ āropyate iti ced yadi tāvat vijñāna nayam ālambya etat ucyate tad ālocanasya api eṣā eva gatiḥ iti tasya api āropa rūpa tvāt grāhya ākāre aprāmāṇyam vikalpasya api sva ātmani ca saṃvedana tvāt ubhayoḥ api prāmāṇyam eva iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.195–1.1.4.196	 atha bāhyam artham adhikṛtya prastutā iyam kathā tathā api yādṛśa ākāraḥ vikalpaḥ tādṛśa ākāraḥ eva bāhya tayā pratibhāseta na ca asau sādhāraṇa ākāraḥ samasti tatas yeda tat sādhāraṇam rūpam ābhāti tat na vikalpa ākāram abhiniviśate iti bahis eva avatiṣṭhate bāhya tva vat sādhāraṇa tvam api asi a āropyate iti ced na asādha araṇyasya pāramārthikasya kvacid api anupalabdheḥ āropayitum aśakya tvāt asat ullekhe tu alīka ālambana tvam eva vikalpasya abhyupagatam syāt tatra cāra upasaṃbhāvanā eva na asti iti uktam 
NVTP_1.1.4.197^1	 pūrva aparayoḥ vikalpa ākārayoḥ abheda anusandhānam eva sādhāraṇyam iti ced na ākāriṇām bheda pratītau= ākārāṇām ekatvena pratisandhātum aśakyatvāt tayoḥ tādātmyāmi upagamāt vikalpasya ātmā api ākāraḥ bhinnaḥ bāhya tayā āropitaḥ tatas vikalpa ātmānām bheda avasāye api na ākārāṇām bheda avasāyaḥ tatas tad ekatayā anusandhānam iti ced hanta yadi ayam ākāraḥ vikalpa ātmā tathā iti pratīyeta katham bāhya tvena āropyeta tādātmya apratītiḥ tūbha yathā api syāt asva saṃvedya tvāt vikalpasya sva saṃvedana tvena vā tatas bhinnātvāt tādātmyasya ādyaḥ tāvat saugataiḥ anabhyupagamāt eva duḥsthaḥ dvitīyaḥ tu sarvaiḥ eva avagataḥ avagatam na tu niścitam iti ced na niścaya aniścaya lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma saṃsarṅgeṇa bheda āpatteḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.197^2	 vyāvṛttyoḥ bhedaḥ eva na tu vastuni iti ced atha kā iyam vyāvṛttiḥ nāma na kiścid iti ced evam astu tathā ca nāra upavārtā api tatas na asya upadarśita artha visaṃvāda gandhaḥ api asat artha prakāśanam eva visaṃvādanam iti ced āstām tāvat evat yathā viṣaya mātram atra vivakṣitam prakṛta upayogāt evam ca aviparīta artha tvāt prāmāṇyam pramāṇasya sataḥ sākṣātkāri tvāt pratyakṣa tvam asmad ādi pratyakṣa tvāt ca indriya artha sāmarthya samuttha tvam evam sati sarve eva saugatena prayujyamānāḥ kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tayā pratipakṣa hetavaḥ padam adhyāropayitum asamarthāḥ prāk eva vikalpasya apratyakṣatām sādhayitum tathā api idam avaśiṣyate yat etāvatā api na paramārtha sat viṣayasya prāmāṇyam sādhitam tatra ca āvayoḥ vivādaḥ iti tatra āha syāt virodhaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.198–1.1.4.199	 nanu paramārtha sataḥ abhilāpa saṃsarga yogya tā aśakya vyutpādana eva kṣaṇika tvāt jagataḥ iti atas uktam sthema bhājam iti nanu sthairya siddhau= api jāti ādīnām durūpa pāda tvāt katham paramārtha sataḥ abhilāpa saṃsarga yogya tā iti atas uktam jāti ādimantam tathā ca iti yadi api ukta rūpa artha vyavasthāpane sati kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ ayam prasaṅga hetuḥ tad darśa neca apakṣa dharmaḥ na hi asti saṃbhavaḥ vikalpasya artha sāmarthya samuttha tvam niścitam aniścitam ca tad arthasya parama artha sattvam tathā api paraḥ api tad nirākaraṇa siddhyā eva pratyavasthitaḥ na rāja ājñayā nirākaraṇīyaḥ tasmāt āpātataḥ tad sandehe sandigdha vipakṣa vṛtti tvam eva astu iti arthaḥ etena viparyayaḥ api nirākṛtaḥ boddhavyaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.200–1.1.4.201	 namu santu jāti ādayaḥ parama artha bhūtāḥ tathā api yadi te api piṇḍa ātma bhūtāḥ katham bhedena pratibhāsaret tathā apratibhāsamānāḥ ca katham viśeṣya tayā viśeṣyam avacchindyuḥ anātma bhūtāḥ ced katham sāmānādhikaraṇyam aśnu vīrat = ityatas āha na ca iti tathā api śabdaḥ bhinna ātmā atadvṛttiḥ katham avacchedakaḥ syāt yadi tad gataḥ tad ātmā vā na pratīyeta evam eva tu avacchede ati prasaṅgaḥ avaccheda pratītau tu bhrāntiḥ iti āśaṅkate na ca iti abheda kalpanam avaccheda kalpanam tat ca tad ātmatayā tad saṃsargi tayā vā uktam etat iti na hi tad vṛtti tayā eva tad saṃsargaḥ iti niyamaḥ api tu taṭa sthena api jñānena iva jñeyasya vācakena vācyasya na viruddhaḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.202	 nanu taṭa sthaḥ api ayam avacchedakaḥ na sattā mātreṇa api tu jñātaḥ na tu śabda jñāne tadānīm śravaṇasya vyāpāraḥ viṣayasya viprayogāt sa vya apāre cakṣuṣi manasaḥ tatra vyāsaḍgāt ca tasmāt yathā svpna avasthāyām indriya uparame api pūrva saṃskāra pāṭavān manasā eva ekena avidyamānāḥ api arthāḥ viṣayīkriyante tathā aśabda vyāvṛtti vikalpa janita vāsanā paṭunā cakṣuṣā eva manasā vā śabdaḥ api viṣayīkriyate iti avidyamāna śabda ālambana tvāt bhrāntiḥ eva iti atas āha na ca śabda arthayoḥ iti eka indriya grāhyatā iti atra prasaṅgaḥ iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.203–1.1.4.204	 ayam arthaḥ yadi manaḥ abhiprāyeṇa eka indriya grāhya tā prasajyate na kiñcid aniṣṭam tasya sarva viṣaya tvāt atha bāhya indriyam abhipretya tatra api kim nāma yojana ātmake vikalpe kim vā jāti ādi yojana ātmake tatra nāmnaḥ viśeṣaṇa tva pakṣaḥ tāvat anabhyupagamena eva parihṛtaḥ upalakṣaṇa tvam tu taṭa sthasya eva iti pratipāditam eva tat ca indriya antara upanītasī api nirvahati iti na aindriyake vikalpe nāma sphuraṇam upayujyate jāti ādi yojanāyām tu śabda smaraṇasya api na asti upayogaḥ prāk eva tad grahaṇasya tasya anavacchedaka tvāt kevalam kim iti niyamataḥ smaryate śabdaḥ iti avaśiṣyate tatra idam uktam kim tu iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.205–1.1.4.209	 tat kim idānīm śabda smaraṇasya na kaścid asti upayogaḥ iti atas āha indriya ja vikalpa utpādam prati vyavahāram prati tu asti eva upayogaḥ iti arthaḥ saḍketasamayā iti pūrva avasthā smaraṇa grahaṇayoḥ anyatara upalakṣaṇa param śabdaḥ tu na niveśayati ātmānam gṛhītaḥ smṛtaḥ api iti śeṣaḥ cakṣuṣā api saḥ eva ayam dṛśyate na tu pūrva hṛdaya sthaḥ śabdaḥ api iti arthaḥ etat eva vyākhyāya śloka antareṇa draḍhayati ananena hi ityādi na tu śabda niveśanam api iti śabda rūpam api viṣayam iti arthaḥ yadi api saṃjñā hi ityādi śloke sā taṭastha iti etāvat eva prakṛta upayogi tathā api anāgatam pratividhitsura vayava antaram vyācaṣṭe na artha indriyā iti artha sahitam indrayam artha indriyam yadi api kṣaṇam aṅga pakṣe api pratyekam asamartheṣu yeṣu saṃbhāvyate guṇaḥ saṃhatau hetu tā teṣām 
NVTP_1.1.4.210	 iti nyāyena atiśaya parampara utpādena pūrva avasthā smaraṇa ādi sahakāri madhyam adhyāsīnam yat eva indriyam tat eva vikalpa janakam na itarat iti na asti kaścid virodhaḥ tathā api vikalpasya sthira viṣaya tvāt kṣaṇika tva svīkāre nirviṣaya tvam āpādyeta iti nisphalaḥ prayāsaḥ syāt iti manyamānaḥ sthairyam ālambya eva pariharati na ca janakatvā iti syāt etat iti syāt etat sahakāri tvam saṃskārasya indriyam prati yadi anayoḥ viṣaya bhedaḥ na syāt iti arthaḥ tat kim iti indriya saṃskārayoḥ paraspara ādhipatyam viṣaya bhedāt kīdṛśān na bhavati kim pratipatti anubandhinaḥ vyāpāra anubandhinaḥ vā na tāvat ādyaḥ tathāvidha viṣaya bhede api gandha jñāna cakṣuṣoḥ paraspara ādhipatyena rūpa jñāna utpatti darśanāt dvitīyaḥ tu asiddhaḥ tasya kāryeṇa anuvidhīyamāna tā mātra unneya tvāt etat ca umayam api ubhaya vādi siddham iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.211	 nanu vyāpāḥ anubandhi tayā saṃskārasya yadi purovartī viṣayaḥ tadā atīta avasthā sphuraṇam na syāt eva na hi anya viṣayaḥ vyāpāraḥ anyatra kriyā iti abhyupagamaḥ tasmāt atīta viṣaya tvāt kriyāyāḥ vyāpāra anubandhitayā api saṃskārasya saḥ eva viṣayaḥ na tu purovartī evam indriyasya api yadi atīta avasthasya eva vyāpāravataḥ viṣayaḥ tadā purovarti viṣaya sphuraṇam na syāt tasmāt tasya api vyāpāravataḥ puras varti eva viṣayaḥ iti vyāpārataḥ api katham ekaviṣaya tā iti samanantara pratyayaḥ tu pratipattitaḥ gandha viṣayaḥ api vyāpārataḥ rūpa viṣayaḥ rūpa viṣaya vyāpāram eva cakṣuḥ apekṣate na hi cakṣuṣi api sahakāriṇi gandha jñānāt gamdha jñānam api tu rūpa jñānam eva iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.212–1.1.4.213	 na etat sādhīyaḥ sahakārī bhedāt eva vyāpāra bhedasya api niyamāt na hi cakṣuḥ ādi sahakāri virahe api gandha jñānasya rūpa viṣaya vyāpāra niyamaḥ tathā sati gandha jñānāt rasanā ādi sahakāriṇaḥ api rūpa jñānam eva syāt na rasa ādi jñānam tasmāt kevalasya cakṣuṣaḥ yadi api rūpam eva vyāpāra viṣayaḥ tathā api pūrva avasthā saṃskāra sahakārimataḥ tadvān eva purovartī vyāpāra viṣayaḥ iti na kaścid virodhaḥ pūrva avasthā cakṣuṣā asannikṛṣṭā katham tad vyāpāra viṣayaḥ iti avaśiṣṭam tu śaṅkate nanu atīta iti atra tad saṃbandham eva tad vyāpāra viṣaya tvam syāt saṃbandhasya tad vyāpaka tvam vā ādyam nirākāroti tat kim iti dvitīyam śaṅkate nanu asaṃbaddham iti pradhāna vyāpāra viṣaya tā hi avāntara vyāpāra viṣaya tayā vyāptā sā ca atīta avasthātaḥ nivartamānā tām api nivartayati 
NVTP_1.1.4.214	 atha sa vikalpake janayitavye pūrva avasthā smaraṇam eva avāntara vyāpāraḥ na tu viṣaya sambandhaḥ tadā lakṣaṇa virodhaḥ dūṣaṇam iti arthaḥ mā bhūt iti indriya agocaraḥ indriya sannikarṣa gocaraḥ iti arthaḥ na ca iti ayam āśayaḥ na tāvat sarvathā eva atīta avasthā na indriya sannikṛṣṭaḥ saṃyukta viśeṣaṇa tāyāḥ saṃbhavāt asya api saṃyukta samavāya vat pratyakṣa jñāna utpādaka tayā sannikarṣa padena saṃgrahāt yadi api samavāya itara bhāva rūpa dharmeṣu saṃbandha antara garbhaḥ eva viśeṣaṇa viśaṣya bhāvaḥ tathā api vidyamāna dharma viṣayā eva sā vyavasthitiḥ iti na kaścid sūtra virodhaḥ iti yadi api rahasyam tathā api atīta avasthāyāḥ saṃbandha anabhyupagame api na kācid lakṣaṇa kṣatiḥ na hi yāvat pratyetavya gocaraḥ indriya sannikarṣa 
NVTP_1.1.4.215–1.1.4.216	 iti sūtram kim tarhi indriya artha sannikarṣa janitam vijñānam pratyakṣa phalam tathāvidha phala viṣayor athaḥ pratyakṣaḥ tathāvidha phala sādhanam pratyakṣam pramāṇam iti syāt etat kāryam ekam adhikṛtya indriya sannikarṣa saṃskārayoḥ paraspara sahakāritā tat eva tu ekam anayoḥ kutas iti āśayavān codayati nanu pūrva apara iti sūcī kaṭāha nyāyena paścāt uktam api prathamam vivṛṇoti tathā hi iti yadi api tat iti ullekhaḥ na sarva vikalpa vyāpī tathā api pratisandhāna jñāne tāvat asti tasya ca prāmāṇyam sthira vādibhiḥ avaṣya abhyupetavyam anyathā sarva mālūna viśīrṇam āpadyate pareṇa api tat eva viśeṣataḥ nirākartavyam 
NVTP_1.1.4.217–1.1.4.219	 tad nirākaraṇena eva hi jāti ādi abhāve apratisandhāna ātmakasya api vikalpasya pratyākhyānam ayatna siddham iti abhisandhiḥ nanu viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ api syāt na ca bhedaḥ iti atas āha trailokyasya ekatva prasaḍgāt tathā ca bheda vyavahārasya ākasmika tva prasaṅgaḥ iti arthaḥ viṣaya bhedaḥ ca iti yadi api viṣaya bhedavataḥ api sarvajña vijñānasya eka tvam akṣatam eva tathā api kṣaṇikā aneka kālīna nīla ālambana tvam ava yadi pratisandhānasya paraḥ abhyupagacchet na tasya kācid iṣṭa siddhiḥ na api asmākam idam aniṣṭam kim tu tad aparispharaṇam eva vikalpe tasmāt āropita eka tva viṣaya tvam asya pāramārthika ekatva viṣaya tvam vā tatra prathamam yadi paraḥ abhyupagacchet anukūlayet eva asmān tasmāt nānā avasthā viśiṣṭa pāramārthika eka viṣaya tayā asti eka tvam para abhiprāya gocaraḥ tat ca viṣaya bheda āpādanena eva nirasyate iti ami sandhiḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.220	 atra ucyate iti yadi api tat idam iti jñānam pūrva avasthāyām api aparokṣam eva na hi tat iti ullekhāt eva parokṣa tvam tathā sati śābdalaiḍgika vikalpānām tat iti ullekha virahiṇām aparokṣa tva prasaḍgāt na api idam āspada tvāt eva sākṣātkāraḥ iti bauddhasya abhyupagamaḥ apasiddhānta prasaḍgāt kim tu sannihita viṣayam asat nihita viṣayam vā yat eva liḍga ādi nirapekṣeṇa indriyeṇa vijñānam janyate tat eva aparokṣa rūpam samutpadyate anindriya jam tu parokṣam iti vibhāgaḥ tatra parokṣam aparokṣam vā anubhūta avasthā viśiṣṭa viṣaya tayā tat iti ullikhyate sannihita viṣaya tayā idam iti saḥ ayam viṣaya kṛtaḥ viśeṣaḥ tathā api abhyupagama vāde api na kaścid virodhaḥ iti pratibandi grahaḥ iti mantavyam tasmāt viṣaya bhedāt avirodhaḥ iti tvayā samādhātavyam iti ced nanu iha api iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.221–1.1.4.222	 tat kim idānīm vikalpa vikalpanīyayoḥ yathā bhedaḥ tathā eva tat idanta āspadayoḥ api iti nanu evam sati dattaḥ sva hastaḥ bauddhānām iti atas āha sambandha iti viśeṣaṇe uttaratra api evam viśeṣyam tu ekam eva tatra ca aparokṣa tvam eva asya iti āśayaḥ yaḥ api iti atra apinānādiś deśa sambandhaḥ pratibandīkartavyaḥ nanu pratyabhijñānāt nānā kāla sa baddha ekatva siddhau paraspara avinābhāva bhaṅga prasaṅgaḥ tat ca lūna punar jāta kadalī kāṇḍa ādau vyabhicāra darśanāt apramāṇam eva na ca kadalī kāṇḍa pratyabhijñānataḥ padmarāga pratyabhijñānasya kañcid viśeṣam upalabhāmahe nanu nānā diś deśa saṃbaddhasya api tava kadācid eka tvam upalabhyate tat katham tasya api ekatva niścayaḥ atha nānā diś deśa saṃsargaḥ sva āśrayam bhedayitvā na nivartate iti niḥsvabhāva tā vā āpādayet anaikāntikaḥ vā syāt atas na ayam viruddhaḥ siddhāḥ tarhi saṃyoga avayavi ādayaḥ tulyam ca etat kāla bhede api tathā hi yadi pūrva apara kāla saṃbandhaḥ vastuni virudhyeta vijñāne api virudhyeta tathā ca vijñānam api ekam atīta vartamāna viṣayam na syāt 
NVTP_1.1.4.223	 evam ca buddhīnām niyata artha tayā pratisandhāna gandhaḥ api na syāt tathā ca mūla abhāvāt nirīham jagat jāyeta sarvajñaḥ ca datta jala añjaliḥ prasaktaḥ atīta vartamāna viṣaya tve api na ekam jñānam atītam vartamānam ca svīkriyate iti ced atha kim idra ca vartamāna tvam sattvam sat antara saṃbandhaḥ vā evam ca atīta tvam api naṣṭa tvam naṣṭa antara saṃbandhaḥ vā tatra sa t antara naṣṭa antara saṃbandhaḥ pratisandhāne sarvajña vijñāne ca asti eva naṣṭān aṣṭa viṣaya tvāt tad aviṣaya tve 
NVTP_1.1.4.224	 pratisandhāna tva sarvajña tva anupapatteḥ sattva naṣṭa tve parasparam virudhyete te ca ekatra pratisandhāne na staḥ iti ced evam tarhi pad rāgamaṇiḥ api utpatteḥ ārabhya sva avayava vibhāga paryantam sat svarūpaḥ na asya naṣṭa tva saṃsargaḥ saḥ eva tu satā kenacid saṃsṛṣṭaḥ kenacid asatā pratisandhānam iva sat asabhdyām viṣayābhyām iti tat na asti viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ tatas parimāṇa bheda ādayaḥ viruddha dharma saṃsargāḥ vaktavyāḥ te yatra padmarāga ādau na santi tatra autsargikam eka tvam eva iti samaḥ samādhiḥ iti abhiprāyeṇa deśam antar bhāvya upasaṃharati tasmāt iti na ca anyasya saṃbandhinaḥ kālasya bhedaḥ viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ anyasya padmarāga maṇeḥ bhedam nānātvam na ca indriyā iti yadi vikalpa jātīyam pratīndriya artha sannikarṣaḥ na kāraṇam 
NVTP_1.1.4.225–1.1.4.226	 vyabhicārāt iti parasya abhiprāyaḥ tadā anujñā eva uttaram na hi vayam api vikalpa mātram prati tasya kāraṇa tvam brūmaḥ kim tu sākṣāt kāri vijñānam prati na ca asau indriya artha sannikarṣam antareṇa api bhavati iti sāram nirvikalpaka pratibandi grahaḥ tu imam artham sukhena grāhayitum syāt etat vikalpasya ubha yathā saṃbhave hi sāmānya vyabhicārāt viśeṣam ādāya kārya kāraṇa tā avadhāraṇam syāt na tu sākṣātkārādiḥ asya viśeṣaḥ asti aupādhika tvāt tasya iti āśaḍkya nirākaroti na ca vikalpa gataḥ iti vikalpa gataḥ sākṣātkāra lakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ tāvat anubhūyate iti avivādam tasya aupādhika tvam na tāvadānubhavikam iti āha sarvā 
NVTP_1.1.4.227	 eva hi ityādi tasmāt darśana vyāpārāḥ vikalpāḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa janmānaḥ iti yojanā na api aupapattikam upapatteḥ prāk eva nirākṛta tvāt iti āśayaḥ nanu indriya viṣayaḥ eva yadi śabdaḥ api pravarteta saḥ api sākṣātkāriṇam eva vikalpam ādadhyāt indriyam apica utprekṣā vyāpāriṇam viṣaya viśeṣam antareṇa jñāne viśeṣa abhāvāt tasmāt śabda eka viṣaya tayā pravartamānaḥ vikalpaḥ na indriya viśayam spṛśati tad asparśe ca na svābhāvikam asya sākṣātkāri tvam iti āśana yavān āśaḍkya nirākaroti na ca śabda iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.228–1.1.4.229	 ekatra arthe indriyam kāraṇam anyatra tad nirapekṣaḥ śabda ādiḥ iti arthaḥ tucchatayā upekṣaṇīyam api śiṣya hita tayā dūṣayati na ca vahni iti vahni jñānāt uṣṇa jñānāt iti arthaḥ śīta dravya apagamaḥ tad apagame vā tad anupalambhaḥ tad hetuka duḥkha abhāvaḥ vā śīta apanodaḥ iti ucyate sa ca uṣṇa dravya upagama sādhyaḥ na tu tad upalambha sādhyaḥ anyathā sannipāta mūḍhasya svedane api doṣa apagamaḥ na syāt uṣṇa dravya anupalambhāt tuhina acala guhā madhya vartini ca sarvajñe vaḍavānala sākṣātkāravati tuhina acala vilayaḥ syāt iti arthaḥ yasya api ityādi vārttika artham dūṣayati na ca ekena iti upādhayaḥ sattva ādayaḥ taiḥ viśiṣṭa tvam taiḥ viśeṣaṇaiḥ sambandhaḥ ayam arthaḥ ekena eva svabhāvena tāvat upakaroti sarva upādhīnām iti parama arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.230^1	 tatra upakārakasya eka svabhāva tayā upakārāṇām avacchedānām upakāryāṇām ca upādhīnām tadā ekatvam syāt yadi upakāra svabhāva antarbhūta tvam teṣām abhyupeyeta na ca evam ātiṣṭhāmahe tvayā api evam eva samarthanīyam kim tu alīka viṣaya tayā iti viśeṣaḥ saḥ eṣa nyāyaḥ yadi parama artha sati api syāt kīdṛśaḥ doṣaḥ na kevalam kālpanike vyavahāre tava idam samarthanam api tu pāramārthike api iti āha api ca iti paramāṇu svabhāvaḥ iti ṣaṣṭha tatpuruṣaḥ paramāṇavaḥ jñānasya svabhāvaḥ iti api draṣṭavyam paramāṇu svabhāva tve jñānasya api nānātva prasaḍgāt 
NVTP_1.1.4.230^2	 tathā ca ekeka paramāṇu niyame sthūla pratibhāsaḥ bhrāntaḥ api na syāt jñāna svabhāva tve api ca paramāṇunām api ekatva prasaḍgāt amūrta tva ādi prasaḍgāt ca iti saḥ eva doṣaḥ ityādi uttānam dūṣaṇam utsṛjya anyam āha teṣām sarvān prati iti paramāṇūnām eka jñāna svabhāva tve vā na te dvitīyena viditā syuḥ iti api draṣṭavyam yadi api tādātmya abhāve api jñāna jñeyayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ saṃbandhaḥ viṣaya viṣayi niyama artham bauddhena svīkṛtaḥ tathā api kārya kāraṇa bhāve api kaḥ niyantā iti tulyaḥ anuyogaḥ atas svabhāvena eva uttarayati svabhāvaḥ eva iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.231	 bhāva abhāvayoḥ samavāya tadvatoḥ viṣaya viṣayiṇoḥ ca vayam api svabhāvena eva paraspara upahitam sambandham ātiṣṭhāmahe dravya guṇa karma jāti tadvatām yadi api svabhāvena eva upādhi upādhim abhdāvaḥ tathā api sambandhaḥ api anubhūyamānaḥ vinā bādhakam na upekṣitum yujyate yathā sva bhāvike viṣaya viṣayībhāve kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tvayā na upekṣitaḥ tasmāt atirikta sambandhe kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhanam bādhakam avaśiṣyate iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.232–1.1.4.233	 na tāvat viśiṣṭa vyavahāraḥ eva na asti tasya spaṣṭa tayā nihnotum aśakyatvāt tad abhāve sarva vyavahāra abhāva prasaḍgāt ca tasmāt asmad ukta prakāra īrṣyayā prakāra antareṇa ayam upapādanīyaḥ tatra āha bhinna jñāna agocara tve api iti api śabchaḥ codya ābhāsa tulya tā mātreṇa nanu asti vyavahāraḥ na tu vāstavaḥ sa ca yathā kathañcit vāsanā dvāreṇa api nirvahet yeṣām tu ayam vāstavaḥ taiḥ artha dvārā eva asya nirvāhaḥ cintanīyaḥ inyāśaṅkate tābhayām iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.234	 tvad uktam eva vāsanā dvāram upādāya yā iti vāstavaḥ eva ayam vyavahāraḥ syāt tadā kīdṛśaḥ doṣaḥ iti āśayavān āha astu tāvat iti tathā api vāstavaḥ eva ayam iti atra kim pramāṇam iti atas āha tathā sati iti asya indriya artha sannikarṣa ja tve svābhāvikam sākṣātkāri tvam eva pramāṇam iti arthaḥ nirvikalpa kopadhānam kalpeta vinā pramāṇam iti śeṣaḥ yadi hi sva kāraṇa balena na utpatteḥ avicāraka tvam mānasasya api avicāraka tva prasaṅga 
NVTP_1.1.4.235	 iti āśa yavānāḥ hantā iti manasaḥ sarva viṣaya tvam na tāvat vyāpāra anubandhi tayā parasya vivakṣitam indriya artha sannikarṣasya api saṃskāra sahitasya tathā abhāva vyavasthāpanāt tasmāt pratipatti anubandhi tayā vā syāt sarva vāsanā ādhāra tayā vā ādyam dūṣayati yadi pūrvakam iti asmākam tu manaḥ sarva viṣayakam api na pratipatti anubandhi tayā asarva viṣayam apratipatti rūpa tvāt iti bhāvaḥ na ca sakala saṃskāra ādhāratayā iti āha acetana tayā na vicārakam iti vicāra aupayika sakala vāsanā anādhāra tvāt iti arthaḥ tvad abhipretasya ca manasaḥ sakala vāsanā dhāraka tvam niṣetsyate iti anena abhiprāyeṇa āha tasmāt ātmā eva iti sthitam jñānam jñāna vāsanā iti arthaḥ atra hetuḥ sa hi bauddha iti atra 
NVTP_1.1.4.236–1.1.4.237	 pramāṇam gamyate iti atas smaraṇe asya sāmarthyam caḥ hetau nanu yadi evaṃbhūta cetanā adhiṣṭhitam indriyam tarhi nirvikalpaka utpatti kāle eva labdha saskāra saciva tayā vikalpam eva janayet iti atas āha sa khalu iti prāc ālocyaḥ udbuddha saṃskāra samupajāta smṛti sahāyaḥ paścāt vikalpayati iti yojanā evam tarhi indriya artha sannikarṣāt ālocanam saṃskāra udbodhaḥ tatas smṛtiḥ tad sahāyaḥ ca vikalpayati iti na cakṣuṣaḥ kaścid upayogaḥ iti atas āha cakṣuṣā iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.238	 nanu evaṃbhūtā sāmagrī militā api yadi cakṣuḥ vyāpāra virahe na vikalpikām dhiyam upajanayet tatas tasya api kāraṇa tvam kalpyeta na tu etat asti iti atas āha gauḥ ayam iti etena sākṣātkāram prati tasya anvaya vyātiḥ ekau staḥ iti darśitam etat eva abhipretya uttaraślokam āha yathā aha iti saha cetanayā vartate iti sa cetanaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.239	 tathā api kaḥ upakāraḥ samarthitaḥ iti atas āha tena iti jñāpyajñāpaka bhāvaḥ iti upalakṣaṇam kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ api na sarvatra asti iti draṣṭavyam kvacid tu dravya guṇa karmaṇām asti iti na udāhṛtaḥ tad artha ālocana anugatam smaraṇam yayoḥ te viśeṣaṇa viśeṣye tathā ukte tayoḥ atad adhi karaṇa vyavaccheda pratīti jananam eva viśeṣaṇena viśeṣyasya upakāraḥ iti arthaḥ yadi api svābhāvikaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ na upakāram apekṣate iti tatra tatra vakṣyati na ca upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ api upakāra antara prāptaḥ tathā satya navasthāpātāt tathā api iha saṃbhava prācuryeṇa abhidhīyate iti mantavyam 
NVTP_1.1.4.240	 nanu yadi svābhāvikam anayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tvam prathamatas svabhāve gṛhyamāṇe kim na gṛhītam na ca svabhāvaḥ tadānīm na gṛhītaḥ iti atas āha arthau hi iti na khalu rūpa paramāṇuṣu sparśa ādi paramāṇavaḥ api svabhāvataḥ sthitāḥ iti etāvatā eva pratīti patham avataranti sāmagrya bhāvāt na tathā iti ced saḥ iha api samānaḥ iti arthaḥ atas eva pramāṇam kṛtsna vṛtti iti matvā yat āpāditam tat api na asti iti atas āha tena iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.241	 sva rūpa abhiprāyeṇa kṛtsna vṛtti tvam pramāṇasya anumanyāmahe eva svābhāvika samasta sambandha abhiprāyeṇa tu sarvajñetara dhiyāma prāmāṇyam āpādayati iti upasaṃhāram sthāne saṃkalayya ahai sa vikalpakam tu iti paścāt api jāyamānam iti yojanāḥ ālocanāt iti śeṣaḥ tasmāt sarvam tulyam kṣaṇa bhaḍge param vivādaḥ avaśiṣyate iti āśayavān āha akramasya api iti vivāda adhyāsitāḥ iti sākṣātkāriṇaḥ iti arthaḥ tena tad itara vyudāsaḥ sidva sādhya tā vyudāsā artham sva gocaraḥ iti pītaḥ śaḍkhaḥ ityādinā vyabhicāra nivṛtti artham avyabhicāri tve sati iti atra ca kṛtaḥ prayatnaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.242–1.1.4.243	 na ca etat mantavyam iti bhāṣyam iti indriya artha sannikarṣam antareṇa api saṃśaya utpatti darśanāt atad kāraṇa tayā prasaṅgaḥ eva asya na asti kutas anvācīyamāne api vyudāsaḥ iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yadi api na savaḥ saṃśayaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa jaḥ tathā api sākṣātkāravān avaśya tat janyaḥ tasmāt vyudāsaḥ anvācīyate iti prakāraṇa arthaḥ syāt etat ityādi manaḥ eva kevalam indraya nirapekṣam bahis vyāpriyamāṇam sākṣātkāri saṃśaya ādi janayati dṛṣṭaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.244	 hi asya anuvyavasīyamāna jñāna viśeṣaṇe ghaṭa dau vyāpāraḥ indriya vyāpāra vigame api saudāminī saṃpāta ādau sakṛt upajātasya artha niścayasya samandhakāre api anuvyavasīyamāna tvāt tasya ca anuvyavasāyasya sākṣāt kāri jātīya tvāt tasmāt aprasaṅgaḥ eva punar āpatitaḥ iti manasā hi anuvyavasīyamāna jñāna lakṣaṇa viśeṣya sannikṛṣṭena asannikṛśṭaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ avacchedaka tayā vyavasīyate cakṣuṣā iva ghaṭa sannikṛṣṭena prāk upalabdhā tad avasthā saṃśaya jñānam tu na ūrdhva artha upalabdhi viṣayam na api sthāṇu puruṣa smṛti viṣayam kim tu anirdhārita sthāṇu puruṣa tva ūrdhva padārtha viṣayam na ca tat sannikṛṣṭam manaḥ bāhyena viśeṣyeṇa api asannikṛṣṭam manaḥ katham iva jñānam utpādayet utpādane 
NVTP_1.1.4.245–1.1.4.246	 vā andha badhira ādeḥ api utpādayet iti siddhāntaḥ tat pūrvam vyavasāya utpattau sva viṣaya prāpti sampattayaḥ iti śeṣaḥ tathā ca saṃśaya jñāna utpāde api iti sahakāritayā iti śeṣaḥ avyāpaka tvena ityādi codayati pārśva sthaḥ pariharati pūrva pakṣī punar pārśva sthasya śaḍkāḥ mā bhūt iti atas āha iti pūrva pakṣī na ca sukha ādau pramāṇa antaram asti pratyakṣam vihāya iti śeṣaḥ saṃvedana tve hi teṣām sva saṃvedana tā śaḍkā āspadam api syāt iti śeṣaḥ nanu indriyasya vai sataḥ iti vadataḥ bhāṣya kṛtaḥ manasaḥ indriya tvam iṣṭam eva iti atas āha na ca tat iti manasaḥ indriya tva abhyupagamaḥ vātsyāyanīye gautamīya sūtra viruddhaḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.247^1	 mā bhūt vibhāga param idam sūtram tathā api sūtra ākārasya manaḥ indriyam yadi abhimatam indriya prakaraṇaḥ eva lakṣayet iti atas āha tatra ca iti indriya tvena tad prakaraṇaḥ eva abhighāne prāpte yat anyatra karoti tena adhikam asya kiñcid rūpam vijñeyam iti sūcayati na tu indriya tvam eva na sahate iti arthaḥ darśayiṣyati hi vātikakāraḥ iti āgāmikā phakkikā bhrama nirāsa artham bhūta abhūta iti śabdaḥ atra duṣṭaḥ na tu abhiprāyaḥ iti upalakṣaṇam ca etat
