NVTP_1.1.4.247^2	 sa guṇānām cakṣuḥ ādīnām indriya bhāvaḥ manaḥ tu na sa guṇam indrayam iti atra api yaḥ viśeṣa guṇaḥ yena indriyeṇa gṛhyate tad jātīyena guṇena saha vṛttiḥ sa guṇa tvam grāhya viśeṣa guṇa jātīya virahaḥ ca manasaḥ iti yadi abhipretam bhāṣya kṛtā tadā etat api vaidharmyam eva kim tu ebhiḥ akṣaraiḥ etat api abhidhātum na śakyate vibhakti vipariṇāmena tu bhāṣyam sugamam tathā hi indriya bhūtānām eṣām sa guṇa tvam grāhyaiḥ guṇaiḥ saha saṃbandhaḥ cakṣuḥ ādīnām manasaḥ tu indriya mūtasya eva na sa guṇa tvam na grāhyena guṇena saha saṃbandhaḥ iti tasmāt atra api śabda doṣaḥ na tu abhri pāya doṣaḥ iti mantavyam 
NVTP_1.1.4.248–1.1.4.250	 nanu anabhimata niṣedhena mata sunneṣyate iti śaṅkate na ca iti nirācaṣṭe abhāvasya iti yāvat anabhimata niṣedhena abhimata lābhe garīyaḥ gauravam āpadyeta tat tad niṣedhyam anupanīya niṣedhasya pratipādayitum aśakyatvāt viśeṣa vidhau tu śeṣa niṣedhaḥ laghīyān iti bhāvaḥ satra ākāra vacanasya vivāda āspada tvāt katham tena eva nirṇayaḥ iti atas āha iti pūrayati bhāṣya kāraḥ iti śābda iti anena śabda indriya samāhāra jam ayam asau= aśvaḥ iti jñānam vyavacchedyam abhimatam vārttika kṛtaḥ iti keṣāñcit matam apanayati na khalu iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.251	 vācya tvena hi viśeṣaṇa tayā gṛhītena niśeṣya niṣṭhena bhavitu ayam atas kevala vācya tva prastāve api tathā eva udāhṛtam indriya vyatireka vyabhicārāt ca tad vyatirekaḥ na śaḍkitaḥ gṛhīte hi aśva tve tat asannikarṣe api yaḥ ayam piṇḍaḥ tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ ayam asau= aśvaḥ iti upadeśāt kevalāt eva vācya tva pratīti darśanāt nasmāt indriyasya saṃbandhi samarpaṇaḥ eva vyāpāraḥ evam uttaratra api tavya arthaḥ saḍketayituḥ abhiprāya viśeṣaḥ yadi api para abhiprāyaḥ tad upahitaḥ vā arthaḥ na indriya gocaraḥ tathā api abhyupagamya aśaṅkate atha ayam api iti idam aindriyakam idam atīndriyam iti hi sākṣātkāra asa akṣāt kāra unneyaḥ ayam arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.252–1.1.4.253	 tatra spaṣṭa grahaṇa rūpa tvāt sākṣātkāra apara vyapadeśāt aindriyakam etat iti yuktam syāt na tu asā akṣātkārāt api tayoḥ ca kaḥ atra manasā vedyate iti bhavān eva paribhāvayatu tatra sākṣātkāri tva pakṣe pratyakṣam eva idam atas na vyavacchedanīyam asākṣāt kāri tva pakṣe ca na idam aindriyakam iti prathama padena iva vyudastam na avi apadeśya padasya avakāśaḥ iti gāthā pāṭhasya arthaḥ kimartham tarhi avyavadeśya padam kaḥ ca asya vārttikasya arthaḥ iti atas āha vyavasāya ātmaka padena tu iti eka pada parigraham sphuṭam manvānaḥ api dvipada parigraham vyācaṣṭa dvipadā iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.254	 uttara prabandha upayogam darśayan= āha tat evam iti lakṣaṇam idam anumānam tat ca tad ābhāsāt vivekena sugamam bhavati sa ca tad ābhāseṣu āviṣkṛteṣu bhavati iti āśayavataḥ ayam ārambhaḥ iti arthaḥ tator athāt iti atra hi pañcamyā hetu tvam arthasya vijñānam pratidarśitam tad paraḥ ca eva kāraḥ evam saṃbadhyate sa vyapadeśa kor atho hetuḥ eva yasya na punar ahetuḥ api tat vijñānam pratyakṣam iti evam ca ayoga vyavacchedaḥ eva tathā api anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ api vārttika kṛtā nirākartavyaḥ iti vyākhyāyām ubhayam darśitavān yadi tatas eva tabhdavati na artha antara āditya vyapadeśa kāt iti ataḥ na virodhaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.255–1.1.4.257	 nanu anumāna viśeṣaḥ tāvat kaścid avyapadeśakāt eva utpadyate tatas na tasya vyudāsaḥ kṛtaḥ iti atas āha tator athāt iti atra hi iti pratyakṣa jāteḥ idam lakṣaṇam tasyāḥ ca pratiyogini anumāna ādi jātiḥ eva tathā ca tasyāḥ eva jāteḥ vyavacchedaḥ vivakṣitaḥ sa ca etāvatā eva siddhaḥ iti arthaḥ yatra eva yat jātīyaḥ eva tad ayogaḥ tasya vyapadeśakasya hetu tvena ayogaḥ tat apratyakṣam iti tena vyapadeśaḥ hi tad upādhikam nirūpaṇami vivakṣitam na ca jñānam kartrā karaṇena vā nirūpyate api tu karmaṇā eva iti arthaḥ abhidhāna aparyavasānāt śabda vyāpāra aparyavasānāt tad śabdasya pūrva prakrāntaḥ eva arthe saḍketita tvāt tad anabhidhāne avācaka tva prasaḍgāt iti bhāvaḥ pūrva prakrāntaḥ ca vyapadeśakaḥ eva sa ca arthaḥ eva iti viśeṣyaḥ prāpyate na antarīyaka tvāt iti arthaḥ na evam vārttikam iti atas āha abhyupetya tu iti anumāna ādi vyudāsa artham hi ayoga vyavacchedaḥ sa 
NVTP_1.1.4.258–1.1.4.259	 ca anya yoga vyavacchede api sidhyati iti arthaḥ nanu anyoga vyavacchedaḥ aśakyaḥ eva indriya ādeḥ avyapadeśakasya api tad kāraṇa tvāt atas āha anya vyavacchede api iti indriya ādayaḥ hi avyapadeśakāḥ api vyapadeśaka ādhipatyena eva jñāna janakāḥ iti avirodhi tayā na te vyavacchedyāḥ liḍgādayaḥ tu vyapadeśaka ādhipatyanirapekṣa tayā tad virodhinaḥ iti te eva anye vyavacchettavyāḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.260	 nanu sarvam ca sva viṣayāt iti vārtti kam asaṅgatam eva smṛti anumiti bhrāntīnām sva viṣaya apanutpatteḥ atas āha yad saṃvṛti tvena iti nanu bhrānti jñānam api na vyapadeśakam antareṇa bhavati tat kutas ca udyamatasmāt api iti atas āha purovarti iti atasmāt api iti atra yadi api na śrūyate tathā api vyapadeśakāt api na bhavati iti boddhavyam iti arthaḥ tat idam uktam yena viśeṣa rūpeṇa tasya vyapadiśyate na tatas tabhdavati iti tasmāt yat tatas eva bhavati tatas bhavati eva iti arthaḥ atataḥ ca na tatas ca iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.261	 nanu vyapadeśakāt anutpatteḥ iti avyapadeśakāt utpatteḥ iti vā codyam upakrābhya aśakte rajatāt na utpadyate iti vāc chala mātrām iti atas āha na hi atasmāt āropitāt rūpāt iti ayam arthaḥ mithyājñāna nirāsaḥ hi anya yoga vyavacchedena vā ayoga vyavacchedena vā na tāvat ādyaḥ anya yoga vyavacchedasya tatra api bhāvāt tadā hi sa na syāt yadi avyapadeśakasya eva vaṇij vīthyām svatantrasya rajatasya hetu tvam syāt na ca etat asti tat idam uktam na hi atasmāt āropitāt tatra asataḥ tad mithyā jñānam bhavati na api dvitīyaḥ vyapadeśakasya hetu tvāt eva rajatam vyapadeśakam na hetuḥ iti ced katham punā rajatam vyapadeśakam svātantryeṇa purovarti ātmanā vā na tāvat ādyaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.262	 sāmānādhikaraṇya anupapatteḥ sva mithyā tva prasaḍgāt ca puras varti ātmanā ca pratyantare tat bhavati vyapadeśakam sa ca purovarti ātmā hetuḥ eva iti ayoga vyavacchedaḥ eva tat idamukam āropitam tu rajatam asya viṣayaḥ dṛśyamāna ākāratayā iti ayam tu abhiprāyaḥ syāt yādṛśa ākāreṇa vyapadeśa kor athaḥ tādṛśāt utpannam jñānam pratyakṣam iti na tu ayam lakṣaṇa padānām arthaḥ na ca abhiprāya viśuddhi mātreṇa paraḥ pratipādayitum śakyate pratyabhijñāsu asaṃvedanā vyāpaka tvāt ca etat ca jaiminīye sphuṭībhaviṣyati 
NVTP_1.1.4.263	 tat etat lakṣaṇam ābhiprāyikam api asmat naye kadācid saṃbhāvyeta tvad nate tu viruddham asiddham ca id am uktam vārttika kṛtā tat etat vyutpādayati yadi api etat iti vyapadeśakaḥ hi arthaḥ vartamāna tayā sarvatra pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ sa ced hetuḥ eva evam atītaḥ syāt tathā ca pratyakṣa tve sādhye apratyakṣa tvam eva sidhyati iti bhavati viruddha tvam iti arthaḥ atha vartamānaḥ eva vyapadeśakaḥ tadā samāna kāla tayā tator atha āditya siddham āha tad samānā iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.264–1.1.4.266	 yat tu kenacid pralapitam aparokṣa jñāna avabhāsitā eva vartamāna tā iti tat tuccham iti upekṣitavān tathā hi aparokṣa eka sarvajña vijñāna avabhāsitayā sarveṣām arthānām eka kāla tvāt savya itara go viṣāṇa vat kārya kāraṇa bhāva vārtā eva ucchidyeta pūrva uktaḥ ca anuyogaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti bhinna kālam katham grāhyam ityādinā kārya kāraṇa bhāva viśeṣaḥ eva grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ sa ca bhinna kālayoḥ eva bhavati iti sva bhāṣayā samarthitam pareṇa na ca vayam bhinna kālayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva viśeṣam avajānīmahe kim tu atītasya vartamāna tayā avabhāsanam tasya vā satya tvam na ca tat anena samarthitam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.267	 nanu jñāna ākāra arpaṇa kṣamam iti vadatā eva samarthitam etat anene hi na pratibhāsamāna tayā arthaḥ grāhyaḥ iti vyavahniyate kim nāma ākāra arpakatayā iti darśitam ākāraḥ eva tu avabhāsamamāna tayā grāhyaḥ sa ca jñāna ātma bhūta tayā vartamānaḥ eva iti na kaścid virodhaḥ iti atas āha anahaḍkāra iti vijñānāt bhinnasya nīla ādeḥ anubhavaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.4.268–1.1.4.271	 yadi satyaḥ na jñāna gata ākāra vedanam asatyaḥ ced na prata yakṣam pramāṇam iti sā iyam ubhayatas pāśāḥ rajjuḥ iti arthaḥ api ca bhavatu ākāra vedanam bhavatu vā arthasya ākāra arpaka tvam vā tathā api tator athādvijñānam pratyakṣam iti asiddham lakṣaṇam tathā hi pratibhāsamānasya eva jñānam vyapadiśyate na tu apratibhāsamānasya ākāraḥ ca pratibhāsane na tu janakaḥ api arthaḥ tasmāt vyapadeśa kona janakaḥ janakaḥ ca na vyapadeśakaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.272–1.1.4.273	 atra śaṅkate na ca iti pratibhā samāna ākāra dvāra arthaḥ vyapadeśakaḥ janakaḥ ca iti api na ca iti arthaḥ kutas bhākta tva prasaḍgāt kim atas yadi evam iti atas āha na ca gauṇa mukhya iti yathā hi avinā abhāvam antar bhāvya eva gaḍgā śabdaḥ tīre lakṣyamāṇa guṇa yogam antar bhāvya siha śabdaḥ māṇavake vartate na tathā dhūma pratyakṣam agnau siṃha pratyakṣam māṇavake pramāṇa antara uccheda prasaḍgāt iti arthaḥ tat idam uktam bhinna prasthāna tvāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.274	 etena etat api nirastam yat āhuḥ pratyakṣa siddhena ākāreṇa arthaḥ anumīyate iti phalatas pratyakṣoḥ atha iti anumīyate iti kor athaḥ anumitau parisphurati iti tat ca bauddha naye svapne api durlabham anumiteḥ api svākāra alīkayoḥ eva anyatarasmin paryavasita tvāt yaḥ ca sarvathā eva jñāna agocaraḥ sa vyavahniyate iti kutas tasmāt ākāra vāda pakṣebāhyor atho heyaḥ tad abhyupagame vā ākāra vādaḥ iti anena abhiprāyeṇa āha tasmāt nirākāram iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.275	 śaṅkataḥ iti na hi kiñcid vastu bhūtam vācyam nāma saugatānām samasti lakṣaṇa vākyena tu vyavahāra mātram prasādhyate sa ca atad vyāvṛtti niṣṭhaḥ iti arthaḥ jñānasya kalpanā apoḍhasya pratyakṣa tayā vyutpādyamānasya katham sarver athā pratyakṣa tayā prasajyerat nityatas āha na hi iti dignāgasya ati vyāpaka tayā alakṣaṇam kīrteḥ tu avyāpaka tayā vikalpa pratyakṣa an avarodhāt tasya ca pratyakṣa tayā vyutpādanāt aniṣṭa mātrasya ati prasañjaka tvāt iti siddhāntaḥ sva darśana samādhitsayā vārttikam iti darśayitum codayati nanu yadi iti sāmānya anvitam abhidhīyate iti vārttika śeṣaḥ manuṣya tva jātimān iti arthaḥ iti manuṣya śabdasya brāhmaṇaḥ brāhmaṇa tva ādi jāti mat tayā avācyaḥ api manuṣya tva jāti mat tayā vācyaḥ eva iti arthaḥ paunaruktyam pariharan= āha atha aścakarṇa iti 
NVTP_1.1.4.276	 nanu vyatyaye api sat saṃprayogaḥ iti syāt na tu tad tad śabdasya prakṛta tayā viṣayaḥ kaścid asti iti āha buddhyā iti yadi api pratyakṣa jñānam api anena lakṣaṇena sva ātmani pratyakṣam na syāt eva tathā api indriya artha sannikarṣa janya tva mātram tāvat tatra api asti iti kadācid paraḥ brūyāt iti atas āha anumāna ādi iti etena tator atha ādityasya abhiprāya śeṣaḥ dūṣitaḥ pratyabhijñāna sva saṃvedanayoḥ avyāpaka tvāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.1–1.1.5.3^1	 atha tad pūrvakam trividham anumānam pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ca sūtram paṭhati vyākhyātum iti śeṣaḥ sūtra avatāra mātram asahamānam pratyāha atra iti sādharmyeṇa hi niyamavatā iti śeṣaḥ upalakṣaṇam ca etat vaidharmyeṇa iti api draṣṭavyam aprāmāṇya vidhānam prāmāṇya niṣedhaḥ eva na apratyakṣam pramāṇam iti anena hi viśeṣa niṣedhena kaṇṭhataḥ anumāna prāmāṇya niṣedhoḥ athatas pratyakṣa prāmāṇya vidhiḥ ca vivakṣitaḥ na ca etat ubhayam api pramāṇam antareṇa sidhyati na ca atra pratyakṣam eva prabhavati iti cintitam ādi vākye na api śabda upamāne sva pratyaye tayoḥ anavakāśāt para pratyaye api dharmya siddheḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.1–1.1.5.3^2	 siddhau= api parasya āptatva aniḥ cayāt tasmāt atīndriya vidhi niṣedhayoḥ anumānam anaḍgīkṛtya aśakya tvāt aśakyā apahnavam anumānam iti arthaḥ dṛṣṭa sādharmyam ca niyatam iti śeṣaḥ katham tena eva tasya aprāmāṇyam iti vyāghāta mātram vivakṣitam tena ayam arthaḥ yadi anu mānam apramāṇam katham tena eva vidhi niṣedha siddhiḥ atha tena vidhi niṣedha siddhiḥ katham tasya aprāmāṇyam iti kim ca anumānam anaḍgīkṛtya para pratyāyanāya śabda prayogaḥ api ayam aśakyaḥ para vedana pratipatteḥ ava tad antareṇa aśakya tvāt na ced para pratyāyanam nūnam aunmattyam āviṣkaroti vaktuḥ iti āha api ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.4–1.1.5.5	 sūtre vibhāgaḥ api asti iti vyavacchidya āha lakṣaṇa sūtra tātparyamāhā iti syāt etat ativyāpakam iti atra avyāpakam ca iti api draṣṭavyam atas ubhaya vyutpādana upasaṃhāra virodhaḥ vigraha traya pradarśanam vigraha trayam draṣṭavyam iti arthaḥ vyāpti smṛti sahāyāt dvitīya liṅga darśanāt eva anumiti siddheḥ alam tṛtīya liṅga darśana kalpanayā iti yathā śruta bhāṣya anusāriṇaḥ tān risyati na ca iti saḥ eṣa saṃskāra udbodham adhikam abhyupagacchataḥ doṣaḥ uktaḥ yaḥ tu sahakāri lābhāt anyaḥ na kaścid udbodhaḥ nāma iti manyate tam pratyāha vinaśyat avasthasya iti na hi vyāpti smaraṇa mātrāt anumitiḥ na api liṅga darśana mātrāt kim tarhi 
NVTP_1.1.5.6–1.1.5.7	 vyāpti viśiṣṭa liṅga darśanāt na ca vyāpti viśiṣṭam liṅgam ekaikasya ubhayasya vā gocaraḥ kim tu svatantram ubhayam ubhayasya na ca svatantra ubhaya jñāne api viśiṣṭa jñānam bhavati tat idam uktam paraspara vārtā anabhijña tayā svatantra sva sva viṣaya paryavasita tayā mithas ghaṭanā yogaḥ viśiṣṭa pratyaya yogaḥ iti arthaḥ na ca svatantram etat ubhayam eka ātma samavāya mātreṇa anum iti bhāvayiṣyati iti vācyam dvitīya liṅga darśanam hi vasatu gatyā liṅga viṣayam iti etāvatā eva vyāpti smṛteḥ saha kāri liṅga tva rūpa ullekhitayā vā na tāvat ādyaḥ dūrāt dhūma viṣaya vastu tva jñānasya api prakāra antara āyāta vyāpti smṛtim prati sahakāri tva prasaḍgāt dvitīyaḥ tu dvitīya liṅga darśane na asti eva tat idam uktam vṛttyā salvayam ghaṭayet vyāpāreṇa na rūpataḥ na ubhaya samavāyitā mātreṇa atiprasaḍgāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.8	 tasmāt liṅga tva ullekhi tṛtīyam liṅga darśanam āstheyam itti āha tasmāt iti iha tādātmya tad utpatti svarūpa ādi niścaye pratibandha niścayaḥ tadā na syāt yadi te eva pratibandhaḥ tābhyām samāna upāyaḥ vā pratibandhaḥ tayoḥ eva vā pratibandha paryavasānam te eva vā pratibandha niścaya upāyaḥ tatra upāya tvam sahacāra avasāye vā vyabhicāra śaḍkā nirāse vā vyabhicāra śaḍkā api upādhi darśanāt vā upādhi śaṅkayā vā bhūyas bhūyas sahacaritayoḥ api ulabdhayoḥ kayoḥ cidarthayoḥ vyabhicāra anusandhāna mātreṇa vā iti tatra ca sahacāra avasāyaḥ tāvat indriya sannikarṣa adhīna utpattiḥ tad utpatti aniścaye api vahni dhūmayoḥ sidhyati vyabhicāra śaḍkā api darśana yogya upādhi adhīnā yogyā anupalambha bādhāt eva nirastāḥ atīndriyāḥ tu upādhayaḥ anyatra pramāṇa paridṛṣṭāḥ śaḍkitāḥ api yathā nivartante tathā vakṣyāmaḥ pramāṇa patha anavatīrṇa upādhi śaḍkā tu tad utpatti niścayam api āskandati iti katham sā 
NVTP_1.1.5.9	 tena nivartanīya iti āha atra ucyate iti sahacaritayoḥ vyabhicāra darśana mātreṇa tu vyabhicāra śaḍkā kārya kāraṇayoḥ api samānāḥ tad utpatti lakṣaṇa viśeṣa siddhau vipakṣe bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā śaḍgāni vṛttiḥ iti yadi tadā asmākam api svābhāvika saṃbandha siddhau vipakṣe bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā eva śaḍkā nivṛttiḥ iti samaḥ samādhiḥ viśeṣaḥ tu svābhāvika saṃbandhasya vyāpaka tvam avyāpaka tvam tu tad utpatti ādeḥ iti āha api ca iti tat idam uktam sa ca yaḥ vā sa vā iti na ca samāna upāya tvāt ubhayoḥ anyatarā niścaye na anyatara niścayaḥ iti sāmpratam pratibandhā niścaye api hutāśa bhasmanoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva avadhāraṇāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvā niścaye api dhāma dhūmayoḥ pratibandha avabodhāt yat anatītam eva vahnim anumimataḥ iti āha api ca kāryāt iti tayoḥ eva pratibandhaḥ paryavasyati iti pakṣam nirācaṣṭe api ca rasāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.10	 yat tu bhede sati vyāpya vyāpaka abhāvaḥ eva kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti vyudapādi prajñā kareṇa tat pāpāt api pāpīyaḥ tathā hi niyāmaka virahe bhinnāyoḥ avyabhicāraḥ śaṣ kāka laḍka aḍkita tvāt duravadhāraṇaḥ iti tām apanetum kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ anena upanītaḥ sa ced rūpaḥ eva katham tat niścayena eva avyabhicāra niścayaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.11	 na ca etat kīrteḥ anumatam yat rasena rūpa anumāne anyathā abhyupāyam āha yadi ca sarva loka siddham ativāhya svayaṅkṛta lakṣaṇaiḥ vyavahāraḥ tadā bhede satī iti etat api parihīyatām avyabhicāra mātram tad utpattiḥ iti eva astu laghu ca evam sati lakṣaṇam syāt tad ā ātmanaḥ api etat asti iti ced astu śiśapā api vṛkṣa kāryam katham tena eva tat kartavyam iti ced kaḥ doṣaḥ asiddham siddhena sādhyate na tu tat eva siddham asiddham ca iti ced hanta evam anāgatam api katham vyāpaka tā mātreṇa kāraṇam asiddha tvāt vartamānam api katham vyāpya tā mātreṇa kāryam siddha tvāt evam samāna kāle api katham avinā abhāva mātreṇa kārya kāraṇa bhūte asiddha avasthāyām ubhayoḥ api asādhaka tva aviśeṣāt siddha avasthāyām ubhayoḥ api asādhya tva aviśeṣāt tasmāt pūrva kāla bhāva niyamaḥ kāraṇa tvam kaścāt bhāvita aniyamaḥ kāryatvam avinābhauvaḥ tu niyama mātram iti eva jyāyaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.12	 api ca rasa rūpayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva niścayaḥ vahni dhūmayoḥ iva pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhyaḥ vā syāt kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhau puñjāt puñja antara utpāttiḥ iti nyāyena vā ādyaḥ tāvat kṣaṇayoḥ aśakyaḥ eva tayoḥ eva pratyakṣān ārohāt tatra tasya aniścāyaka tvāt santānayoḥ api duravabodhaḥ na hi vahneḥ iva rūpasya pūrva kālatā niyamam dhūmasya iva rasasya praścāt bhāvitā niyamam laukikāḥ pratipadyante kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhi nyāyaḥ tu na laukikaḥ iti vastutas laukikānām rasataḥ rūpa anumānam na syāt iti āha laukikānām ca idam iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.13–1.1.5.14	 api ca iti anena te eva pratibandhaḥ iti nirastam tādātmyam tu gamya gamaka bhāve pratyuta viruddham iti āha api ca iti na hi tat eva karma niśceyam kartṛ ca sva niścayena niścāyakam ca niścitā niścitayoḥ paraspara virodhāt iti arthaḥ bhavatu abhede api gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ tathā api na śiśapā tvena vṛkṣatva anumānam anavasara dusthātvāt na hi asti saṃbhavaḥ sāmānyam aniścitam niścitaḥ tu viśeṣaḥ iti āśaḍkya kenacid samarthitam utthāpya dūṣayati yatu iti bhinnayoḥ eva vyāvṛttyoḥ gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ kim tu abhinna adhyavaseya saṃbandhāt tayoḥ api tādātmyam vyavahniyate iti sa yadi abhinna deva datta saṃbandhāt chatra kuṇḍalayoḥ api abhedam vyavaharati kaḥ vārayitā kevalam pramāṇa prayojanayoḥ vyāvṛttiḥ laukika virodhaḥ ca iti anena abhiprāyeṇa upasaṃharati tasmāt itas asya idam kāryam kāraṇam iti ekaḥ saṃbandhaḥ svābhāvikam saṃbandham upasaṃhṛtya tasya svarūpam āha tathā hi iti svābhāvikaḥ nirūpa ādhiḥ iti arthaḥ yadi api vyabhicāra avi abhicāra vyāpte aupādhika tvān aupādhika tve tābhyām ca 
NVTP_1.1.5.15	 vyabhicāra avi abhicārau= iti niyamaḥ tau hi na tāvat nirnimittau sārvatrika tva prasaḍgāt niyata viṣayau ca upalabhyete na api animittau sa upādheḥ api avyabhicāre nirūpa ādheḥ api vyabhicāre aniyama prasaḍgāt  tathā sati kārya ātmanoḥ api kāraṇa ātma vyabhicāraḥ prasajyeta tasmāt upādhau= avaśyam vyabhicāraḥ anupādhau avaśyam avyabhicāraḥ vyabhicāre avaśyam upādhiḥ avyabhicāre avaśyam upādhi abhāvaḥ tathā api yatra sphuṭaḥ vyabhicāraḥ tatra niṣphalam upādhi anusaraṇam tad artha tvāt tasya asphuṭe tu vyabhicāre tasya upayogaḥ na tu upādhi ta damau= asiddhaye vyabhicāra avi abhicāra paryeṣaṇam upayujyate vyabhicāra ādi siddhau satyām upādhi tada bhāva parīkṣāyāḥ niṣphala tvāt tasmāt anyonya vyāpti pradarśana mātra prayuktaḥ vyabhicāram udbhāvyā api upādhim āha yadā tu iti yatas na svābhāvikaḥ na nirūpa adhikaḥ tatas na niyataḥ na avyabhicāri iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.16–1.1.5.17	 atha dhūma ādīnām api vahni ādibhiḥ katham svābhāvikaḥ iti atas āha svābhāvikaḥ tu iti nanu asphuṭe vyabhicāre saphalam upādhi anusaraṇam tat kim atra na asau sphuṭaḥ iti atas āha kvacid vyabhicārasya adarśanāt iti nanu kvacid kadācid vyabhicāraḥ api syāt ayogya tvāt ca na dṛśyeta api iti atas āha anupalabhyamānasya api kalpanā anupatteḥ anupalabhyamāna vyabhicāra kalpanā t vārī bhūta upādhi abhāvāt iti arthaḥ atas niyataḥ avyabhicāri iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.18	 nanu upādhyabhāve anupalabhyamāna vyabhicāra kalpa nāna vakāśaḥ saḥ eva tu upādhya bhāvaḥ kutastyaḥ iti āśaṅkate na ca iti pariharati avaśyam iti upādhiḥ hi pramāṇa padavīm avatīrṇaḥ eva vaktavyaḥ anyathā sarvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ sarvadā sarvatra sarveṣām jātyā kaścid anupalabhyamānaḥ api syāt upādhiḥ iti śaḍkā tad utpattau= api brahmaṇā api apanetum aśakyā nānā pramāṇa gocara artha sākṣāt kāravataḥ sarvajñasya api svabhāvataḥ eva anupalabhyaḥ kaścid arthaḥ bhavet bhavet ca sarva pramāṇa apoḍham api kadācid advaitam prakṛti puruṣau vā niḥsvabhāva tā vā jagataḥ vedānām vā aprāmāṇyam tat katham caitya vandana ādau= api bhikṣuḥ pravarteta artha sandehāt pravṛttiḥ iti ced yatra pramāṇāni paribhūya śaḍkā pi śācī prasarati kutas tatra artha saṃbhāvanā api āstām tāvat para loka pravṛttiḥ ihaloka pravṛttiḥ api na 
NVTP_1.1.5.19–1.1.5.22^1	 syāt iti āha antatas iti yadi api viśiṣṭa āhāra anantaram bhūyas bhūyas puṣṭi dhātu sāmya ādi daśyate maraṇam tam roga ādi anantaram eva tathā api āhāra viśeṣaḥ maraṇasya eva hetuḥ kadācid bhavet katham anyathā ante tad antaram asya upalambhaḥ yat tu iyantam kālam na māritavān tad mantra pratibaddha vahni vat kenacid pratibaddha tvāt saḥ eva pratibandhakaḥ puṣṭi ādi hetuḥ iti api saṃbhāvyeta roga ādikam eva ca puṣṭi ādi hetuḥ tat tu puṣṭi ādi kāle adṛśya tvāt eva na apalabhyate 
NVTP_1.1.5.19–1.1.5.22^2	 na hi puṣṭi ādi kāraṇaiḥ dṛśyaiḥ eva bhavitavyam iti api kadācid syāt yathā ca aprāmāṇika upādhi śaḍkyā vyabhicāri tva śaṅkayā vā anumāna nivṛttiḥ tathā prāmāṇika anartha śaṅkayā eva viśiṣṭa āhāra bhojana ādi nivṛttiḥ iti arthaḥ tasmāt utprekṣita artha niścaya vat tad śaḍkā api bandhyā eva pramitasya eva tu niścaya vat śaḍkā api samīha upayoginī iti āha tasmāt iti tat ayam saṃkṣepaḥ vyabhicāraḥ eva pratibandha abhāvaḥ upādheḥ eva vyabhicāra aśaḍkāḥ pramāṇa niścitaḥ eva upādhi tvena śaṅkanīyaḥ sādhane sa upādhiḥ sādhye nirūpa ādhiḥ eva upādhi tvena niśceyaḥ atas anyaḥ ca anyathā tvena iti pramāṇa paridṛṣṭeṣu eva kaścid upādhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti atas āha prayatnena iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.23	 ayam prayatna arthaḥ pratyakṣa upalabhyāḥ tāvat yogyā anupalabdheḥ eva nirastāḥ pramāṇa antara paridṛṣṭānām api vyāpakānām upādhi tve vahneḥ sārvatrika tva prasaṅgaḥ avyāpakānam api nityānām upādhi tve bahneḥ sadā anuvṛtti prasaṅgaḥ anityāḥ tu trividhāḥ ubhaya avi abhicāriṇaḥ ubhaya vyabhicāriṇaḥ anyatara avyabhicāriṇaḥ ca iti tatra prathama dvitīyā upādhi lakṣaṇa abhāvāt eva na upādhayaḥ anyatara avyabhicāriṇaḥ ca dvividhāḥ dhūma mātra avyabhicāriṇaḥ vahni mātra avyabhicāriṇaḥ ca iti pūrve lakṣaṇa abhāvāt eva na upādhayaḥ vahni mātra avyabhicāriṇaḥ api dvividhāḥ vyāpya mātra rūpāḥ ubhaya rūpāḥ ca iti pūrvavat eva pūrve ubhaya rūpāḥ tu sāmagrītaḥ na api pare vidyante sā ca na kvacid upādhiḥ dhūmasya vahninā iva tayā api svabhāva saṃbandhāt vahni janana sāmagryām vahneḥ api antar bhāvāt ca na ca kṛtaka tvān uṣṇa tvayoḥ saṃbandhe tejaḥ jātīya itaratva vat iha api sādhya dharma jātīya itara tvam upādhiḥ tasya pramāṇa bādha eka mātra niyata tvāt 
NVTP_1.1.5.24–1.1.5.25^1	 atas eva upādhim apaśyantaḥ api virodhi pramāṇa sadasadbhāva niścaya vyagra tayā muhūrtam anumitau vilambāmahe tat evam sarvathā upādhi anupalambhāt tad abhāva niścayaḥ yathā dhūma saṃbandhe tathā anyatra api draṣṭavyaḥ tarkaḥ ca sarva śaḍkā nirākaraṇa paṭīyān vijayate iti nanu pramāṇa siddhe vastuni svabhāvaḥ avalambanam na tu svabhāva avalambanena eva vastu vyavasthā iti āśayavān pṛcchati kena punar iti prathama darśanena eva vahni dhūmayoḥ avyabhicāra grahaṇam dvitīya ādibhiḥ tu śaḍkā mātram apanīyate iti keṣāñcit matam apanayan= eva prakṛtam prapañcayati yadā tāvat iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.24–1.1.5.25^2	 atra ca eṣa parama arthaḥ yaḥ ayam upādhim ādāya yena saha saṃbadhyate sa nirūpa adhyavasthāyām tasya āgamakaḥ yathā vahniḥ dhūmasya sa upādhi avasthāyām api upādheḥ kevalasya eva sāmarthye saḥ eva gamakaḥ na tu upahitaḥ yathā āhāra pariṇati bhedasya eva gamaka tve maitra tanaya tvam yatra tu upādhiḥ kevalaḥ vyabhicārī tatra sa upādhiḥ api gamakaḥ eva yathā ārdra indhanavān vahniḥ dhūmasya iti tat kasya hetoḥ viśiṣṭasya nirūpa adhi tvāt iti bhūyas darśanam iti tad janita saṃskāra sahitam indriyam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.26–1.1.5.27	 agre ca etat eva sphuṭīkṛtam iti avirodhaḥ maṇi bheda tattva vat iti yathā maṇiḥ yaiḥ yaiḥ viśeṣaiḥ tad tad vyavahāra viṣayaḥ bhavati dhārayituḥ ca tad tad phala bheda saṃpādakaḥ ca unnīyate te te sūkṣmāḥ viśeṣāḥ parīkṣakaiḥ bhūyobhiḥ darśanaiḥ ūnnīyante tathā atrāpi iti tathā hi prathamatas tāvat bhūyas darśanam kākatālīya nyāya vyudāsāya tatas sātatya ūrdhva gati ādi viśeṣa avasāyāya tatas upādhi śaḍkā nirāśāya atra ca na vāraṃsakhyā niyame abhyupayogaḥ mṛdu madhya adhimātra buddhi bhedena puṃsām vicitra śakti tvāt na ca evam sati lakṣaṇa śāstra vaiyarthyam aniyata vāra viśiṣṭa tattva sākṣātkārau= adhiyoga abhyāsa upadeśa vat iha api nirūpa ādhi saṃbandha bodha avadhi niyamāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva avagame api ayam eva mārgaḥ na tu pañca pratyakṣa anupalambhāḥ anyatas anāgatasya tatra asataḥ tad anantaram upalambhe api tatas anyasmāt anutpatteḥ bhāva mātreṇa niścetum aśakyatvāt kākatālīya nyāyena api saṃbhavāt bhūyas pravṛttau tu yadi na vyabhicāra upalambhaḥ upādhi upalambhaḥ api na syāt dvaya upagame tu tat niyataḥ saṃbandhaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.28–1.1.5.30	 syāt etat dhūma ādīnām maitra tanaya tva ādīnām ca bhūyas darśana tva aviśeṣe api kutas viśeṣāt ekasya gamaka tvam aparasya nati atas āha na ca iti yat tu atra uktam yathā hi anārda indhane vahnau na dhūmaḥ iti vahneḥ tad saṃbandhe tathāvidham indhanam upādhiḥ tathā yadi maitrāt jātasya api kasyacid vivakṣita āhāra pariṇati viraheṇa śyāmatā upālapsyata saḥ upādhiḥ niraceṣyata na tu etat asti tathā sati api ca upādhivādaḥ vyarthaḥ vyabhicārāt eva maitra tanayasya ahetu tvāt iti tat idam anavadhārita upādhi lakṣaṇasya sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānam na kiñcid eva 
NVTP_1.1.5.31^1	 tathā hi na upahitasya niścitaḥ eva sādhya vyabhicāraḥ upādheḥ lakṣaṇam kim nāma sādhana avyāpaka tve sati sādhya vyāpaka tvam tat ca sādhya abhimata dhūma śyāma tve prati vyāpaka tvem ārdra indhana anna pāna pariṇati bhedayoḥ aviśiṣṭam aviśiṣṭam ca sādhana abhimata dahana maitra tanaya tve prati tayoḥ avyāpaka tvam iyān= tu viśeṣaḥ vahneḥ dhūmena iva ārdra indhanena api sākṣāt eva vinā abhāvaḥ upalabhyate maitra tanayasya tu śyāma tvena iva anna pāna pariṇāmena api upādheḥ eva unnīyate iti nanu vajre loha lekhya tvam prati pārthiva tva hetoḥ kaḥ upādhiḥ praśithila avayava tvam tarhi tad nivṛttau paveḥ iva sphaṭika ādau= api loha lekhya tva nivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ na khalu nibiḍa avayava tvena ubhayoḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ na mṛd ādibhyaḥ nibiḍa avayava tve api sphaṭikasya praśithila avayava tvāt eva 
NVTP_1.1.5.31^2	 na hi adbhyaḥ medinī nibiḍa iti na praśithila avayavāḥ iyān= tu viśeṣaḥ yathā yathā śaithilya apakarṣaḥ tathā tathā lekhituḥ prayatna prakarṣaḥ yadi tu śaithilyam aprayojakam tadā mṛd kāṣṭha pāṣāṇa ādiṣu prayatna prakarṣaḥ api viphalaḥ pārthiva tvasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt sphaṭike katham eṣā pratipattiḥ iti ced loha lekhya tvāt eva loha lekhya tva praśithila avayava tvayoḥ samavyāptika tvāt atas eva anayoḥ ekatara pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ eva anyatara pravṛtti nivṛttī na tu pārthiva tva pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ eva loha lekhya tva pravṛtti nivṛttī vajre adarśanāt jala ādau darśanāt ca vahnau= anuṣṇa tva sādhanasya tu kṛtaka tvasya tad jātīya itara tva lakṣaṇam upādhiḥ sa ca bādha eka niyata viṣayaḥ iti na ati prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam tat etat sarvam hṛdi nidhāya āha ityādayaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.32–1.1.5.33	 yadi api dvitīya liṅga darśanasya smṛtyā saha vinaśyat avasthasya eva parāmarśa janaka tvam kvacid tathā api yatra dṛṣṭa mātraḥ eva vahni nivṛttau nivṛttaḥ dhūmaḥ kāla antare jijñāsā vaśāt parāmṛśyate tatra dvayoḥ api liṅga darśanayoḥ atīta tvam iti āśayavata uktam yadi api ityādi yena ca parāmarśaḥ na iṣyate tena vākyasya caturthaḥ avayava apanayaḥ api na īṣitavyaḥ pakṣa dharma tā pratipādanena tasya upayogaḥ para artha anumāne sva artha anumāne tu sā dvitīya liṅga darśanāt eva avagata iti kim parāmarśena iti ced na pakṣa dharma tā hi vyāptyā saha pratisaṃhita anumāna upayoginī tādṛśī ca upanayena pradarśyate na tu dvitīya liṅga darśanena 
NVTP_1.1.5.34	 tasya tu vyāpti anusandhāna rahitam pakṣa dharma tā mātram eva gocaraḥ na ca tad anumāna upayogi tasmāt upanaya arthaḥ na dvitīya liṅga darśana viṣayaḥ tatas sva artha anumāne yadi asti tasya upayogaḥ nūnam parāmarśaḥ api tṛtīyaḥ svīkartavyaḥ na asti ced para artha anumāne api liṅga parāmarśa eka arthaḥ upanayaḥ api na ādaraṇīyaḥ tulya viṣaya tva āditi āśayavān saṃkalayya anayoḥ samāna viṣaya tvam āha saṃbandha iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.35	 nanu vyāpāra anubandhi tayā viṣaya tvam viṣaya tve ca vyāpāra anubandhaḥ iti paraspara āśraya tvam atha vyāpāra anubandhi tayā eva viṣaya tvam tathā api asaṃbaddha tva aviśeṣāt katham tasya eva vyāpāra anubandhitā iti āśaḍkya pariharati na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ iti na dhūma jñānasya agniḥ svatantrasya vyāpāra viṣayaḥ yena asaṃbaddha tva aviśeṣāt ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt kim tu jñeya viśeṣaṇasya tasya ca jñāyamānasya dhūmasya agninā saha niyāmakaḥ svabhāva saṃbandhaḥ eva atas na ati prasaṅgaḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.36^1	 pūrvam lakṣya padārtha praśna avasare anumīyate anena iti kāraṇa arthaḥ iti uttaram dattam idānīm anumitiḥ kasyāñcit avasthāyām anumānam pramāṇam bhavena vā iti vijñāsā praśne bhāvaḥ karaṇam vā iti uttaram atas na virodhaḥ aśataḥ pauna rūktyam vā atas ṭīkā kṛt api vyāpāra tvena apramāṇyam pūrva pakṣayitvā phala antara hetu tvena prāmāṇyam samarthayati sma iha yadi api vijñāna pramāṇayoḥ anyatara adhikāreṇa saṃskāra nirṇayayoḥ vyudāsaḥ vijñāna adhikāre hi tad pūrvakam anubhava kāraṇam anumānam iti sūtra saṃbandhaḥ na ca evaṃbhūtau saṃskāra nirṇaya viśeṣau tayoḥ anubhavam pratyahetutvāt 
NVTP_1.1.5.36^2	 pramāṇa adhikāra api phalatas saḥ eva arthaḥ tad pūrvakam pramākaraṇam anumānam iti sūtra saṃbandhāt tathā api vivakṣā bhedāt vikalpena ubhayam ubhayatra saṃbhantsyate iti vivakṣitvā ekaika kaniṣṭhatayā ekaikam darśitam iti tathā eva vyākhyātavān vastutas tu ubhayam ubhayatra saṃbaddham iti nigarvaḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ iti vārttike bahu vrīhi samāsa sthitaḥ viśeṣaṇa tayā vyatirekaḥ niṣkṛṣya sva pradhāna tayā tad puruṣa padena pradarśitaḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ vyatirekaḥ iti atas na vārttike hetu sāmānādhikaraṇya virodhaḥ vyatireka abhāvam vyatireka nirūpaṇa abhāvam iti arthaḥ iha avastunaḥ vidhi niṣedha vyavahāra viṣaya tvam laukika samīha anurodhāt vā 
NVTP_1.1.5.37–1.1.5.38	 śukti rajata vat rajju sarpa vat ca pramāṇa anurodhāt vā gandham prati pṛthivī vat udaka vat vā vacana mātra anurodhāt vā pradhāna vat śaśa viṣāṇa vat ca mūḍha praśna anurodhāt vā dharma antaram prati pūrvavat eva sva vacana virodha bhayāt vā iti tatra prathamaḥ tāvat avastuni asaṃbhavī laukika pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ vastu mātra viṣaya tvāt dvitīya ādiṣu eva ca paramparayā praviśati iti na 
NVTP_1.1.5.39–1.1.5.40	 pṛthak nirākriyate dvitīya nirākaraṇāya prāmāṇika niṣedha vyavahāra rītim āha sadbhyām iti yadi tad viviktā itara svabhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ yadi coma yatha atirikta svabhāvaḥ ubhayathā api niṣedhya niṣedha adhikaraṇābhyām eva nirūpyate na tu ekena satā niṣedhyena niṣedha adhikaraṇena vā iti arthaḥ nanu sataḥ eva kutaścid pramāṇa pratītāt nivartsyati iti atas āha pakṣāt anyasya iti tad anena asati adhikaraṇe nivṛtti nirūpaṇam pratiṣiddham nivṛttau tu mūka tā eva ucitā iti hṛdayam nivṛttiḥ eva pratiṣiddhā iti bhrāntaḥ tu codayati na nivartate ced iti nirūpaṇam ādāya eva pariharati yasya iti yatra khalu bhāvaḥ sarvathā eva na nirūpitaḥ tad adhikaraṇa tayā 
NVTP_1.1.5.41–1.1.5.47	 tasya anyatra upalabdhasya abhāvaḥ nirūpyate iti dṛṣṭam yathā gavi dṛṣṭasya śruṅgasya śaśe yatra tu śṛḍga abhāvaḥ api gagana kamala ādau nirūpayitum na śakyate tatra śṛṅgam eva nirūpyate iti alaukikam iti arthaḥ punar bhrāntaḥ śaṅkate tat kim idānīm iti sva vacana virodha bhayam āśaṅkate nanu ca iti tat uktam jñāna śriyā dharmasya kasyacid avastuni māna siddhā bādhā vidhi vyavahṛtiḥ kim iha asti naḥ vā kkā apyasti ced katham iyanti na ḍhūṣaṇāni na asti eva ced sva vacana pratirodha siddhiḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.48–1.1.5.54	 yadi api sva vacana virodha bhiyā api sarvathā vicāra asahor athaḥ svīkartum na śakyate vacanāt vicāraḥ garīyān iti nyāyāt anyathā vikalpa śabdau na vastu gocarau= iti sva vacana virodhāt eva parihartavyam tathā hi sva lakṣaṇasya asādha araṇyena aśakya samaya gocara tayā śabdasya ca samaya adhīna pravṛttika tayā vikalpasya ca tad eka viṣaya tayā na tayoḥ vastu gocara tvam iti vicāre śabdasya kācid api vastuni māna siddhā bādhā vidhi vyavahṛtiḥ kim āha asti naḥ vā asti eva ced katham iyanti na dūṣaṇāni na asti eva ced sva vacana pratirodha siddhiḥ iti tulyā vibhīṣikā tathā api tattvam nirūpayan pariharati na vai tattvataḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.55–1.1.5.56	 nanu yadi na ekatara niṣedhaḥ vidhiḥ vā tat kim ubhaya vidhiḥ niṣedhaḥ vā tathā sati atitarā durghaṭam āpadyeta iti atas āha no khalu iti nanu sarva vyavahārā bhājanam iti api niṣedha vyavahāra bhājana tvena eva nirvahet anyathā punar api sva vacana pratirodhaḥ iti atas āha upayoge vā iti sva vacana pratirodha bhayāt hi tadā niṣedha vyavahāra gocara tva svīkāraḥ syāt yadi tathā sati bhayam nivarteta na tu etat asti no khalu sakala vyavahārā bhājanam ca tad niṣedha vyavahāra bhājanam ca iti vacanam 
NVTP_1.1.5.57	 parasparam avirodhi vidhi vyavahāra mātra abhiprāyeṇa abhājana tva vyavahāre kutas virodhaḥ iti ced hanta ! sakala vidhi niṣedha vyavahāra abhājana tvena kiñcid vyavahniyate na vā ubhayathā api sva vacana virodhaḥ ubhayathā api avastunā eva tena bhavitavyam vastunaḥ sarva vyavahāra viraha anupapatteḥ na iti pakṣe sakala vidhi niṣedha vyavahārā bhājanam iti anena eva vyavahāreṇa virodhāt avyavahṛtasya niṣeddhum aśakyatvāt vyavahniyate iti pakṣe tu viṣaya svarūpa paryālocanena eva virodhāt na hi sarva vyavahāra ābhājanam ca vyavahniyate ca iti ca 
NVTP_1.1.5.58–1.1.5.60	 api ca yadi avastunaḥ niṣedha vyavahāra gocara tvam vidhi vyavahāra viṣaya tā api kim na syāt pramāṇa abhāvasya ubhayatra api tulya tvāt bandhyā sutasya avaktṛ tve acetana tva ādikam eva pramāṇam vaktṛ tve tu na kiñcid iti ced na tatra api suta tvasya vidyamāna tvāt na hi bandhyāyāḥ sutaḥ na sutaḥ tathā sati sva vacana virodhāt vacana mātram etat na tu paramārthataḥ sutaḥ eva asau= iti ced acetanasya api evaṃrūpa tvāt cetanāt anyat svabhāva antaram eva acetanam iti ucyate caitanya nivṛtti mātram eva vivakṣitam iha tat ca saṃbhavati eva iti ced na tatra api asuta tva nivṛtti mātrasya eva vivakṣita tvāt asuta tva nivṛtti mātrasya svarūpataḥ kṛti jñaptyoḥ asāmarthye samartham artha antaram avaseyam anantarbhāvya kutas hetu tvam iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.61	 ced na acaitanye api asya nyāyasya samāna tvāt vyāvṛtti rūpam api ca tat eva gamakam yat atasmāt eva yathā śiṃśapā tvam bandhyā sutaḥ tu asutāt iva ghaṭa ādeḥ sutāt api devadatta ādeḥ vyāvartate atas na hetuḥ iti ced nanu acaitanyam api asya evam rūpam eva na hi bandhyā sutaḥ cetanāt iva devadatta ādeḥ acetanāt api kāṣṭha ādeḥ na vyāvartate atas na hetuḥ iti vaktṛ tvam vastu eka niyataḥ dharmaḥ sa katham avastuni sādhyaḥ virodhāt iti ced sa punar ayam virodhaḥ kutas pramāṇāt siddhaḥ kim vaktṛ tva viviktasya avastunaḥ niyamena upalambhāt āhosvit vastu viviktasya vaktṛ tvasya anupālambhāt iti na tāvat avastu kenacid pramāṇena upalambha gocaraḥ tathā tve vā na avastu na api uttaraḥ samāna tvāt na hi avaktṛ tvam api vastu viviktam kasyacid pramāṇasya viṣayaḥ tad vivikta vikalpana mātram tāvat asti iti ced 
NVTP_1.1.5.62–1.1.5.63	 tad saṃsṛṣṭi vikalpane api kaḥ vārāyitā nanu vaktṛ tvam vacanam prati kartṛ tvam tat katham avastuni tasya sāma arthya viraha lakṣaṇa tvāt iti ced atha avaktṛ tvam api katham tatra tasya vacana itara kartṛ tva lakṣaṇa tvāt sarva sāmarthya virahe vacana sāmarthya virahaḥ na viruddhaḥ iti ced atha sarva sāmarthya virahaḥ bandhyā sutasya kutas pramāṇāt siddhaḥ avastu tvāt eva iti ced nanu etat api katham sarva sāmarthya virahāt eva iti ced soyam kevalaiḥ vacanaiḥ itas tatas nirdhana adhamarṇikaḥ iva sādhūn bhrāmayan paraspara āśraya doṣam api na paśyati 
NVTP_1.1.5.64–1.1.5.65	 krama yaugapadya virahāt iti ced na tad viraha siddhau= api pramāṇa anuyogasya anuvṛtteḥ suta tve ca parāmṛṣyamāṇe tad avinābhūta sakala vaktṛ tva ādi dharma prasaktau kutas krama yaugapadya viraha sādhanasya avakāśaḥ kutastarām ca avastu sādhanasya kutas tamām ca avaktṛ tva ādi sādhanānām tatas ca pramāṇam eva sīmā vyavahāra niyamasya tad atikrame tu aniyamaḥ eva iti anena abhiprāyeṇa idam uktam upayoge vā niṣedha vyavahāra upayoge vā na nirūpa ākhyaḥ na vidhi vyavahāra aviṣayaḥ yasmin kiñcid niṣidhyate pramāṇena tasmin kiñcid vidhīra api iti niyamāt iti arthaḥ tatra praṣṭuru uttare vaktavye na viruddham anarthakam vā vaktum ucitam iti āśayavān āha kasatarhi iti uttaram atha iti anuttara viṣaye ahṛdayaiḥ yat eva uttarīkriyate tat eva viruddham iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.66	 na ca kevalam atra uttara daḥ praṣṭāpya hṛdayaḥ eva na hi apratīte devadatta ādau sa kim gaura kṛṣṇaḥ vā iti vaiyātyam vinā praśnaḥ tatra api yadi ekaḥ apratīta parama artha viṣayaḥ eva uttaram dadāti na gauraḥ iti aparaḥ api kim na dadyāt gauraḥ iti na ca evam sati kācid artha siddhiḥ pramāṇa abhāva virodhayaḥ rūbha yatra api tulya tvāt tat idam uktam ahṛdaya vācām iti nanu apratīte vyahāra abhāvaḥ iti yuktam kūrma roma ādayaḥ tu pratīyante eva na hi ete vikalpāḥ kañcid artha bhedam anullikhantaḥ eva utpadyante na ca pramāṇa āspadam eva vyavahāra āspadam iti asti niyamaḥ iti atas āha na ca atyanta iti yadi api sarvathā pratīte vyavahāra abhāvaḥ iti vadataḥ bauddhasya api sva vacana virodhaḥ eva tathā api ayam virodhaḥ prāk eva udbhāvita prāyaḥ iti enam upekṣya śaḍkā mātram samarthitam 
NVTP_1.1.5.67	 tathā hi śaśa viṣāṇam iti jñānam anyathā khyātiḥ syāt asat khyātiḥ vā na tāvat ādyaḥ te rocate tathā sati kiñcid āropyam kiñci d āra upaviṣayaḥ iti syāt tathā cāra upaviṣayaḥ tatra eva asti āropaṇīyam tu anyatra iti jitam naiyāyikaiḥ na api dvitīyaḥ kāraṇa anupapatteḥ indriyasya jñāna janane sva viṣaya ādhipatyena eva vyāpārāt liṅga śabda ābhāsayoḥ api anyathā ākhyāti janaka tvāt apahastitasva arthayoḥ ca asat khyāti janaka tve śaśa viṣāṇa śabdāt kūrma roma ādi vikalpānām api utpatti prasaṅgaḥ niyāmaka abhāvāt 
NVTP_1.1.5.68	 sa hi saḍketaḥ vā syāt śabda svābhāvyam vā na tāvat ādyaḥ saḍketa viṣaya apratīteḥ nirākṛta tvāt atas eva pratīteḥ itaretara āśraya tvam pada saḍketa balena tu pravṛttau sva artha aparityāgāt tathā ca ananvitāḥ padārthāḥ eva anvitatayā parisphuranti iti viparīta khyātiḥ eva āvartate sva artha parityāge tu punar api aniyamaḥ asāmayika artha pratyāyanāt śabda svābhāvyāt tu niyame vyutpannavat avyutpannasi api tathāvidha vikalpa udaya prasaṅgaḥ vāsanā viśeṣāt iti ced atha āsat ullekhinaḥ pratyayasya vāsanā eva kāraṇam uta vāsanā api na tāvat ādyaḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādi pratyayānām 
NVTP_1.1.5.69–1.1.5.71	 sadātana tva prasaḍgāt kadācid vāsanāyāḥ prabodhāt kadācid iti ced na prabodhaḥ api sahakāri antaram vā atiśaya paramparā paripākaḥ vā ādye vāsanā eva iti pakṣa anupapatti dvitīyaḥ api yadā artha antara pratyāsatteḥ tadā pūrvavat sva santati mātra adhīna tve tu bāhya vāda vyāghātaḥ nīla ādi buddhīnām api vāsanā paripākāt eva utpādāt vāsanā api iti pakṣe tu tad anyaḥ api kaścat hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ sa vicāryamāṇaḥ pūrvam nyāyam na ativartate iti na ca śaśa viṣāṇa ādi śabdānām asat arthaiḥ saha sambandha avagamaḥ api tathā hi para buddhīnām anullekhāt tad viṣayasya api anullekhaḥ eva na ca artha kriyā viśeṣaḥ api asti yatas viṣaya viśeṣam unnīya tatra saḍketaḥ gṛhyatām na ca 
NVTP_1.1.5.72^1	 saḍketayituḥ eva vacanāt tad avagamaḥ tad viṣayāṇām vacanānām sarveṣām eva apratīta viṣaya tvena agṛhīta samaya tayā apratipādaka tvāt na ca śaśa viṣāṇa śabdam uccārayataḥ kaścid abhiprāyaḥ vṛttaḥ tad viṣayaḥ asya vācyaḥ iti sugrahaḥ samayaḥ iti vācyam na hi evam ākāraḥ samaya grahaḥ gām badhāna iti ukte apratīta śabda arthasya abhiprāya mātra pratītau samaya graha prasaḍgāt na ca viśeṣa antara vinākṛtaḥ kalpanā mātra viṣayaḥ asya vācyaḥ iti sāmpratam ghaṭakūrma roma ādīnā api tad artha tva prasaḍgāt na ca sarve pratipattāraḥ sva vāsanayā asat artha śabda sambandha pratipatti bhājaḥ iti sāmpratam paraspara vārtā anabhijña tayā apara artha tva prasaḍgāt 
NVTP_1.1.5.72^2	 na hi svayaṅkṛtam saḍketam agrāhayitvā paraḥ vyavahārayitum śakyate na ca vyavahāra upadeśau= antareṇa grāhayitum api na ca gām badhāna iti vat śaśa viṣāṇa apadārthe vṛddha vyavahāraḥ na ca ayam asāvaḥ ca itivat upadeśaḥ na ca yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti vat upalakṣaṇa atideśaḥ na ca iha prabhinna kamala udare madhūni madhukaraḥ pibati iti vat prasiddha pada sāmānādhikaraṇyam tat amūḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādi kalpanā na asat khyāti rūpāḥ tathā tve kāraṇa abhāvāt bhūka svapna vat asā vyavahārika tva prasaḍgāt ca tasmāt anyathā ākhyāti rūpā eva iti na etat anurodhena api avastunaḥ niṣedha vyavahāra gocara tvam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.73	 bhavatu tathā api na asau siddhi upālambha yogī iti āha kalpita gocaraḥ ca iti tathā hi kaḥ ayam vyatirekaḥ nāma yadi atas vyatiricyate tasya tatra abhāvaḥ vā tad abhāva svabhāva tvam vā tatra na tāvat krama yaugapadyayoḥ śaśa viṣāṇe abhāvaḥ pramāṇa gocaraḥ vṛkṣa rahita bhūbhṛt kaṭaka vat krama yaugapadya rahitasya śaśa viṣāṇasya pramāṇa aviṣaya tvāt na api krama yaugapadya abhāva rūpa tvam śaśa viṣāṇasya prāmāṇikam ghaṭa abhāva vat śaśa viṣāṇasya pramāṇeṇa anupalambhāt 
NVTP_1.1.5.74	 ghaṭa abhāvaḥ api na pramāṇa gocaraḥ iti ced na tasya tad viviktā itara svabhāvasya api pramāṇataḥ eva siddheḥ asiddhau vā tatra api avyavahāraḥ eva ghaṭaḥ tāvat svābhāva viraha svabhāvaḥ pramāṇa siddhaḥ tādrūpyeṇa kadācid api anupalambhāt etāvatā eva tad abhāvaḥ api ghaṭa viraha svabhāvaḥ siddhaḥ iti ced na ghaṭa abhāvasya tad viraha svabhāva tva anabhyupagamāt na ca anyasya svabhāve pramāṇa gocare tad anyaḥ api siddhaḥ syāt ati prasaḍgāt evaṃbhūtau= eva ghaṭa tada bhāvau yat ekasya paricchittiḥ eva aparasya vyavasthitiḥ iti ced na ghaṭa vat ghaṭa abhāvasya api prāmāṇika tva anabhyupagame svabhāva vāda anabhyupagamāt pramāṇa siddhe hi vastuni svabhāva vāda ālambanam na tu svabhāva vāda ālambanena eva vastu paricchittiḥ iti hi bhavatām eva tatra tatra jayadundubhiḥ yat uktam vārtikā laḍkāre 
NVTP_1.1.5.75–1.1.5.79	 yaktiñcit ātma abhimatam vidhāya nirūttaraḥ tatra kṛtaḥ padeṇa vastu svabhāvaiḥ iti vācayam ittham tadā uttaram syāt vijayī samastaḥ tat kim idānīm svābhāva viraha svabhāvaḥ ghaṭaḥ pramāṇānā eva siddhaḥ tava dṛṣṭyā evam etat ghaṭaḥ hi yādṛś tādṛś svabhāvaḥ tāvat pramāṇa patham avatīrṇaḥ tasya yadi paramārthataḥ abhāvaḥ api kaścid syāt paramārthataḥ saḥ api tad viraha svabhāvaḥ iti tathā eva pramāṇa āveditaḥ syāt na ca etat abhyupagamyate bhavatā tasmāt ghaṭa vat tad abhāvasya api prāmāṇika tvena eva anayoḥ paraspara viraha lakṣaṇa vyatireka siddhiḥ aprāmāṇika tve vai anayoḥ api na tathā abhāvaḥ iti śaśaviṣāṇa ādiṣu apīyam eva gatiḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.80	 nanu kālpanika rūpa saṃpattiḥ eva astu anumāna aṅgam iti atas āha tasyāḥ sarvatra sulabha tva āt itas dahanavat tva ādi sādhane prameya tva ādau śabda anitya tva ādi sādhane cākṣuṣa tva ādau nitya tva ādi sādhane kṛtaka tva ādau= iti arthaḥ nanu pakṣa sa pakṣa vipakṣāḥ tāvat vastu avastu bhedena dvi rūpāḥ tatra ye kalpanā upanītāḥ tatra kālpanikā eva 
NVTP_1.1.5.81^1	 pakṣa dharma tva anvaya vyatirekāḥ pramāṇa upanīteṣu tu prāmāṇikāḥ eva iti vibhāgaḥ tat iha kālpanikāt niragneḥ yadi api prameya tva ādeḥ vyāvṛttiḥ kālpanikī siddhāḥ tathā api prāmāṇikāt jalahnada ādeḥ prāmāṇikyevaiṣitavyāḥ sā ca na siddhā iti kutas tasya hetu tvam evam prāmāṇikāt śabde api pakṣīkṛte prāmāṇikaḥ eva hetu sadbhāvaḥ vaktavyaḥ na ca asau cākṣuṣa tvasya asti iti saḥ api katham hetuḥ evam kṛtaka tvasya api vastu eka niyatasya dharmasya vāstavaḥ eva anvayaḥ vaktavyaḥ vastunaḥ vipakṣāt ca vāstavaḥ eva vyatirekaḥ vaktavyaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.81^2	 na ca tasya tau staḥ tat katham asau= api hetuḥ iti  pralapitam etat na hi niyāmakam antareṇa saṃpadam prati kalpanā tvarate vipadam prati tu vilambate iti śakyam vaktum tathā ca niragnikam api kūrma roma sa dhūmam iti kalpanā mātreṇa vipakṣa vṛtti tvāt dhūmaḥ na agni gamayet vāstavyām rūpa saṃpattau kim amena kālpanika doṣeṇa iti ced tarhi vāsta vyāmasaṃpattau kim kā alpa nikyā tayā iti samānam virodha avirodhau viśeṣaḥ iti ced kutas etat ubhayoḥ ekatra vastu avastu tvāt anyatra avastu vat iti ced tat kim kālpanikaḥ api 
NVTP_1.1.5.82–1.1.5.84	 dhūmaḥ vastu bhūtaḥ yena kūrma romṇaḥ tena saha virodhaḥ syāt kvacid vastu bhūtaḥ iti ced nirdhūma tvam api kvacid vastu bhūtam iti tena api virodhaḥ eva tasmāt yathā kālpanikī vipattiḥ na doṣāya tathā kālpanikī saṃpattiḥ api na guṇāya iti tasyāḥ ca sarvatra sulabha tvāt iti ṭīkā arthaḥ etat ca abhyupetya uktam vastutas tu na na nirūpa ākhyam kasyacid vyavahārasya bhājanam iti nanu yadi āvayoḥ akuśala tayā sva vacana virodhaḥ atha praṣṭuḥ kim uttaram vaktavyam iti avaśiṣṭam upasaṃharan pariharati tasmāt iti yatra vacane sarvathā eva virodha sa tatra avacanam eva śreyaḥ iti arthaḥ etena mūka tā hetu vikalpāḥ parihṛtāḥ boddhavyāḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.85	 nanu eka rūpam avikalam idam katham gamakam gamaka tve vā vyatireka vikala vat rūpa antara vikalam api tathā kim na syāt aviśeṣa ādityāśaḍkyāha na ca etāvatā iti rūpa antara vaikalya vat na vyatireka vaikalyam avinā abhā= a kṣatim āvahati iti arthaḥ evam tarhi sati api vipakṣe vyatirekaḥ na paryeṣaṇīyaḥ iti atas āha vipakṣa sambhave tu iti vipakṣe sati tatra vṛtti śaḍkāḥ tatas tad nivṛtti artham tad upayogaḥ vipakṣa abhāve tu śaḍkā eva na asti yathā uktam prāk na hi tāya abhyavaharaṇe api asamarthasya mumūrṣoḥ śaṣkulī bhakṣaṇam śaṅkate cetanaḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.86	 sva mate tu iti asya tu kālpanikaḥ api vipakṣaḥ pareṇa abhidhātum na śakyate abhidhāne sa pakṣatva āpatteḥ asapakṣa tve anabhidhāna prasaḍgāt tatas ca abhidheya tve sādhye yaḥ kaścid hetu rūpa ādīyate tasya kim vipakṣe vṛttiḥ avṛttiḥ vā iti praśne anena uttara kovidena kim vaktavyam mūkībhūya tiṣṭhāsoḥ tu na kaścid pratimallaḥ iti svayam eva ullapitam anena na tu evaṃbhūtaḥ ahetuḥ eva doṣa abhāvāt arūci mātrasya sarvatra sulabha tvāt iti bhāga asiddhi nirākāraṇāya vyāptyā iti vadataḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.87–1.1.5.88	 pūrvavat iti atiśāyane matupaḥ vidhānam atiśayaḥ ca vyāptiḥ eva iti āśayaḥ tat idam uktam ṭīkā kṛtā asti gandhava tu asya sādhyam na tu vyāptyā iti nanu sādhyasa jātīye śeṣa śabdasya na kācid vṛttiḥ iti atas āha sādhyasya upayukta tvāt iti pauna rūkti abhramam apākaroti padāni vibhajya iti na mantarbhāvya vyākhyāne sāmānyatodṛṣṭa padam evam yojanīyam ukta viśeṣa rahita tvena vipakṣaḥ eva sāmānyaḥ iti ucyate tatra adṛṣṭam saptamyāḥ tasiḥ yogya darśana nivṛttyā ca dṛśya nivṛttiḥ vivakṣitā tena vipakṣe asat iti arthaḥ atas siddha vat trirūpa saṃpattim abhyupetya rūpa dvaya saṃpade cakāram avatārayati tathā ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.89	 tat evam tat pūrvakam iti anena liṅga parāmarśaḥ anumānam iti lakṣaṇa arthe vyākhyāte atha kim liṅkam katividham vā iti jijñāsāyām trividham iti avacchedena vyākhyāya kim lakṣaṇam iti jijñāsāyām pūrvavat ityādi eka vākya tayā vyākhyānena parāmarśa viṣayaḥ saṃjñitaḥ vibhaktaḥ lakṣitaḥ ca viṣaya viṣayiṇoḥ abheda vivakṣayā ca sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti mantavyam evam anyāni api iti tat yathā manojña mattakāśinī saṃdarśanena saṃsāri rāga anumānam śatru darśanena krodha anumānam viṣaya bhogena sukha anumānam roga ādinā duḥkha anumānam avikala indriyasya yogya viṣaya avadhānena jñāna anumānam śraddhāvatām yathāvidhi yāga ādi anuṣṭhānena dharma anumānam niṣiddha ācaraṇena adharma anumānam paṭu abhyāsa ādara pratyayaiḥ saṃskāra anumānam mithyā pratyayena bhaviṣyat saṃsāra pravāha anumānam iti adhyātmam bāhye ca jvalantam tṛṇa rāśim upalabhya bhaviṣyat bhasma anumānam tathāvidha vṛṣṭyā bhaviṣyat nadīpūra ādi jñānam prakāra antara avagatena vāyunā tvarāvatā vṛkṣa ādi saṃkṣobha anumānam ityādi na iyam 
NVTP_1.1.5.90–1.1.5.91	 durava bodham iti sāmānyatodṛṣṭa svarūpasya eva avivecanāt iti arthaḥ udāharaṇa dvāreṇa tad vivecanam bhaviṣyati iti āha śeṣavat udāharaṇa an atargatam ca iti śeṣavat lakṣaṇa yoge api tad udāharaṇa antara vailakṣaṇyena idam eva sāmānyatodṛṣṭa padārthe bhaviṣyati iti atas āhāḥ na ca etāvatā iti na tāvat aśva karṇa ādi śabda vat ayam sūrya vrajyā anumāne vartate anyatra api vṛddha prayogāt na api sūtrakārasya eva paribhāṣeyam niṣprayojana tvāt tasmāt udāharaṇa vailakṣaṇya mātra vivakṣayā it am ucyate tathā ca atiprasaṅgaḥ iti arthaḥ tasmāt bhāṣya kāra vyākhyāna viruddha udāharaṇa mātra ākhyān am arocayamānaḥ sāmānyatodṛṣṭa padam vyākhyāyāni athā udāharaṇam āhā iti yojanāḥ kṣaya vṛddhi pratyaya aviṣaya tve sati iti spaṣṭa artham prāḍmukha upalabhya tve parivṛttya tad pratyaya viṣaya tvāt iti paryālocanayā eva avināśasya prāpta tvāt 
NVTP_1.1.5.92–1.1.5.93	 na hi upalabdha vināśe upalabdham pratyabhijñāyate bhrāntau= api anupalabdham eva upalabdha tayā iti prāḍmukha upalabhya tve ca iti asya ṭīkayā sphoritasya prāḍmukha upalabdhasya prāḍmukhena anupalambhe sati iti arthaḥ nara antarasya tad samāna deśa sthasya iti mantavyam anyathā mārtaṇḍa maṇḍalasya api loka antara varti puruṣa apekṣayā prāḍmukha upalabhyatā durvāra iti asiddham viśeṣaṇam syāt tat etat nara padena sūcitam tad abhimukha deśa saṃbandhāt iti śiṣya hita tayā vyabhicāra aupayika pāda viharaṇa jñāpanāya na hi yathā tathā pāda vihāraṇa mātram asya hetoḥ kṣatim āvahati iti satya vināśe iti ca draṣṭavyam sati draṣṭavya tvaḥ iti vā iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.94	 iha yadi api diśaḥ pratyakṣa tve sādhye aḍgulyā nirdeśaḥ vyadhikaraṇaḥ tarū nagara ādiṣu eva aḍgulyā vyapadeśāt diśaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam tvaḍgulī vyapadeśasya na tad adhikaraṇa tā sādhanam anyathā siddha tvāt tathā api yasyām diśi ete taravaḥ sā prācī iti tarvādi bhedena api aḍgulyā vyapadeśaḥ asti iti na vyadhikaraṇa tvam āhatya abhidhātum śakyate iti anena abhiprāyeṇa anyathā siddhim eva vārtika artham āha anyathā siddha tayā iti upalakṣaṇam ca etat calantīm patākām upalabhya ayam vāyuḥ vātī iti aḍa gulī nirdeśasya ācākṣuṣe vāyau= api gata tvena vyabhicārasya api saṃbhavāt rūpeṇa sparśa anumānam iti ādau= ādi grahaṇena rasena rūpa anumānam gandhena rasa anumānam ityādi vṛkṣa adarśane sandehe vā na śiśapa ādarśana niścayaḥ vā tatas anavasara parāhatam eva anumānam vṛkṣa śabda prayoga lakṣaṇa vyavahāra anumānam tu na sva artham avidita samayena aśakya tvāt vidita samayasya ca vyartha tvāt paraḥ api yadi vyutpannaḥ yadi vidita śabda pravṛtti nimittaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.95	 tadā svayam eva vyavaharet viparītaḥ tu śiśapā tvam api na pratīyāt avyutpannaḥ ced samayam agrāhayitvā vyavahārayitum aśakyaḥ eva na ca ayam samaya graha prakāraḥ tathā sati śiśapā tu ādayam vṛkṣaḥ vyavahartavyaḥ iti śiśapā tvam eva vṛkṣa śabda pravṛtti nimittam ākalayet na ca śiśapā tu ādayam vṛkṣa śabda pravṛtti nimittavān iti vākya arthaḥ vidita tad nimittam prati vyartha tvāt viparītam pratyapraddhi viśeṣaṇa tva prasaḍgāt sāmānya upakrame samaya graha anupapatteḥ puruṣa icchā mātra adhīna tvācaca samayasya pakṣa dharma tayā niyantum aśakyatvāt avidita samayam prati ca anvaya upakramasya ayukta tvāt iti atas āha śrutena iti tat anena ye ca anye sādhya samāna kālāḥ te sarve sāmānyatodṛṣṭa anumāna saṃgrāhya tvena upalakṣitāḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.96	 sva matena vyākhyāna antaram na tu tātparya antaram iti arthaḥ pūrvam sādhyam tat yasya vyāptyā iti anena eka tātparya tvāt anena eva abhiprāyeṇa āha atra api yathāsaṃbhavam iti na anantarbhāva cakāra nirapekṣate ca asmin vyākhyāne pūrvasmāt viśeṣaḥ sāmānyena kāryam vā kāraṇam vā anubhaya ātmakam vā avinā bhāvitayā dṛṣṭam niścitam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam eva ca yojanāḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.97–1.1.5.98	 tat idam uktam asandigdha tām āha iti tatra tad pūrvakam iti sva rūpa vipratipatti nivṛttiḥ sva lakṣaṇa sāmarthyena nyūna adhika saṃkhya tva aśaḍkā nivṛttiḥ prathamam tātparyam niyama jñāpane tu aśakya lakṣaṇa tva śaḍkā nivṛttiḥ tātparyam iti na pauna rūktyam iti vṛttavartiṣyamāṇa anukīrtana phalam yadi api pratipannam pratyanumānasya na saṃśaya viparyaya nivṛttiḥ ajñāta jñānam vā upayogaḥ tathā api adhyavasita abhyanujñānam vastu bala āyātam apekṣite viṣaye anupekṣaṇīyam eva iti tasya api anumāna pratipādyeṣu gaṇanā tena ādi vākye pratipannaḥ pratipādayitā iti pratipannaḥ eva pratipādayitā na tu pratipannaḥ pratipādayitā eva iti boddhavyam 
NVTP_1.1.5.99	 punar paunarūkti aparihāra artham vṛttavartiṣyamāṇe anukīrtayati pūrvam siddha vat iti sākṣātkṛtya numityoḥ kriyayoḥ tulya tā viṣaya gatāḥ draṣṭavyā tena ayam arthaḥ vyāpti grāhaka pramāṇa yogyaḥ dharmaḥ yatra anumīyate tat pūrvavat anumānam tat ayogyaḥ tu yatra tat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam iti dhūma tvā eka artha samavāyibhiḥ iti satātparyam viśeṣaṇam na hi saṃtatam ūrdhva gamana mātreṇa agniḥ anumātum śakyate dhūlī paṭala ādau vyabhicārāt eka dravya tva āditi asya sa pakṣe rūpa ādau= anvayasya 
NVTP_1.1.5.100	 spaṣṭa tvāt vipakṣa vyatirekaḥ eva uktaḥ dvividham eva hi iti na tu atra anvaya abhidhāna mātreṇa kevala vyatireki śaḍkā kartavyā samāna jātīya ārambhaka tvam śabdasya asiddham atas sādhayati kāryatvāt iti kāryatvam punar asya anupalabdhi kāraṇa bhāve sati anupalabdhasya upalabhyamāna tvāt vā pratyakṣāt vā iti sarvatra upalabdhi prasaḍga ādityasya viparyayeṇa hetuḥ prayogaḥ tu evam avyāpya vṛttiḥ śabdaḥ āśraya aprāptau= api kvacid anupalabhyamāna tve sati kvacid upalabhyamāna tvāt saṃyoga vat iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.101–1.1.5.102	 yadi api ca etāvat mātreṇa guṇa tvam sidhyati tathā api bhāṣya kārīyaḥ hetu rūpekṣitaḥ syāt iti atas avyāpaka tā mātram prasādhya eva prakṛte lagayati karṇa iti atra api prayogaḥ śabdaḥ vīcī taraṅga nyāyena karṇa śaṣkulīm antam ākāśa deśam āsādayati prakāra antara asaṃbhave sati upalabhyamāna tvāt iti vyatirekī udāharaṇa artham vivecayati idam tu iti sadādi abhedaḥ sattā yogaḥ anitya tvam kāraṇavat tvam sāmānya viśeṣavat tvam iti sādhya dharmiṇī asmad ādibhiḥ kadācid pratyakṣeṇa anupalambhāt iti arthaḥ ābhiprāyikaḥ hi arthaḥ pakṣa dharma tāyāḥ viṣayaḥ saḥ eva abhiprāyeṇa vyāpyate yena vinā pratijñātor atho na upapadyate ubhayathā saṃbhāvanāya akekataratra bādhaka upapattau= anyataraḥ pramāṇa antara gocaraḥ tatra vidhāyaka pramāṇa abhāve kevala vyatirekiṇaḥ avatāraḥ tathā hi 
NVTP_1.1.5.103	 kṣiti ādikam sa kartṛkam kārya tvāt iti atra sarvajña tvam antareṇa kṣiti ādīnām kartṛ tvam eva na upapadyate paramāṇu adṛṣṭa ādīnām ajñāne tad adhiṣṭhāna anupapatteḥ tad adhiṣṭhāne vā asarvajña tva anupapatteḥ tasmāt sarvajña tvam antareṇa pratijñāta artha anupapattau tad abhiprāya vyāptam ābhiprāyika tvāt ca pakṣa dharma tā gocaraḥ icchā ādayaḥ paratantrā guṇa tvāt iti atra punar ātmā na abhi prāya vyāptaḥ na hi icchā ādīnām kṣiti ādi pāratantryam asaṃbhā vit api tu mānasa pratyakṣa vedya tva ādi bhaḥ bādhitam dhūma gata nīla tvena iva dhūmasya apālāla tvam tasmāt ubhayathā api saṃbhavāt ātmā na eva abhiprāya vyāptaḥ tad avyāpta tvāt ca na pakṣa dharma tā tam aṅkam āropayitum arhati api tu icchā saṃbaddha para mātram ādāya eva nivartate etat uttara kālam kṣiti ādau bādhite tad anyā siddhau vidhāyaka pramāṇa abhāvāt niṣedha mukhena vyatirekī pravartate tam imam viśeṣam hṛdi nidhāya uktam bādhakaiḥ apanīte dravya aṣṭaka guṇa tvaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.5.104–1.1.5.105	 nanu sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt yat rūpam siddham na tat kevala vyatirekiṇā sādhyam yādṛśam ca tena sādhyam tādṛśam na kvacid siddham tathā ca aprasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ pakṣaḥ na ca tathābhūte sandehaḥ api kāraṇa abhāvāt samāna asamāna dharma vipratipattīnām anupalabdha cara aviṣaya tvāt iti atas āha yadi api ca ayam iti svarūpeṇa asādhāraṇa rūpeṇa iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.106	 na hi vākya artha sayā pūrva tayā padārthānām viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ vihanyate tathā sati anvayinopi anutthānam iti pralīnam anumānena na ca dravya aṣṭaka atirikta ādi padārthāḥ eva apūrve yena aprasiddha viśeṣaṇa tā syāt pakṣasya na ca evam sati śaśa śṛṅga dhanuḥ dhara ādau= api prasaṅgaḥ tatra api tadā artha mātrā prasiddheḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt iti vācyam sāmānyatodṛṣṭa pūrvakatva niyama sīmāyāḥ durlaḍghya tvāt anyathā sāmānyatas api asiddhaḥ katham niṣpramāṇaka śabda sāmarthya mātram āśritya parāmṛśyeta aparāmṛṣṭaḥ ca katham pramāṇa vyavahāram avatārayet tat idam uktam adūra viprakarṣeṇa parāmṛṣṭaḥ iti viśeṣa siddheḥ sāmānya sidbhiḥ adūra viprakarṣaḥ tat asiddhiḥ tu tad viparyaya 
NVTP_1.1.5.107–1.1.5.108	 iti arthaḥ evam ca saṃśayaḥ api atra vādi vipratipatteḥ eva sugamaḥ icchā ādīnām ubhaya vādi siddhe sāmānyatas adhikaraṇe dravya aṣṭaka atiriktā n atiḥ eka koṭyā ūrūbhābhyām samutthāpanāt athavā pratyeka utthitaḥ saṃśayaḥ samudāye viśrāmyati iti nyāyaḥ tathā hi guṇa tvam pṛthivī āśrite gandha ādau tad atirikta āśrite sneha ādau ca dṛṣṭam icchā ādiṣu ca dṛśyate tat kim icchā ādayaḥ pṛthivī āśritā uta tad atirikta āśritāḥ iti anena ākāreṇa sarva dravyeṣu bhavan sandehaḥ samāna dharma darśanāt eva dravya aṣṭaka tad atirikta koṭyoḥ eva paryavasitaḥ bhavati tat idam uktam dharmiṇi ca ityādi 
NVTP_1.1.5.109	 vibhāga vacanāt eva ityādi bhāṣya vakra vyākhyāyāḥ śaḍkā poṣaṇe tātparyam nanu sadasatī tattvam iti atra sat asat śabdābhyām bhāva abhāvau= uktau tat iha vartamāna āvartamāna artha tva vyākhyānam tat viruddham api kutas upādīya iti atas āha pratyakṣam hi iti atha tathā eva kim na syāt iti atas āha yadi api iti na viśeṣaṇtvam svātantryeṇa svātantrya abhidhānena iti arthaḥ āho nyāya upyasti iti asya akṣara arthena naḥ saṃbandha anupapatteḥ tātparya arthena saṃbandham āha na sandeha 
NVTP_1.1.5.110–1.1.5.111	 iti nyāya abhāvena hi tarkasya niścaya aparyāptau sandehaḥ tad avasthaḥ iti āśaḍkitam atas tad niṣedhaḥ eva uttaram yuktam iti asti eva nyāyaḥ sandeha virodhi niścaya samarthaḥ yatas iti śeṣaḥ nimitta tvam yadi viṣaya tvam tat na ātmani dṛṣṭānte atha upādāna tvam na tad sādhye samavāyaḥ iti atas āha nimitta tvam kāraṇa tvam iti nanu vyāpaka tvam parama mahat parimāṇa yogaḥ sarva saṃyogi samāna deśatā vā tat ubhayam api samavāye na saṃbhavati iti ata 
NVTP_1.1.5.112^1	 āha sati upalabdhī iti upalabhyata iti ucyamāne ghaṭa ādeḥ api vyāpaka tva prasaṅgaḥ atas uktam sarvatra iti deśasya avacchedaka tā mātreṇa saptamyāḥ nirdeśaḥ vane siha nādaḥ iti vat tathā api asiddham lakṣaṇam na hi ātma ādayaḥ sarvatra upalabhyante iti atas uktam sati upalabdhi kāraṇaḥ iti tathā api viṣayasya api upalabdhi kāraṇa tvāt yatra yatra ghaṭa ādi paramāṇu antāḥ sva upalabdhi sāmagrī sahitāḥ tatra tatra upalabhyante eva iti taiḥ eva vyabhicāraḥ iti atas uktam antarā iti etat ca dravya rūpa kāraṇa antara abhiprāyeṇa draṣṭavyam 
NVTP_1.1.5.112^2–1.1.5.113	 anyathā yatra ghaṭa ādayaḥ na santi tatra tatas anyasya tad upalabdhi kāraṇasya tad indriya saṃyogasya abhāvāt eva teṣām anupalambhaḥ tad sadbhāve tu sarvatra upalambhaḥ eva iti etat api āśaḍkyeta tathā api paramāṇu ādi guṇaiḥ eva yāvat dravya bhāvibhiḥ āśraya adhīna nirūpaṇaiḥ vyabhicāraḥ tad nivṛtti artham aneka saṃbandhi tve sati iti draṣṭavyam etat ca sarvatra iti anena ṭīkā kṛtā sūcitam yadi api ca sarvatra astitvam vyāpaka tvam tathā api lakṣaṇam antareṇa tat duravabodham iti tat eva uktam iti nyāya iti kartavya tā bhūtam tarkam pṛcchati kartrā avyāpāryamāṇasya karaṇasya svayam vyāpāra ayogāt itya āśayavān iti bhāvaḥ atha uktam anavasthāna prasaṅgam avatārayitum kim iti anādhāra tva prasaṅgaḥ ucyate yāvatā svatantraḥ eva ayam prasaṅgaḥ kim 
NVTP_1.1.5.114	 na syāt na hi kāryasya anādhāra tvam asya iṣṭam eva iti atas āha syāt etat iti paścāt turyā saṃyuktaḥ iti śeṣaḥ na hi utpannaḥ api asaṃyuktaḥ eva turyā prathama īkṣaṇe paṭaḥ iti kasyacid niścayaḥ atha ca pramāṇa bala ādiṣṭaḥ eva ayam arthaḥ tathā utpanne api prathame kṣaṇe tantuṣu asamavetaḥ eva iṣyate iti pādau prasārya tiṣṭhataḥ na idam uttaram iti arthaḥ tasmāt anavasthā prasaḍga avatāraṇāya eva idam uktam iti āha samavāyaḥ ca iti iti yadi api upādhi kathanena eva vṛttimat tvasya prāpti dharma tvam nirākṛtam tathā api prāpti tvasya anaikāntika tva sūcanāya punar api anavasthā prasaṅgam avatārayati atha iti anavasthā abhiyā avaśyam antatas kācid prāptiḥ ca na ca vṛttimatī iti svīkartavyam tatas ca tathā eva prāptimat tvam anaikāntikam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.115	 atha anavasthā svīkāre kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āśaḍkya nirākaroti nanu iyam iti anāditāyām hi aḍkurotpāda anuguṇa samaya saṃbhavinā bījena janite aḍkureṇa janite bīje vartamānam bīja tvam tasyāt kura pūrvaka tām avagamayati iti yujyate avikalasya hetoḥ pramāṇasya vidyamāna tvāt idaṃprathama tāyām tu kārya utpāda anuguṇa samaye bhaviṣyat pravāhasya asattvāt prathamasya anutpāde tad āśrayasya hetoḥ tasmin= asati āśraya asiddha tayā sarvasya āgamaka tve pramāṇa abhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.116	 abhyupeta kaṇāt āpta tvasya śāstra virodhaḥ ca ityādi kāryam akṛtaka saṃbandha vat iti pratijñāyām ghaṭa ādeḥ bhū tala ādinā api akṛtakaḥ eva saṃbandhaḥ syāt sa ca aniṣṭaḥ iti pratijñām viśinaṣṭi sva upādānena iti sva samavāyinā iti arthaḥ kāryam iti ca samaveta mātra upalakṣaṇa param anyathā jāti ādiṣu vipakṣeṣu saṃbhave hetoḥ virodhaḥ syāt athavā pratijñā yathāśrutā eva ādhāravat tva āditi atra ādhāra śabdena na āśraya mātram vivakṣitam kim tu adhikaraṇam kārakam 
NVTP_1.1.5.117	 tena adhikaraṇa kāraka vat tvāt iti arthaḥ na ca vācyam kāraka vat tva mātreṇa eva paryāptau kim adhikaraṇa grahaṇena iti pradhvaṃsena virodha prasaḍgāt na kāryasya kāryaḥ saṃbandhaḥ iti arthaḥ mithas saṃbadhyete ādhārya ādhāra bhāvena avatiṣṭhete iti arthaḥ saḥ api samavāye na asti samavāya antara abhāvāt iti arthaḥ san= api asau na kāryam ādhāra vat karoti sva samavāyena eva tasya ādhāravat tvāt tad abhāve tu eka artha samavāyaḥ api na syāt iti arthaḥ saha utpāde kāryam anādhāram syāt sarvadā iti śeṣaḥ samavāyi kāraṇa abhāve asamavāyi kāraṇa śaḍkā api na asti tad pratyāsanna svabhāva tvāt tasya iti abhiprāyavatā tad upekṣya nimitta mātrāt utpattiḥ āśaḍkya nirākṛtāḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.118	 nanu vidhīyamāna niṣidhyamāna vyatirekeṇa jagati na svatantraḥ nāma tat katham dharma traividhyam iti atas āha atra ca iti vidhīyamānaḥ vartamānaḥ iti arthaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ avartamānaḥ iti arthaḥ tatra ye vartamānāḥ teṣām kaścid paratantraḥ vṛttimān iti arthaḥ kaścid svatantraḥ vṛtti rahitaḥ iti arthaḥ pratiṣidhyamānāḥ tu paratantrāḥ na santi asattvāt eva iti tat evam vidhīyamānaḥ svatantraḥ vidhīyamānaḥ paratantraḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ svatantraḥ ca iti tisraḥ vidhāḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.119	 tat evam avartamānaḥ gharmaḥ pratiṣidhyamāna tayā eva vyavahriyate na ca asau pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ kim tu anumāna viṣayaḥ iti darśitam tat ca anupapannam iti śaḍkā vārttika artham āha nanu iti asan= iti uddeśyam tena ayam arthaḥ asanna vartamānaḥ na kevalam pratiṣedha vyavahāra viṣayaḥ kim tu vidhīyamānaḥ api vidhi vyavahāra viṣayaḥ api evam asau na kevalam anumāna viṣayaḥ pratyakṣaḥ ca kvacid pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ ca iti arthaḥ kkā iti atas āha yathā iti katham asau vidhīyamānaḥ iti atas āha jāyamānaḥ iti katham asau pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ iti atas āha visphāritā iti katham asau= avartamānaḥ iti atas āha na ca asau= iti asat tayā sat tayā vā anabhyupagamāt iti sattāyāḥ jāyamāna tayā virodhāt asat tayā vidhi viṣaya tayā iti bhāvaḥ katham na abhyupagamyate na hi sattā sattābhyām anyaḥ prakāraḥ asti iti atas āha niṣedha viṣaya tayā tu iti vidhīyamāna tā pakṣe hi jāyam āna tā abhyupagame ubhayathā api virodhaḥ na tu pratiṣidhyamāna tā pakṣe api iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.120	 tasmāt jāyamāne ghaṭe na vidhāyaka pratyakṣa pravṛttiḥ virodhāt niṣedhakam tam pratyakṣam pravartamānam api tat niṣedham eva gocarayet na tu niṣedhyam ghaṭam tatas siddhaḥ viṣaya bhedaḥ iti sāram upapādanīyaḥ iti satkārya vādam apanīya apare tu iti artha atireka mātram artha padātireka mātram evam uttaratra api 
NVTP_1.1.5.121	 nanu kena etat uktam yad u bhaya pada vyabhicāraḥ eva viśeṣaṇa samāsaḥ bhavati iti atas āha viśeṣaṇam iti nanu tathā api ubhayoḥ api pṛthivī dravya śabdayā ūru ubhaya vāci tvāt katham viśeṣa pratipattiḥ iti atas āha na ca iti na hi bhavati pṛthivī tvam dravya tvam iti upalakṣaṇam pṛthivī tvam dravyam dravya tvam ca pṛthivī iti api na bhavati iti api draṣṭavyam na ca na antarīyaka artha śabdayoḥ api iyam eva gatiḥ astu iti vācyam aniyama prasaḍgāt na antarīyaka tva arthayoḥ api sāmānādhikaraṇyāt artha tvanā antarīkayoḥ api iti tatas tad vyavaccheda artham punar api prayatna antaram āstheyam 
NVTP_1.1.5.122	 tasmāt aneka artha tve api viśeṣa paraḥ eva ayam na antarīyaka śabdaḥ iti akāmena api abhyupeyam tathā ca pūrva dūṣaṇā nivṛttiḥ iti nanu aniyata prasareṇa asati na asti iti sahitena iṣṭalābhaḥ yadi api tathā api sarvathā sa pakṣa āvṛtti rasādhāraṇaḥ api nivartayitavyaḥ na hi pakṣa vyāpakaḥ vipakṣe ca na asti eva etāvatā eva tasya nirākaraṇam tasya api evaṃbhūta tvāt tasmāt tad tulye sadbhāvaḥ iti kartavyam eva iti āśaḍkyāha prasaktam apratiṣiddham anumatam eva iti prasaktasya pratiṣedhāt upādāne tad viparītasya hānam artha āyātam iti arthaḥ na ca asaṃbhavaḥ api prasaktaḥ yena aniṣedhāt 
NVTP_1.1.5.123	 tasya api upādāne tad viparīta hānam saṃbhāvyeta prathame pade saṃbhavasya vidheya tvena iva asaṃbhavasya niṣedhya tvena anupādānāt iti samuccīyamāna ityādi vaicitryeṇa hi nipāta saṃbandhe vākya bheda prasaṅgaḥ atha eka vākya tvam icchanna vaicitryeṇa eva nipāta saṃbandham icchet iti arthaḥ etat eva anūdyamāna samuccayam āśaḍkyamānaḥ sphuṭayati na ca iti uditam hi anūdyate na tu anuditam na ca ubhaya tva viśiṣṭam havirūditam kim tu haviḥ mātram tathā ca anuvāda pakṣe ubhaya tvam avivakṣitam ubhaya tva vivakṣāyām tu na ayam anuvādaḥ kim tu vādaḥ eva tathā ca vākya bhedaḥ evam dārṣṭa antike api yadi sādhya ayoga vyaccheda viśiṣṭaḥ hetuḥ ūditaḥ yuktam idānīm yat tathā asāvanūdyate na tu etat asti hetu mātram tu aviśiṣṭam uddiṣṭam viśiṣṭasya tu tasya ayam eva prathamaḥ vāda avatāraḥ tat yadi yasya iti ayam anuvādaḥ nūnam anumeye sadbhāvaḥ eva iti avivakṣitam viśeṣaṇam vivakṣite tasmin= anena eva vākyena viśiṣṭaḥ vādaḥ kartavyaḥ paścāt idam eva āvṛttyā anuvādaḥ iti vākya bhedaḥ iti arthaḥ saḥ ayam prayatna āntarīya sthāna śabdasya arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.124	 nanu yadi anūdyamānam aśakyam viśeṣṭum atha ārtiḥ api katham haviṣā viśeṣyate iti atas āha atra hi yadi api iti ananya gatika tvāt prāptena haviṣā viśeṣaṇam ārteḥ ubhaya tvasya tu na pūrva prāpta tvam na api tad antareṇa ārtiḥ aśakya pratipattiḥ sādhya ayomavyavacchedaḥ api hetoḥ īdṛśaḥ iti arthaḥ yadi evam ubhaya vacanam kimartham iti atas āha pratīyamānam api ubhaya tvam avivakṣitam viśeṣaṇa tayā iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.125–1.1.5.127	 ayam vākya arthaḥ ārti viśeṣaṇa tayā haviḥ tāvat upādātavyam tasya ca ājya puroḍāśa ādi aneka rūpa tvāt ubhaya tvam api asti iti prāyika tayā tat api upāttam tena idam siddham bhavati ekam anekam vā haviḥ yasya ārtim ārcchet ityādi ubhaya tva vivakṣā pakṣe tu na eka eka haviḥ ārtau prāyaścitta vidhiḥ syāt iti doṣaḥ na ca evam astu iti vācyam vākya bheda prasaṅgasya tādavasthyāt iti na ca anumeye sadbhāvaḥ eva tad tulyaḥ eva sadbhāvaḥ iti vākya dvayam eva idam ubhaya vidhāya kam aḥ tu kaḥ doṣaḥ iti vācyam trirūpa saṃpannasya hetu rūpasya ekasya arthasya alābha prasaḍgāt vākya bhede hi avaśyam artha bhedaḥ iti nyāyāt śaṅkate atha iti avāntara vākya bhede api mahā vākyasya eka tvāt vivakṣita eka artha pratilambhaḥ iti śaḍka arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.5.128	 atra naiyāyika samādhānam āśaḍkya bauddhaḥ sva bhāṣayā nirākaroti na ca iti yadi api tad tulyaḥ eva iti anya yoga vyavacchedasya vipakṣa mātra viṣaya tvam tadā syāt yadi viṣaya antara saṃkocaḥ syāt sa ca tat eka vākyatayā iti paraspara āśraya doṣaḥ anyathā ubhayoḥ api tad tulya anyatva aviśeṣe vipakṣa yogasya vyavacchedaḥ na tu anumeya yogasya iti kutas vihita tvāt tasya iti ced atas eva virodhāt eka vākya tva asaṅgatiḥ iti ucyate yasmāt tad eka vākya tāyām eva satyām vipakṣa mātra viṣaya tvam asya vaktum śakyate sā api tasmin sati eva iti durūttara doṣa āpattiḥ tathā api bauddha naye śābddham vyavahāram āśritya samuccayaḥ eva na nirvahet kṛtam anayā virodhe sūkṣma īkṣikayā iti āśa yavān āha anya apoha iti saḥ ayam sādhāraṇaḥ api nyāyaḥ aprastuta tva bhiyā viśeṣa niṣṭhatayā avatāritaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.6.1	 yathoddeśam ca lakṣaṇāt iti bhāva padam lakṣaṇam āha iti anayoḥ madhye itiḥ pūraṇīyaḥ atra api iti apiśabdaḥ pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa upakṣayā nanu sādhyate anena iti sādhanam iti eva astu saṃbhavati ca ayam arthaḥ jñānasya karaṇa tāyām tasya prasiddha sādharmya samuttha tvāt iti atas āha tat etat iti na sāmānya atiriktam sādṛśyam anāśritasya anya āśraya tve dravya tva prasaḍgāt ananya āśritasya api ayuta siddha ubhaya vyaḍgya tve samavāya tva prasaḍgāt gogavaya ādi yuta siddha niṣṭhā abhivyakti anupapatteḥ ca yuta siddha abhivyaḍgya tve abhāva tva prasaḍgāt ayutasiddha avayavi avayava ādi niṣṭhā abhivyakti anupapatteḥ ca nityasya aneka āśraya tve jāti tva prasaḍgāt eka āśraya tve tasya nāśe anāśrayasya avasthāna anupapatteḥ nitya tve pramāṇa abhāva prasaḍgāt ca sāmānyam hi eka āśraya nāśe api āśraya antare tādrūpyeṇa eva 
NVTP_1.1.6.2–1.1.6.4^1	 pratyabhijñānāt nityam iti vyavasthāpyate idam tu na tathā iti katham nityam iti jñātavyam pratyuta anitya eka āśraya tvāt eva anitya tvam eva anumīyate nitya eka vṛtti tve tu svarūpa sataḥ viśeṣa tva prasaṃgāt sattāsataḥ guṇa tva āpatteḥ anityeṣu ca sadṛśa vyavahāra hāna prasaḍgāt anityasya tu aneka āśraya tve guṇavataḥ dravya tva prasaḍgāt nirguṇa tve guṇa tva prasaḍgāt eka āśraya tve saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ anapekṣa kāraṇasya karma tva prasaḍgāt tad viparītasya tu guṇa tva prasaḍgāt guṇeṣu ca karmasu ca sādṛśya vyavahāraḥ na syāt teṣām samavāyi kāraṇa tva abhāvena anitya dharma ayogāt 
NVTP_1.1.6.2–1.1.6.4^2	 āśraya sādṛśyena tad vyavahāra upapattau visadṛśa āśrayāṇām guṇa karmaṇām tad vyavahāra anupapatteḥ kāraṇa traya vicāra anupapatteḥ ca iti arthaḥ sādharmya prasiddhiḥ api draṣṭavyā iti sūtre sā ca karma dhāraya samāśrayeṇa iti āpta vākyāt iti vākyāt ārabhyam pratyakṣa paryantena iti hṛdayam prajñāpanīyasya gavaya śabda vācyatayā iti vadatā atideśa vākyasya akṛta samaya saṃjñā samabhivyāhāraḥ darśitaḥ tathā api karaṇa vyutpattyā sādhana pada vyākhyānasya parityāge na kācid upapattiḥ darśitāḥ prajñāpanapadasya api karaṇa vyutpatti saṃbhavādata 
NVTP_1.1.6.5	 āha piṇḍasya hi iti pratyakṣāt sādṛśyāt prajānan tena prajñā api atas iti vadan sādṛśyasya eva prajñāyamānasya kāraṇa tvam abhipraiti tathā ca tena saha sādhya sādhana padasya vyadhikaraṇa tvāt anyasya ca karaṇasya abhāvāt sādhya sādhana padam anarthakam āpadyeta yadi bhāva sādhanam na syāt na ca tat jñānam eva astu karaṇam iti vācyam avāntara vyāpāra virahiṇaḥ karaṇa tva ayogāt asamīcīne api sādṛśya jñāne tathā abhāva prasaḍgāt ca tat api hi sādṛśya jñānam eva pramāṇa anuvṛttyā tat nivṛttiḥ iti api na vācyam vṛttaiḥ eva padaiḥ samīhita siddhau= anuvṛtteḥ anavakāśāt sā api hi grantha vaicitryam āpādayantī pada antara vṛttiḥ eva tathā api prajñānam prasiddhi padārthona tu prajñāpanam iti atas āha iti etad arthe pramāṇasya vyāpāraḥ avyavadhānena phala uparaktā prātisvikī kriyā jñāyamānasya sādṛśyasya karaṇa tvam āviṣkartum tasya anyatra acarita arthaḥ phala anuguṇaḥ vyāpāraḥ darśitaḥ iti tātparyār athaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.6.6	 tatra iti tātparya artha akṣara arthayoḥ lakṣya padam hi lakṣaṇa vyavasthāpakam na bhavati paraspara āśraya tvam agatiḥ vā iti doṣāt nanu upasthāpakam api iti āśa yavān āśaḍkya dvitīya pada upādāna tātparyam āha yadi api iti nanu evam sati prathamā eva astu na ca iyam aśoka vanikā tasyāḥ prathama tvāt eva prathamam buddhau= upanipātāt na sādhya sādhana padena phala vācinā sāmānādhikaraṇya anupapatteḥ astu tarhi tat api karaṇa sādhanam evam yatas iti adhyāhāra kaṣṭa sṛṣṭiḥ api na syāt satyam eva etat kintu phala abhāvena eva hetunā upamānasya prāmāṇyam apanīyate pareṇa tasmāt tad avabodhāya niṣkṛṣya phalam asya darśanīyam iti tathā eva sūcitavān etat ca agre sphuṭam iti na iha ṭīkā kṛtāḥ darśitam 
NVTP_1.1.6.7–1.1.6.9	 bhāṣya vārttikayoḥ virodham āśaḍkya āha vārtikakāreṇa iti tṛtīyā samāsaḥ iti upalakṣaṇam artha siddhaḥ karma dhāraya samāsaḥ api na nirastaḥ iti draṣṭavyam aviruddha tvāt prasiddham sādharmyam yasya iti bahu vrīhau= api karma dhāraya arthasya praviṣṭa tvāt evam prasiddhena sādharmyam iti atra tṛtīyā tatpuruṣasya praveśāt virodha antaram āśaḍkya āha bhāṣya kāreṇa hi iti na ayam arthaḥ bhāṣya akṣarebhyaḥ śrūyate iti atas āha ākṣipra iti praścāt niṣkṛṣya abhidhānam kṛtam samaya pratipatteḥ phalasya tat āha samākhyā iti tathā api kim āyātam vārttika vi rodhasya iti atas āha etat eva iti pratipadyatām ayam ityādi śaḍka uttara artha sūtra uktam karoti prasiddha sādharmyāt iti atra iti 
NVTP_1.1.6.10	 atra upamānasya phale vipratipadyamānān prati sa aśaḍkam jarat naiyāyika jayanta prabhṛtīnām parihāram āha yadi api iti saṃjñā akarma saṃjñā karaṇam māna antaram śabdaḥ vā śabda arthaḥ vā liṅga bhūtaḥ tatra liṅgapakṣe upalakṣitaḥ pratipāditaḥ śabdāt avagatena go sādṛśyena pratipādyamānaḥ piṇḍa samāna asamāna jātīyebhyaḥ vyavacchinnaḥ śakyam avaganatum iti saṃbandhaḥ śabda pakṣe tu go sādṛśyena upalakṣitaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ śabdāt avagamyamānaḥ piṇḍaḥ samāna asamāna jātīyebhyaḥ vyavacchinnaḥ śakyaḥ avagantum guṇa karma ādi vat sādṛśyasya api samāna samāna jītīya vyavacchedaka tvāt iti sugamam go sadṛśaḥ gavaya śabda vācyaḥ iti tāvat astu atha go sadṛśaḥ eva kaḥ iti āśaḍkā nivartana asāmarthya mateḥ pariplavaḥ enam eva artham kaścid ityādinā darśitavān tatra iti tarhi viśiṣṭā eva pratipattiḥ vākyāt aḥ tu iti atas āha na ca iti pratyakṣa mātrāt bhaviṣyati iti atas āha na ca iti 
NVTP_1.1.6.11–1.1.6.12	 etena vākya pratyakṣa samāhāraḥ api nirastaḥ sa hi pramāṇa samāhāraḥ vā syāt phala samāhāraḥ vā ādye api pramāṇa tve sati samāhāraḥ samāhṛtayoḥ vā prāmāṇyam iti na tāvat prathamaḥ phala anekatve sati samāhāra anupapatteḥ tasya eka phalam prati paraspara ādhipatya rūpa tvāt na api dvitīyaḥ vākya pratyakṣayoḥ bhinna kāla tvāt vākya tad arthayoḥ smṛti dvāra upanītau= api gavaya piṇḍa saṃbaddhena api indriya ādinā tad gata sādṛśyānupanaye samaya pariccheda asiddheḥ phala samāhāre tu tad antarbhāve anumāna śabdayoḥ api pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ tat kim tad phalasya tad pramāṇa bahis bhāvaḥ eva antarbhāve vā kiyatī sīmā tad tad asādhāraṇa indriya ādi sāhityam asti tarhi sādṛśya ādi jñāna kāle api vistāritasya cakṣuṣaḥ vyāpāraḥ na tasmin sati 
NVTP_1.1.6.13–1.1.6.14	 tasya anupayogāt upalabdha gosādṛśya viśiṣṭa gavaya piṇḍasya vākya smṛtimataḥ kāla antare api anusandhāna balāt samaya pariccheda upapattiḥ iti tat etat jarat naiyāyika matamāskandati nanu iti pūrve hi yathā gauḥ tathā iti eva vākyam gavaya padena apratīta samayena api prayoga mātra upayoginā sahitam saṃbandha pratipatti hetuḥ pratisaṃbandhinaḥ tu śabdāt vā upalakṣaṇāt vā upasthāpanam iti āhuḥ ādhunikāḥ tu pratisaṃbandhi upasthitiḥ pūrvavat eva samaya paricchedaḥ tu prayoga anumānāt iti āhuḥ avācaka prayogasya vākyān aṅgatayā iti tad virahiṇaḥ ca saṃbandhi upalakṣaṇa paryavasānāt iti manyamānāḥ etat eva 
NVTP_1.1.6.15	 prayogam āropya darśayanti yaḥ hi iti etena eva pariplavaḥ nirastaḥ yadi hi saṃbandhaḥ viditaḥ kaḥ pariplava arthaḥ atha na viditaḥ iti tatra akāḍkṣa anuvṛtteḥ evam ucyate iti ced tat api ayuktam na hi viśeṣa niṣṭhaḥ samayaḥ tathā satya śakya graha tvāt api tu kiñcid nimittīkṛtya deśa kāla ādi viśeṣa vinākṛta vyakti mātra niṣṭhaḥ tat eva nimittam na avagatam iti ced avagatiḥ eva tarhi saṃndhasya saṃbandhinaḥ anavagamāt iti kim pariplutam pramātuḥ na ca eṣa parama arthaḥ sādṛśya viśiṣṭa piṇḍa upakṣepe nimittasya api upakṣepāt anyathā piṇḍa upakṣepe api nimittān upakṣepe manaḥ dharma ādi śabdānām jāti śabda tvam na syāt avācaka tvam eva vā syāt tad jātīyānām nitya parokṣa tvāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.6.16	 atra ucyate abhinava naiyāyikaiḥ pañcadhā hi vācya vācaka bhāva vyavasthā nimitta upalakṣaṇa rahite śṛṅga grāhikayā caitra maitra vat nirnimitte antar bhūta upalakṣaṇe nirvacanikayā pācaka ādi śabda vat nirnimittaḥ eva taṭastha upalakṣaṇe paribhāṣaṇikayā ākāśa ādi śabda vat sa nimitte taṭastha upalakṣaṇaḥ evaṃprakārikayā pṛthivī ādi vat viśeṣa vat nimitte nimitta saṃḍkocanikayā svarga ādi vat iti tatra prathama dvitīyayoḥ asaṃbhāvita tvāt iha vidita vṛttānta tayā tṛtīyam prakāram nirasya pañcamaḥ caturtham upayāti iti caturtham vyavasthāpayati na tāvat iti avidita gavaya śabda vṛttāntasya tu yat bhaviṣyati tad anantaram eva vakṣyati tat idam uktam iti parama arthaḥ vastu gatiḥ tatas ca tathābhūtaḥ eva piṇḍe saṃbandhaḥ grāhyaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.6.17–1.1.6.19	 na tu sādṛśya upalakṣaṇa upanīte piṇḍa mātraḥ iti arthaḥ nanu nimittam api avagatam iti atas āha na ca iti na ca go sādṛśyena upalakṣyate iti upalakṣaṇam anumāpanam smāraṇam vā ubhayam api adṛṣṭa saṃbandhe anupapannam smaraṇa mātra apekṣayā daṇḍa puruṣa udāharaṇam etāvat eva ca syāt yat uta gavaya śabdaḥ vā gavaya tvam gamayet yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti śabda arthaḥ vā anumāpayet avyabhicāra pakṣe vyabhicāra pakṣe tu smārayet iti nanu sādṛśyam eva jāti bhedam anantarbhāvya pratyetum na śakyam tasya bhinna pradhāna sāmānya vyakti guṇa avayava karma sāmānya bāhulya rūpa tvāt tasmāt sādṛśayathā tathā ādi śabdāḥ eva tasya pratyāyakāḥ kevalam prasiddha aprasiddha sandehaḥ avāśiṣyate tatra hasti tva ādikam go śabdena nirastam mahiṣa tva ādikam tu anucita viṣaya tayā anyathā upamāna svīkāre api apratīkārāt 
NVTP_1.1.6.20^1	 tat ayam go sadṛśaḥ iti asya arthaḥ gotaḥ bhinna jātīyaḥ tad gata guṇa avayava ādi sāmānya bāhulyavān iti na etat api sādhīyaḥ darpaṇaḥ iva candraḥ candraḥ iva mukham mukham iva aravindam adaḥ aravindam iva idam aravindam iti caturdhā sādṛśya gatau bhinna pradhāna sāmānya niyama ayogena tad anantar bhāvya eva sādṛśya pratipatti upapatteḥ kvacid dṛṣṭam iha smaryeta tāvat iti ced smaryatām tāvat atra avagatam na tu iha tat avagatam iti brūmaḥ tasmāt go sāmānyena upalakṣyamāṇaḥ piṇḍaḥ kim tadvān eva gavaya śabdasya vācyaḥ bhavatu 
NVTP_1.1.6.20^2	 paci kriyayā upalakṣyamāṇaḥ kartā iva pācaka śabdasya āhosvit taṭa stham eva go sādṛśyam tad upalakṣitaḥ eva piṇḍe ākāśa vat tasya vācyaḥ bhavet kim vā upalakṣaṇam vihāya gandha apalakṣita pṛthivī tva jātimān iva go sādṛśya upalakṣita jāti viśeṣavān eva piṇḍaḥ asya vācyaḥ bhaviṣyati itara niyata koṭi saṃśaya tiraskāreṇa koṭi traya avalambī sandeha eva jarat naiyāyikairūpa plutaḥ saṃbandha paricchedaḥ iti ucyate etāsu avaśyam anyatamā koṭiḥ gavaya padārthaḥ bhaviṣyati iti nirdhāraṇa saṃbhāvanām hṛdi nidhāya aitena manaḥ dharma ādi pratibandi grahaḥ pratyuktaḥ tatra api anumānena unnīyamānānām manaḥ vyaktīnām samāna guṇa tayā samāna artha kriyā kāritayā 
NVTP_1.1.6.21–1.1.6.22	 samāna jātīyatva anumānāt sāmānya anavagatau tu tatra api aśakyaḥ eva samaya grahaḥ sāmānyam vā na tasya pravṛtti nimittam iti tat idam uktam sarvathā anupalabdheḥ iti yadi api gavayatva avagame api saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha an avagame tatra prayujyamāna tvāt iti hetuḥ asiddhaḥ eva na hi asati vṛtti antare tad viṣaya tayā prayogaḥ saṅgatim avijñāya jñātum śakayate prāk eva pramāṇa antarāt tad avagame tu kim anumānena sādhanīyam atas eva pratyakṣe api gavaye anumānam anavakāśam eva tathā api saṃbandhi avagame gavaya pada samabhivyāhṛtam vākyam eva saṃbandham bodhayiṣyati avācakasya api ca samabhivyāhāraḥ upayokṣyate upamāna pakṣaḥ iva tat api hi ati deśa vākyam 
NVTP_1.1.6.23–1.1.6.24	 vākyam eva iti matvā tad nirāsa artham saṃbandhinaḥ eva apratipatti rūpa pāditā atas eva āha kutas vākyāt vā iti atas eva vākyasya vyāpti para tā api nirākṛtāḥ saṃbandhinaḥ anavagamāt na ca vyatireke tātparyam saṃketayituḥ abhiprāya upādhika tvāt sat pratipakṣa tvāt ca iti yadi api vinigamanāyām hetu abhāve api na upamānasya kācid kṣatiḥ ubhayoḥ api vācya tve saṃbandhasya tadānīm avadhāraṇāt tathā api vastu gati vivecayati tathā api 
NVTP_1.1.6.25	 kim ityādi tad anujānāti iti antam karabha vṛttāntam pariharati sādhyarmya grahaṇam ca iti upalakṣaṇa pada prayogaḥ ca avāntara bheda saṃsūcanāya tena iyam sūtra gatiḥ prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam sa ca prasiddhaḥ dharmaḥ samānaḥ pratiyogi tayā tad upakṣiptaḥ asamānaḥ ca iti bahuvrīhi pakṣe tu prasiddha dharmaṇaḥ iti śeṣam pūrvavat 
NVTP_1.1.6.26	 jarat mīmāṃsaka matam go sādṛśyam gavaya stham pratyakṣam eva iti vadatā nirastam śābaramatamāśaḍkya nirācaṣṭe go sthām iti jāti antara varti jāti antarasya iti prāyovādaḥ tathā api gavaya vyakti avacchinnasya na go vyakti avacchedaḥ avagataḥ tatra upamānam avatariṣyati iti atas āha tasmāt yathā iti dṛṣṭānte tātparyam prayogaḥ tu ityādi akṛta samaya saṃjñā samāna adhikaraṇa vākya artha upadhānam pramāṇa vailakṣaṇyam iha draṣṭavyam viṣaya svarūpa vailakṣaṇyayoḥ asiddha tvāt ati 
NVTP_1.1.7.1–1.1.7.3	 iha śabde trividhā vipratipattiḥ prāmāṇyataḥ bhedataḥ lakṣaṇataḥ ca iti tatra prathamaḥ kalpaḥ vacana virodhāt eva nirastaḥ tat prāmāṇyam anabhyupagamya vivakṣita arthasya pratipādayitum aśakyatvāt pratipādane vā tatas eva tad prāmāṇya siddheḥ iti bhedaḥ tu parīkṣā parvaṇi nirūpaṇīyaḥ leśataḥ tu iha api vyāvartaka dharma yogāt eva bheda vyavahāraḥ api lakṣaṇam ca tathā tatas tat eva vivecanīyam tatra vipratipadyamānam prati tu parīkṣā avatāraḥ iti āśayavān siddha vat saṅgati bhāṣyam vyākhyāya lakṣaṇam avatārayati atha iti tatra samaya balena samyak parokṣa anubhava sādhanam śabdaḥ iti eke iha ca ādyena padena anumānam dvitīyena śabda ābhāsaḥ tṛtīyena sa vikalpaka pratyakṣam caturthena padārtha smaraṇam pañcamena kartṛ karmaṇī nirasyete apare tu ceṣṭāyām api gatam etat iti ati vyāpakam mattvā śabda tva samavāye satī iti āhuḥ
