NVTP_1.1.7.4	 atra prācayāna āmayam āśayaḥ yadi ceṣṭā na prāmāṇam aprasaṅgaḥ eva tasyāḥ kim śabda tva samavāye sati iti anena nirvartanīyam pramāṇam ced tasyāḥ pratyakṣa ādi anantarbhāve pañcama pramāṇa abhyupagama prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt śabdaḥ eva ceṣṭāyāḥ praveśaḥ samaya bala pravṛtteḥ śabdaḥ eva tu śabda vyavahāraḥ laukikaḥ prāyika tvāt cākṣuṣe jñāna darśana vyavahāra vat iti te api sthūla dṛśvānaḥ ceṣṭā hi abhiprāya stha śabda smaraṇa mātra upayoginī lipi vat śabdaḥ eva tu ceṣṭā utpādita smaraṇa samārūḍhaḥ pramāṇam arthena ca smṛti utpādanāt śabda viṣayam eva asyāḥ prāmāṇyam pramāṇa phalasya pramāṇa tvāt na ca smṛtiḥ asyāḥ avāntara vyāpāraḥ yadi ceṣṭā upadhānam antareṇa avagataḥ api śabdaḥ na artham gamayet evam api saṃbhavet na ca etat asti 
NVTP_1.1.7.5–1.1.7.6	 nanu evam sati ceṣṭayā eḍamūka vyavahāra anupapattiḥ na hi asau tatas śabda smṛtimān agṛhīta samaya tvāt iti ced  atas eva tam prati samaya balena śabda vat arthe api ceṣṭāyāḥ kuṇṭha tvam eva vyavahāraḥ tu anvaya vyatirekābhyām niyata viṣaya avinābhāva grahe pravṛtti nimitta aupayikaḥ abhiprāya anumānāt eva eḍamūkasya kari turagayoḥ kaśāḍkuśa abhighātāt iva atha kṛta samayā api ceṣṭā eva kim na syāt avinā abhāva abhāvāt smārayatu vā padārthān tathā api na pramāṇam 
NVTP_1.1.7.7	 dvividhā hi sā samaya pramāra bhedāt kṛtī anvayinī jñapti anvayinī ca tatra kṛtī anvayinī prayojaka abhiprāyam smārayantī pravartayati na tu kiñcid pramāṇayati śaḍkha dhvani vat atas apramāṇam eva jñapti anvayinī tu kārakeṣu pratipadikā artha pradhānāḥ kriyāsu vartamāna artha pradhānāḥ tathā ca gauḥ aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ ityādi padaiḥ iva svatantreṣu padārtheṣu smāriteṣu paraspara anvaya yogaḥ pada eka deśa vibhakti viśeṣa vat ca iṣṭā eka deśa viśeṣāt prakaraṇa ādi viśeṣāt vā kāraka ādi smṛti niyamaḥ iti ced ceṣṭā eka deśa viśeṣa abhāvāt na hi atīta anāgata vartamāna pāka ādi pratipādakam ca iṣṭā eka deśa viśeṣam paśyāmaḥ prakaraṇa ādayaḥ tu viṣaya viśeṣe śabdān niyamayanti na tu kāraka kāla viśeṣeṣu pravartayanti tathā tve vā gauḥ aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ hastī ityādau= api karma tva ādīni unnīya vivakṣita artha avasāyaḥ syāt na hi ceṣṭā kalāpe prakaraṇa ādayaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.7.8–1.1.7.9	 kāraka viśeṣa ādīn ākṣeptum alam na tu padakadambkaḥ iti asti niyamaḥ tathā ca kāla saṃkhyā kāraka viśeṣa pratipādaka vibhakti samabhivyāhāra vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ katham tarhi tatas vyavahāra viśeṣāḥ saṃśaya pratibhayoḥ anyatarasmāt viśeṣa anupalambhe vidūra vartini samāna dharmiṇi sthāṇu arthinaḥ iva iti tasmāt ubhayathā api ceṣṭāḥ na pramāṇam atas kasya caturṣu praveśa apraveśau cintanīyau etat ca saṃbhāvita prāmāṇyam aitihyādi antar bhāvayatā ceṣṭā apa bhraṃśa lipi dhvani pada eka deśān sāvyavahārikān api akīrtayatā sūtra kṛtā sūcitam api manda matayaḥ na gṛhṇanti iti tad anukampayā lakṣaṇam vyācakṣāṇaḥ eva kiñcid udbhāvayati 
NVTP_1.1.7.10	 vākya jñānam tad artha jñānam vā iti ākāḍkṣā yogya tā sattimat pada kadambakam vākyam tasya jñānam jñāna mānam tat iti arthaḥ yathāśrutam uttaratra kim tu tatra api vākyam eva pradhānam asādhāraṇa tvāt indriya ādi vat sannidhi tāratamya vivecane tu sarvasmin= ayam nyāyaḥ hāna ādi buddhiḥ parāmarśa lakṣaṇā itarasyāḥ anumāna phala tvāt tat anena nirākāḍkṣā yogyānāsannāni padāni nirasya atā ceṣṭā ādayaḥ api nirastāḥ bhavanti iti vijātīya vyudāsaḥ sva artha dvārakam ca akāḍkṣa ādikam iti saṃgati graha pada pratisandhāna tad artha smaraṇa yogya tā ādi anusandhāna prakaraṇa ādikam uktam bhavati anena eva abhiprāyeṇa uktam padārtha smṛti ādayaḥ tu iti tat anena pratyakṣa ādeḥ samāna jātīyasya vyudāsaḥ anāpta vacasām ca āpta grahaṇena nirākaraṇam iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa lābhaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.7.11	 nanu na ayam upadeśa śabdasya arthaḥ yathāśruti ca avyāpaka tā siddhārtha asaṃgraha ādi vat iti atas āha yadi api iti na kevalam bhūta artha asaṃgrahaḥ sādhya artham api na kiñcid saṃgṛhṇāti iti āha yadi api ca iti nanu pravartaka tvena vidheḥ ājñā adhyeṣaṇayoḥ kaḥ viśeṣaḥ yena anayaḥ rūpa deśa padena asaṃgrahaḥ iti atas tābhyām vidheḥ vaidharmyam pratipādya tayoḥ api tatas vaidharmyam uktam te hi iti tat kim ājñā adhyeṣaṇā saṃgrahe api prayatnaḥ kartavyaḥ na iti āha tathā api iti 
NVTP_1.1.7.12	 ayam āśayaḥ yadi api lakṣaṇayā te api saṃgrahītum śakyete para sthāne prayoktṛ padam prakṣipya tathā api na asti asmākam tad asaṃgrahe api kācid prayojana kṣatiḥ svarga apavarga upāya viṣayasya śabda viśeṣasya lakṣaṇa ārambhāt śāstrasya tad adhikāreṇa pravṛtteḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇe tu akṛte viśeṣa lakṣaṇān avatāraḥ iti atas prathamam tathā eva vyākhyātam vakṣyati ca 
NVTP_1.1.7.13	 diś nāga nirākaraṇa prastāve para padam apahāya prayojanavān iti eva vākya artha pratipattiḥ phalam iti ca lākṣaṇika pada prayogasya ca ayam eva upayogaḥ yad ubhaya lakṣaṇa lābhaḥ prayojanam artha gatam asādhāraṇam grāhyam ca sādhāraṇam tu śabdasya sva artha pratipādaka tvam tat ca parasya eva tatas tad apekṣayā parā iti viśeṣaṇam anarthakam syāt 
NVTP_1.1.7.14	 nanu yadi upaniṣadaḥ prayojanavatyaḥ nūnam kañcid artham pratipādayantyaḥ kvacid param pravartayeyuḥ pravṛtti aḍkita tvāt prayojana sadbhāvasya na ced param pravartayeyuḥ katham para prayojanavattyaḥ pravṛtti viraha aḍkita tvāt prayojana abhāvasya iti atas āha yadi api iti na kvacid ityādau sākṣāt iti śeṣaḥ buddha ṛṣabha ādīnām anāpta tve kārakaḥ hetuḥ māyā moha nimitta tvam jñāpakaḥ tu pramāṇa aviruddha sarva dharma kṣaṇika nairātmya ādi vacanam yathāśrutam bhāṣyam avyāpakam manvānaḥ āha su dṛḍhena iti su dṛḍham paritas nirasta vibhrama āśaṅkam pramāṇam pramā tathā avadhāritāḥ viṣayīkṛtāḥ iti na iyam nitya aniti a vyāptim abhisandhāya 
NVTP_1.1.7.15–1.1.7.16	 nanu kāraṇam adhitiṣṭhate eva īśvarasya api kartṛ tvam tathā ca sthāna karaṇa ādīnām anvaya vyatirekābhyām varṇa nipatti prati sāmarthya avagamāt tad adhiṣṭhāna śūnya tayā tasya na āgamakartṛ tvam bhavet na ca śarīram antareṇa tasya sthāna karaṇa ādi saṃbhavaḥ teṣām tālu ādi vivṛta ādi rūpa tvāt iti āśayavān āśaṅkate tathā api iti bhāṣyam uttarayati atas āha upadeṣṭa iti 
NVTP_1.1.7.17–1.1.7.18	 na vayam asya bhagavataḥ kārya viśeṣeṇa anuvihita bhāva abhāva tayā upakaraṇam śarīram nirākurmaḥ tri aṇuka ādi niṣpattaye dvi aṇuka ādi vat śarīra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi kārya niṣpattaye tad upagrahasya apīṣyamāṇa tvāt api tu āyatana tayā kartṛ tva nirvāhaka tayā vyāpaka tayā ca tat tasya na iṣyate bhoga abhāvāt kartṛ tvasya nitya tvāt kāryasya kartrā nirūpa adhi saṃbandhāt śarīrasya vyabhicārāt ca iti abhiprāyavataḥ vivaraṇam sthāna karaṇa iti tat evam rūpaḥ āptaḥ kutas pramāṇāt niścetavyaḥ para citta vṛttīnām apratyakṣa tvāt kāya vāc vyāpārayoḥ ca buddhi pūrvakam anyathā api saṃbhavādityāśaḍkya mlecchāḥ api hi ityādinā bhāṣyatāt paryam bruvāṇaḥ tad niścaya upāyam api leśataḥ darśayati hetu darśana śūnyāḥ iti ayam āśayaḥ dvividhaḥ hi puruṣaḥ asarva jñaḥ sarvajñaḥ ca iti tatra pūrvasya tāvat sattva prasādhakāt eva pramāṇāt rāga dveṣa moha viraha siddhau= anāpta tvam nirastam uttarasya api jñāna icchā prayatna sthāna karaṇa pāṭavāni tāvat upadeśa mātreṇa eva niścīyante iti 
NVTP_1.1.7.19	 tatra sarveṣām avivādaḥ eva jñānam tu yathārtham ayathārtham vā syāt icchā api pratipipādayiṣā vipralipsā vā syāt iti sandehaḥ avaśiṣyate tatra api abhyāsa daśā āpanne ayam arthaḥ asya iti sāmānyatas niścaye bhavati eva tat jñānasya yathārtha tva niścayaḥ yathā abhyāsa daśa āpannam idam araṇyam amīṣām mlecchānām atas asmin= ete mārgāḥ mārga vibhāga jñāḥ iti pānthānām evam niścayaḥ vipralipsā ca hetu darśanena vyāptā hetau sati syāt sa ca dvi rūpaḥ sva upakāraḥ para upakāraḥ vā tatra tāvat pāntheṣu vimārgeṇa pratiṣṭhamāneṣu mleccha ādīnām na kaścid sva upakāraḥ svasya gṛhīta tvāt śarīra mātrasya ca karaṇīya antara abhāvāt bhāve vā aparityāgāt na api dvitīyaḥ na hi anunmattāḥ anapakāriṇam apakurvate na api para apakāra mātram puruṣa arthaḥ tathā sati sarvaḥ sarvam apakuryāt iti evam vipralipsā api nivāryate anabhyāsa daśā āpanna viṣaye tu pravṛtti sāmarthyāt pramāṇa antara saṃvādāt vā moha vipralipsayoḥ nivṛttiḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.7.20–1.1.7.23	 mlecchāḥ api āptāḥ bhavanti yatas pratīti gocarāḥ tatas kaḥ sandehaḥ mahā dhiyām āryāṇām ca tattva avadhāraṇaḥ iti api śabda arthaḥ etena yat yena rūpeṇa na niścitam na tat tena vyavahriyate yathā rathyā puruṣaḥ sarvajña tvena na pratīyate ca abhimataḥ puruṣaḥ āpta tvena iti vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ asiddha tvam uktam pareṣām avyāpakam āpta lakṣaṇam yathā aśrutasya ārī amlecchayoḥ abhāvāt viśeṣaṇa antara prakṣepe tu asmad lakṣaṇa abhyupagamaḥ iti arthaḥ viparyastasya ayam praśnaḥ viparyāsaḥ ca pramāṇa ābhāsa mūlaḥ atas tam āha asti iti bhāga asiddha tām āśaḍkyāha atra yāvatī iti nanu para prayogam adūṣayitvā svātantryeṇa prayoga antara upādānam prakaraṇa sama ajātiḥ sat pratipakṣa tayā ced svarga ādīnām pratyakṣa tvam kutas setsyati iti atas āha yoga je tu iti hetu abhāve phala abhāvāt pramāṇe asati na pramā cakṣuḥ ādi ukta viṣayam paratantram bahis manaḥ iti tasmāt āpātataḥ tāvat sat pratipakṣāḥ eva ete hetavaḥ iti atas āha asmākam tu sabhyañcaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.7.24	 ayam āśayaḥ dṛśyate hi tāvat bahis andriya uparame api asannihita deśa kāla artha sākṣātkāraḥ svapne na ca vācyam smṛtiḥ eva asau paṭīyasi iti na hi smaraṇa anubhava vibhāge api sākṣī praṣṭavyaḥ kim tarhi idam smarāmīdam anubhavāmi iti pratītyā sva sākṣikaḥ ayam arthaḥ na ca āropitam tatra anubhava tvam ap ādhānāt smṛtitva anullekhanāt anupalabdhasya sva śiraśccheda ādeḥ avabhāsanāt ca smṛti viparyāsaḥ asau= iti ced yadi smṛti viṣaye viparyāsaḥ iti arthaḥ tadā anumanyāmahe atha smṛtau= eva ayam anubhava tva viparyāsaḥ iti arthaḥ tadā prāk eva nirastaḥ na ca saṃbhavati api na hi anyena ākāreṇa vyavasāya viṣayībhūtaḥ ayam arthaḥ anyena jñāna avacchedaka tayā anuvyavasīyate tathā ca sa ghaṭaḥ iti utpannāyām smṛtau bhrāmyataḥ tam ghaṭam anubhavāmi iti syāt na tu imam ghaṭam na hi ayam ghaṭaḥ iti smṛteḥ ākāraḥ tasmāt anubhavaḥ eva asau svīkartavyaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.7.25–1.1.7.26	 asti ca svapna anubhavasya api kasyacid satya tvam saṃvādāt tat ca kākatālīyam api na nirhetukam sarva svapna jñānānām api tathā tva prasaḍgāt hetuḥ ca atra dharmaḥ eva sa ca karma ja vat yoga jaḥ api yoga vidheḥ avaseyaḥ karma yoga vidhyoḥ tulyogakṣema tvāt tasmāt yoginām anubhavaḥ dharmaja tvāt pramā sākṣātkāri pramātvāt pratyakṣa phalam dharma ājanaka bhāvanā prabhavaḥ tu na pramā iti vibhāgaḥ iti tad sāmagrī rahita tva āditya siddhaḥ hetuḥ iti sūktam asmākam tu sabhyañcaḥ iti bahavaḥ ca iti anvācaye cakāraḥ yadi api ca asmākam parama sarvajña siddhau= avāntara sarva jñe na sidhyati api na kācid prakṛta hāniḥ tathā api tad sadbhāve api pramāṇa sadbhāvāt saḥ api na upekṣām arhati iti 
NVTP_1.1.7.27	 iha dignāgena bhāva sādhana tva karma sādhana tvābhyām upadeśa padam vikalpya dūṣitam karaṇa sādhana tva pakṣaḥ tu asmat amitaḥ api kutas upekṣitaḥ iti atas āha anyasmāt anyasya iti arthena hi sākṣāt pratibandhaḥ pratyakṣasya eva paramparā pratibandhaḥ anumānasya tat asya śābdasya vijñānasya sākṣāt artha pratibandhe pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ paramparā pratibandhe tu anumāna tva āpattiḥ apratibandhe tu aprāmāṇyam eva iti asaṃbhavaḥ eva karaṇa vyutpatti pakṣasya iti manyate iti arthaḥ atra bhāva vyutpatti pakṣe āpta tva niścayaḥ śabda phalam tad dvārā vākya artha niścayaḥ vā nanu āpta tvena niścitānām kim aparama visaṃvādi tvam avaśiṣyate yat niśceyam iti atas āha upadeṣṭa dṛṣṭṭṭaṇām iti arthaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.7.28–1.1.7.29	 arthasya sākṣātkāraḥ pratyakṣa tvam iti varṇa yojanāḥ tena ayam arthaḥ āpta upadeśaḥ tasmin= eva āpte niścayam kurvan śabdaḥ pramāṇam atha vā āpte niścayam kṛtvā tad sahāyaḥ vākya artha niścayam janayan= iti ubhayam dūṣayati iti āha imam iti anumānāt karūṇa abhyāsa hetu darśana śūnya tva ādeḥ karma sādhana tva pakṣam utthāpayati dvitīyam iti atra api upadarśita artha prāpti niścayaḥ tad dvārāḥ artha tathā tva niścayaḥ vā śabdasya phalam tatra prathamam darśayati yasmāt iti dvitīyam darśiyati evam ca iti upadiśyamānor athaḥ prāptaḥ prāpta tvena niścitaḥ yasmāt iti vā tathā tvena niścitaḥ iti vā sūtra yojanā ubhayam api 
NVTP_1.1.7.30–1.1.7.32	 dūṣayati iti āha dūṣayati iti nanu artha prāptyā artha tathā tvam niścīyamānam liṅga bhūtayā eva niścīyate tat katham āha pratyekṣeṇa iti atas āha āptyā hi iti āpti niścaye api śabdasya vyāpāraḥ na asti iti darśayitum artha tathā tva niścayaḥ api pratyakṣeṇa iti uktam mūla bhūta tvāt tasya iti arthaḥ nanu śabda upalabdhasya arthasya kvacid anumānema api pratipattiḥ asti iti atas uktam prāyeṇa iti atra ca ubhayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ āpta ukta tva pravṛtti sāmarthya hetu pradhānayoḥ śabdasya prāmāṇya niścayaḥ phalam iti śaḍkitum ucitam api na śaḍkitam prāmāṇya niścaya avinābhūta tvāt artha niścaya tat tathātva niścayayoḥ tasya tayoḥ eva antarbhūta tvāt iti manyamānena iti tam imam iti na āptatva sahāyaḥ na āptatva niścaya sahāyaḥ iti arthaḥ prāptyā prāpti niścayena iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.7.33	 nanu anabhyupagatebhyaḥ pakṣebhyaḥ na kañcid abhyupagatasya viśeṣam paśyāmaḥ iti atas āha etat uktam bhavati iti na āptatva hetukam na āptatva niścaya hetukam avisaṃvādi tvam avisaṃvādi tva niścayaḥ anena sūtreṇa āgama artha tayā āgama phala tayā pratipādyate na api artha tathā tvam artha tathā tva niścayaḥ iti na iyam upalakṣaṇa tayā ca vidhādvayam udāhṛtam yathā tu pūrva pakṣe vyākhyātam tathā atra api draṣṭavyam kim tarhi phalam asya iti atas āha kim tu iti anena ullekhena anuvyavasāyena yaḥ pratipattiḥ viṣayīkriyate sā iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.7.34–1.1.7.35	 yadi evam tarhi kkāptā ukta tva niścayaḥ upayujyate iti atas āha āpta tvam ca iti āpta ukta tvam ca iti arthaḥ nanu prāmāṇyam artha avyabhicāraḥ sa khalu katham artham apratyāyya pratyāyayitum śakyet tatas ca punar āpta ukta tvena artha niścayaḥ āyātaḥ iti atas āha na ca yatas iti prameyam iti svātantryeṇa iti śeṣaḥ avacchedaka tayā tu tasya api sphuraṇam iṣyate eva manasā eva ghaṭasya iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.7.36	 tat ayam saṃkṣepaḥ bhūta artha upadeśaka tvam hi prāmāṇyam tat eva prameyam anupadarśayataḥ śabdasya na syāt tathā anāpta ukta tvena api hetunā kim niścīyeta tathā ca kasya avacchedaka tayā arthaḥ api parisphuret tasmāt yathā sattā mātra avasthitaiḥ aduṣṭaiḥ indriyaiḥ pratyakṣam janyate jātāduṣṭa tvaiḥ tu pramāṇa tayā niścīyate tathā sattā mātra avasthitena āptena pramāṇam śabdaḥ janyate jñāta āpta tvena tu upadeṣṭrā tathātvena niścīyate iti pratyakṣa vat sva viṣaye vyavasthā iti jñāna mātram anumāpayet avyutpannam iva vyutpannam api iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.7.37	 ayam āśayaḥ asti tāvat vākyāt artha viśeṣa avasāya iti avivādam na ca ayam laiḍgikaḥ vacana mātrasya anaikāntika tvāt āpta ukta tvasya prāk eva asiddheḥ na ca vacanasya liṅga tva pakṣe sādhyam api asti tathā hi na tāvat tādātmya tad prāptī saṃbhavataḥ na api tad utpattiḥ āpta vacasām api atīta anāgata gocarāṇām paramparayā api arthāt anutpatteḥ tasmāt artha jñāpaka tvam eva śabdānām arthavat tvam na ca tat eva anumeyam tasya svātantryeṇa bhavadbhiḥ anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā vivāda vicchedāt na ca liṅgasya sva ātmanaḥ laiḍgika jñāna janaka tvam eva anumeyam tasya liḍga antara viṣaya tvāt tasmāt vacana mātra liṅga pakṣe yat vacanam tat buddhi pūrvakam iti udāharaṇīyam buddhiḥ tu kiñcid ullikhantī jāyate iti svabhāvā deva ullekhya mātra pratilambhaḥ na tu tatra api bhūtābhūta vibhāgaḥ na tu tarām prakāra vibhāgaḥ tasmāt jñāna mātram anumāpayet iti sūktam 
NVTP_1.1.7.38–1.1.7.39	 kim atas yadi evam iti atas āha tathā ca iti vyavahāra anubhavābhyām vyavasthāpitā api na anurodhitā syāt vyutpatti prayāsa vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ ca iti arthaḥ nanu jñāna viśeṣāt eva artha viśeṣaḥ setsyati iti atas āha na ca iti jñānena arthaḥ sādhayitavyaḥ tasya ca na kaścid viśeṣoḥ atha ahita ākāra ādi lakṣaṇaḥ samasti sa ākāra tve api atīta anāgata ādi gocarasya tasya arthāt anutpatteḥ tasmāt ullekhya tayā arthaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ vaktavyaḥ sa ced jñāna siddhau= antarbhūtaḥ kim aparam tena sādhanīyam na ced antarbhūtaḥ punar api aviśiṣṭam eva jñānam iti arthaḥ syāt etat tad jñāna siddhi arnbhataḥ eva arthaḥ avacchedaka tayā sidhyatu yadi api vacana mātram artha viśeṣa ullekhi 
NVTP_1.1.7.40	 jñāna pūrvaka tām vyabhicarati tathā api yaḥ pada kadambaka viśeṣaḥ yat padārtha jātam smārayati sa tad saṃsarga jñāna pūrvakaḥ iti asti niyamaḥ evam ca samaya grahasya api upayogaḥ iti ced na gauḥ aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ ityādi pada kambakena vyabhicārāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvena avasthitau na vyabhicarati iti ced saḥ ayam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ na tāvat svarūpataḥ padānām parasparam svātantryāt na api arthataḥ tasya anavagamāt avagame vā kaḥ tatas aparaḥ padārthānām saṃsargaḥ yaḥ jñāna avacchedaka tayā anumātum iṣṭaḥ ākāṅkṣa ādimattve satī iti viśeṣaṇāt na vyabhicāraḥ iti ced atha kā iyam ākāṅkṣā na tāvat avinābhāvaḥ svarūpator athataḥ ca tasyāḥ abhāve api 
NVTP_1.1.7.41	 vākya artha pratipatteḥ bhāve api apratīteḥ vākya artha pratipādanena vinā aparyavasānam ākāṅkṣā iti ced evam tarhi vākya artha viśeṣa pratipādakam yat pada kadambakam tat tad smārita artha saṃsarga jñāna pūrvakam iti prayoga arthaḥ tathā ca prāk eva sādhya viśeṣa siddhaye hetu viśeṣa siddhim icchatā vākyāt eva vākya artha viśeṣa pratyayaḥ eṣitavyaḥ iti upasaṃharan= āha tasmāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.7.42^1	 syāt etat tathā api asaṃbaddhasya prakāśaka tve atiprasaṅgaḥ iti atas āha na ca iti nanu na hi saṃbandhaḥ iti eva gamakaḥ ati prasaḍgāt api tu avinābhāvaḥ eva sa ca śabdasya arthena na asti iti atas āha na ca āvinā iti yat tu atra uktam cakṣuḥ api rūpa kārya tvāt eva rūpam prakāśayati iti tat ayuktam yadi hi tad kṛta tvāt eva tat gamayet rūpam iva rasa ādīn api gamayet avana abhāva jñānam vā apekṣeta na hi avinābhāvasya eṣa mahimā yat ayam sattā mātreṇa eva gamayati tathā tve vā dhūmāt api cakṣuṣaḥ iva sattā mātra avasthitāt eva agniḥ pratīyeta api ca jñāna sama samayaḥ vā arthaḥ prakāśate anantara samayaḥ vā 
NVTP_1.1.7.42^2	 tasmāt ca na cakṣuṣaḥ janma sva kāraṇāt eva ayam asya svabhāva bheda lābhaḥ yat anātmānam api akāraṇam api kāraṇa tva aviśeṣe api vā rūpam eva ajñātam eva sat prakāśayati iti rūpaḥ labdhi lakṣaṇa kārya darśana balena eva tad vyavasthāpyate tasya aśakyā pahnava tvāt iti ced tarhi yasya yatra pratibandhaḥ na asti na tasya tatra prāmāṇyam yathā dahane apratibaddhasya rāsabhasya iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ tvayā eva anaikāntikī kṛtā kim asmābhiḥ atra vaktavyam kiṃnibandhanaḥ tarhi pramāṇa vyavahāraḥ śabde yat nibandhanaḥ cakṣuḥ ādiṣu tatra eva kim nibandhanaḥ iti ced idam mahā pāṇḍityam yat siddhamātṛkāyām api adya api sandehaḥ bhūta artha anubhava janana nibandhanaḥ hi pramāṇa vyavahāraḥ sarvatra iti bālaḥ api āha tabdalena eva śabdasya api tad anuguṇaḥ sa 
NVTP_1.1.7.43–1.1.7.44	 svabhāva bhedaḥ sva kāraṇāt āyātaḥ vyavasthāpyate yatas tad tad saḍketa upadhāna sūtram artham pratipādayati iti tathā api samayasya puruṣa āyatta tvāt kim ayam sāṃvyavahārika saḍketān eva śabdān prayuḍkte kim vā svayam idānīm artha bhedeṣu saḍka ityeti sandehaḥ na nivartate iti ced na ubhayathā api asaṃbhavāt yadi asau pratipādakaḥ katham sva hṛdaya guhā nikṣipta samayān eva śabdān uccārayet jānāti eva hi ayam na avidita samayāḥ ete pratipādakāḥ iti atha vipralambhakaḥ tathā api samaya antara karaṇe kaḥ upayogaḥ prasiddha samayaiḥ eva vipralambha saṃbhavāt yatra api hi gupta samayaiḥ vyavahāraḥ tatra api na pratipādyam prati samayaḥ gopyaḥ api tu aviśvastān prati iti hṛti nighāya āha tasamāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.8.1–1.1.9.2	 na dvividhaḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa artha tvāt su acchāḥ svabhāva śucayaḥ atiśayena gurvyaḥ durbandha durdhara durāgraha durvibhāvyāḥ ṭīkā giraḥ viśada pārada vipruṣaḥ vā yeṣām vaśe nanu vaśe jagat eva teṣām nanu yadi prameyam eva mumukṣuṇā pratipitsitam tat ullaḍghya kim iti prathamatas pramāṇam ami hitam iti atas āha tat ca iti tarhi uktāni pramāṇāni idānīm parīkṣayantām kim prameya lakṣaṇena iti atas āha lakṣaṇam ca iti tarhi prameya lakṣaṇam eva āmidhīyatām kim pratyakṣa ādi lakṣaṇena iti atas āha na ca iti nanu pramāṇam tāvat prathamatas eva vaktavyam 
NVTP_1.1.9.3	 tad itarasya tad adhīna tvāt iti prāk eva saṃgamitam etat idānīm tu pañcadaśasu prathamam kim abhidhīyatām iti jijñāsā abhidhīyamāna saṃgati paryālocane ca saṃśaya ādīnām anupayogāt anabhidhānam eva prasaktam kutas pūrva apara bhāva spardhā iti atas āha aparīkṣitam ca iti etena saṃśaya ādīnām upayogam darśayatā vaktavyatā darśitāḥ etasmāt viśeṣāt pramāṇa prakaraṇāt 
NVTP_1.1.9.4	 apakarṣaḥ saṃśaya ādi prakaraṇebhyaḥ ca utkarṣaḥ prameya prakaraṇasya iti samudāya arthaḥ ārabhyatām tahi prameya lakṣaṇam kim antar gaḍunā vibhāgena iti atas āha tat iha iti prameyanā antarīka tvam prameya ālambna phala tvam kim tad artha jātam iti bhāṣya kārīyaḥ praśnaḥ śliṣṭaḥ ki lakṣaṇam katividham ca iti asmin= arthe vibhāga vat sāmānya lakṣaṇam antareṇa api viśeṣa lakṣaṇānavatārāt tatra dvitīye sūtra pāṭhe na uttaram prathame tu śabda vyākhyānena iti bhāṣya gatiḥ tat atra dvitīya praśna arthaḥ vibhāga uddeśa sūtram avatārayitum iti anena darśitaḥ prathamaḥ tu viśiṣṭam prameyam adya api na sidhyati iti tad artham praśnaḥ iti anena tatra vārttikakāreṇa tuśabda sūcitam sāmānya lakṣaṇam gṛhītvā vibhāga niṣṭhaḥ praśnaḥ iti anena tatra vārttikakāreṇa tuśabda sūcitam sāmānya lakṣaṇam gṛhītvā vibhāga niṣṭhaḥ praśnaḥ kṛtaḥ iti āha sa ca viśeṣaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.9.5–1.1.9.7	 nanu ayam eva ca sūtra arthaḥ iti vibhāgaḥ eva asya sūtra āsya arthaḥ iti gamyate tathā ca na vivakṣita viśeṣa lābhaḥ sūtrāt evam ca prameya mātra vibhāgaḥ anarthakaḥ asatyaḥ ca iti atas āha yeṣām iti prakṛta upayogi prameya viśeṣa lakṣaṇa kroḍīkṛtānām eva vibhāgaḥ asya sūtrasya arthaḥ iti vārttika arthaḥ iti arthaḥ yeṣām ityādinā yathāsaṃkhyam lakṣaṇa dvayam naḥ ca tattva padena saṃbandhaḥ sākṣāt iti ca pūraṇīyam apavargaḥ mithyājñāna nivṛttiḥ tad ādi tvāt saṃsāraḥ rāga dveṣau tad eka deśa tvāt iti paramāṇūnām iti upalakṣaṇam tena aśarīrān indriyā tad artha rūpāṇām dvi aṇuka ādīnām tad guṇa karmaṇām api iti nanu yadā diś ādayaḥ abhihitāḥ eva arthataḥ iti samādhānam tadā tad abhidhāne kaḥ upayogaḥ iti api samarthanīyam iti atas āha kauśala mātram iti 
NVTP_1.1.10.1	 nanu pratyakṣam api ātmani pramāṇam eva aham iti vikalpasya paraiḥ api iṣṭa tvāt na ca ayam avastukaḥ saṃdigdha vastukaḥ vā aśābda tvāt apratikṣepāt ca na ca ayam laiḍgikaḥ ananu saṃhita liṅgasya api sva pratyayāt na api smṛtiḥ iyam ananubhūte smaraṇa ayogāt anādi vāsanā avaśāda nādiḥ ayam avastukaḥ vikalpaḥ iti api na yuktam nīla ādi vikalpeṣu api evam vaktum sukara tvāt kādācid ka tvena tatra vastu kalpanam iha api samānam artha kriyā sthiteḥ sūtra prāmāṇya siddheḥ vastu sthitiḥ iti api na yuktam artha kriyā sthiti niścayasya api vāsanām ā dāya upaplāvayitum śakya tvāt atas eva pramāṇa antara pravṛtteḥ iti api gatam tasmāt vāsanā vāda mātram vihāyaḥ āgantukam api kiñcid kāraṇam vācyam tad ca āptān āpta śabdau vā liṅga tad ābhāse vā pratyakṣa tad ābhāse vā tatra yathā prathama madhyama prakāra abhāvāt nīla vikalpa śyaramam kalpam ālambate tathā aham itti vikalpaḥ api tatra ayam 
NVTP_1.1.10.2–1.1.10.4	 pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvi tve sākṣāt eva sa vastukaḥ tad ābhāse tu mūle asya pāramparyāt sa vastu tā iti na ca bāhya pratyakṣa nivṛttau= eva nirmūla tvam buddhi vikalpasya api nirmūla tva prasaḍgāt tatra sva saṃvedanam mūlam iha api mānasam iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ tat katham ātmani pratyakṣa pratiṣedhakam bhāṣyam iti atas āha aham iti 
NVTP_1.1.10.5–1.1.10.6	 yadi api sa vastukaḥ ayam tathā api śarīra pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇyāt tad vastukaḥ eva ayam iti api syāt atas na tad atirikte vastuni pramāṇayitum śakyate tāvat yāvat deha ādibhyaḥ bhinnaḥ ātmā pramāṇa antareṇa na sādhyate iti arthaḥ tat idam uktam drāk iti ghaṭa ādi jñāna vat iti vyatireki dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā hi ghaṭa ādi jñānam śarīra ādi pratyaya vaiyadhi karaṇyāt tad atirikte vastuni drāgeva pramāṇayitu śakyate tathā na idam iti arthaḥ nanu yadi nāma na drāk eva vicāra krameṇa tu pramāṇayiṣyate tathā hi nirūpa adhi śarīra buddhi tad samudāya ālambana tvena aham pratyayasya atiprasaḍgāt sva saṃbandhini śarīrāt au= ayam ahaṃpratyayaḥ iti vācyam 
NVTP_1.1.10.7^1	 tatra ātma vyatirekeṇa kaḥ sva arthaḥ iti cintanīyam ananya tvam sva tvam sarva bhāvānām tathā ca yadā tena eva tat anubhūyate tadā pratyetuḥ pratyetavyāt ananya tvāt aham iti syāt atas eva ghaṭa ādayaḥ na kadācid api ananya anubhavitṛkāḥ iti na kadācid api aham āspadam iti ced evam tarhi tvad mate api ayam aham iti pratyayaḥ śarīra ādau= āroparūpaḥ eva tatas pratyetuḥ anyatvāt buddhau mukhyaḥ iti ced na tasyāḥ kriyā tvena anubhūyamānāyāḥ bhinnasya tat kartuḥ aham chinadmīti vat aham jānāmi iti anubhavāt nīla ādi pratyeta vyākāra vat pratipattra ākāraḥ api pratīteḥ eva ayam ātmā tathā bhāsate iti ced tarhi pratyeta vyākāra samāna yogakṣema tvena pratipatra ākārasya api siddham naḥ samīhitam 
NVTP_1.1.10.7^2	 astu sva upādāna mātram iti ced na tad pratibhā āsane tad gata artha ākārasya api pratibhāsa prasaḍgāt ākāram antareṇa ākāriṇaḥ anavabhāsanāt pravṛtti vijñāna saṃtānāt anyaḥ eva ayam buddhi saṃtānaḥ pratipattā yama ālaya vijñānam ācakṣate iti ced evam tarhi pravṛtti vijñāna upādānam anādinidhanaḥ siddhaḥ adhikaḥ pratipattā sa kim saṃtanyamāna jñāna rūpaḥ tad viparīta rūpaḥ vā iti cintā pariśiṣyate tasyāḥ ca raṅga bhūmiḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅga bhaṅgaḥ iti atas āha parā iti dṛḍhataram viśeṣa niṣṭham smṛtyā saha pūrva apara pratyayayoḥ eka viṣaya tva mūka jñāna gocara tvam pūrva anubhūti tad kārya smṛti tad kārya anubhūtīnām ekena anuvyavasāyena 
NVTP_1.1.10.8^1	 etena pratisaṃdhānam pratyabhijñānam vā syāt kārya kāraṇa viśeṣayoḥ eka saṃtāna niyamaḥ vā ādye tattvataḥ pratyabhijñānam asiddham abhimānataḥ viruddham aviśiṣṭam anaikāntikam dvitīye api virodhaḥ eva iti nirastam tat āha tat anena iti tat atra pratisaṃdhāne kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pareṇa upanyastaḥ kim upādhi tayā vipakṣa vyāvṛtti saṃdeham udbhāvayitum atha sva darśane pratisandhāna vyavasthām pratipādayitum pratisandhānasya tu kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhanam eva bādhanam iti āśayaḥ tatra pratyabhijñānam pratisandhānam iti gṛhītvā upādhi lakṣaṇam apaninīṣān kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratisandhānayoḥ paraspareṇa vyāpti khaṇḍayati na hi yatra iti punar bauddhaḥ na hi kārya kāraṇa bhāva mātram pratisandhāna nibandhanam ācakṣmahe 
NVTP_1.1.10.8^2	 kim tarhi sādṛśya viśiṣṭam iti śaṅkate vastutas iti tat idam uktam sa bhāgeṣu iti etat vyatireka vyabhicāreṇa dūṣayati tat na iti viśiṣṭaḥ api kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na pratisandhānam prati prayojakaḥ yatas tad nivṛttau= api na idam nivartate iti arthaḥ na ca sādṛśya mātram eva astu tat nibandhanam iti sāmpratam bheda grahe tasya api vyabhicārāt tad agraha pakṣaḥ tu vācyaḥ iti tam upekṣya asmad abhipretam pratisandhānam ādāya śaṅkate pūrva aparā iti yatra kartari pratisandhānam tatra avaśyam pratisandhayānām buddhīnām kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ yatra ca eṣaḥ eva bhūtaḥ tatra avaśyam kartṛ pratisandhānam iti na vyabhicarati iti arthaḥ dūṣayati hantā iti nairātmya sākṣātkāra sātmībhāvaḥ iti sarvajña upalakṣaṇa param 
NVTP_1.1.10.9	 tat ayam arthaḥ sarvajñaḥ tāvat ubhaya vādya vivāda viṣayaḥ sa kimātmanaḥ pūrva apara pratyaya aneka kartṛka tayā pratisaṃdhatte na vā ādye tad pratisandhānāt eva pratisandhātuḥ eka tvam siddham jñānānām bhedasya dhiyām asthaiḥ yasya sarvaiḥ eva pratīteḥ pratisandhātuḥ kṣaṇika tāyāḥ sarvajñena api apratīteḥ atha na pratisandhatte na tarhi kārya kāraṇa bhāva nibandhanam kartari api pratisandhānam na hi asti saṃbhavaḥ yat anvaye api yasya ananvayaḥ tat tāvat mātra nibandhanam iti sā eva ca ityādi sa utprāsam vyarthaḥ iti sva nibandhana anuvṛttau sattva dṛṣṭeḥ durapahnava tvāt avaśyam ca tasya pratisaṃdhānena bhavitavyam katham anyathā upadiśet avaśyam ca upadeṣṭā svīkartavyaḥ yadi pāralaukiker athe vipralambhakāḥ eva vaktāraḥ iti niścayaḥ saṃbhāvanayā api prekṣāvantaḥ na pravarteran tasmāt ubhayathā api pratisandhātuḥ eka tvam siddham 
NVTP_1.1.10.10	 atra śaṅkate atha asat api iti tatas ca na kāṣa kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na tasya nibandhanam avyabhicārāt na api anupadeśa prasaṅgaḥ tad nibandhanasya pratisandhānasya bhāvāt na api doṣa avakāśaḥ sva rasa vāhinaḥ tasya tad hetu tvāt asya tu āhārya tvāt iti arthaḥ śaṅkate na ca iti saḥ ayam kārya kāraṇa abhāve sati eva draṣṭavyaḥ upadeśaḥ tu pūrva pratisandhāna bala upanīta karūṇa abhyāsa prakarṣāt eva virodha pratisandhāna balena suptasya iva prabodhaḥ iti śaḍka arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.10.11	 uttaram pravṛtti iti na ca sphaṭika vat viṣaya uparāga parihāreṇa buddhiṣu bheda grahaḥ iti yuktam sphaṭika vat upādhi parihāreṇa buddhīnām pratyetum aśakyatvāt tathā abhāve buddhi mātreṇa bheda agrahe pārthiva tayā vṛkṣāt kāṣṭham kāṣṭhā t aḍgāraḥ tatas bhasma ādi bhedena na gṛhyeta gṛhyate ca tasmāt nimitta vyāvṛttau pratisandhānam na syāt bhavat vā nimitta antaram ākṣipati iti arthaḥ na ca upadeśaḥ pratisandhānam antareṇa samarthitaḥ syāt sa hi vivakṣā ya ūniḥ sā ca saḍketita śabda smaraṇa ādi yoniḥ tat eva ca pratisandhānam 
NVTP_1.1.10.12	 nanu ālaya vijñāna bheda agrahāt pratisandhānam bhaviṣyati iti atas āha ālayā iti sa hi ālaya santānaḥ aham āspadam pravṛtti vijñānāt anyaḥ eva syāt tad antar pātikādācitka aneka ahaṃpratyaya rupaḥ vā na tāvat ādyaḥ na hi aham ahamikayā paraspara svatantra santāna dvayam anubhūyate sati api vā parasparam anupādāna an upādeya bhāvāt na paraspara pratyākalita artha anusandhāna bandhaḥ tathā tve vā caitra maitra ādiṣu api prasaṅgaḥ ubhayoḥ vā ubhaya upādāna tve ekam api aneka āśritam iti kim aparāt dhama vayavi saṃyoga ādibhiḥ na 
NVTP_1.1.10.13	 cālaya vijñāna upāttam pravṛtti vijñānam na kiñcid upādattaḥ iti api yuktam tathā sati nimitta tām api na yāyāt upādāna tva vyāpta tvāt nimitta tāyāḥ evam ca yadi jñāna antaram upādadīta tadā apūrva ananta santāna pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt na ālaya santānaḥ ānubhavikaḥ na ca aupapattikaḥ iti arthaḥ dvitīye tu āha aham iti 
NVTP_1.1.10.14	 ayam āśayaḥ asya hi bheda āgrahaḥ svarūpataḥ vā syāt viṣayataḥ vā svarūpataḥ api pūrvā aham iti pratyaya mātrāt vā pravṛtti vijñānebhyaḥ api vā na tāvat ādyaḥ aham iti ajñāsiṣam aham iti jānāmi aham iti jñāsyāmi iti atīta tva ādi pratīteḥ bheda niścayam antareṇa anupapatteḥ kathañcid bheda āgrahe api tad arthasya eva pratisandhānam ucitam na pravṛtti vijñānānām na ca tebhyaḥ api bheda āgrahaḥ iti ca uktam eva na api viṣayataḥ sa hi su a ākāraḥ vā syāt 
NVTP_1.1.10.15^1	 vastu antaram eva vā alīkam vā na ādyaḥ prāk dūṣaṇena eva gata tvāt na hi anena su ākāraḥ sva ātmanaḥ bhedena āropitaḥ api tu sva ātma viṣayaḥ eva darśitaḥ tasya ca bhedaḥ niścitaḥ iti na api dvitīyaḥ svayam anabhyupagamāt na api tṛtīyaḥ aham iti vikalpasya sa vastuka tāyāḥ prāk eva prasādhanāt avastuka tve api na tatra prakṛta upayogi bheda agraha saṃbhavaḥ sa hi vidyamānaḥ eva bhedaḥ na gṛhyate avidyamānaḥ eva vā āropitaḥ vā āropita asattvaḥ vā na tāvat ādyaḥ alīkasya ajñāyamāna bheda sampattau= analīka tva prasaḍgāt na api dvitīyaḥ pāramārthikasya bheda abhāvasya pāramārthika abheda paryavasāyi tvāt 
NVTP_1.1.10.15^2	 na ca paramārthataḥ eva nānā vikalpa ullikhitam alīkam eka ātmakam anātmaka tvāt tathā tve vā kva bheda agrahasya upayogaḥ eka tvāt eva eka tvena anusandhānāt na api tṛtīyaḥ virodha parāhata tvāt yadi hi tatra bheda āropaḥ katham tat agrahaḥ tad agrahe vā katham bheda āropaḥ na ca bheda ārope abheda āropasya api avakāśaḥ na api caturthaḥ ātma āśraya prasaṃgāt pāramārthika bheda prasaḍgāt ca ghaṭa paṭayoḥ yaḥ bhedaḥ pāramārthikaḥ śaśa viṣāṇa nara viṣāṇayoḥ vā yaḥ bhedaḥ kālpanikaḥ saḥ iha na gṛhyate iti abheda anusaṃdhānam iti ced na anya viṣaya bheda agrahe anyatra abheda ārope ati prasaḍgāt catuṣkoṭi vinirmukta vyapadeśya bheda agrahe tu abheda ārope trailokya eka tāra upaprasaṅgaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.10.16	 tatra bheda grahaḥ api asti iti ced tarhi yathābhūtaḥ bhedaḥ tatra gṛhyate tad agrahe eva abhedāropaḥ iti eva sādhu na ca etat alīka viṣaya tva pakṣe saṃbhavati iti sthira vastu gocara tvam eva sattva buddheḥ jyāyaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ tu niṣetsyate iti bhāvaḥ tat ida mukta rūpam pratisandhānam nimittavat tayā vyāptam nirnimitta tve niyama anupapatteḥ tat ca aneka kartṛ tve na asti iti vyāpaka anupalabdhyā vipakṣān nivartamānam nimittavati eka kartṛka tve viśrāmyati iti pratibandha siddhiḥ iti anena abhiprāyeṇa upasaṃharati tasmāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.10.17	 tat etat sarvam buddhīnām upādāna upādeya bhāvam abhyupetya uktam vastutas tu tatra eva ayam vivādaḥ tathā hi vyavahita kālāḥ api pratyayāḥ yadi eka kartṛkāḥ kva buddhīnām upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ sa ced kva teṣām eka kartṛka tā sā hi ekopādāna tā eva na ca eka jātīya tve sati tad utpattiḥ eva upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ śiṣyaḥ pādhyāya buddhyoḥ api tathā abhāva prasaṅgat bheda agrahe satī iti api na yuktam samasta upādhi svīkāra parihāreṇa śiṣya ācārya buddhyoḥ api bheda agrahāt sa upādhi bheda grahasya prakṛte api bhāvāt śarīra bheda āgrahasya janma antareṇa vyabhivacārāt anupalabdha pitṛkeṇa bālena ca ati prasaḍgāt ghaṭakapāla kṣaṇayoḥ atathā bhāva prasaḍgāt c eka ādhāra tā niyamaḥ iti api na yuktam tasya vāstavasya kṣaṇika pakṣe viṣaya samayānām kṣaṇānām abhāvāt kālpanikasya tu ati prasaṃjaka tvāt asti hi sarveṣām abhimānaḥ yatra eva ghaṭe 
NVTP_1.1.10.18–1.1.10.19	 gandhaḥ tatra eva rūpa rasa sparśāḥ iti yatra eva śarīram tatra eva jñānam iti etena ca abhrānta samatā eka avasāyaḥ prakṛti vikriye tatas hetu phalasya upādāna upādeya lakṣaṇam iti nirastam kāṣṭhasya tu prakṛteḥ vikṛti ḥ aḍgāraḥ iti kutas niścitam bhavatā yāvatā vahneḥ eva asau vikāraḥ kim na syāt vahni saṃbandhe kāṣṭhāt eva tat utpatteḥ iti ced na kāṣṭha saṃbandhe vahneḥ eva tad utpattiḥ iti evam kim na syāt pārthivam pārthiva upādānakam eva iti niścayāt iti ced kutas etat sa bhāgeṣu kṣaṇeṣu tathā darśanāt iti ced tat api kutas abhrānta samatā eka avasāyāt iti ced na nīla paramāṇuṣu paraspara pratyāsanneṣu nirantaram 
NVTP_1.1.10.20	 jñāyamāneṣu paraspara upādāna tva prasaṃgāt asti hi teṣām tad utpattau satyām mamatā ābhimānika eka tva avasāyaḥ ca pāramārthikaḥ tu na kvacid api astu piṇḍitānām rūpa rasa paramāṇūnām sarveṣā sarva upādāna tvam iti api na yuktam aneka vṛtteḥ ekasya svayam anabhyupagamāt sa prasidhānām samāna deśa tva abhāvāt ca etena bhrānta saṃmata eka avasāyaḥ iti pāṭhā antaram apāḥ tam laukikānām bhrānta saṃmateḥ tatra api tulya tvāt parīkṣakāṇām tu prakṛte api asattvāt tasmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva mātram avaśiṣyate sa ca na upādhiḥ ati prasaṃgāt kiñcid eva sva kāraṇa sāmagrī vaśāt utpadyate jñānam yat kāṃścid eva kāraṇa sāntānikān pratyayān pratyavekṣate na anyat na aparān iti etat api asādhīyaḥ niyāmakam antareṇa śiṣyasya api upādhyāya citta pratyavekṣaka jñāna utpāda prasaḍgāt tatra teṣām anabhisaṃskāraka tvāt na evam iti ced kāraṇa tva jñāna tva aviśeṣe api etat eva kutas vicitrā hi kāraṇānām śaktiḥ tat 
NVTP_1.1.10.21–1.1.10.22	 kim ati nirbandhena yatra yathā kāryam dṛśyate tatra tathā kalpyate iti ced tat kim idānīm kiṃbhūtasya kutra sāmarthyam iti anuyogaḥ anuttaraḥ eva evam tarhi sarvatra jñāpaka janakeṣu anāśvasāt nirīham jagat jāyeta kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhana bādhita tvāt pratisandhāna hetoḥ evam kalpyate iti ced atha anena etat kim na bādhayate tasya nirdeṣa tvāt iti ced asya tarhi doṣa antaram vacanīyam agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tvāt aḥ tu ubhayoḥ sat pratipakṣa tvam iti ced nanu idam api te vyasanam nivartayiṣyāmaḥ mā tu ariṣṭāḥ iti upasaṃhāra śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.10.23^1	 yadi hi sarvajñasya cetasaḥ asmad ādi cittam ālambana pratyaya tvena udāhniyate vaisadṛśyāt daṇḍa ghaṭa vat na pratisaṃdhattaḥ iti api pariharet atas uktam yogi cittam api iti tasya api yogi cittena pratisandhānam syāt iti viparyayaḥ hetu viparyāsasya api saṃbhavāt tasya api yogi cittena pratisandhānam syāt iti viparyayaḥ hetu viparyāsasya api saṃbhavāt saha arthe vā tṛtītā iha anubhavaḥ vā kāla antara bhāvinīm smṛtim janayati jat janitaḥ vā saṃskāraḥ saḥ api atīndriyaḥ adhyakṣa siddhaḥ vā atīndriyaḥ api tad kāla sthāyī saṃtanyamānaḥ vā 
NVTP_1.1.10.23^2	 adhyakṣa asiddhaḥ api tad uttara buddhi dhārā rūpaḥ vā tad anyaḥ vā tad viśeṣaḥ vā viśeṣaḥ api anubhava prasava tva mātram vā anubhavitṛ santāna vaijātyam ca iti tatra prathamam dūṣayati na hi ajāta iti adhyakṣa siddhaḥ tu tad uttara buddhi dhārā rūpāt anyaḥ tāvat anupalabdhi bādhitaḥ taiḥ anabhyupagataḥ ca anubhava prabhavatā mātra lakṣaṇaḥ tu viśeṣaḥ aviśeṣaḥ eva na hi karmakara kara upanītam eva bījam kṣiti māsāt yaḍkuram kurute na tu tathābhūtam api pramāda patitam tathā nīla ādi anubhava santānaḥ pīta ādi anubhavena vā upanīyatām 
NVTP_1.1.10.24	 nīla ādi anubhavena eva vā iti na kaścid svarūpa kṛtaḥ viśeṣaḥ evam ca ananubhūte api smaraṇa prasaḍgaḥ na ca anubhūte api iti vaijātyam tu viśeṣaḥ bhavet yathā kṣīra avasekāt amla tvam parihṛtya mādhuryam ādāya anuvartamāna āmalakī kāla antare api phale mādhuryam unmīlayati lākṣā rasa avasekāt dhavala tām parihṛtya rakta tām upādāya anuvartamānam kārpāsa bījam kusumeṣu rakta tām na ca evam prakṛte saṃbhavati javā kusuma ādi upadhānāt tad rūpa tām parihṛtya dhava limānam upādāya eva saṃtanyamānasya sphaṭikasya iva jñānasya api viṣaya uparāgam parihṛtya cit rūpa tā mātram upādāya anuvṛtteḥ sarva ākāra tvam eva sarva vijñānānām kim tu kaścid ākāraḥ ḥ 
NVTP_1.1.10.25	 sphuṭaḥ anye tu apaṭavaḥ iti tu sva darśana śraddhā yatas viruddha dharma adhyāsāt api na bhīḥ nirākāra pakṣe api yāvān arthaḥ buddheḥ viṣayaḥ tatra sphuṭā eva sā yatra tu asphuṭāḥ na asau tasyāḥ viṣayaḥ tathā tve vā viṣaya itara vyavasthā na syāt tasmāt atīndriyaḥ saṃskāraḥ pariśiṣyate sa ced kāla antara sthāyī nūnam tad upādānam api tathā eva sthāyi na hi upādāna nivṛttau= api upādeyam avatiṣṭhate iti āśayavān āha iti pūrva utpannaḥ iti saṃtanyamānaḥ eva atīndriyaḥ saṃskāraḥ bhaviṣyati iti āśa yavān āśaṅkate punar paraḥ ityādi pṛthak saṃskāra santānaḥ hi na tāvat para abhyupetaḥ na api upapannaḥ ālayasya prāk eva pratiṣedhāt tatas api adhika tve tatra eva smṛti ādi phala prasaḍgāt tasmāt pravṛtti santāne phala an avakāśāt anyatra saṃskāre anyatra phale ati prasaḍgāt tasmāt pravṛtti santāne phala an avakāśāt anyatra saṃskāre anyatra phale ati prasaḍgāt tasmāt pravṛtti santāne phala an avakāśāt anyatra saṃskāre anyatra 
NVTP_1.1.10.26–1.1.10.27	 phale ati prasaḍgāt tasmāt yatra anubhavaḥ tatra saṃskāraḥ yatra ca sa tatra smṛti ādi phalam iti param upapadyate evam ca kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhanam pratirodhakam avaśiṣyate tatra āha upapādayiṣyate hi iti etena yaḥ yaḥ saṃskāraḥ kvacid santānaḥ āhitaḥ sa tatra eva phala dāna yogyaḥ na anyatra ityādi nirastam atiriktasya saṃskārasya āśraya asiddha tvāt viśeṣa lakṣaṇasya ca svarūpa asiddha tvāt aviśiṣṭa uttara kārya pravāha lakṣaṇasya ca viruddha tvāt iti anitya tvasya hetoḥ viśeṣa vyāvartaka tva utkīrtanam guṇa tva siddhi upayogāt atas eva na itaretara āśraya tva śaṅkā 
NVTP_1.1.10.28	 anitya tvena pāratantryam sādhayitvā tena guṇa tva prasādhānāt guṇa tvam tu yad artham sādhitam tat tad sādhakena eva sādhitam iti vaiyarthyam avaśiṣyate tat upasaṃharati tasmāt iti nanu yadi vaiyarthyam asya hṛdi nihitam eva vārttika kṛtā tat kim atham amum eva hetum upanyastavān iti atas āha tat api pūrva mūktam na tu prasādhitam na ca asiddham sādhanam nāma iti kṛtvā iti garbha śoṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.10.29	 ayam arthaḥ yathā anitya tvam dravya pāratantrya avinābhūtam tathā guṇa tvam api yathā ca tad iccha diṣu tathā guṇa tvam api iti na tāvat anayoḥ sādhana tvam prati kaścid viśeṣaḥ kevalam anumāna kāla abhāvaḥ vivakṣitaḥ saḥ api na asti eka hetu siddhe api hetu antara jijñāsum prati bhāvāt ananu saṃhita anitya tvam api tad lakṣaṇa yoga na guṇa tva vyavahāriṇam prati ca 
NVTP_1.1.10.30	 dṛśyate hi icchā ādīnām sāmānyavatām acalana ātmakānām guṇa antara ayogaḥ atra vipratipattau tu anitya tvāt erūpa nyāsaḥ tat ayam apeḥ arthaḥ anitya tvena pāratantryam api sādhayati tad sādhakam guṇa tvam api iti uttara prabandha upayogam āha na ca etat iti dravya pāratantryeṇa viśeṣitena iti śeṣaḥ tat etat viśeṣaṇam kutas siddham iti atas āha yadi api iti 
NVTP_1.1.10.31^1	 ayam āśayaḥ pratyakṣa grahaṇa yogyāḥ tāvat asya avayavāḥ pratyakṣānupalambhena eva nirastāḥ atīndriyeṣu anumānam pramāṇam tat ca dvividham samavyāpti kam asam avyāptikam ca iti tatra yadi api dvitīyasya nivṛttau na sādhya nivṛttiḥ tathā api prathamasya nivṛttau= avaśyam nivarteta tathā hi kvacid upalabhyamāna sparśavat tayā duvyasya ārambhaka tvam kalpyeta ārambhake sati ca tat kārya dravyam sa avayavam vyavasthāpyeta vāyu vat na ca iha kvacid upalabhyamāna sparśa vattā asti iti na ārambha saṃbhavaḥ tad abhāve na sāvayava tvam ākāśa vat tat idam uktam tad avayava kalpanāyām pramāṇa abhāvena iti na tāvat aṇu iti vyāpakam iti arthaḥ viśeṣa niṣadhasya śeṣa abhyanujñā viṣaya tvāt 
NVTP_1.1.10.31^2–1.1.10.32	 kutas ityaḥ āha tatra tatra iti tathā sati eva hi icchā ādīnām sārvatrika tvam upapadyate yatas iti arthaḥ tat upapādayati kvacid iti anyatarat śarīra ādi kvacid svabhāvataḥ kārya dravya utpatteḥ ārabhya tad karaṇa saṃyoga ādeḥ atha gateḥ eva kim na tam tam āpnoti iti atas āha gati kalpanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt gati kalpanā pramāṇam hi mūrtiḥ tayā aparidṛśyamānā api gatiḥ kalpyate manasi paramāṇuṣu ca tad abhāvaḥ ca ātmani tathā hi na paramāṇu āśrayāḥ icchā ādayaḥ anitya tve satyasmad ādi pratyakṣa tvāt śabda vat niravayava t ravya āśrita tvam ca sādhayatā sa avaya āśrita tvam prāk eva nirastam atas amūrta tvāt na gati saṃbhavaḥ mūrteḥ gatyā samavyāptika tvāt iti pūrvavat neyam nanu na etat ekam api vārttika stham iti atas āha tat etat ādi grahaṇa iti nanu tathā api kim anayā kaṣṭa sṛṣṭyā yāvatā guṇa tvam anyathā api amīṣām sādhayitum śakyam tathā hi icchā ādayaḥ guṇāḥ anitya tve sati eka indriya grāhya jātimat tvāt rūpa ādi vat ityādinā iti atas āha tat anayā iti 
NVTP_1.1.11.1	 yasya kṛte apavargaḥ mṛgyate sa tāvat lakṣitaḥ atha idānī puruṣasya apekṣitatama tvāt apavargaḥ lakṣayitum ucitaḥ tat kim antarāle śarīra ādi lakṣaṇam iti atas āha ātmānam ityādi apavargasya abhāva rūpa tvāt pratiyogi adhīna nirūpaṇa tayā duḥkhāt apakarṣaḥ tasya api hetu adhīna utpattika tayā tad hetu rūpebhyaḥ indriya ādibhyaḥ apakarṣaḥ teṣām api śarīram āśritya tathā abhāvāt śarīrāt apakarṣaḥ iti saṃgati saṃkṣepaḥ sākṣāt śarīram āśritya iti indriyāṇām manasaḥ aṃśator atha ādeḥ paramparayā tu śarīra āśrita tvam buddheḥ deṣāṇām artha ādi aṃśasya ca asmin= eva arthe bhāṣyam iti āha tat avatārāya iti 
NVTP_1.1.11.2^1	 atra hi ceṣṭāyāḥ śarīra avyabhicāra pakṣe artha indriya samuccayaḥ anupapannaḥ sambhave vyabhicāre ca viśeṣaṇasya arthavat tvāt samuccaya pakṣe vyabhicāra darśinaḥ katham ceṣṭā āśrayaḥ iti praśnaḥ anupapannaḥ pratyeka vyabhicāre sati eva hi samuccaya sambhavāt atas vikalpam gṛhītvā bhāṣyam utthāpayati atra iti yadi api ceṣṭā kāya vyāpāraḥ tathā api tasya eva lakṣya tvāt itaretara āśraya bhiyā vyāpāra mātram vaktavyam iti āha ceṣṭā vyāpāraḥ iti prayuktasya iti satāt paryam padam atas vyācaṣṭe prayuktasya utpādita prayatnasya iti tena kāraṇa dvārā ceṣṭā nirūktiḥ prayatna vat ātma saṃyoga asamavāyi kāraṇa antya avayavi kriyā ceṣṭā phala dvārā tu hita ahita prāpti parihāra phalā iti tat idam ubhayam vivakṣata uktam api tu viśiṣṭaḥ vyāpāraḥ iti tena phala dvāra nirūktau vyabhicāra udāharaṇam 
NVTP_1.1.11.2^2	 dārūyantra ādi kāraṇa dvāra nirūktau tu prāṇa ākhyaḥ vāyuḥ manaḥ kara caraṇa ādayaḥ tu antya avayavi padena eva nirastāḥ tatra ubhaya vyabhicāram udbhāvayan dārūyantra ādi iti ahā dvayam api pariharati mūrta antarā iti atra ca sparśavat dravya parimāṇam mūrtiḥ iti para lakṣaṇa abhiprāyeṇa mūrti śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ tena ca sparśavat dravya antara aprayoge sati iti arthaḥ prayogaḥ ca kriyaupayikaḥ guṇaḥ sa ca dārūyantra ādau nodana ādiḥ prāṇe tu prayatnaḥ tena yadi api śarīrasya prayojakam manaḥ asti eva tathā api na tat sparśa vat yadi api ca śarīreṇa api tatra prayatyate tathā api na tat tatas anyat tat idam anyara grahaṇa phalam atas na asiddham viśeṣaṇam iti etat ca yathāśrutam bhāṣya vārttika anurodhena viśeṣaṇam āgāmi vārttika parya ālocanāyām tu ceṣṭā śabdaḥ eva ayam evambhūter atha viśeṣe vartate iti na nyūnam sūtram āśaṅkanīyam 
NVTP_1.1.11.3–1.1.11.4	 pāṣāṇa ityādi na ca tasya api prāṇi tvena ucchvāsa niḥśvāsa anumānāt nayana udara ādi avayava saṃkoca vikāśa lakṣaṇā ceṣṭā asti iti vācyam ucchvāsa niḥśvāsa avakāśa abhāvāt antyauvayavinaḥ niṣkriya tvāt ca api ca mṛta śarīra avyāpti parihārāya yogya tā eva śaraṇam na ca udāharaṇam ādaraṇīyam iti nanu yadi api indriyāṇi śarīre na samavayanti tathā api saṃyujyante tāvatā eva āśraya arthaḥ upapannaḥ iti atas vārttikakārasya bhāvam āviṣkaroti saṃyogitayā tu iti yadi api golakasya abhidhāte api cakṣu rūpa hanyate tad anugrahe ca anugṛhyate tathā api viśeṣa anupādānāt sarva indriya abhiprāyam etat draṣṭavyam na hi golaka mātrasya upadhāte anugrahe vā tvac ādīni upahanyante anugṛhyante vā 
NVTP_1.1.11.5–1.1.11.6	 yathā jarā yauvana ādinā śarīra upaghāta anugrahābhyām sarvāṇi vikalāyante paṭūni vā sampadyante iti tat etat bhāṣya vārtti kakārābhyām eva anugṛhyante upahanyante iti bahuvacana prayogeṇa spaṣṭam darśitam iti upekṣitavān na sva rūpeṇa śarīram āśrayante iti avyāpti ati vyāptī vihāya iti śeṣaḥ nanu sukha ādi upalabdhi hetu tvam arthānām kārya upahitam rūpam na tu tat eva kāryam iti atas āha prayojanam tad adhikāreṇa tatra pravṛtteḥ iti tat ayam lakṣaṇa arthaḥ yad avacchinne ātmani arthāḥ bhogam janayanti tat śarīram tena na ātmanā vyabhicāraḥ na hi ātma ātmanā eva avacchidyate na api manasā tasya śarīra anavacchedena pravṛtteḥ abhāvāt na api indriyaiḥ tad avacchedena tatra bhoga utpattau bahis api bhoga prasaṅgat iti tat etat tasya bhogadhiṣṭhānam iti vadatā bhāṣya kṛtāḥ eva prāk darśitam sphuṭam iti 
NVTP_1.1.11.7	 na iha vitanyate codayati iti artha gatim samarthya śabda gatau= iti śeṣaḥ ceṣṭā ādayaḥ sāmānya śabdāḥ iti vārttike bahuvacanam dṛṣṭānta brahmaṇā ādi śabda antarbhāvena āśraya śabda āvṛtti bheda vivakṣayā vā iti atas manda āśaṅka tvāt upekṣitam aśeṣa brāhmaṇa bhojanasya aśakya tvāt iti anupapattivarṇanam sampātāyātamasya pakṣasya agre varṇanīya tvāt atas eva tat upekṣya prakṛta upayuktam vivṛṇoti viśeṣeṇa iti bubhukṣita tva ādinā sannidhīyamānam iti anena sambandhaḥ atra anayoḥ prakaraṇa ādi ityādi pada saṃgṛhītayoḥ madhye iti arthaḥ pramāṇāsambhavaḥ anupapattiḥ bādhaḥ iti arthaḥ yasya api pramāṇena śarīra tvam bādhitam bhavati tatra api vyāpāra śraya tvam gatam iti 
NVTP_1.1.11.8^1	 atha samavāya abhiprāyeṇa iti atra hi indriyā āśrayaḥ iti ṣaṣṭhī tatpuruṣaḥ bahuvrīhiḥ vā tatra samavāya abhiprāyeṇa ubhayam dūṣayati tathā api iti upalakṣaṇam ca etat śarīrasya indriyeṣu iti api draṣṭavyam prathama pakṣe mūrtānām samāna deśatā prasaḍgāt ekasya dravyasya anārambhaka tvāt pṛthivyāḥ ap ādi dravya anārambhaka tvāt ca dvitīya pakṣe tu vijātīyānām anārambhaka tvāt śrotra manasoḥ dravya anārambhaka tvāt iti arthaḥ indriya viśeṣam gṛhṇāti ghrāṇasya iti śliṣṭam vākyam atra ayam anuyogaḥ śarīra avayava antareṇa ghrāṇasya samavāyaḥ vā saṃyogaḥ vā 
NVTP_1.1.11.8^2	 prathame api dvayī gatiḥ ghrāṇasya vā śarīra avayave samavāyaḥ tasya vā ghrāṇaḥ iti tat etat anuyoga dvayam abhipretya āha na tasya iti śarīra avayava samavāyi kāraṇa tvena śarīre asamavāyāt na hi kāraṇam kārya kārye samavaiti iti arthaḥ iti ṣaṣṭha tatpuruṣa pakṣe bahu vrīhi pakṣe api śarīrasya asamavāyāt na hi kāraṇa kāraṇe kāryam samavaitīti arthaḥ ghrāṇasya śarīra avayave samavāyaḥ iti tu na sambhavati eva mūrtayoḥ eka āśraya tva anupapatteḥ iti atra ṭīkā sphuṭāḥ saṃyoga pakṣam gṛhṇāti atha tad ādhāram iti 
NVTP_1.1.11.8^3	 tatra saṃyuktam iti arthaḥ atra api dvayī gatiḥ ārambhaka tayā anārambhaka tayā vā tatra prathamam dūṣayati tathā api iti ārabhyamāṇam hi dravyam aindriyakaiḥ eva avayavaiḥ ārabhyate yathā ghaṭaḥ atīndriyaiḥ eva vā yathā dvi aṇuka ādikam na tu miśraiḥ iti vyāptiḥ tām upobdalayitum apratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ uktaḥ anārambhe tu saṃyogi dravya mātra syāt keśa ādi vat tathā ca na tatra śarīra samavāya sambhavaḥ iti kim anena śaḍkitena api iti upekṣitavān etena śarīra samavetam etat iti nirastam atīndriya dravyasya aindriya keṇa anārambhāt eka dravyasya ca dravyasya abhāvāt 
NVTP_1.1.11.8^4	 alpa parimāṇasya mahatā anārambhāt śarīra vyāpaka tve ca tasya sarvatra gandha upalabdhi prasaḍgāt api ca iti yadi artha śabdaḥ rūpa ādi mātra vacanaḥ tadā evam dūṣaṇam yadā tu indriya viṣaya vacanaḥ tadā vāyavīya śarīra avyāptiḥ yoginaḥ tat api tathā iti yadi tadā indriya paramāṇubhiḥ eva vyabhicāraḥ teṣām api tathā abhāvāt iti tat etat sarvam śabda gatim upekṣya carcitam paramārthataḥ tu yadi dvandva anantaram bahuvrīhiḥ kaḥ liṅga saṅgatiḥ artha saṅgatiḥ ca atha prathamatas eva bahuvrīhiḥ kka ekapadyam iti  
NVTP_1.1.12.1	 indriyasya iti kenacid upādhinā śarīra ādīnām eva phala tvam iti sva bhāvika rūpa pratīti adhīna tvāt ca aupa adhika rūpa pratīteḥ tebhyaḥ phalasya apakarṣaḥ śarīra ādīnām eva dharmaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ dharmi nirūpaṇa adhīna tvāt ca dharmasya tebhyaḥ pretyabhāvasya apakarṣaḥ artha ādīnām doṣa antānām śarīram āśritya duḥkha hetu tva aviśeṣe api paramparayā śarīra āśriya tvāt indriyāṇām tu sākṣāt tathā abhāvāt ebhyaḥ teṣām apakarṣaḥ manasaḥ tu evaṃrūpa tve sati api bāhya indriya vaidharmya jñāpana artha tvāt buddhi krama anumeya tvāt ca buddheḥ sakāśāt apakarṣaḥ tat idam uktam upanāyaka tvena iti sākṣāt śarīram āśritya pratiniyata viṣaya ādi upanaya dvārā duḥkha hetu tvena iti arthaḥ śarīra saṃyuktam sat iti śeṣaḥ atas na ubhaya avadhāraṇe bhāga asiddham asiddham vā iti doṣaḥ sarpa maṇi pradīpa ādīnām tu saṃskāra padena eva nirāsaḥ etāvān= tu viśeṣaḥ yat añjana ādīnām indriya saṃskāraka tvam pradīpa ādīnām tu viṣaya saṃskāraka tvam iti 
NVTP_1.1.12.2–1.1.12.4	 nanu bhāṣya kṛt āha bhoga sādhanāni iti tat katham etat tena sūcitam iti atas āha sākṣāt iti yadi api bhujyeta iti bhogau sukha duḥkhe iti sākṣāt eva bhoga sādhana tvam sarveṣām sambhavati tathā api bhogaḥ buddhiḥ iti tatra tatra bhāṣya darśanāt tad anusāreṇa vyācaṣṭe pāramparyeṇa ca iti yathā ca sāmānya lakṣaṇam antareṇa na viśeṣa lakṣaṇa avasaraḥ tathā vibhāgam antareṇa api iti saḥ api vaktavyaḥ syāt tat etat evaṃlakṣaṇakam indriyam bāhyam ābhyantaram ca iti indri prakaraṇāt manaḥ anyatra nayatā sūtra kṛtāḥ eva sūcitam 
NVTP_1.1.12.5–1.1.12.6	 bāhyam api pañcadhā iti gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdāḥ iti pratiniyata artha vibhāgam kurvatā sūtra kṛtāḥ eva darśitam yadi hi aparam api bāhyam indriyam syāt katham pañca eva pratiniyatāḥ viṣayāḥ iti tat eva vyavacchedyam darśayan= eva manāk smārayati rasanā ādi pratiniyata viṣayam manaḥ ādi sarva viṣayam iti ca ādi grahaṇena ātma śarīre na tu ātma ādi prameya uddeśa sūtre sāmānyena indriya mātram uddiṣṭam iha tu ghrāṇa ityādi ucyate tat katham tatas na viśeṣaḥ iti atas āha pramāṇa ādi udyeśena iti uddeśa viśeṣeṇa atha vibhāga sūtra tve api lakṣaṇa sūtram kim na syāt na hi anayoḥ kaścid virodhaḥ iti atas āha lakṣaṇam hi iti jñātam ca uddiśyate vidhi viṣaya tayā anūdyate iti arthaḥ ajñātam ca vidhīyate jñāpyate iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.12.7^1	 para artha anumāne virodham uktvā sva artha anumāne api āha na api lakṣya lakṣaṇa tve iti lakṣyasya pakṣa rūpa tayā sādhya tvāt lakṣaṇasya ca liṅga rūpa tayā siddha tvāt iti arthaḥ tathā api katham ebhyaḥ eva padebhyaḥ vivakṣita ubhaya lābhaḥ iti atas āha atra ca iti kvacid kvacid sāmānya viśeṣaḥ iti jāti rūpe sādharmya rūpe ca iti arthaḥ tena śrotra padam api avayava artham nimittīkṛtya nabhasaḥ viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa upagṛhīta karṇa śaṣkulī avacchinna tve vartate iti tarhi yogaḥ eva astu iti atas āha avayava artha yoge api iti tathā api ubhaya abhidhāyaka tva aviśeṣe katham lakṣya lakṣaṇa pada vyavasthā iti atas āha tathā ca iti nanu kevalena avayava arthena lakṣaṇe ativyāptiḥ ghrāṇa tva ādi sahitena tu itaretara āśraya tvam iti atas āha na ca iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa yuktasya iti yāvatā vyabhicāraḥ nivartate tāvat upalakṣaṇa param na tu samuccitam padam nirūcyate tvac padam tu anavayavam vṛddhi kṣaya vat dravya sahaja āvaraṇa mātre vartate iti abhiprāyavatā bhāṣya kṛtā lakṣaṇam tat bījam ca darśitam 
NVTP_1.1.12.7^2	 tathā api na prakṛta siddhiḥ na hi evam api lakṣya lakṣaṇa vyavasthā sidhyati iti atas āha nirvacana grahaṇena iti kriyā tvāt iti kāryatvāt iti arthaḥ saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt iti grāhyasya mṛga mada ādi gandhasya tatra asamavāyāt mṛga mada ādīnām sva avayava samavāyena samaveta samavāya abhāvāt svātantryeṇa grahe viśeṣaṇa tva abhāvat aprāptasya ca agrahaṇāt itara sannikarṣa trayasya saṃyoga garbha tvāt saṃyogaḥ siddhaḥ eva iti upakramaḥ atha kaḥ niyama arthaḥ kim yat jātīyam yat indriyam tat tad jātīyasya eva guṇa viśeṣam gṛhṇāti atha yat jātīyam yat indriyam tad jātīyasya tena eva guṇa viśeṣaḥ gṛhyate iti atas āha na ca evam iti yadi api prathamam api avadhāraṇam ghrāṇa śravasoḥ saṃbhavati tathā api rasanā ādiṣu vyabhicārāt tad upekṣya uttaram grahītavyam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.12.8–1.1.13.1	 tathā api bhūtebhyaḥ iti sūtrapadasya kim tātparyam iti atas āha anena khalu iti yadi api viśeṣa siddhiḥ eva śeṣam niṣedhati tathā api viparyaye bādhakam vaktavyam iti atas āha nirākaraṇa hetum āha iti na tu eka prakṛtika tvam āha sāṃkhyaḥ na tu eka svābhāvyam indriyāṇām iti atas āha śliṣṭam padam iti ekaḥ pākyaḥ sarva sādhāraṇaḥ iti śeṣaḥ evam uttaratra api stoka bhṛya sva niḥśeṣa tvena iti prārabdha pāka apekṣayā tathā ca lakṣya hāniḥ iti na hi asti saṃbhavaḥ nirhetukaḥ vyavahāraḥ iti bhāvaḥ indriya prakṛti tvam bāhya indriya prakṛti tvam iti 
NVTP_1.1.14.1–1.1.14.2	 pravṛtteḥ deṣa apakarṣe manasaḥ pravṛtti apakarṣe vakṣyate buddheḥ manaḥ apakarṣe ca uktam viṣaya nirūpaṇīya tvāt carthebhyaḥ buddhet apakarṣaḥ tator atha lakṣaṇam eva krama prāptam iti āha krama prāptam iti sūtre vibhāga bhāgasya api vidyamāna tvāt śliṣṭam tu śabda artham āha yeṣām iti yeṣām ukta lakṣaṇa yogaḥ ta hame vibhajyante iti arthaḥ yeṣām mithyājñāna viṣayīkṛtānām nimitta anuvyañjana saṃjñā viṣayīkṛtānām saṃsāra hetu tvam te hame lakṣyante iti arthaḥ tatra ca ādye pade vibhāga pare tatas tad arthāḥ iti lakṣaṇa padam ced lakṣya padam na asti lakṣya padam ced lakṣaṇam na asti iti ata 
NVTP_1.1.14.3–1.1.14.4	 āha atra ca iti artha animitta anuvyañjana saṃjñā viṣaya tayā saṃsāra hetavaḥ iti arthaḥ ke te yaḥ indriyāṇām arthāḥ viṣayāḥ iti arthaḥ āgāminaḥ vārttikasya bhāṣyeṇa virodham parijihīrṣuḥ āha na ṣaṣṭhī iti ghrāṇa ādayaḥ śabdāḥ iti śeṣaḥ vyadhikaraṇa bahuvrīhau na kevalam lakṣaṇa abhāvaḥ prayojana abhāvaḥ ca iti āha na ca iti tad arthāḥ iti lakṣaṇam avyāpakam syāt iti yadi vāyu ādayaḥ paramārthator athāḥ iti śeṣaḥ ādi grahaṇena vāyu ādi saṃgrahe lakṣaṇa vibhāgayoḥ vyāghātaḥ iti arthaḥ eteṣām ca ityādi tat yathā danta oṣṭham iti anurāgaḥ asthi māṃsam iti vairāgyam śyāmā iti harṣaḥ pākajam idam māṃsa pārthiva rūpam iti mādhyastham mukha āmodaḥ iti pramodaḥ aupādhikaḥ ayam asya sahajaḥ tu pūtiḥ iti vaimukhyam aho 
NVTP_1.1.14.5^1	 madhuram idam etad mukha ā= arjitam tāmbulam iti pravṛttiḥ ucchiṣṭam idam iti nivṛttiḥ preyasī sparśaḥ iti utsavaḥ pārthiva dravya mātra sparśaḥ iti na kiñcid bahu keśī iti anurāgaḥ majja dhātu malāḥ hame bahavaḥ śmaśāne tarau= iva śarīre saṃyuktāḥ iti udvegaḥ pīna stani iti ānandaḥ sphiḍniḥ viśeṣau palala piṇḍau= iti alaṃpratyayaḥ mṛta śarīrāt acetanāt pṛthak iyam iti harṣaḥ cetanāt ātmanaḥ pṛthak iyam sahaja śava bhūta acetanādapṛthak bhāvaḥ tu bhrāntaḥ iti aratiḥ divya mālya ābharaṇa vasanavatī iti prītiḥ pārthivam pārthivena saṃyuktam iti viratiḥ 
NVTP_1.1.14.5^2	 hasati iti harṣaḥ asthi māṃsa vibhāgaḥ iti viṣādaḥ mama priyā parāparā vā iti harṣa viṣa ādau śarīra apekṣayā para apara bhāvaḥ na mad apekṣayā iti na kiñcid nṛtyam iti ratiḥ sat pratyaya asat pratyaya karma santānaḥ māyā śarīraḥ iva iti viratiḥ gamya jātīya iti strī iti ca utsāhaḥ tvaṣ māṃsa śoṇita snāyu asthi majja śukra mūtra purīṣa samudāyaḥ ayam caṇḍālī sādhāraṇaḥ iti alaṃbuddhiḥ vakra bhrūḥ ṛju romarājī gabhīra nābhiḥ u unnata payodharā pṛthu nitambā kṛśa madhya iti snehaḥ anna pāna pariṇatiḥ iyam bhedaḥ māṃsa ādi a pacayā apacaya saṃsthāna bhedavatī 
NVTP_1.1.14.6–1.1.14.9	 acirasthāyinī iti nirvedaḥ iti nimatta saṃjñayā saha aśubha saṃjñā iti anuvyañjana saṃjñayā api saha draṣṭavyā iti asti tāvat iha darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha anusandhānam tat idam ekaika viṣayam vā samudāya viṣayam vā tad atirikta vastu viṣayam vā vastu anurodha ākāra viṣayam vā atīka viṣayam vā iti na tāvat ādyaḥ na hi bhavati yat eva rūpam saḥ eva sparśaḥ iti na ca rūpam dvi indriya grāhyam andhasya api nīla pīta ādi prayatyaya prasaḍgāt na ca ekam eva vastu kāraṇa bhedāt anyathā prathate iti yuktam anātmaka tva prasaḍgāt bheda abheda vyavasthā anupapatteḥ ca 
NVTP_1.1.14.10^1	 na api dvitīyaḥ sa hi eka deśa tayā vā eka kāla tayā vā eka kārya tayā vā eka kāraṇa tayā vā iti na tāvat upādāna lakṣaṇa eka deśa saṃbhavaḥ tayoḥ pratiniyata upādānāt saṃbhave vā tat eva dravyam iti paryavasitam vivādena na api adhikaraṇībhūta bhū tala ādya ādhāra tayā tad saṃbhavaḥ tathā hi cakṣuṣā upalabhyamāne bhū tale rūpa viśeṣe ghaṭaḥ api cakṣuṣā eva upalabhyamānaḥ rūpa viśeṣaḥ tad ādhāraḥ iti śakyate niścetum tayoḥ adhara uttara bhāvena eka jñāna saṃsargi tvāt tad adhikaraṇāḥ sparśa ādayaḥ api iti tu kasya pramāṇasya viṣayaḥ na hi sparśa ādayaḥ cākṣuṣe cetasi cakāsati tvacaḥ ayam vyāpāraḥ iti api na yuktam tayā api bhū tale ghaṭa sparśayoḥ eva ādhāra ādheya bhāva pratīteḥ 
NVTP_1.1.14.10^2–1.1.14.11	 na ca samudāyayoḥ eva ādhāra ādheya bhāva anubhavaḥ paraspara āśraya prasaḍgāt eka ādhāra tayā samudāya anusandhānam tad anusandhāne ca eka ādhāra tā anubhavaḥ iti anavasthā prasaḍgāt ca bhūlatasya api hi samudāya tvam kiṅkṛtam iti anuyoga anivṛtteḥ atas eva na eka kāla tayā api tayoḥ eka kāla tāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt bhāve vā rāsabha kara bhayoḥ api eka kāla tayā samudāya tva prasaḍgāt bheda agra hastu atra asaṃbhāvitaḥ eva atas eva na eka kārya tayā api upadeya lakṣaṇasya ekasya kāryasya abhāvāt atas eva eka udakāraṇa kriyā ityādi api na yuktam rūpa ādi atiriktasya udakasya anabhyupagamāt ekaikasya aneka āhārya tve pramāṇa abhāvāt samudāyasya ca asiddheḥ atas eva na eka kāraṇa tayā api nimittam antareṇa samudāya vyavahāre ati prasaḍgāt tṛtīye tu na vivādaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.14.12	 na api caturthaḥ sa hi vijñāna nayam āśritya vā syāt dvi candra ādi vat visaṃvādāt vā sthairya vat bādhakāt vā iti ādye rūpa ādiṣu kaḥ pakṣapātaḥ prāpteḥ artha kriyā sthiteḥ ca na dvitīyaḥ api te dve api rūpa ādīnām eva iti ced na teṣām kim tu tasya eva iti eva kim na syāt bādhakāt iti ced sa yadi krama yaugapadya virodhaḥ kṣaṇikam tāvat astu rakta ārakta ādi virodhaḥ ced paramāṇu rūpam tāvat astu saṃbandha abhāvaḥ iti ced asaṃbaddham tāvat astu katham tadvat pratīyeta iti ced taiḥ saha tathā utpādāt iti parihāraḥ astu bhavatām eva yathā śarīram cetanāvat iti rūpa ādibhiḥ eva samasta artha kriyā siddheḥ kim tad atirikta vastu kalpanayā iti ced na tāvat mātreṇa eva samasta artha kriyā siddheḥ kim rūpa ādi kalpa nayā iti asya api vācāṭa vacasaḥ avakāśa prasaḍgāt pratīyamāna tvāt iti ced 
NVTP_1.1.14.13–1.1.14.15	 tulyam etena eva alīka viṣaya tā nirastāḥ abheda sādhanāni pramāṇāni bādhakam iti tu cintyate iti āśayavān paryanuyoga artham āha sva saṃvedanena iti atra paraḥ āha anākalita samayaḥ iti śeṣaḥ anurañjana ādikayā tu iti atad rūpasya svarūpa saṃkrāntiḥ anurañjanam yathā nīla dravya samparkāt dhavalaḥ api nīlaḥ mahārajana saṃparkāt raktaḥ iti atra nīla ādayaḥ dravya vyapadeśam vihāya rūpa vyapadeśam eva labhante nīla rūpaḥ paṭaḥ rakta rūpaḥ paṭaḥ iti ādi śabdena gandha ādīnām vāsanā ādikāḥ vāsanā ādikāḥ kriyāḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ śabda gati dūṣaṇam etat iti vibhāvayat nirākaraṇam 
NVTP_1.1.14.16	 vivṛṇoti tathā arthasya iti artha gatiḥ api tridhā utpāda mātram vā trailokya vilakṣaṇa utpādaḥ vā sa bhāga santāna bheda utpādaḥ vā iti tatra dvayam dūṣayati iti āha dūṣaṇa antaram iti tṛtīyam utthāpayati iti āha śaṅkataḥ iti dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi viṣaye hi kasmiścid ghaṭaḥ iti vyavahāraḥ sa ced anayā vacaḥ bhaḍgya atiriktaḥ samarthitaḥ siddham naḥ samīhitam iti āha anyatva iti ananya tve vyartha abhidhānam iti tathā sati hi rūpa paramāṇavaḥ sparśa paramāṇavaḥ ca iti eva te ca katham api utpadyantām na kadācid api dvi indriya grāhyāḥ samudāyaḥ ca durūpa pādaḥ tathā ca dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi viṣayaḥ na ekaḥ samarthitaḥ syāt atas niṣprayojanam uttara abhidhānam iti arthaḥ śaṅkataḥ ityādi yadi api kṣaṇika paramāṇu rūpe dravye na kaścid vicāra virodhaḥ tathā api sthira avayavi abhiprāyeṇa śaḍkāḥ saḥ api hi asmākam prasādhya iti atas eva āha eka aneka vicāra asaha tvāt iti asantaḥ iti upalakṣaṇam bāhyān anurodhi jñāna ākāra rūpāḥ iti api draṣṭavyam bījam iti 
NVTP_1.1.14.17–1.1.14.18	 atra prayogaḥ ye ghaṭa ādi pratyayāḥ na satyāḥ te evambhūta samyak pratyaya pūrvakāḥ mithyā pratyaya tvāt taimirika keśa pratyaya vat iti atra ca upādhim udbhāvayati yaḥ tu iti yadi api hi ādi mānanādiḥ iti vibhāgaḥ anupapannaḥ eva tathā hi keyam anāditā kim evaṃrūpa mithyā jñāna pravāha avicchedaḥ kim vā pūrvam api evaṃbhūtasya vibhramasya kadāpi bhāvaḥ na tāvat ādyaḥ asambhavāt dvitīye tu taimirika keśa jñānam api anādi eva anādau saṃsāre viplutasya keśa jñānasya abhūta cara tva anupapatteḥ tathā ca anāditā na upādhiḥ tasyām satyām api keśa jñānasya satya jñāna nimitta apekṣaṇāt 
NVTP_1.1.14.19^1	 na ca viparyaye bādhaka abhāvāt vibhramaḥ ca syāt satya pratyayān anukārī ca iti śaṅkayā bhavitavyam iti vācyam ananyathā siddha anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna siddha kāraṇa bhāva parihāre mithyā pratyayānām ākasmika tva prasaḍgāt satya pratyaya an anukāre ghaṭa ādi pratyayānām apravartaka tva prasaḍgāt ca tathā hi mithyā pratyayāḥ api ābhimānika pākṣikam vā prāmāṇyam upādāya eva pravartayeyaḥ vibhrama tva niścaye tu apravṛtteḥ na ca pramāṇān anukāre prāmāṇya abhimāna saṃśayaḥ na ca pramāṇa bheda āgraha mātreṇa tattva abhimāna saṃbhavaḥ visadṛśa artha gocara tve tasya abhāvāt sadṛśa artha gocara tve tu satya pratyaya anukāraḥ akāmena api svīkartavyaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.14.19^2	 tathā api ghaṭa ādi pratyayānām satya tve kim nibandhanā bauddhasya īrṣyā iti jijñāsum pratibubodhayiṣuḥ āha iti āha tam prati iti avayavinaḥ iti dravya mātra upalakṣaṇa param yadi asmāt iti vārttikam yat tadoḥ vyatyāsena sugamam eva iti upekṣitavān vyakti abhiprāyeṇa anaikāntika tve dahana ayaḥ ga ulakam udāharaṇam vārttika uktam tu vyāghāta sphoraṇāya jāti abhiprāyeṇa buddhi tad viṣayau= udāhāryau asti hi viṣaya āgrahe buddhi jātīya āgrahaḥ na ca abhedaḥ bāhya sthitau satyām guṇa guṇivāda ārambhāt dvividhāṇuḥ śabda ātmakaḥ aśabda ātmakaḥ ca tatra anantaraḥ aṣṭa dravyakaḥ iti kavaḍīkāra āhāra paryantāḥ kāmadhātavaḥ dhyāna āhārāḥ rūpa dhātavaḥ ānanda āhārāḥ arūpa dhātavaḥ iti vibhāgaḥ sā hi iti yatas tvayā eva uktam 
NVTP_1.1.14.20–1.1.14.22	 para rūpam sva rūpeṇa dhiyā saṃvriyate yayā eka artha pratibhāsinyā tām āhuḥ saṃvṛtim kila iti arthaḥ udbhāvana prakāra saṃkalana artham pūrva ukta eka deśam smārayitvā paramatam avatārayati tat evam iti tad atra anaikāntika tvena hetvābhāsaḥ nigraha sthānam tad abhyupeta prāmāṇya āgama vyāghātena apasiddhāntaḥ tad śabda paryālocanayā niṣprayojana tvena apārthakam pratijñā padayoḥ vyāghātena virodhaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.14.23	 ānuśāsanikam vacana bhedam ādāya virodhaḥ udbhāvitaḥ tatas na pāribhāṣikeṇa vyabhicāra śaḍkā samāna arthānām prakṛtīnām iti prakṛte abhyupagama vādaḥ utpanna tad hitāyāḥ prakṛteḥ adhika artha tvāt spārthikasya pratyayasya nirākariṣyamāṇa tvāt nanu āpaḥ iti api toya gatām eva bahu tva saṃkhyām ācaṣṭām kaḥ doṣaḥ iti atas āha iti ekasyām api iti yadi upanibandhena yadi toya paramāṇau= api āpaḥ iti śiṣṭa prayogaḥ tadā evam na iyam vastutas tu yathā eka vacanāt toyam anuśāsana balāt asādhuḥ tathā eka saṃkhyā avacchinne pāthasyapi iti na kaścid virodhaḥ dārāḥ iti atra tu eṣā eva yuktiḥ iti arthaḥ krandate iti anādare ṣaṣṭhī bhavataḥ iti pūraṇīyam 
NVTP_1.1.14.24–1.1.14.26	 ṣaṇṇagarīti ādiṣu tu sugamam eva samāhāre samāsa anuśāsanāt sa ca samāhriyamāṇa artha atiriktaḥ eva abhyupagamyate asmābhiḥ yadi yathāloka vyavahāram ādriyase kim iti sa vikalpakam pratyakṣam pariharasi kutas ca na śabda ādīni pramāṇāni pṛthak eva abhyupagacchasi iti āha anyathā iti vārttika ukta udāharaṇa anurodhena ahnīkam pratyāha na ca nīlasya iti vastutas tu pīta śaḍkha vibhrame ayam api na pītasya eva śaḍkhasya utpādam icchati puruṣa antareṇa api tathā upalambha prasaḍgāt tatas 
NVTP_1.1.14.27^1	 dhavalimni pratīte api tad āśrayam śaḍkha dravyam abhipretya iti eva toya virahaḥ ityādi na ca etat vaidharmya mātram upaṣṭambhakasya avinirbhāgena eva avasthāna niyamāt yathā hemni pārthivaḥ bhāgaḥ taile payasi sarpiṣi ca pāthasīyaḥ na ca saṃyogi mātram yūṣe jalam tad asaṃyoge yūṣa tva nivṛtteḥ iti taiḥ vyapadeśaḥ taiḥ viśeṣaṇaiḥ tasya vyavacchedyasya vyavacchedaḥ sa ca atra anubhavikaḥ vivakṣitaḥ sa hi evam pravartate candanaḥ ayam surabhiḥ tiktaḥ śuklaḥ śītaḥ iti tādātmya bhrama nirāsa artham tu śabdaḥ vyapadeśaka tayā upāttaḥ candanasya śuklam rūpam ityādi etat ca āgambhīram iti matvā yathāśrutam eva upādāya tātparya mahā asti hi iti 
NVTP_1.1.14.27^2	 na kevalam hetu svarūpa ālocanena pratijñā locanena api candanasya upālambha abhyupagamaḥ avasīyate parasya na hi anupalabdhasya eva rūpa ādi abhedam sādhayati tathā satya prasiddha viśeṣyaḥ pakṣaḥ syāt svātantryeṇa vā sattve sādhye āśraya asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti tṛtīye vyutpādanīyam iti iha upekṣitavān iti ekāntataḥ vyapadeśam vyāvartayitum iti prayoga antara sūcanāya tathā hi ayam cakṣuḥ gocaraḥ candanaḥ rasa ādibhyaḥ bhidyate tad anupalambhe api etasya upalabhyamāna tvāt yadi asmin= anupalabhyamāne api upalabhyate tat tatas bhidyate yathā rūpa ādibhyaḥ śabdaḥ tathā ca ayam candanaḥ tasmāt tathā iti spa mātrāt tu vyavacchedaḥ sandigdhaḥ tatra vyapadeśaḥ hetuḥ iti 
NVTP_1.1.14.28^1	 prayoga antaram āha iti vailakṣaṇyasya hetoḥ vyakti apekṣayā anaikāntika tvāt jāti apekṣayā asiddha tvāt viṣaya vailakṣaṇyasya ca sādhya tvāt tad āhita ākāra lakṣaṇasya anabhyupagamāt iti a āśayavān iti śeṣaḥ atra ca hetu tayā vyāpti pradhānīkṛtya ṣaṣṭhī antaḥ heturūktaḥ pañcamī antaḥ ca sādhyaḥ parvataḥ ayam agnimān kasmāt dhūmavat tvāt kim kāraṇam dhūmavataḥ agnimat tvāt iti vat grantha gaurava bhiyā tu yathāśrutam vyācaṣṭe ghaṭa pratyayasya iti viṣayaḥ ghaṭaḥ eva nimittam ghaṭa tvam tat hi nimittīkṛtya ghaṭa pratyayaḥ ghaṭe vartate ghaṭa pratyayaḥ tu anubhavaḥ smaraṇam ca 
NVTP_1.1.14.28^2	 tat iyam prayoga pariśuddhiḥ ghaṭa ādiṣu eka ādi pratyayāḥ ukta nimitta vyatirikta pravṛtti nimitta adhīna janmānaḥ ukta nimittam antareṇa api jāyamāna tvāt teṣu eva ghaṭa ādiṣu nīla ādiṣu nīla ādi pratyaya vat iti atra yadi ghaṭa manatareṇa api jāyamāna tvāt iti etāvat mātram kriyeta tadā eka ghaṭa parityāge ghaṭa antare jāyamāna ghaṭa pratyayena vyabhicāraḥ tathābhūtasya api nimitta antara anapekṣa tvāt tad nimittam antareṇa iti etāvat mātre tu ghaṭa nirvikalpakena vyabhicāraḥ tasya tad nimitta nirapekṣasya api nimitta antara anapekṣaṇāt tad pratyayam antareṇa iti etāvat mātre api tena eva vyabhicāraḥ 
NVTP_1.1.14.28^3	 prathama dvitīya pada upādāne api tad smaraṇa anuvyavasāya vibhramaiḥ vyabhicāraḥ tad pratyaya viṣaya nimitta vyatirekeṇa api teṣām janma na ca pravṛtti nimitta antara apekṣā dvitīya tṛtīyayoḥ api nirvikalpakena vyabhicāraḥ prathama tṛtīyayoḥ api ghaṭa antara pratyayena vyabhicāraḥ iti samasta upādānam atas yat nyūnam tat pūrayati bhājaḥ iti atra api iti tat etat ghaṭa ādi pratyaya vailakṣaṇyam eka ādi pratyayānām iti sthāṇuḥ dravyam iti evam sādhu na ca jāti saṃkaraḥ tatra khadira jāteḥ abhāsāt tad guṇa yogāt tu tad vyavahāraḥ māṇavake siṃha vyavahāra vat tad avayava ārabdha tvāt tadīyatā vyavahāraḥ kṣīrasya dadhīvivat 
NVTP_1.1.14.28^4	 sarpeṇa antyauvayavinā ekena anārambhāt tad avayavānām kārya avaṣṭabdha tvāt sarpa kuṇḍalakam saṃsthānam eva sphuṭam pratimāyāḥ iti śarīra lakṣaṇa abhāvāt na tatra mukhyaḥ śarīra śabdaḥ tad eka artha sama vesaṃsthāne aupacārikaḥ iha prayujyate tad sādṛśyāt rāhoḥ śiraḥ iti atra tu saṃsthāne śiraḥ śabda upacāra mātram suvarṇa āsyāj gurīyakam iti atra jāti saṅka prasaḍgāt saṃsthānam eva aḍgurīyakam rajata ādeḥ api aḍgurīyaka darśanāt iti sphuṭam śilāputrakasya iti atra ukta yukti smārayan= āha evam iti vyatireka upadeśa vivekaḥ yadi syāt tadā buddhi śarīrābhyām eva anaikāntikam syāt atas āha atādātmya iti 
NVTP_1.1.15.1–1.1.15.3	 artha kathana pūrvakam saṅgati vārttikam avatārayati ātma ādīnām iti kāraṇa tve api manasaḥ apakarṣe tu uktam sarva janīnena api samayena go śabda vat yadi artha antare api ete pravarteran tadā kaḥ virodhaḥ iti atas āha tatra sarva janīnaḥ śaknoti iti sva abhidheya dvāreṇa iti śeṣaḥ tena ayam arthaḥ eteṣām śabdānām vyavahriyamāṇānām yat ekam pravṛtti nimittam tad yogāt itarebhyaḥ buddhiḥ bhidyate iti tat idam uktam sūtra kṛtā iti anarthāntaram iti tena etat nirastam gṛhīta samayaiḥ ebhiḥ bṛddhiḥ samāna asamāna jātoyebhyaḥ vyāvartanīyāḥ tathābhūtāyām ca tasyām eteṣām samayaḥ grāhyaḥ iti anyonya āśraya tvam vyavahāre tu sādhye 
NVTP_1.1.15.4	 ātma āśraya tvam iti tarhi buddhiḥ jñānam iti eva astu kim aneka śabda uccāraṇena iti āśaḍkya paramatam apākartṛm iti āha bhāṣya kāraḥ eva iti sphuṭam iti upapatti sārthyāt iti bhāṣya avayayavam vyācaṣṭe paryāya iti tatra upapatti padārthaḥ paryāya śabda abhidhānam iti anene vyākhyātaḥ śeṣeṇa sāmarthya padārthaḥ tena ayam arthaḥ paryāya śabda abhidhāna lakṣaṇāyāḥ upapatteḥ sāmarthyam aneka artha tva pratiṣedha ākṣepaka tvam tasmāt iti 
NVTP_1.1.15.5^1	 tat etat nirākāraṇam sūcitam yat upapatti sādhyam tām pṛcchati vārttikakāraḥ kā punar ūpa pattiḥ atra iti nirvikalpa kavya apārāṇi indriyāṇi sa vikalpaka vyāpāram manaḥ adhikāra abhimāna vyāpāraḥ ahaṅkāraḥ kṛtī adhyavasāya vyāpārā buddhiḥ nirvyāpāraḥ eva kalpita buddhi vyāpāraḥ puruṣaḥ iti tena ayam arthaḥ akāraṇam akāryaḥ ca puruṣaḥ ādi kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ādi kāryam buddhiḥ tatas ahaṅkāra ādi sargaḥ iti puruṣaḥ kūṭastha caitanya rūpaḥ itarat a cetanam iti sa ākhyāḥ tatra buddhiḥ aṃśa trayavatī puruṣa uparāgaḥ viṣaya uparāgaḥ vyāpāra āveśaḥ ca iti aṃśāḥ bhavati hi mayā idam kartavyam iti 
NVTP_1.1.15.5^2–1.1.15.8	 mayā iti hi cetanā uparāgaḥ darpaṇasya iva mukha uparāgaḥ bheda agra hāda tāttvikaḥ idam iti viṣaya uparāgaḥ indriya praṇālikayā pariṇāti bhedaḥ darpaṇasya iva mala saṃbandhaḥ pāramārthikaḥ tat ubhaya āyattaḥ vyāpāra āveśaḥ api iti tatra evaṃrūpa vyāpāra lakṣaṇā buddhiḥ viṣaya uparā lakṣaṇam jñānam tena saha yaḥ puruṣa uparāgasya atāttvikasya saṃbandhaḥ darpaṇa pratibimbitasya mukhasya iva tad gata mali nimnā sa upalabdhiḥ iti teṣām rahasyam tat utthāpayati buddhiḥ kila iti sā ca na tāvat buddheḥ tasyāḥ acaitanyāt iti yadi api acetanaḥ eva bhrāmyati iti sāṃkhya abhyupagamaḥ yathā āhuḥ yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti tāḥ tu pramāṇa saṃśaya viparyaya svapna smṛtayaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.15.9	 iti tathā api vyāptyā pratyavasthānam yatra hi cetanā cetanayoḥ asaṃsarga agrahe saṃsarga bhramaḥ tādātmya bhramaḥ vā tatra cetanasya eva yathā darpaṇa caitrayoḥ śarīra śarīriṇoḥ vā na hi tatra darpaṇasya śarīrasya vā bhramaḥ iti api ca buddhiḥ ātmānam cetayamānāḥ bhrāmyet puruṣeṇa vā ca ityamānāḥ na ubhayam api prāk ukta yukteḥ eva na ca svatas paratas vā aprakāśa mānā eva buddhiḥ bhrāmyati iti yuktam na hi adṛśyamānaḥ eva darpaṇaḥ timire maitra sannidhāna mātreṇa tad pratibimbam udgrāhayati tasmāt ubhayathā api buddheḥ sahajam caitanyam āpannam iti upasaṃhāra vyājena āha tasmāt kṛpaṇa iti 
NVTP_1.1.16.1–1.1.16.2^1	 vaidharmyāt indriya prakaraṇāt apasāritasya buddhi krama unneya tayā pravṛtti hetu tayā ca tayoḥ madhyer atha ādavasaraḥ manasaḥ iti āha krama praptam iti yasmāt ityādi vārttikam vākya bhedena sūtrakāra ukta sva ukta hetu papādaka bhāṣya vyākhyānam iti āha anindriyā iti yadi api nimitta antaram iti anena eva ākāśaḥ api vyavacchidyate avyāpi iti anena eva vā sahakārī iti anena eva ātma ādi upādāna atiriktasya eva sahakāri tva prasiddheḥ tathā api yathā vivakṣam go balīvarda nyāyena vyavasthā indriyam pradhānīkṛtya vā ātmani sahakārivādaḥ iti nanu manaḥ vibhu sarvadā sparśa rahita dravya tvāt viśeṣa guṇa śūnya dravya tvāt nitya tve sati anārambhaka dravya tvāt jñāna samavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt iti ādeḥ tat katham ucyate avyāpi iti na etat evam sa veṣām eṣām āpātatas svarūpa asiddha tvāt tathā hi yadā sukha ādi upalabdhīnām kriyā tvena karaṇa tayā manaḥ anumitam tadā na dravya tva siddhiḥ adravyasya api karaṇa tvāt atha āsām eva sākṣātkāritayā indriya tayā tad anumātavyam tathā api śarīravayavasya upādhi tvam tadā tāvat mātre vṛtti lābhaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.16.2^2	 tad doṣe ca vṛtti nirodhaḥ śrotra vat prasajyeta tatas śarīra mātram upādhiḥ abhidheyaḥ tathā ca tad avacchedena vṛtti lābhe śirasi me vedanā pāde me sukham iti ādya vyāpya vṛtti tva pratīti virodhaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa anurodhena vibhu kāryāṇām deśa niyamāt śarīra tad avayava avayava paramāṇu paryanta upādhi kalpanāyām ca kalpanā gaurava prasaṅgaḥ niyama anupapattiḥ ca iti tatas anyava ekam sūkṣmam atīndriyam upādhi tvena kalpanīyam tathā api tasya eva indriya tve svābhāvike adhika kalpanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt dharmi grāhaka pramāṇa bādhaḥ atha jñāna krameṇa indriya sahakāri tayā tad anumānam tadā sutarām eva prāc ukta doṣaḥ yadi tu manasaḥ vaibhave api adṛṣṭa vaśāt kramaḥ upapadyate tadā manasaḥ asiddheḥ āśraya asiddhiḥ eva vaibhava hetūnām iti atha yatra adṛṣṭasya dṛṣṭa kāraṇa upahāreṇa upayogaḥ tatra tad pūrṇa tāyām kāryam utpadyate eva anyathā antya tantu saṃyogebhyaḥ api kadācid paṭaḥ na jāyeta jātaḥ api vā kadācid nirguṇaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.16.3^1	 syāt balavatā kulālena dṛḍha daṇḍa nunnam api cakram na bhrāmyet yatra tu dṛṣṭa anusaṃhāreṇa adṛṣṭasya vyāpāraḥ tatra tad veguṇyāt kāryānudayaḥ yathā paramāṇu karmaṇāḥ tat iha api yadi viṣaya indriya ātma samavadhānam eva jñāna hetuḥ tad sadbhāve sadā eva kāryam syāt na hi etat atiriktam api adṛṣṭasya upaharaṇīyam asti na ca sadā eva jñāna udayaḥ tatas atiriktam apekṣaṇīyam asti tat ca yadi api sarvāṇi eva indriyāṇi vyāpnoti tathā api karaṇa dharma tvena kriyā kramaḥ saṃgacchate akalpite tu tasmin na ayam nyāyaḥ pratipad tuḥ akaraṇa tvāt cakṣuḥ ādīnām aneka tvāt tasmāt antaḥkaraṇam asti iti ced nanu evam api yugapad jñānāni mā bhuvan yugapad jñānam tu kena vāryate bhavati eva samūha ālambanam ekam jñānam iti ced na eka indriya grāhyeṣu iva nānā indriya grāhyeṣu api prasaḍgāt teṣu api bhavati eva iti ced na vyāsaṅga kāle jñāna krameṇa vivāda viṣaye krama anumānāt 
NVTP_1.1.16.3^2–1.1.16.4^1	 bubhutsā viśeṣeṇa vyāsaḍge kriyā kramaḥ iti ced na evam na hi eṣa bubhutsāyā mahimā yat abubhutsite viṣaye jñāna sāmagryām satyām api na jñānam api tu tatra saṃskāra viśeṣa ādhāyakaḥ pratyayaḥ syāt yadi tu abubhutsite sāmagrīm eva sā nirūndhyāt tathā ca ghaṭāya unmīlitam cakṣuḥ paṭam na darśayet tasmāt bubhutsāpi indriya antarāt ākṛṣya bubhutsita artha grāhiṇī indriye manaḥ niveśayantī yugapad jñāna anutpattau= upayujyate na tu svarūpataḥ iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ tasmāt suṣṭhu uktam avyāpi iti 
NVTP_1.1.16.3^2–1.1.16.4^2	 gandha ādi kriyā anya tve sati iti vārttikam yathāśrutam dravya karma ādi jñānena anaikāntikam atas vyācaṣṭe cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ iti nanu smṛti ādiṣu saṃskāra ādayaḥ santi tatas na ete karaṇa antara kalpanāyām prabhavanti iti atas āha atra ca iti indriya janmānaḥ śarīra saṃyukta dravya rūpa karaṇa janmānaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu indriya tvena eva manaḥ api janakam smṛti ādīnām tathātve sākṣātkāri tva prasaḍgāt iti atha ityādi vārttike pratibhāsamāna vyadhikaraṇa tām upādāya codyam eka deśi samādhānam ca vyāptiḥ vyadhikaraṇayoḥ aśakya graha iti vastu gatim upādāya samādhānam sphuṭam iti āha sautram iti 
NVTP_1.1.17.1–1.1.17.2	 pretyabhāvāt utkarṣe sati pravṛtteḥ manaḥ apakarṣe hetum āha manasaḥ api iti pravṛtteḥ vikalpa samuccayāmyām avyāpaka tayā na idam sāmānya lakṣaṇam na ca tad antareṇa viśeṣa lakṣaṇa avakāśaḥ iti āśaḍkya sūtra vākyam bhinatti ārambhaḥ pravṛttiḥ janma hetuḥ sthira ātma viśeṣa guṇa janakaḥ prayatnaḥ ārambhaḥ na ca evam dayā ādi avyāptiḥ tatra api tad artham prayatnasya vidyamāna tvāt yadi tvayatamānasya eva icchā mātram jñāna mātram dveṣa mātram vā pravṛttiḥ 
NVTP_1.1.17.3	 syāt pravartamānam prati prayojaka tvam amīṣām nivarteta tatas ca uttara sūtra vyāghātaḥ iti atra yadi api vāc ityādi yathā śruta viśeṣa lakṣaṇa avasare dayā ādi asaṃgrahaḥ iti vuddhi padam manaḥ abhiprāyeṇa vyākhyātam bhāṣya kṛtā tathā api viśiṣṭa devatā ādi anucintana ādi asaṃgrahaḥ iti atas āha sa ca dvividhā iti jñātum jñāpayitum vā prayatnaḥ ubhayathā api jñāna hetuḥ tena vāc gocaraḥ api prayatnaḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ kartum kārayitum vā prayatnaḥ ubhayathā api kriyā hetuḥ tena steya hiṃsā ādau ajñāna ādi gocaraḥ api prayatnaḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ etena yat siddham tat āha tatra iti tad artham prayatnaḥ jñānam janayan jñāpaka hetu viṣayaḥ bhavati iti jñāpaka eka deśena vācā upala kṣaya tā sva samaveta jñāna mātra hetuḥ iti api bhramaḥ nirastaḥ kāya nimittā iti kāyaḥ nimittam viṣaya tayā yasyāḥ sā tathā uktā dāna steya ādi artha yaḥ khalu prayatnaḥ sa kāya viṣayaḥ bhavati evam manaḥ nimittam dayā droha ādi artham yaḥ khalu prayatnaḥ sa manaḥ viṣayaḥ bhavati iti na iyam anyathā na asti eva asau puruṣa vyāpāraḥ yatra kāya manasī na nimittam iti 
NVTP_1.1.18.1–1.1.18.3	 pravarttanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ pretyabhāvāt utkarṣe sati doṣāṇām pravṛtti apakarṣe hetum āha prayojya iti puruṣam pravartayataḥ utka rūpa prayatna yoginam kurute iti arthaḥ ānantaryāt anayoḥ abhidhānam mohaḥ api pravartayati iti draṣṭavyam moha eka artha samavāyaḥ moha saṃskāra eka artha samavavāyaḥ moha antareṇa vā etat eva āha tāvat hi ayam iti tasya arthaḥ iti bhāṣyasya iti bhāvaḥ iti ca udakasya atra ca samavāyaḥ yadi api na vyāpāraḥ tathā api moha ādeḥ pravartakasya sva āśraya samaveta rāga dveṣa moha janana avāntara vyāpārasya pravartaka tvam iti adūra viprakarṣeṇa sambandha sambandhinoḥ etat draṣṭavyam tena phala gocarau moha rāgau moha dvaiṣau vā tad sādhana viṣayau moha rāgau moha dveṣau vā janayantau puruṣam pravartayataḥ tatas phala viṣayāḥ rāga dveṣa mohāḥ pravartakāḥ sādhana viṣayāḥ tu tad eka artha samavāyinaḥ pravartanāḥ iti vastu gatiḥ vyāpāraḥ api ca kārya anuguṇaḥ iti kṛtvā rāga ādayaḥ pravartayanti pravṛtti hetu tvāt doṣāḥ iti ucyatante 
NVTP_1.1.19.1–1.1.19.3^1	 punaru utpattiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ śarīra ādīnām doṣa paryantānām parityāga pūrvakaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ iti tad anantaram eva asya avasaraḥ iti āha uddeśa krama iti nanu pūrva śarīra ādi parityāgāt iti sūtre na asti eva na ca utpatti mātram pretyabhāvaḥ ekasmin= api janmani tathā avyavahāra prasaḍgāt na ca punar śabdasya ayam arthaḥ tasya abhyāsa mātra artha tvāt atas uktam vārttika kṛtā punar iti tat vyācaṣṭe punar iti abhyāsa māha iti abhyāsam vadan= eva na antarīyaka tayā pūrva śarīra diparityāgam pratipādayati iti arthaḥ tathā api kim vakra ukteḥ prayojanam iti atas āha tathā ca iti nanu dvitīya sūtre duḥkha ādīnām kārya kāraṇa bhāva saṃsāraḥ iti uktam iha tu punar u utpattiḥ iti tat kutas na virodhaḥ iti āśayavataḥ vārttika kṛtaḥ ākṣepaḥ kaḥ punar iti duḥkhān dīnām kārya kāraṇa bhāve sati pūrva deha ādi parityāgāt anya deha ādi prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ 
NVTP_1.1.19.3^2	 tatas teṣām tathābhūta pravāha vicchede pretyabhāva apara nāmā saṃsāraḥ vicchidyeta iti tulya pravṛtti nimitta tvāt saḥ eva tatra saṃsāraḥ uktā etyayaḥ na virodhaḥ iti āśayavataḥ parihāraḥ duḥkha ādīnām iti tat etat smaraṇa mātreṇa vyācaṣṭaiḥ tat etat vārttika jātam iti sā iyam ukta rūpā punar u utpattiḥ yadi acetanasya manasaḥ saṃsāraḥ kim iti nivartanīyaḥ atha ātmanaḥ tadā aśakya nivṛttiḥ muktasya api saṃsāri deha ādi parityāgāt tadīya apara deha ādi prāpti saṃbhavāt iti āśayavatā vārttika kṛtā śaḍkitam saḥ ayam iti na iyam bhogena viśeṣitā punar u utpattiḥ saṃsāraḥ iti āśayavatā parihṛtam yadi iti tatra asphuṭam padam sphuṭayati kriyām iti 
NVTP_1.1.20.1–1.1.20.3^1	 pravṛtti doṣa janitor athaḥ phalam śaḍkām apanayan= eva saṅgati karoti yadi api iti sāmānyena jñātāḥ hi viśiṣṭa tayā jñātum śakyante tatas sāmānya rūpeṇa lakṣitānām viśiṣṭa lakṣaṇa avasaraḥ ubhayoḥ ca ākārayoḥ nirveda upayogāt ubhaya upādānam iti arthaḥ atra ca sūtre pada dvayam atiriktam tatra prathama upayogam āha atra ca iti yadi api svarūpataḥ api pravṛtteḥ kārya bhūtau dharma adharmau prati doṣāṇām atiśayena upayogaḥ vakṣyati ca doṣa tuṣa avanaddhāḥ hi karma taṇḍulāḥ ityādi tathā api pravṛtti phale doṣāṇām upayogaḥ darśanīyaḥ sūtre prakṛta tvāt 
NVTP_1.1.20.1–1.1.20.3^2	 na ca dharma adharmayoḥ phala vyavahāraḥ tatas vyāpāra dvāram upādāya upayogam āha api tu iti tat eva dvāram sphorayati doṣa salilā iti atas dharma adharma śrutyāḥ na lakṣaṇā bhramaḥ kartavyaḥ svarūpataḥ tu pravṛtti prati doṣāṇām sahakāri tvam sūtrakāraḥ eva caturthe vakṣyati iti tat kim nirdeṣasya sukha duḥkhe na staḥ iti upātta karma pracayasya tādavasthyam adatta phalasya eva vā vināśaḥ iti atas āha na ca asti iti na brūmaḥ nirdeṣasya upabhogaḥ eva na asti api tu yādṛśaḥ saṃsāra hetuḥ tādṛśaḥ na asti doṣa antara janakaḥ hi tādṛśaḥ iti arthaḥ artha padasya upayoma āha sūtre iti
