NVTP_1.2.1.1^3	 iha tu tattva nirṇayaḥ jalpe sva śakti parāśakti khyāpanam vitaṇḍāyām para aśakti mātra prakhyāpanam ca phalāni vivakṣitāni tāni ca na kathā mātra sādhyāni iti viśeṣataḥ eva uddeśaḥ tatra yaugikam kathā śabdam upādāya anavasarat ustha tayā bhāṣyam ākṣipya vārttikena samādhatte tat ayuktam ityādinā na ayam kathā śabdaḥ yoga mātra anurodhī api tu sati eva tasmin rūḍhi niyate iti anavasara doṣam pariharan= āha api tu iti nanu pūrva pakṣa uttara pakṣa bala abala nirūpaṇam vicāraḥ sa ca na kathāyāḥ āśrayaḥ kim tu viṣayaḥ iti atas āha vicāra viṣaya iti prauḍha gauḍa naiyāyika mate catasraḥ kathāḥ sa pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ vitaṇḍā iti atra jalpa vat vādasya api parāmarśāt puruṣa abhiprāya anurodhena caturtha udāharaṇasya api upapatteḥ iti sānātaniḥ ekaḥ eva ayam kathā mārgaḥ iti bāhyāḥ te dve api tisraḥ eva iti niyamayatā nirākṛte tattva bubhutsu kathā ca vitaṇḍā ca iti vyāhatam na hi prathama sādhana nivṛttau= eva tattva nirṇayaḥ niḥsādhanasya tasya anupapatteḥ 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^4	 na api pratipakṣa sādhanam anivartya prathamasya sādhanatva avasthitiḥ śaṅkita pratipakṣa tvāt yadi tu pratipakṣa sādhanam anirūpya eva vijigīṣu vitaṇḍā vat tāvatā eva vādinau kṛtinau na tarhi tattva bubhūt sū evam ca yadi vijigīṣuḥ katham apratibhā ādi anudbhāvanam na ca vijaya tattva nirṇayābhyām phala antaram avaśiṣyate kathāyāḥ yad artham vādavitaṇḍā anutpannasya hi tattva nirṇayasya utpādanam utpannasya pālanam pālitasya ca viniyogaḥ sa ca svayam abhyāsaḥ kāruṇika tayā para vyutpādanam 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^5	 etat ca sarvam kathā traya paryavasitam na api eka kathā nirvāhyam iti nanu etāvatā api na sāmānya lakṣaṇam vibhāvitam iti atas āha tathā ca iti nānā pravaktṛkāḥ mithas karma tayā yuddha vat āliṅgana vat ca etena vākya saṃdṛbdhiḥ mahā vākyam uktam syāt mithas karma tayā sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt vijaya ādi aneka prayojana vat tvāt ca iti vaktroḥ ca praśabdena prakarṣaḥ darśitaḥ sa ca kathā rūpa mahā vākya nirvāhaka tvam tathā ca svasthaḥ sarvañjana pratyayānapalāpī mata mātra avalambī avahitaḥ akalahakāraḥ ca iti kathā adhikāriṇaḥ darśitāḥ viparyayeṇa heyāḥ iti 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^6	 vasati iti nirukti bhaṅga bhayāt āha artha abhidhānā iti vāda iti anadhikāriṇaḥ hātum iti bhāvaḥ te api prakṛta uktikaḥ avipralambhakaḥ yathākāla sphūrtikaḥ anākṣepakaḥ yukti siddha saṃpratyayī ca iti pañca vāde upādeyāḥ viparyayeṇa heyāḥ evam bhūtāḥ ca viṣya ādayaḥ eva prāyeṇa iti te eva uktāḥ evam ca sati heyān vihāya yaḥ yathābhūtaḥ sa tathābhūtena vaktum arhati tathā sati kathā mahā vākya siddhau phala siddheḥ na hi yuyutsuri raṃsū pratipadya ciram asiddham saṃbhūya samīhitam sādhayataḥ yathoddeśam iti tattva pratipatti hetu tvāt vādasya ādau= uddeśaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^7	 vārttikam upaveśayitum pīṭham āracayati tad anavasāyāt iti evam iti atideśa artham āha na vicāram iti śruti vyavacchedya tayā vitaṇḍām tāvat vyavacchinat tiyat yapi iti tātparya vyavacchedya tayā idānīm jalpam vyavacchinatti yadi api ca iti pramāṇa mūlaiḥ pramāṇa mūla abhimataiḥ niyamena iti śeṣaḥ nābhi prāya niyamaḥ śrūyate iti atas āha yathā ca etat iti sādhane ca tarkasya pramāṇa apekṣā upālambhe tu kevalaḥ api samarthaḥ pratitarka pratihatasya asādhana tvāt āgāminam bhāva sādhana tva svīkāram iva dṛṣṭvā prāha ubhayathā iti 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^8	 tad gata ākṣepaḥ tu uddeśaḥ eva pramāṇa tarka śabdasya sādhana upālambha śabda vat sva vācaka lakṣaṇayā vā śabda avāntara vyāpāra tayā vā śabda pratipādita tayā vā samarthita prāyaḥ tatas siddha vat āha yada tu iti aparādha pratipādanam hi upālambhaḥ na ca acetanaḥ aparādhyati na api pratipādyate kim puruṣaḥ tat idam uktam puruṣa dharma upālambha iti karma karaṇayoḥ hi pradhāna vyāpāraḥ phalam ekam eva tad dvārā ca viṣayaḥ prakṛte karma karaṇayoḥ api karma eva iyān= tu viśeṣaḥ yat karma tvadaśāyām śabda ādeḥ anitya tvam dharmaḥ karma karaṇayoḥ api karma eva 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^9	 iyān= tu viśeṣaḥ yat karma tvadaśāyām śabda ādeḥ anitya tvam dharmaḥ jijñāsita tayā viṣaya tvadaśāyām tu vastutayā iti āśayavān yathā aśruta vārttika anurodhena vyācaṣṭe dharmī iti anyathā tu viṣayaḥ śakti viṣayaḥ śakyam kāryam iti yāvat iti evam api sugamam etat atra hi jalpe nigraha sthāna viniyogāt ityādi bhāṣye na hiṃsyāt sarva bhūtāni iti vat vāde sarva nigraha sthāna pratiṣedhe agnīṣomīyam paśum ālabheta iti vat siddhānta aviruddhaḥ ityādi viśeṣa vidhiḥ iti arthaḥ sphuṭaḥ pratīyate 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^10	 vārtikakāraḥ tu rāgataḥ sarva pañca nakha bhakṣaṇa prāpti vat upālambha grahaṇāt sarva nigraha sthāna prāptau pañca pañcanakhāḥ bhakṣyāḥ iti vat parisaṃkhyāna artham uttara pada ārambhaḥ iti vyākhyātavān tat etat ati kuśala tayā mithas avirodhayan= āha jalpaḥ iti tathā api niyama arthe iti asaṃgatam pākṣika vyavaccheda phalaḥ hi niyamaḥ na ca atra apratibhā ādi pākṣikam upālambha padena nirāśaṅkam eva pratipādita tvāt iti atas āha niyamaḥ parisaṃkhyā iti ayam arthaḥ yadi api vidhiḥ atyantam aprāptau niyamaḥ pākṣike sati tatra ca anyatra ca prāptau parisaṃkhyā iti kīrtyate 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^11	 iti bhedaḥ darśitaḥ tathā api alpīyā anayam iti manyamānena parisaṃkhyāyām api niyama padam prayujyate itara vyavaccheda lakṣaṇasya phalasya aviśiṣṭa tvāt iti iha vāde caturdhā nigraha sthāna gatiḥ kiñcid asaṃbhāvanīyam eva yathā hāniḥ sannyāsaḥ nirarthakam artha antaram avijñāta artham apārthakam iti ṣaṭkam kiñcid saṃbhavat api anudbhāvyam eva yathā pratijñāntaram hetu antaram ajñānam apratibhā vikṣepaḥ mata anujñā paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam iti saptakam kiñcid tu udbhāvya mātram yathā virodhaḥ aprāpta kālam nyūnam adhikam punar uktam ayathā anubhāṣaṇam apasiddhāntaḥ iti saptakam 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^12	 kiñcid ca kathā avasānikam yathā hetvābhāsaḥ niranuyojya anuyogaḥ ca iti dvayam iti tatra hāni ādīnām aśakti saṃguhana prakāra tvāt tattva bubhut sutayā ca vāde tad abhāvāt teṣām asaṃbhavaḥ saṃbhavatām anudbhāvane hetum āha na khalu iti kathām aparyavasāyayatām api udbhāvane hetum āha adhikam tu iti tattva pratipatteḥ sākṣāt vyāghātaḥ viparīta pratipattiḥ yathā hetvābhāsān udbhāvane niranuyojya anuyoga anudbhāvane ca pāramparya vyāghātaḥ vyāsaṅga ādīnā tad sāmagrī pratirodhaḥ tatra adhika an udbhāvane prathamaḥ yadi na syāt tathā api dvitīyaḥ syāt eva 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^13	 tathā hi virodhe yogyatā virahaḥ aprāpta kāle ākāṅkṣā virahaḥ nyūne ākāṅkṣita asam abhivyāhāraḥ sa ca anāsakti viśeṣaḥ adhike anākāṅkṣita samabhivyāhāraḥ punarukte api evam saḥ api ākāṅkṣā viraha viśeṣaḥ ayathā anubhāṣaṇe uktā pratisandhānam apasiddhānte saṃmukha pramāṇa bādha ākrāntiḥ iti ākāṅkṣā yogya tā sattimattayā pratisaṃhitam pramāṇa antara apratihatam ca vākyam tattva pratipatteḥ aṅgam na anyathā tasmāt etat artham idam udbhāvyam iti tat etat sarvam abhiprāyam niyamayataḥ sūtrakārasya saṃmatam sūtrāt eva ca labhyate 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^14	 vārttika kṛtā tu nyūna ādi catuṣṭayam udāharaṇa artham darśitam na tu niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ iti vyājena darśayati tathā ca iti nanu vyatisaṅgaḥ vyatihāraḥ sa ca sādhana upalambhavān iti etāvatā eva ukte gamyate tatas pramāṇa tarka grahaṇam atiricyate iti atas āha pūrvasmin= iti tathā api asmin pakṣe kim asya prayojanam iti atas āha sādhana upālambha viśeṣaṇāya ca iti anuvidheya stheya sabhyapuruṣavatī janatā sabhā iti ucyate tatra anuvidheyasya yathāśakti yathā niyamam saṃmāna asaṃmāna vyañjakam karma na etat vāde tatra hi tattva bubhut sutayā svayam avātattva jñaḥ tattva jñāninam upāsīta 
NVTP_1.2.1.1^15	 stheyānām tu vāda sthāna kathā viśeṣa vyavasthāpanam pūrva uttaravāda sthāpanam vivadamānayoḥ guṇa doṣa avadhāraṇam bhagna prativādi prabodhanam loke niṣpanna kathā phala pratipādanam ca karmāṇi etad artham ca tatra prāśnika upayogaḥ yat vādinau kāraṇa graheṇa evam kartum aśaktau na ca evam vāde tatra tayoḥ eva vīta rāga tayā śakta tvāt ityāśayavān āha na vāde prāśnikānām iti tat kim parivarjanam eva tatra teṣām na iti āha daiva āgatānām tu iti sa vādena prāmādika kathā ābhāsa śaṅkām apanetum natu ukta karmāṇi kārayitum iti bhāvaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.2.1–1.2.2.2^1	 yathā ukta upapannaḥ chala jāti nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ ubhaya sādhana vat tva sādharmyāt vāda anantaram jalpa uddeśa siddhiḥ tad siddhau satyām saṃgatim āha uddeśa iti nanu jalpasya ubhaya sādhana vat tva asaṃbhavāt na vitaṇḍa avyavacchedaḥ tathā hi yadi pūrva sādhanam dūṣitam nigṛhītaḥ tarhi vādī jitam dvitīyena nivṛttā kathā na dūṣitam ced uttara ābhāsa vacanena ca avacanena ca nigṛhītaḥ tarhi dvitīyaḥ jitam prathamena nivṛttā kathā iti na asti dvitīya sādhana avasaraḥ iti na etat evam yathā hi vāde sva sādhana sthitau para sādhana nivṛttau ca tattva nirṇayaḥ na viparyaye tathā jalpe api sva sādhana sthitau para sādhana nivṛttau ca vijayaḥ viparyaye bhaṅgaḥ ubhaya sthiti nivṛttyoḥ pariṣad eva vijayate 
NVTP_1.2.2.2^2	 tat ayam jalprapavṛtti kramaḥ vādini sādhana mātram prayujya saṃkṣepataḥ vistarataḥ vā ābhāsān uddhṛtya virate sati ucyamāna grāhya nigraha aprāptau ābhāsa bahirukta grāhya nigraha alābhe tad vacana artham avagamya ānūdya dūṣayitvā prativādī sva pakṣe sthāpanām prayuñjīta aprayuñjānaḥ tu dūṣita para pakṣaḥ api na vijayī ślādhyaḥ tu syāt ātmānam arakṣan para ghātī iva vīraḥ tasmin= api evam virate sati anukta ucyamāna grāhya nigraha alābhe tat vavacanam avagamya anūdya dūṣaṇa aṅgam prati dūṣya ābhāsa bahis ukta grāhya nigraha alābheda prathama vādī sthāpana aṃśam dūṣayet adūṣayaṃsatu rakṣita sva pakṣaḥ api na vijayī ślādhyaḥ tu syāt vañcita para prahāraḥ iva tam apraharamāṇaḥ anukta ucyamāna grāhya ābhāsa bahis ukta grāhya nigraha lābhe tu tāvatā eva kathā viratiḥ na sādhana vicāra avakārśaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.2.2^3	 śara sandhāna samayaḥ eva yaḥ mūrcchitaḥ tad vāṇa vāraṇa tad praharaṇa anuṣṭhāna vat viphala tvāt tatra anukta grāhyam apratibhā ādi ucyamāna grāhyam aprāpta kāla ādi ābhāsa bahis ukta grāhyam pratijñā virodha ādi eṣu asatsu ābhāsa cintā tatas punar pratidūṣaṇa uktau ābhāsa bahis pratijñāhānyādi etat ca pañcame prapañcanīyam iti yadi api nigraha sthāna padena aviśeṣāt sarva prāptau siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ iti pada dvaya atideśaḥ mandaḥ tathā api gorbalīvarda nyāyena api yathā śruta bhāṣya upapattau kṛtam tad bhāṅgena iti manyamānaḥ bhāṣyam vārttikena samañjasayan= āha ukta mātram ityādi 
NVTP_1.2.2.2^4	 yadi api aparādha saṃgūhana artham pratijñāhāni pratijñā antara pratijñā saṃnyāsa hetu antara artha antara nirarthaka avijñāta artha vikṣepa apa siddhāntānām upādānam saṃbhavati tathā api na sarva nigraha upādāna saṃbhavaḥ api ca pramāda skhalite api chala ādibhiḥ eva pratyavasthātum ucitam nigraha sthāna apekṣayā teṣām anudbhaṭa aparādha tvāt tasmāt udbhāvyatayā eva amīṣām sarveṣām avatāraḥ tathā ca na ayukta tvam iti abhiprāyavān āha tat kim iti sādhu sādhana upādāne ca vādinā kṛtaḥ iti upalakṣaṇam pareṇa sādhu sādhana upādāne ca kṛtaḥ iti api draṣṭavyam nanu bhāṣyam dūṣayitvā kim adhikam ami hitam tena api tattva rakṣaṇa artha tva pratipādanāt iti ataḥ āha tat anena prakāreṇa iti prakāre bhāṣyam asaṃgatam na tu prayojane tatas tat api evam eva na iyam iti chala ādi vyutpādanam prayojyatayā iti śeṣaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.3.1–1.2.3.2^1	 sa pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ vitaṇḍā nanu vitaṇḍāyāḥ pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīna tvam asaṃgatam eka sādhana tāyām puruṣa śakteḥ api anirūpaṇāt tathā tve vā kṛtam jalpena prayāsa bahulena antatas sat pratipakṣa tayā api dvitīya sādhana praveśāt na etat evam puruṣa śakti nirūpaṇa aviśeṣe api jalpe pratyavekṣā parāghāta ubhaya gocara śakti nirūpaṇāt kṛta vidya kṣatriya dvaya yuddha vat vitaṇḍāyām tu daśaratha daśānana tanayatamasi vamīyuddha vat kāka ulūka yuddha vat vā ekasya sva pratyavekṣā śaktiḥ aparasya parāghāta naipuṇam nirūpyate 
NVTP_1.2.3.1–1.2.3.2^2	 katham ayam viśeṣaḥ iti ced vādinoḥ abhiprāya vaśāt anuvidheya stheya anurodhāt vā iti na kiñcid etat dvitīya sādhana praveśa satu dūṣaṇa tayā na pratiṣidhyate api tu sthāpanā tvena na ca ayam niyamaḥ asiddha tvāt udbhāvanena api kathā paryavasānāt iti samākhyā nirvacana sāmarthyāt eva gamyate iti na ca evam astu iti vācyam jalpe api para pakṣāghātasya gata tvena ati vyāpaka tvāt mātra grahaṇāt tu tad nivṛttiḥ iti ced na tena sādhana anivṛtteḥ tatra sādhana upālambha samudāye dūṣaṇa mātram vitaṇḍa iti evam api upapatteḥ iti 
NVTP_1.2.4.1^1	 evam kathā prakaraṇam samarthi matam tasyāḥ ca śarīram sādhanam dūṣaṇam ca tatra sādhana vādinā prathamatas tad ābhāsa parihāre dūṣaṇa vādinā api sat uttara parigrahe yatnavatā bhavitavyam sat uttara alābhe hi asat uttara avatāraḥ iti śikṣā artham hetvābhāsāḥ prathamam chala ādibhyaḥ uddiṣṭāḥ iti sā eva saṃgatiḥ iha api iti āha uddeśa iti atra triṣoḍaśyām vyāpaka avyāpaka bhedena yā dvi ṣoḍaśī sā asiddha viśeṣaṇa asiddha viśeṣyā samartha viśeṣaṇā samartha viśeṣya sandigdha viśeṣaṇa sandigdha viśeṣya bhedena vivakṣitāḥ dvānavatam śatam bhavati iti sā eva asiddhi sandehayoḥ vādi prativādi saṃbandhāt aṣṭāviṃśatam śatam bhavet sā eva anyatarā siddhyā vyadhikaraṇa samartha sandigdha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhedāt dvāvanatam śatam aparam syāt 
NVTP_1.2.4.1^2	 sā eva umayāni atara āśraya asiddha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya saṃbandhāt aparam aṣṭāviṃśatam śatam bhavet sā eva āśraya asiddha viśeṣaṇa avyadhikaraṇā samartha sandigdha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya saṃbandhāt aparam dvānavatam śatam sā eva sandigdha vyadhikaraṇa asamartha sandigdha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya saṃbandhāt aparam dvānavatam śatam iyam eva āśrayā siddhi prakṣepeṇa aparam dvānavatam śatam sā eva sandigdha tām parityajyānyathā siddhim upādāya aparam dvānavatam śatam iyam eva āśrayā siddhi prakṣepeṇa aparam dvānavatam śantam sā eva anyathā siddhim vihāya viruddha tām upādāya aparam dvānavatam śatam atra eva punar āśraya asiddhim prakṣipya aparam dvānavatam śatam iti 
NVTP_1.2.4.1^3	 saḥ ayam asiddha viruddha anaikāntikānām prapañcaḥ prakaraṇa samam prapañcayitum vastu gatim tāvat āha iti āha tat na iti antatas iti agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa daśāyām iti arthaḥ kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa ḥ tu uddeśaḥ eva prapañcitaḥ iti atra ca atīta kālaḥ mandatama prayogaḥ kāla abhāvāt yasya hi avasaraḥ na asti tasya artha kriyā prati vicārataḥ sattvam na asti iti mandatara prayogaḥ tu asiddhaḥ sati sva kāle svayam eva abhāvāt yaḥ tu svayam eva na asti tasya deśa kāla avasthā virodha sāmarthānām na avakāśaḥ manda prayogaḥ tu sat pratipakṣaḥ satoḥ kāla deśavat tvayoḥ avasthā bhāvāt avasthā bhāve avirodha sāmarthyayoḥ anavakāśāt sa avakāśa prayogaḥ tu viruddhaḥ kāla deśa avasthāsu satīṣu virodhāt 
NVTP_1.2.4.1^4	 yaḥ tu evam tasya kutas sāmarthyam prāyas prayogaḥ tu savyabhicāraḥ kāla deśa avasthā virodheṣu satsu sāmarthya mātra abhāvāt iti anena hetunā savyabhicāra ādi krama uddeśaḥ yat vā sugrahaḥ savyabhicāraḥ viccheda mātra siddhau tad siddheḥ upadarśita viparīta grahaṇe tad siddhiḥ yatna grāhyaḥ vireddhaḥ atiyatna grāhyaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ tad itara samasta rūpa sampannam anyat apanīya tad siddheḥ durgrahaḥ asiddhaḥ asiddha āśrayaḥ api kaścid hetuḥ iti parama tanirākaraṇa avaṣṭambhena tad siddheḥ durgrahataraḥ kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ bādhakasya ananyathā siddhyā prāmāṇyam vyavasthāpya tad siddheḥ iti tad vivakṣayā krama niyamaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.2.5.1^1	 nanu vibhāga sūtre savyabhicāraḥ iti uddiṣṭam padam iha māṣyakāraḥ lakṣaṇa tvena eva vyācaṣṭe evam ca uddiṣṭam na lakṣitam lakṣitam ca na uddiṣṭam iti atas āha atra ca iti tathā api lakṣaṇe vaktavye pada niruktiḥ kva upayujyate iti atas āha etat uktam bhavati iti kim tu ekasmin= ante yaḥ niyataḥ iti anvayataḥ vyatirekataḥ vā sādhyena eva sahacaritaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti arthaḥ tad viparyayāt anaikāntikaḥ aniyataḥ sādhyena eva sahitaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ ubhaya pakṣa gāmī iti yāvat iti ubhaya pakṣa prasañjakaḥ iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.5.1^2	 etena sādhāraṇa asādhāraṇa anupasaṃhāryāḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ iti sphuṭam bodha ābhāsa prasañjitām ati vyāptim anena vyākhyānena vyudastām āha na ca evaṃbhūtā etat ca tatra tatra vakṣyate tat evam iti anaikāntika pada vat sa vyabhicāra padam api vyākhyeyam iti arthaḥ nanu etāvatā eva sarvam vyākhyātam tat kim aparam avaśiṣyate yad artham sarvaḥ ayam ityādi vārtikam iti atas āha avagatam iti na nu anyatra prameyāt iti asaṃgatam sādhya tad viparyayau hi anta dvayam na ca tat asya na asti atha ayam arthaḥ na tatra ayam anvayataḥ vyatirekataḥ vā niyataḥ iti 
NVTP_1.2.5.1^3	 tathā api na ayam eva evaṃbhūtaḥ sarveṣām eva anaikāntikānām evaṃrūpa tvāt tat asya eva varjanam anupapannam udāharaṇa mātra artha tvāt na doṣaḥ iti api na yuktam nityaḥ ca anityaḥ ca ityādi saṃgrāhya koṭau= anaikāntikasya apradarśanāt iti ataḥ āha prameya padārthasya tu iti tat ayam vārttika arthaḥ kaścid dharmaḥ sarvasyaprameya tva ādi lakṣaṇaḥ kaścid kasyacid eva nitya tva ādi lakṣaṇaḥ tatra sarvasya vā kasyacid vā yaḥ dharmaḥ hetu tayā upāttaḥ ubhau= antau sādhya dharma tad viparyayau āśritya prasajya pravartate dharmiṇi saḥ anaikāntikaḥ iti vyatirekya vyatirekitayā dharma dvaividhya pradarśanena anaikāntikasya viṣaya vivecanam sūcitam vyatirekiṇī ā iva hi dharme sādhye anaikāntikaḥ saṃbhavat prayogaḥ na tu avyatirekiṇi na nu paryudāsa abhiprāyeṇa eva prāk vyākhyātam tat katham tat pratiṣedhaḥ iti atas āha paryudāsa pakṣaḥ iti tathā api na abrāhmaṇaḥ iti prasajya pratiṣedha udāharaṇam na hi go ghaṭā dau= abrāhmaṇaḥ iti vaktāraḥ bhavanti api tu kṣatriya ādau= ityāha na punar ityādi su bodham 
NVTP_1.2.6.1–1.2.6.2^1	 siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ sūtre samāna kartṛka tva abhāvāt ktvā apratyaya anupapattyā śabda doṣam āha na khalu iti artha doṣam āha na ca pakṣaḥ iti upalakṣaṇa ca etat etasmin sati virodha apasiddhāntau nigraha sthāne niravakāśe tayoḥ satorayam vā mīmāṃsaka abhimataḥ viśeṣa virodhaḥ api viruddha syāt iti api abhyupagama iti siddhānta śabdena atra pakṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ atas na prakṛta hānam na api apasiddhānta vaiyarthyam iti arthaḥ viśeṣa viruddha prasaṅga nivārayati viśeṣa iti abhyupetya iti anena pratijñāya iti vivakṣitam na tu abhipretya iti na ca viśeṣaḥ pratijñāyate api tu abhipreyate na ca tathābhūtena virodha upalambha saṃbhavaḥ asiddhidaśāyām anupambhena siddhidaśāyām saha upalambhena anavasara parāhata tvāt 
NVTP_1.2.6.2^2	 evaṃbhūtasya abhiprāya gocara tvam api katham iti api na yuktam sva artha anumāna samaye prakṛta upapādaka tayā tad siddheḥ anupapādakaḥ tu viśeṣaḥ na sidhyati atas eva nābhi prāya gocaraḥ api tadā api katham sarvathā anupalabdha caraḥ sidhyati iti api na vācyam ākāṅkṣa ādi saṃpattau padārthānām iva apūrva artha pratipādane vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā māhātmyasya apahnotum a śakyatvāt tasmāt yayoḥ eva paraspara dharmi parihāreṇa niyamavatoḥ sthiti rūpalabhyate tayoḥ eva virodhaḥ na anyathā iti arthaḥ anuktaḥ ca saṃgṛhītaḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham iti atas āhar idṛśam vyākhyānam iti syāt etat virodhe hi hetuḥ na syāt sādhya vā ādye asiddhaḥ eva dvitīye tu kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kva idānīm viruddhaḥ anyatarā niścaye api sandigdhā asiddhaḥ iti āśakṅkya uktam vārttika kṛtā yasmāt ami upagatam bādhataḥ iti na asiddhaḥ pakṣe niścita tvāt 
NVTP_1.2.6.2^3	 na api kāla atītaḥ pramāṇa antareṇa balavatā abādhanāt kim tu ayam eva sisādhayipitam bādhataḥ iti vārttika arthaḥ sugamaḥ eva dvitīyam vārttikam abhyupagatena bādhyate iti tat api yadi api pratijñā arthena tad bādhane asiddhaḥ syāt tathā api virodhasya eva yatra udbhaṭa tvam tatra tad ullaṅghanena prayatna sādhyam asiddha tvam na udbhāvyam eva daivataḥ tad pratīkāre niranuyojya anuyoga āpatteḥ viruddha dvāreṇa eva asiddheḥ api vyavasthāpane tad udbhāvanasya āvaśyaka tvāt ca iti sugamam uttara vārttika anurodhena tu vyācaṣṭe svarūpeṇa hetu tvena vā iti arthaḥ atra udāharaṇa bhāṣyam ityādi uktam iti arthaḥ iti antaṣṭīkāyām bhāṣyasya iti śeṣaḥ virodha nigraha sthānāt etasyām a idam āśaṅkya yathā parihṛtam vārttika kṛtā tad anurodhena vyākhyātam 
NVTP_1.2.6.2^4	 pratijña āśrita tvam iti virodha vaibhavena ca udāharaṇāni vārttike vastutas tu sva mate māna antara siddhasya arthasya anyathā vacanam apasiddhāntaḥ vākya aṃśayoḥ eka artha bhāva abhāva viṣaya tvena vyādhātī virodhaḥ viparyaya vyāpta tvena niścitaḥ viruddhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ sa ca vidhi sādhane svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ iti trividhaḥ tat yathā dhūmavān ayam yogyasya sataḥ tadvat tayā anupalabhyamāna tvāt niragnika tvāt jalāśaya tvāt iti niṣedha sādhane api svabhāva upalabdhiḥ vyāpya upalabdhiḥ iti dvividhaḥ tat yathā niragnikaḥ ayam tadvat tayā upalabhyamāna tvāt dhūmavat tavāt iti sarvaḥ ca ayam viśeṣaṇa dvārā api pratisandheyaḥ yathā kṛṣṇa aguruḥ āru prabhava vahnimānayam kaṭukā surabhi vipāṇḍura dhūmavat tvāt iti saṃkṣepaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.7.1–1.2.7.2^1	 yasmāt prakaraṇa cintā sa nirṇaya artham apadiṣṭaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ iha khalu hetvābhāsānām tat tya anusaṃhitānām yathāsaṃkhyam saṃśayaḥ vivakṣita viparīta jñānam jijñāsā ajñānam vyāpti bādhaḥ ca iti phalāni tatra phala dvārakam prakaraṇa sama lakṣaṇam upakramyateyasmāt ityādi tat etat bhāṣya mukhane vyācaṣṭe prakaraṇa iti yasmāt prakriyamāṇa artha jijñāsā mātram bhavati sa prakara samaḥ iti saṃkṣepaḥ tathā hi pakṣe sama bala bādhaka saha pravṛtteḥ na tattva nirṇayaḥ pratibalena pratiruddha tvāt na api tatas anusandhānena api sahasā vyāpti bādhaḥ anugṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tayā sama bala tvāt 
NVTP_1.2.7.2^2	 na api ajñānam eva pakṣe vidyamāna tayā eka koṭi prasañjaka tvāt na api viparīta jñānam tena avyāpteḥ na api sandehaḥ koṭi dvaya anupanāyaka tvāt tasmāt ekām koṭim upanayan sama balena pratiruddhaḥ katham atra nirṇayaḥ bhavatu iti jijñāsām janayan prakaraṇa samaḥ itarebhyaḥ bhidyate iti tat ca sat pratipakṣa tvam siddha ubhaya hetukam asiddha ubhaya hetukam siddha sādhya ubhaya hetukam ca prathamam arūpa dravya tva ulabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhāna tvayoḥ tṛtīyam śrāvaṇa tva kṛtaka tvayoḥ madhyamam iha udāhariṣyate tad anurodhena vyācaṣṭe sa khalu iti 
NVTP_1.2.7.2^3	 yadi api jijñāsā mātram atra upayoti tathā api saṃśaya anuvṛtti nivṛttyoḥ jijñāsā anuvṛtti nivṛttī iti mattvā uktam tatra sandigdhe tat vā jijñāsate iti nanu yatas eva jijñāsā katham tam eva prekṣāvān tattva nirṇayāya prayokṣyate iti atas āha vicitra abhisandhitayā iti pūrva samayaḥ duṣpratyayaḥ jātu prayojya buddhiḥ iti hi sādhana uttara ābhāsa prayoge hetavaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu eka eka pakṣa niyata tayā katham ubhaya pakṣa sāmyam anupalabdheḥ iti atas āha sā iyam iti nanu vyutpattim āśritya ced prakaraṇa sama padam pravartate kṛtam tarhi yasmāt ityādi lakṣaṇa antareṇa iti atas āha vyutpatti iti 
NVTP_1.2.7.2^4	 atha etat eva pravṛtti nimittam kim na syāt iti atas āha anyathā iti atra bhāṣya kāreṇa savyabhicārāt prakaraṇa samam bhedayatā tasya saṃśaya hetutvam asya ca prakaraṇa pravṛtti hetu tvam uktam tat ca saṃmugdham pakṣa pratipakṣau prakaraṇam iti prāc vyākhyānāt sūtra virodhāt ca na hi yasmāt prakaraṇam iti sūtram api tu yasmāt prakaraṇa cintā iti atas āha etat uktam bhavati iti api tu sat pratipakṣa tayā eva hetvābhāsa tvam iti jijñāsā mātra hetu tayā nirṇaya anutpādaka tvāt iti bhāvaḥ etena bhāṣye prakaraṇa śabdaḥ jijñāsā paraḥ iti uktam 
NVTP_1.2.7.2^5	 nanu nitya dharma anupalabdhiḥ kādācid kī vivakṣitā sa dātanī vā ādyā anaikāntikī a iva ākāśa ādau= api kadācid nitya dharma anupalabdheḥ dvitīyā tu asiddhā eva na hi nitya dharma upalabdhyā śabde kadācid api na bhavitavyam iti pramāṇam asti tathā ca asiddhatvam vihāya kutas prakaraṇa sama tvam udbhāvayati iti atas āha na ca tattva anupalabdhiḥ iti ayam arthaḥ yasya evam viśeṣa grahaḥ tasya tāvat asiddhaḥ eva ayam iti aḥ tu yaḥ tu upalambha abhāvena sulabhām anupalabdhim matvā viśeṣam apratisandhāya pratibalena ca pratibandham upanyasyati tam prati kim ayam ābhāsa tām yātu na vā 
NVTP_1.2.7.2^6	 na tāvat na yāti tathā sati sādhayet evam ca tatas agṛhīta viśeṣāḥ dvitīyā api sādhayet eva na ca evam na ca anābhāsam asādhaka mati prasaṅgāt na ca tadānīm doṣa antaram atra parisphurati anyatra pratibalena pratibandhāt iti yatra api yugapad aneka doṣa parisphuraṇam tatra api sat pratipakṣa tvam api udbhāvya viramyate na hi yāvat asti tāvat udbhāvyam anyatra saṃbhūya pratijñāyām sarvatra udbhāvana niyamāt iti yadi api pratyakṣa vat tattva anupalabdhiḥ api na kevalāḥ api tu samāna dharma darśana ādi sahitā eva saṃśaya kāraṇam 
NVTP_1.2.7.2^7	 tathā ca codya cuñcoḥ abhimata bhraṃsaḥ tathā api tam upekṣya sva siddhānta avarodhena pariharati na hi akāraṇānām iti nanu ubhaya iti ekasmin pakṣe ubhaya padam vihāya aparasmin vyāvṛtti dvāra iti padam adhyāhṛtya phakkikā bodhaḥ api tu tattva anupalabdhiḥ eva asmad uktā prakaraṇa sama udāharaṇam iti śeṣaḥ evam jijñāsā hetutva abhāvāt prakaraṇa sama lakṣaṇa ayogi tayā śarīrāt anya tvam na tat udāharaṇam iti uktam idānīm saṃśaya hetu tayā anaikāntika lakṣaṇa ayogāt tat udāharaṇam eva idam iti āśayavān āha iti āha itas ca iti 
NVTP_1.2.7.2^8	 kecid tu manyante tattva anupalabdhiḥ eva param prakaraṇa samaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ tad nirākaraṇam sūcayati evam anyāni api iti na agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa daśāyām anupalabdhyoḥ anyayoḥ vā dharmayoḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa daśāyām tu yathā anyasya anyatra hetvābhāse antarbhāvaḥ tathā anupalabdheḥ api iti sā api tyājyāḥ na ca anupalabdhyoḥ ātyantikam agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tvam ubhayoḥ siddha tve vastunaḥ ubhaya anubhaya ātmaka tva prasaṅgāt ekasya asiddha tve vā katham agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tvam ātyantikam ubhayoḥ api vāsta vyām asiddhau punar ubhaya anubhaya ātmaka tva prasaṅgāt iti 
NVTP_1.2.8.1–1.2.8.2^1	 sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhya tvāt sādhya samaḥ tasmāt sādhya tvāt asiddha tā iti sādhya tayā asiddha tayā sādhyena aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ sā ca asiddha tā kasyacid ityādi sugamam tat evam śiṣya pratipatti lāghavāya vākya gauravam vastutas tu asiddhaḥ sādhya samaḥ iti etāvat eva lakṣaṇam uktam asiddhaḥ iti asya api pakṣa dharma tayā na niścitaḥ iti arthaḥ parāmarśa viṣayaḥ pakṣa dharma tā sā ca sva sādhyena nirupādhi saṃbandhasya pakṣa saṃbandhaḥ tathā api ca vyāpti niścaya sahitena saṃbandhi dvaya niścayena niścīyate vyāpti liṅga pakṣeṣu tu ekatamā niścaye api na iti tatra pakṣā niścayāt āśraya asiddhaḥ liṅgasya eva aniścayāt sva rūpa asiddhaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^2	 vyāpteḥ aniścayāt anyathā siddhaḥ eteṣām ca aniścayaḥ sandehāt vā abhāva niścayāt vā iti na kaścid phalam prati viśeṣaḥ etena vyoma padmām sugandhi padmātvāt iti ādayaḥ api saṃgṛhītāḥ bhavanti anyathā yaḥ pakṣe asan= iti lakṣaṇena etat labhyate yathā hi asati sa pakṣe vipakṣe ca pratiṣedhaḥ kartu na śakyate tathā pakṣe api iti satyā eva iti satyena abhyupagatāyāḥ iti arthaḥ tasyāḥ nitya tva abhāvāt iti tat asiddham iti ced na kadācid upalambha lakṣaṇena api anitya tvena sādhya siddheḥ teṣām vyañjaka vaicitrye api vyakti āśraya saṃbandhinām upalambham antareṇa anupalambha niyamāt 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^3	 upalambhe vā tattva anupapatte sadā upalambha prasaṅgāt ca tejasā abhibhūta tvāt na tathā iti ced na āśraya anabhibhave teṣām anabhibhāvāt tad abhibhave tu teṣām upalambhe tad upalambha prasaṅgāt atas eva na bhā bhāvasya tat vyañjaka tvam tasmāt kadācid upalambhe eva asyāḥ sāmānya avirūpa tām pratikṣipati iti na api karma iti sva āśrayam prāc deśāt vibhajya deśa antaram prāpayat karma tat tāyām vyavatiṣṭhate na atas anyathā calana vyavahāra sya anākasmika tvāt anya nimitta abhāvāt evaṃbhūta artha anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt ca chāyāyāḥ tu āśrayaḥ eva tauvat na upalabhyate prāk eva tasya viprayojana saṃprayojane iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^4	 na guṇaḥ dravya asamavāyāt iti dravya asamavetam hi adravya samavetam vā asamavetam eva vā syāt ubhayathā api guṇave vyāghātaḥ sāmānyavataḥ svatantrasya dravya tva āpatteḥ niḥsāmānyasya guṇa lakṣaṇa vyāghātāt sāmānyavāna guṇaḥ ityādi hi tat guṇa karmaṇām nirguṇa tayā guṇasya tatra samavāya virodhena tad samavāye sāmānya rūpa tva upapatteḥ iti arthaḥ dravya asamavāyāt iti hetum sādhayati na manaḥ iti teṣām viśeṣa guṇa virahāt sāmānya guṇaḥ ayam bhavet tathā ca āśraya saha upalambha niyame tad apratyakṣa tāyām niyamāt apratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ iti arthaḥ na api ātma guṇaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^5	 iyam hi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣatā idantā sāmāna adhikaraṇyena vyāptā tad ātma guṇa tām ādāya nivartamānam anātma guṇa tāyām viśrāmyati iti arthaḥ na api nabhaḥ nabhasvatoḥ iti cākṣuṣataḥ hi guṇānām rūpi dravya samavāyena vyāptāḥ tat ca rūpi tvam gagana pavanābhyām vyāvartamānam cākṣuṣa guṇa saṃbandham api vyāvartayati iti arthaḥ na api tejasaḥ tad guṇa tvam hi pratītau tad avirodhi tvena vyāptam anyathā guṇinaḥ sva guṇa pratīti paripanthi tve guṇasya nitya anupalambha prasaṅgāt sati samavāye upalambha virodhāt asati samavāye ca asattvāt tat ca atas nivartamānam tad guṇa tvam api nivartayati iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^6	 tad sahacarita guṇa antara anupalabdheḥ ca iti ayam arthaḥ na tāvat chāyā tejasaḥ rūpam etat rūpasya śukla bhāsvara tu aniya mātṛ na ca indranīla prabhā rūpa vat āśrayaḥ vidhānāt tasmāt guṇa antaram eva idam tasya iti vācyam tathā ca cakṣuṣā upalabhyamānam na rūpam anantar bhāvya upalabdhum śakyate cakṣuṣaḥ tathā eva sāmarthya akalanāt iti atas eva iti ayam arthaḥ cakṣuḥ mātra grāhya tayā tāvat chāyā na guṇa antara tvena śaṅkā āspadam rūpam tu saṃbhāvyeta tat ca upalabhyamānam pāthasaḥ upalabhya śaitya drava tva ādi vyāptam atādṛśaḥ toya tva ayogāt pṛthivyāḥ tu upalabhya gandha ādi vyāptam atathābhūtasya pṛthivī tva ayogāt 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^7	 tat ca śaitya gandha ādi sāhacaryam atas nivartamānam anupalambhena tad guṇatām api nivartayati iti api ca iti ataijasa dravya rūpa grahaṇe hi bāhya āloka vyāptasya eva cakṣuṣaḥ sāmarthyam adhigatam na ca yat sahitasya yasya yatra sāmarthyam tat rahitena tena tad karaṇam tathā sati vahni rahitam api ārdram indhanam dhūmam vidadhyāt iti arthaḥ virodhakaḥ tu adhikaḥ iti āha tasmiḥ tu iti etena pārthivam rūpam āropitam tamaḥ iti nirastam bāhya āloka sahakāri virahe cakṣuṣaḥ tathā ārope api asāmarthyāt tat eva hi dharmi antare vā samāropyeta pitta pītim avat tatra eva vā niyata deśe avagamyamāne aniyata deśa tvam iti nedīyasi aṇīyasi api mahattva vat 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^8	 ubhayathā api tat prathamam antareṇa anupapattiḥ ekatra āropya tvāt anyatra āra upaviṣaya tvāt tasya eva na ca ālokam antareṇa rūpa grahaṇe cakṣuṣaḥ sāmarthyam iti uktam na cāra upya āropa viṣaya aprathane bhrānti saṃbhavaḥ na ca ubhayoḥ anyatarasmin= avyāpṛtasya eva cakṣuṣaḥ bhrānti janaka tvam na ca ayam acākṣuṣaḥ pratyayaḥ tad anvaya vyatirekayoḥ ananyathā siddha tvāt iti na api dravyam iti na pṛthivī agandha tvāt na jalamarasa tvāt na tejaḥ anuṣṇa tvāt na vāyuḥ asparśa tvāt nākāśam aśabda samavāyi kāraṇa tvāt na dikkālaḥ paratva aparatva asam avāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga anādhāra tvāt na ātmā buddhi anādhāra tvāt 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^9	 na manaḥ jñāna asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga anādhāra tvāt iti arthaḥ na api anyat iti na idam adravyam rūpi dravyam asmad ādi pratyakṣa tvāt asmad ādi pratyakṣam hi indriyeṇa vyāptam tat ca niyata viṣaya sāmarthyena vyāptam tat ca vipakṣān nivartamānam indriyam nivartayat pratyakṣa tvam api nivartayati iti arthaḥ asparśa tvāt iti na idam aneka dravyam dravyam asparśa tvāt asparśa tā hi dravyasya anārabhya tayā vyāptā sa ca niṣedhyāt aneka dravyān nivartamānā sva vyāpyam sparśa rahita tvam gṛhītvā tad viparīte viśrāmyati iti arthaḥ anārambhaka tvena iti avidyamānam ārabhbhakam yasya tat tathā uktam 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^10	 tasya bhāvaḥ tatvat tvam iti etena āśraya asiddhiḥ parihṛtāḥ yat tu uktam manasā dravya antara anārambhe vaiyarthyam upādhiḥ na punar asparśa tvam tat kim vaiyarthyāt anārambhaka tvam unnīyate anārambhakāt vā vaiyarthyam iti na tāvat ādyaḥ sarva utpattimat prayojanasya asmad ādibhiḥ piśita locanaiḥ anākalanāt tasmāt yadi ārambhaka svabhāva tvam manasaḥ tadā kadācid ārambhe prayojanam api kiñcid bhaviṣyati iti na ced tad svabhāvaka tvam prayojana sahasreṇa api na ārambhaḥ svabhāva anuvidhāyīni hi prayojanāni na tu prayojana anuvidhāyinaḥ svabhāvāḥ pratyakṣa bādhaḥ tu tadā syāt yadi tamaḥ eva apahnūyeta 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^11	 dravya tve pratyakṣasya ajāgaruka tvāt nīlima guṇa śālinaḥ pratīteḥ katham evam etat iti cetṛ na vastutas asya nīlatve acākṣuṣa tva prasaṅgāt āloka sahakāriṇaḥ eva cakṣuṣaḥ tatra sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt iti uktam śukla bhāsvara virodhitā sāmyāt tu tathā vyavahāraḥ evam tarhi rakta ādi vyavahāraḥ api prasajyate iti ced na vyavahāre hi sati nimitta anusmaraṇāt na tu nimittām asti iti eva vyavahāraḥ yathā śaṣayoḥ śavī avahāraḥ gauḍānām varṇa tva nimitta aviśeṣe api na ka ādi vyavahāraḥ adṛṣṭa ādi sāmagrī viśeṣāt niyamaḥ na atra api daṇḍa vāritaḥ iti tat kim na kiñcid evat chāyā iti atas āha tasmāt bhā bhāvaḥ evat chāyā iti 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^12	 na ca vācyam saḥ api katham ālokam antareṇa pratiyogi smaraṇa adhikaraṇa grahaṇa virahe vidhi mukhena cākṣuṣaḥ viṣayaḥ iti yat grahe hi yat apekṣam cakṣuḥ tad abhāva grahe api tad apekṣam eva evam hi tad itarasām agrahī sākalyam syāt tat iha api āloka abhāve tad āloka apekṣā syāt yadi āloke api tad apekṣā bhavet na ca etat asti pratyuta virodhaḥ eva tasmin sati hi tad abhāvaḥ eva na syāt kim tad sāpekṣeṇa cakṣuṣā gṛhyeta divā ca pratiyoginaḥ prabhā maṇḍalasya grahe eva pradeśa antare tat grahaṇam iti na kiñcid anupapannam anyadā api na rātrim apratisandhāya andhakāra grahaḥ rātri jñānam ca na diva sam apratisandhāya 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^13	 tathā hi nirasta etat dvīpa varti ravi raśmi jālaḥ kāla viśeṣaḥ atra rātriḥ iti ucyate giridarī vivara vartinaḥ tu yadi yoginaḥ na timira alokinaḥ timira darśinaḥ ced nūnam smṛta ālokāḥ iti adhikaraṇam api dṛṣṭam anumitam smṛtam vā iha idānīm andhakāraḥ iti pratyayāt vidhi mukhaḥ tu pratyayaḥ asiddhaḥ na hi na aprayoga mātreṇa vidhi tvam pralaya vināśa avasthāna ādiṣu vyabhicārāt na artha antarbhāvena vākya arthe pada prayogāt adoṣaḥ iti ced iha api mātsaryam apanīyaḥ eṣā eva rītiḥ anugamyatām iti suṣṭhu upa saṃhṛtam tasmāt bhā bhāvaḥ evat chāyā iti deśa antara prāptimat tva prayuktam hi gatimat tvam 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^14	 na tu deśa antara darśana prayuktam tat ca prayojakam iha niścita vyāvṛtti tathā hi svātantrayeṇa deśa antara prāptau vāraka anuvidhāna niyamaḥ na syāt prabhā tulya tve tejaḥ prabhā āśrayeṣu ratna viśeṣa iṣuc chāyā divase na syāt chāyayā eva abhibhave vā bahalatame tamasi teṣām ālokaḥ na syāt āloka antareṇa eva abhibhave chāyāyāḥ api udbhāvaḥ na syāt iti saṃkalayati sā iyam iti asiddhiḥ anirūpaṇam na ca etāvatā iti vācyam iti śeṣaḥ kutas savyabhicāra tvāt iti ayam arthaḥ yadi api tatra api svābhāvika saṃbandha virahāt asti eva hetu tva asiddhiḥ na hi asti saṃbhavaḥ svabhāva pratibaddhaḥ ca savyabhicāra ādiḥ ca iti 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^15	 tathā api na tāvat svarūpataḥ āśrayataḥ vā tatra asiddhiḥ udbhāvayitum śakyate tayoḥ niścita tvāt na api upādhitaḥ upādhi apekṣayā vyabhicāra ādeḥ laghu pratipattika tvāt upādheḥ tu tad dvārā eva pratipatteḥ yadi ca tena dūṣayitum na śakyate tad dvārā api apādhiḥ eva udbhāvyeta na ca etat asti vyabhicāra ādau hi udbhāvite sutarām nivartate upādhau tu kadācid vipratipadyate tasya durūha tvāt iti astu tarhi savyabhicāra vat aprayojakaḥ nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ tasya api evaṃrūpa viśeṣa śāli tvāt iti ataḥ āha anyathā siddhasya tu iti bhavet evam yadi aupādhika tvam svābhāvika saṃbandha virahāt anyatṛ 
NVTP_1.2.8.2^16	 na tu etat asti anaupādhika tvam hi saṃbandhasya svābhāvika tvam aupādhika tvam ca tad varahaḥ tasmāt viśeṣa antara abhāvāt sādhya sama samāna lakṣaṇavat tvāt ca tatra eva tasya antarbhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ bhāṣye gatimat tvāt iti sandigdhaḥ vārttike satī chāyā gatimatī deśa antare darśanāt iti viśeṣaṇa dvārāḥ āśraya asiddhaḥ ayam eva sattvam vihāya niścita upādhi saha vṛttiḥ anyathā siddhaḥ tat etāvantaḥ eva asiddha bhedāḥ iti bhrama nirāsa artham udāharati te ete iti cākṣuṣa tvāt iti niścita asiddhaḥ aśarīra tvāt iti dharmitaḥ eva āśraya asiddhaḥ maitra tanaya tvāt iti saṃndigdha upādhi saha vṛttiḥ anyathā siddhaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.9.1–1.2.9.2^1	 kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ atra yathā śruta bhāṣya vārttika darśanāt sarvam asamañjasam iti mattvā sva vyākhyām sthāna antarīya bhāṣya ādi upanyāsena saṃvadan= āha atra ityādinā anuṣṇaḥ ityādinā pratiṣedhya vidheya dharma grāhaka pramāṇa bādhaḥ darśitaḥ dharmi grāhaka pramāṇa bādhaḥ tu ghaṭaḥ vyāpakaḥ sattvāt ākāśa vat iti pratyakṣeṇa paramāṇuḥ sa avayavaḥ mūrta tvāt ghaṭa vat iti anumānena meruḥ pāṣāṇa mayaḥ parvata tvāt vindhya vat iti āgamena hetu grāhaka pramāṇa bādhaḥ tu jala anila āviṣṇau pṛthivītas viparīta sparśava tvāt tejaḥ vat iti pratyakṣeṇa manaḥ vibhu jñāna asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt ātma vat iti anumānena brāhmaṇasya rājasūyam karma svarga sādhana tvāt agniṣṭoma vat iti āgamena evam navavidhaḥ ayam ekavidha upamāna bādhena saṃkṣepataḥ daśavidhaḥ iti nanu bādhaḥ nāma na avinā abhāva bhaṅgāt aparaḥ kaścid saḥ api na trairūpya pracyavāt anyaḥ iti atas āha bādhā iti na hi bādham avyavasthāpya anaikāntika tvam apakṣa dharma tvam vā avatārayitum śakyam 
NVTP_1.2.9.2^2	 atas asya avaśya udbhāvyatayā avaśya abhyupagantavyaḥ anyathā virodham api na abhyupagacchet virodhe hi hetoḥ abhāve svarūpa asiddhiḥ sādhya abhāve apakṣa dharma tā durnivārāḥ atha virodhasya eva prathamam buddhau= upanipātāt tad udbhāvanam antareṇa pakṣa dharma tvasya udbhāvayitum aśakya tvāt ca saḥ avaśya abhyupagantavyaḥ tat etat samānam anyatra api iti uktam iti arthaḥ yadi evam bhāṣyam idānīm katham iti atas āha evam iti atha yadi ayam arthaḥ bhāṣya kārasya vivakṣitaḥ kim iti na etat anurūpam udāharaṇam iti atas āha atra ca iti tathā api aihikam udāharaṇam asaṅgatam iti atas āha para matena eva iti atha etat udāharaṇam sva mate pañca koṭiṣu kva antar bhaviṣyati iti atas āha sa punar iti tat kim iti na udbhāvayāṃbabhūvaḥ evam iti atas āha sthūlatayā iti vārttikam idānīm katham iti atas āha yasya apadiśyamānasya ityādi bhadantam pratyeka deśinaḥ parīhāraḥ samīkṛte abhidhānāt iti tat vivṛṇoti ayam arthaḥ iti 
NVTP_1.2.10.1	 evam yatnena udbhāvanīya pariharaṇīya hetu ābhāsava prakaraṇam samarthitam atha sādhana vādī pramādī prativādī vā sat uttara samādhānayoḥ aparisphūrtau tayoḥ vijigīṣuḥ tad ābhāsam api brūyāt iti tad ābhāsa vyutpādana avasaraḥ tatra api jāteḥ sva pakṣa vyāghāta āpādaka tvena jaghanya tvāt chalasya tu tātparyato duṣṭa tve api vacanataḥ aduṣṭattvāt asphūrti daśāyām api tat eva prayoktavyam tasya api asphūrtau jātiḥ iti viśeṣa jñāpana artham jāteḥ pūrvam chala uddeśaḥ sā eva lakṣaṇe api saṃgatiḥ iti bhāṣya artham āha uddeśa iti nanu ati vyāpakam idam lakṣaṇam artha vaicitrya upapattyā vacana vighātasya jātau= api saṃbhavāt iti atas āha yathā vaktuḥ iti iha vāc vṛtti viparyāsena pratyavasthānam na tu tatra iti bhedaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu vibhāgaḥ na udāhṛtaḥ tat katham vibhāge tu udāharaṇāni iti bhāṣyam iti atas āha vibhajyate iti 
NVTP_1.2.11.1–1.2.12.1^1	 yadi evam katham vibhāgaḥ ca iti kṛtvā vibhāga sūtram eva paṭhati iti atas āha vibhajyate anena iti ukti pūrvaka tvāt tātparyasya tad anusaṃdhāna pūrvaka tvāt upacārasya uddeśa kamaniyamaḥ tad anurodhāt ca lakṣaṇa krama niyamaḥ abhidhā vṛtti saṃcāraḥ yatrat chale tad vākchalam iti lakṣaṇa arthaḥ vācī iti viṣaya saptamī bhramam nivārayati vāci nimittaḥ iti nanu etat sarva= chala sādhāraṇam iti atas āha nava kambalaḥ ityādi tat idam vākchalam uttara daśāyām navavidham tat yathā bhūbhṛt ayam vīrya śālī mahā vayavat tvāt iti atra dharmi pada saṃcāreṇa na nakha prasūna āñcita kara pallavaḥ ayam nitya karma kara tvāt iti atra sādhya pada saṃcāreṇa atā garbhavatī rakta vilocana tvāt iti atra ubhaya pada sañcāreṇa tat etat pratijña āśrayam trayam āḍhyaḥ ayam nava kambala tvāt iti atra asiddha tva udbhāvanena gajaḥ ayam viṣāṇī tvāt iti atra virodha udbhāvanena durālokaḥ asau rājā tejaḥ maya tvāditi a tra anaikāntika tva udbhāvanena tat etat hetu āśrayam trayam 
NVTP_1.2.12.1^2	 duvyam vāyuḥ sāvayava tvāt ambara vat iti atra sādhana vikala tvena asmad ādi durāsadāḥ tārakāḥ gaganecara tvāt pataṅga vat iti atra sādhya vikala tvena paśuḥ eṣa viṣāṇi tvāt go vat iti atra ubhaya vikala tvena tat etat dṛṣṭantā śra trayam pratyuttara daśāyām tu pratipakṣa sādhane navavidham eva anyatra tu yāvat dūṣaṇa bhedam tat yathā anyathā siddhaḥ asiddhaḥ ca iti vyāghātaḥ katham api siddha tvāt sādhya viparyaya vyāptaḥ ayam iti guṇaḥ eva anyathā sādhya abheda prasaṅgāt ambareṇa anaikāntikam iti asaṅgatam tasya api anitya tvāt na ayam pakṣī kutas asya pakṣa bādha saṃbhāvanā ityādi svayam ūhyam asya pratyavasthānam ityādi bhāṣyam na pūrva sūtra vyākhyānam na uttara sūtra param vā iti atas āha tat etat chalam iti 
NVTP_1.2.13.1–1.2.13.2^1	 sambhavatoḥ athasya ati sāmānya yogāt asambhūta artha kalpanā sāmānyacchalam yatra tātparya saṃkrāntiḥ tat sāmānyacchalam iti sūtra arthaḥ tat ca kvacid saṃbhava vidhi viśeṣyeṣu yathā saṃbhavat vidyā caraṇa saṃpadayam brāhmaṇa tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ śatam dvijātayaḥ bhojitāḥ iti kvacid tu hetu tva uddeśa viśeṣaṇeṣu yathā brāhmaṇāt upajātaḥ ayam brāhmaṇa tvāt anityam kāryam dvija śatam bhojitam iti tat etat sarvam vivakṣitam āpnoti ca atyeti ca ubhaya samānam ca iti atisāmānyam ucyate etad nimittakam chalam sāmānyacchalam iti bhāṣya anurodhāt viśeṣa niṣṭham vyācaṣṭe saṃbhavate iti tatra ādyam udāharaṇam sphuṭam eva 
NVTP_1.2.13.2^2	 dvitīyam tu anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti ukte dhaṭaḥ api anityaḥ tarhi kṛtaka tvāt śabdaḥ syāt tṛtīyam tu śatam dvijātayaḥ bhojitāḥ iti ukte śata saṃkhyā avacchinnāḥ api bhojitāḥ sanaka ādayaḥ na dvijātayaḥ iti caturtham tu brāhmaṇāt jātaḥ ayam brāhmaṇa tvāt iti ukte saṃbhāvanā viṣayaḥ ayam abhihitaḥ na hetuḥ iti pañcamam tu anityam kāryam anitya tvāt iti ukte sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ hetuḥ iti ṣaṣṭham tu dvija śatam bhojitam iti ukte dvijāḥ bhojitāḥ na tu tad matā śata saṃkhyā iti evam pratyuttara daśāyām api etat ṣaḍvidham eva iti 
NVTP_1.2.14.1–1.2.14.2^1	 dharma vikalpa nirdeśer athasadbhāva pratiṣedhaḥ upacāracchalam upacāra vṛtti vyatyayaḥ yatra tat upacāra= chalam iti lakṣaṇa arthaḥ etat api uttare najavidham tat yathā ayam māṇavakaḥ siṃhaḥ ayam siṃhaḥ rājñaḥ ayam puruṣa siṃhaḥ rāja śārdūlasya iti pratijñām āritya trayam varṣāṣu nausaṃcāryā iyam bhūmiḥ gaṅgā tvāt ghoṣāṇām sukha vasati hetavaḥ te deśāḥ gaṅgā tvāt sa pradeśaḥ dhana kāśa ādi vanaḥ gaṅgā tvāt iti hetum āśritya trayam ye dhvani hetavaḥ te krośanti yathā mañcāḥ ye krośanti te dhvani hetavaḥ yathā mañcāḥ ye krośana prayojanavantaḥ te krośanti yathā mañcāḥ iti dṛṣṭāntam āśritya trayam pratyuttare tu pratisādhane tāvat eva 
NVTP_1.2.14.2^2	 anyatra tu yāvat doṣa bhedam tat yathā aśarīra tvāt iti hetuḥ ayam āśraya asiddhaḥ iti ukte na evam hetu āśrayasya ākāśasya siddha tvāt na ca hetuḥ asiddha tva ādīnā dūṣyate api tu liṅgam eva atas niranuyojya anuyogaḥ bhavataḥ ityādi dharma vikalpa nirdeśa śabdena abhidhāna dharmaḥ dvedhā abhidhīyate iti vārttika eka vākyatām āpādayitum bhūmim racayitvā yathāśruta bhāṣyam upekṣya khaṇḍa khaṇḍam vyācaṣṭe śabdasya iti dyayapi na iha sphuṭam tathā api ekatra vastu sadbhāvaḥ pratiṣidhyate na eva kroṣṭāraḥ mañcāḥ iti parīkṣā vārttikam anāgatam avekṣya āha vārttika mate tu iti 
NVTP_1.2.15.1–1.2.15.2	 vākchalam eva upacāra= chalam tat aviśeṣāt saṃgatiḥ hi dvedhā bhavavati antar bhāva lakṣaṇāḥ ānantarya lakṣaṇā ca tatra na tāvat pūrvā chala parīkṣā sūtrāṇām lakṣaṇasya adhyāya artha tvāt adhyāya anantarbhūtasya ca āhnika prakaraṇayoḥ antarbhāvāt parīkṣā tvena dvitīya ādau= eva antar bhāva arha tvāt ca na api uttarā ṣoḍhā api atra saṃbhāvyate smāraka abhāvena prasaṅga abhāvāt tayā vinā eva prakṛta siddheḥ upodghāta abhāvāt jāti nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇa avarodhena avasara abhāvāt uttara prabandham prati akāraṇa tvena hetu tva ayogāt chala parīkṣāyāḥ uttaratra avyavahāreṇa anirvāhaka tvāt chala parīkṣā jāti ādi lakṣaṇa sūtrāṇām prakṛta upayogi eka kārya ayogena tad nibandhanāya api saṃgateḥ abhāvāt iti atas āha parīkṣā parvaṇaḥ iti prāsaṅgikī saṃgatiḥ prasaṅgāḥ ca parīkṣā parva sannidhānena upodvalitaḥ iti arthaḥ pṛthak sūtraṇāt sādharmya sahitāyāḥ viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ ca saṃśaya parīkṣitam satsu vivacitam sugraham su pariharam chalam bhaviṣyati iti parīkṣā prayojanam sphuṭīkṛtya pūrva pakṣam āha yathā hi iti lakṣaṇa abhedāt eka tvam iti arthaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.16.1–1.2.17.2	 na tad artha antara bhāvāt na tad artha antara bhāvāt iti siddhānta sūtram tatra ca bhāṣyam anya artha antara kalpanā anyor atha sadbhāva pratiṣedhaḥ iti tat etat aviśadam artha antara kalpanāyāḥ ubhayatra api pūrva pakṣe darśita tvāt artha sadbhāva pratiṣedhaḥ tu yathā kathañcid sarva sādhāraṇaḥ anyathā vacana vidhāta tva lakṣaṇa kṣateḥ paramārthataḥ tu na kvacid api vārttikam tu ekatra dharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate anyatra dharmī iti etat ca asiddham na hi atra mañcāḥ eva dharmiṇaḥ pratiṣidhyante api tu kambala dharma saṃkhyā vat mañca dharmaḥ krośanam iha api pratiṣidhyate iti atas āha vidheyam vastu iti atra eva uttara śaṅkā antaram apanayati kim tu iti tat etat samādhānam prakṛta udāharaṇa apekṣam draṣṭavyam sarva vyāpakam tu mukhya upacāra vṛtti anugata tvena anayoḥ bhedakau niyatau dharmau= iti aviśeṣe vā kiñcid sādharmyāt eka= chala prasaṅgaḥ avi ṅgaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.18.1	 yadi api asat uttara tayā jāteḥ chala prakaraṇaḥ eva antarbhāvaḥ yuktaḥ tathā api pratijñāhāni ādeḥ nigraha sthānasya api tathā abhāvāt tām saṃgatim upekṣya artha dūṣaṇa tva abhiprāyeṇa prayogasya sāmyāt uttara prakaraṇaḥ eva antarbhāvaḥ tatra antarbhūtāyāḥ ca jāteḥ pṛthakkaraṇe uddeśaḥ eva prayojanam uktam pratijñāhāni ādi apekṣayā ca anudbhaṭa aparādha tayā para vyāmohana hetutvāt parājaya daśāyām prayoktavya tva jñāpana artham tasmāt prāc uddeśaḥ sā eva saṃgatiḥ iha api iti āha uddeśa iti chalasya samyak dūṣaṇasya ca iti upalakṣaṇam pratijñā ahāni ādeḥ iti api draṣṭavyam na ca chale iti upalakṣaṇam tathā eva tathā api samyak dūṣaṇasya avyudāsaḥ tasya api hetutaḥ vaidharmyeṇa hetvābhāsa sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthāna rūpa tvāt iti atas āha na ca iti ayam ca mātra śabda arthaḥ jātīnām avatāram vāde pratiṣedha tā asat uttara tva khyāpanena eva sūtra kṛtā sūcitaḥ bhāṣye jāti pada vyutpādana prayojanam darśayati jalpe hi iti 
NVTP_1.2.19.1–1.2.19.2^1	 vapratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ ca nigraha sthānam nigraha sthānena eva samasta kathā mudraṇāt arthataḥ asya paścāt abhidhānam tat kim iti atra saṃgati anusaraṇena iti āśayavān sūtram pratyāharati vipra nam iti yadi api loka vyavahāra kathā vyavahārayoḥ puruṣasya aparādhaḥ eva nigraha sthānam aparāddhaḥ hi nigraham śāstim khalīkāram prāpnoti anyatra loke śarīra viḍambanā kathāyām tu aparādha mātra udbhāvāna mātram anyatra vādinoḥ kāma cāraḥ aparādhaḥ ca kathāyām vipratipatti apratipatti bhāga dvaya paryavasitam tātkāli kam atattva jñānam eva tathā api tasya sva rūpeṇa udbhāvayitum aśakya tvāt nirartha ka apārthaka ādi sāmāna adhikaraṇyā anupapatteḥ ca tad unnayana upāya upalakṣaṇa tayā sūtram vyākhyātam tena kathāyām pravṛttayām vādinoḥ atattva jñāna jñāpikā kriyā nigraha sthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ etat ca pratijñāhāni ādi sāmāna adhikaraṇyena prayukta nigraha sthāna pada padārtha ālocanayā sva rūpeṇa śakya udbhāvana pratipādaka vārttika darśanāt ca sugamam bhāṣye api anantaram eva sphuṭībhaviṣyati 
NVTP_1.2.19.2^2	 syāt etat na pratipatteḥ virīta tvāt anyat kṛtsita tvam iti atas āha sūkṣma iti katham asau nigraha sthānam iti katham asau svarūpataḥ apratīyamānā eva sattā mātreṇa nigraha sthānam bhaviṣyati na hi apratītam eva para dāra dharṣaṇam nigrahāya paryāptam iti arthaḥ vipratipadyamānaḥ iti yatas vipratipadyamānaḥ prāpta parājayaḥ bhavati atas parājaya prāpti dvāreṇa unnetum śakyate atha parājaya prāptiḥ eva kā iti atas uktam nigraha sthānam pratijñāhāni ādi khalu spaṣṭam parājaya prāptiḥ iti bhāṣyam sphuṭam iti arthaḥ yadi api adhike vipratipatti apratipattī saṃbhavataḥ tad asaṃbhave nigraha sthāna tva anupapatteḥ tathā api vipratipanna vastu gocara tvena na tu tatra iti tad anigraha sthāna tva bhrama nivāraṇa artham asamāsa karaṇam iti arthaḥ adhikam nāma iti upalakṣaṇam punaruktam api draṣṭavyam dūṣyam vā iti āgāmi pakṣa apekṣayā vā śabdaḥ 
NVTP_1.2.20.1	 yathoddeśam iti yathoddeśa kramam bhavatu lakṣaṇam na tu lakṣaṇa kramānatikrameṇa parīkṣā bhaviṣyati prathamatas eva vyatikramāt iti atas āha yathālakṣaṇam yathāsvarūpam iti arthaḥ iti nanu evam sati prathama dvitīya sūtre tātparya antareṇa avaṣṭabdha tvāt na trividha śāstra pravṛtti antar bhāvinī ārthyā vṛttyā prathama sūtrasya uddeśa antarbhāve api dvitīya sūtram alagnakam asaṃgatika tvāt iti atas āha tasmāt iti aupodghātikyā saṃgatyā prathama uddeśam aṅgatam eva dvi toya sūtram arthāt śrutyā ca prayojana paratayā iti na prakaraṇa asaṃgatiḥ iti arthaḥ śeṣam sūbodham iti kīrtti ate iti kīrtitam tathā ca yathāyogam abhisaṃbandhaḥ iti sukha bodham iti arthaḥ anabhyāsa jñeyāt śruti vivara garbheṣu laghutaḥ sukha grāhyān mandaiḥ kusuma sukumārāt prathamatas manaḥ śrīmat vācaspati vacana vinyāsa visarāt trasatya dyāpi etat muhur iva muhur nirvṛtam api
